Matthew1:1 Ugwalo lokuzalwa kukaJesu Kristu. 
Matthew1:2 UAbrahama wazala; 
Matthew1:3 uJuda wasezala uFaresi loZara kuTamari; uEsiromu wasezala uAramu; 
Matthew1:4 uAramu wasezala uAminadaba; uAminadaba wasezala uNashoni; uNashoni wasezala uSalimoni; 
Matthew1:5 uSalimoni wasezala uBowosi kuRahabi; uBowosi wasezala uObedi kuRuthe; uObedi wasezala uJese; 
Matthew1:6 uJese wasezala uDavida inkosi; 
Matthew1:7 uSolomoni wasezala uRehobhowamu; uRehobhowamu wasezala uAbhiya; uAbhiya wasezala uAsa; 
Matthew1:8 uAsa wasezala uJehoshafathi; uJehoshafathi wasezala uJoramu; uJoramu wasezala uOziya; 
Matthew1:9 uOziya wasezala uJothamu; uJothamu wasezala uAhazi; uAhazi wasezala uHezekhiya; 
Matthew1:10 uHezekhiya wasezala uManase; uManase wasezala uAmoni; uAmoni wasezala uJosiya; 
Matthew1:11 uJosiya wasezala uJekoniya labafowabo. 
Matthew1:12 Kwathi emva kokuthunjelwa eBhabhiloni uJekoniya; 
Matthew1:13 uZerubhabheli wasezala uAbiyudi; uAbiyudi wasezala uEliyakhimi; uEliyakhimi wasezala uAzori; 
Matthew1:14 uAzori wasezala uZadoki; uZadoki wasezala uAkimi; uAkimi wasezala uEliyudi; 
Matthew1:15 uEliyudi wasezala uEleyazare; uEleyazare wasezala uMathani; uMathani wasezala uJakobe; 
Matthew1:16 uJakobe wasezala uJosefa indoda kaMariya, okwazalwa kuye uJesu othiwa nguKristu." 
Matthew1:17 Ngakho izizukulwana zonke ezisukela kuAbrahama zisiya kuDavida ziyizizukulwana ezilitshumi lane; lezisukela kuDavida ziye ekuthunjelweni eBhabhiloni ziyizizukulwana ezilitshumi lane; lezisukela ekuthunjelweni eBhabhiloni ziye kuKristu ziyizizukulwana ezilitshumi lane. 
Matthew1:18 Ngakho ukuzalwa kukaJesu Kristu kwaba nje. 
Matthew1:19 Kodwa uJosefa indoda yakhe engolungileyo. 
Matthew1:20 Kwathi esanakana lezizinto, khangela, ingilosi yeNkosi yabonakala kuye ephutsheni, yathi: Josefa, ndodana kaDavida, ungesabi ukumthatha uMariya umkakho. Ngoba lokho akukhulelweyo kungoMoya oNgcwele;" 
Matthew1:21 njalo uzazala indodana. 
Matthew1:22 Konke lokhu-ke kwenzeka ukuze kugcwaliseke okwakhulunywa yiNkosi ngomprofethi ukuthi: 
Matthew1:23 Khangela, intombi izathatha isisu ibelethe indodana, njalo bazabiza ibizo layo ngokuthinguEmanuweli, okuyikuthi ngokuphendulelwa, uNkulunkulu ulathi." 
Matthew1:24 Kwathi uJosefa esephapheme ebuthongweni wenza njengalokho ingilosi yeNkosi imlayile, wasethatha umkakhe;" 
Matthew1:25 kodwa kazange amazi waze. 
Matthew2:1 Kwathi uJesu esezelwe eBhethelehema yeJudiya, ensukwini zikaHerodi inkosi," 
Matthew2:2 zisithi: Ungaphi ozelwe eyinkosi yamaJuda, njalo sesize ukumkhonza." 
Matthew2:3 Ngakho uHerodi inkosi esezwile wakhathazeka, leJerusalema yonke kanye laye." 
Matthew2:4 Esebuthanisile bonke abapristi abakhulu lababhali babantu. 
Matthew2:5 Basebesithi kuye: EBhethelehema yeJudiya; ngoba kulotshiwe ngokunjalo ngumprofethi ukuthi: 
Matthew2:6 Lawe, Bhethelehema lizwe lakoJuda, kawusuye omncinyane lakanye phakathi kwababusi bakoJuda; ngoba kuzavela kuwe umbusi, ozakwelusa abantu bami uIsrayeli." 
Matthew2:7 Khona uHerodi, esezibizile izazi ensitha, wabuzisisa kuzo isikhathi sokubonakala kwenkanyezi." 
Matthew2:8 Wasezithuma eBhethelehema wathi: Hambani libuzisise ngomntwana; kuzakuthi nxa limtholile, libike kimi, ukuze lami ngiye ngimkhonze." 
Matthew2:9 Kwathi seziyizwile inkosi zasuka zahamba; njalo khangela, inkanyezi, ezayibona empumalanga, yahamba phambi kwazo, yaze yafika yema phezu kwalapho usane olwalukhona." 
Matthew2:10 Zathi ukuyibona inkanyezi zathokoza ngentokozo enkulu kakhulu. 
Matthew2:11 Zasezingena endlini, zabona usane kanye loMariya unina, zawela phansi zalukhonza, zavula impahla zazo eziligugu zalukhunga ngezipho." 
Matthew2:12 Kwathi sezilayiwe nguNkulunkulu ephutsheni ukuthi zingabuyeli kuHerodi, zasuka zabuyela elizweni lakizo ngenye indlela." 
Matthew2:13 Kwathi sezisukile, khangela, ingilosi yeNkosi yabonakala kuJosefa ephutsheni, isithi: Vuka uthathe usane lonina, ubusubalekela eGibhithe, ube khona ngize ngikutshele; ngoba uHerodi uzaludinga usane, ukuze alubulale." 
Matthew2:14 Wavuka-ke wathatha usane lonina ebusuku wasuka waya eGibhithe," 
Matthew2:15 wasehlala khona kwaze kwaba yikufa kukaHerodi; ukuze kugcwaliswe okwakhulunywa yiNkosi ngomprofethi isithi: Ngiyibizile indodana yami iphume eGibhithe. 
Matthew2:16 Kwathi uHerodi, esebonile ukuthi uphicwe yizazi, wathukuthela kakhulu, wathuma wabulala abantwana bonke ababeseBhethelehema lemingceleni yayo yonke, kusukela eminyakeni emibili langaphansi, njengesikhathi abebuzisise ngaso kuzazi." 
Matthew2:17 Kwasekugcwaliseka okwakhulunywa nguJeremiya umprofethi, ukuthi:" 
Matthew2:18 Kwezwakala ilizwi eRama, ukukhala lokulila lokudabuka okukhulu, uRasheli elil el a abantwana bakhe, njalo engavumi ukududuzwa, ngoba benga se kho." 
Matthew2:19 Kodwa kwathi esefile uHerodi, khangela ingilosi yeNkosi yabonakala ephutsheni kuJosefa eGibhithe," 
Matthew2:20 isithi: Vuka uthathe umntwana omncinyane lonina, ubususiya elizweni lakoIsrayeli; ngoba sebefile ababedinga umphefumulo womntwana." 
Matthew2:21 Wavuka-ke wathatha umntwana omncinyane lonina wasefika elizweni lakoIsrayeli. 
Matthew2:22 Kodwa esezwile ukuthi uAkelawu usebusa eJudiya esikhundleni sikaHerodi uyise, wesaba ukuya khona; kodwa esexwayisiwe nguNkulunkulu ephutsheni, wasuka waya kungxenye zeGalili," 
Matthew2:23 wasefika wahlala emzini othiwa yiNazaretha. 
Matthew3:1 Ngalezonsuku kwasekufika uJohane uMbhabhathizi 
Matthew3:2 esithi: Phendukani; ngoba umbuso wamazulu ususondele. 
Matthew3:3 Ngoba nguye okwakhulunywa ngaye nguIsaya umprofethi, esithi: Ilizwi lomemezayo enkangala." 
Matthew3:4 Njalo uJohane lo wayelesembatho sakhe soboya bekamela, lozwezwe lwesikhumba ekhalweni lwakhe." 
Matthew3:5 Kwasekuphumela kuye iJerusalema leJudiya yonke lelizwe lonke elizingelezele iJodani; 
Matthew3:6 basebebhabhathizwa nguye. 
Matthew3:7 Kwathi ebona abanengi babaFarisi labaSadusi besiza ekubhabhathizeni kwakhe, wathi kubo: Nzalo yezinyoka?" 
Matthew3:8 Ngakho thelani izithelo ezifanele ukuphenduka; 
Matthew3:9 njalo lingacabangi ukutsho phakathi kwenu; ngoba ngithi kini: UNkulunkulu ulamandla okumvusela uAbrahama abantwana kulawa amatshe. 
Matthew3:10 Lakhathesi ihloka selibekiwe empandeni zezihlahla; ngakho sonke isihlahla esingatheli isithelo esihle siyaganyulwa siphoselwe emlilweni. 
Matthew3:11 Mina ngilibhabhathiza ngamanzi kubesekuphendukeni; 
Matthew3:12 okhomane lwakhe lokwela lusesandleni sakhe, njalo uzathanyelisisa isibuya sakhe." 
Matthew3:13 Khona uJesu wafika eJodani kuJohane, ukuze abhabhathizwe nguye." 
Matthew3:14 Kodwa uJohane wayemalela esithi: Mina ngiswela ukubhabhathizwa nguwe, kanti wena uza kimi?" 
Matthew3:15 Kodwa uJesu ephendula wathi kuye: Vuma khathesi; ngoba kusifanele ukuthi sigcwalise ngokunjalo ukulunga konke. Wasemvumela. 
Matthew3:16 UJesu esebhabhathiziwe wahle wakhuphuka emanzini; njalo khangela, amazulu amvulekela, wasebona uMoya kaNkulunkulu esehla kungathi lijuba esiza phezu kwakhe." 
Matthew3:17 Njalo khangela, ilizwi livela emazulwini." 
Matthew4:1 Khona uJesu wakhokhelelwa. 
Matthew4:2 Esezile ukudla insuku ezingamatshumi amane lobusuku obungamatshumi amane, ekucineni walamba." 
Matthew4:3 Kwasekusiza kuye umlingi wathi: Uba uyiNdodana kaNkulunkulu, tshono ukuthi lamatshe abe yizinkwa." 
Matthew4:4 Kodwa yena waphendula wathi: Kulotshiwe ukuthi: Umuntu kayikuphila ngesinkwa sodwa, kodwa ngalo lonke ilizwi eliphuma emlonyeni kaNkulunkulu." 
Matthew4:5 Udiyabhola wasemthatha," 
Matthew4:6 wasesithi kuye: Uba uyiNdodana kaNkulunkulu. 
Matthew4:7 UJesu wathi kuye: Kulotshiwe futhi ukuthi: Ungayilingi iNkosi uNkulunkulu wakho. 
Matthew4:8 Udiyabhola wabuya wamusa entabeni ende kakhulu, wamtshengisa imibuso yonke yomhlaba lokukhazimula kwayo," 
Matthew4:9 wathi kuye: Zonke lezizinto ngizakunika zona, uba uwela phansi ungikhonza." 
Matthew4:10 UJesu wasesithi kuye: Suka, Sathane." 
Matthew4:11 Udiyabhola wasemyekela; njalo khangela, kwafika ingilosi zasezimsebenzela." 
Matthew4:12 Kwathi uJesu esezwile ukuthi uJohane; 
Matthew4:13 wasesuka eNazaretha; 
Matthew4:14 ukuze kugcwaliseke okwakhulunywa ngumprofethi uIsaya, ukuthi:" 
Matthew4:15 Ilizwe lakoZebuloni lelizwe lakoNafithali," 
Matthew4:16 abantu ababehlezi emnyameni babonile ukukhanya okukhulu, lababehlezi elizweni lethunzini lokufa ukukhanya kuphumele kubo." 
Matthew4:17 Kusukela kulesosikhathi uJesu waqala ukutshumayela lokuthi. 
Matthew4:18 Kwathi uJesu ehambahamba, loAndreya umfowabo, bephosela imbule olwandle; ngoba babengabagoli benhlanzi." 
Matthew4:19 Wasesithi kubo: Ngilandelani, njalo ngizalenza libe ngabagoli babantu." 
Matthew4:20 Bahle-ke batshiya amambule bamlandela. 
Matthew4:21 Eseqhubeke esuka lapho, wabona ezinye izelamani ezimbili, uJakobe okaZebediya loJohane umfowabo, besemkhunjini kanye loZebediya uyise, belungisa amambule abo; wasebabiza." 
Matthew4:22 Njalo bahle batshiya umkhumbi loyise bamlandela. 
Matthew4:23 UJesu wasebhoda iGalili yonke, efundisa emasinagogeni abo." 
Matthew4:24 Indumela yakhe yasiphumela kuyo yonke iSiriya, lezigoga; wasebasilisa." 
Matthew4:25 Amaxuku amanengi asemlandela evela eGalili. 
Matthew5:1 Kwathi ebona amaxuku wenyukela entabeni; 
Matthew5:2 wasevula umlomo wakhe, wabafundisa, wathi:" 
Matthew5:3 Babusisiwe. 
Matthew5:4 Babusisiwe abalilayo; ngoba bona bazaduduzwa. 
Matthew5:5 Babusisiwe abamnene; ngoba bona bazakudla ilifa lomhlaba. 
Matthew5:6 Babusisiwe abalambela labomela ukulunga; ngoba bona bazasuthiswa. 
Matthew5:7 Babusisiwe abalesihawu; ngoba bona bazahawukelwa. 
Matthew5:8 Babusisiwe abamhlophe ngenhliziyo. 
Matthew5:9 Babusisiwe abalamulayo; ngoba bona bazathiwa ngabantwana bakaNkulunkulu. 
Matthew5:10 Babusisiwe abazingelwayo ngenxa yokulunga; ngoba umbuso wamazulu ungowabo. 
Matthew5:11 Lina libusisiwe, nxa belithuka belizingela, bekhuluma okubi konke bemelana lani beqamba amanga, ngenxa yami;" 
Matthew5:12 thokozani lithabe kakhulu, ngoba umvuzo wenu mkhulu emazulwini." 
Matthew5:13 Lina lilitshwayi lomhlaba; kodwa uba itshwayi seliduma lizatshwaywa ngani? Kalisasizi lutho, ngaphandle kokulahlwa phandle beselinyathelwa ngabantu." 
Matthew5:14 Lina liyikukhanya komhlaba; umuzi omiswe phezu kwentaba ungesitheke; 
Matthew5:15 njalo kabalumathisi isibane basibeke ngaphansi kwesitsha, kodwa phezu kwesiqobane sesibane, besesibakhanyisela bonke abasendlini." 
Matthew5:16 Ngokunjalo kakukhanye ukukhanya kwenu phambi kwabantu, ukuze babone imisebenzi yenu emihle." 
Matthew5:17 Lingacabangi ukuthi ngize ukuchitha umlayo kumbe abaprofethi; angizanga ukuchitha kodwa ukugcwalisa. 
Matthew5:18 Ngoba ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Kuze kudlule izulu lomhlaba, kakusoze kudlule ibadlana libe linye kumbe ichatshana libe linye lomlayo kuze kwenzeke konke." 
Matthew5:19 Ngakho owephula owodwa kulimilayo emincinyane, afundise abantu ngokunjalo, uzathiwa ngomncinyane embusweni wamazulu; kodwa oyenzayo ayifundise, lowo uzathiwa mkhulu embusweni wamazulu." 
Matthew5:20 Ngoba ngithi kini: Ngaphandle kokuthi ukulunga kwenu kwedlule okwababhali lokwabaFarisi, kalisoze lingene embusweni wamazulu." 
Matthew5:21 Lizwile ukuthi kwathiwa kwabasendulo: Ungabulali; laloba ngubani obulalayo, uzakuba lecala lokugwetshwa;" 
Matthew5:22 kodwa mina ngithi kini: Wonke othukuthelela umfowabo kungelasizatho uzakuba lecala lokugwetshwa. 
Matthew5:23 Ngakho uba uletha umnikelo wakho elathini, ubusukhumbula ulapho ukuthi umfowenu ulolutho olumelana lawe," 
Matthew5:24 tshiya lapho umnikelo wakho phambi kwelathi, uhambe, uqale ubuyisane lomfowenu, ubusuzonikela umnikelo wakho." 
Matthew5:25 Phangisa uzwane laye omangalelane lawe, ubusuphoselwa entolongweni." 
Matthew5:26 Ngiqinisile ngithi kuwe: Kawusoze uphume khona, uze ubhadale indibilitshi yokucina." 
Matthew5:27 Lizwile ukuthi kwathiwa kwabasendulo. 
Matthew5:28 Kodwa mina ngithi kini: Wonke okhangela owesifazana ukumkhanuka usefebile laye enhliziyweni yakhe. 
Matthew5:29 Njalo uba ilihlo lakho lokunene likukhubekisa. 
Matthew5:30 Njalo uba isandla sakho sokunene sikukhubekisa, siqume usilahlele khatshana lawe." 
Matthew5:31 Kwathiwa-ke: Loba ngubani owala umkakhe, kumele amnike incwadi yesehlukaniso;" 
Matthew5:32 kodwa mina ngithi kini: Loba ngubani owala umkakhe, ngaphandle kodaba lokufeba, umenza afebe, njalo loba ngubani omthathayo owaliweyo uyafeba." 
Matthew5:33 Lizwile futhi ukuthi kwathiwa kwabasendulo. 
Matthew5:34 Kodwa mina ngithi kini: Lingafungi lakanye; 
Matthew5:35 loba ngomhlaba, ngoba uyisenabelo senyawo zakhe;" 
Matthew5:36 njalo ungafungi ngekhanda lakho, ngoba ungelwenze unwele lalunye lube mhlophe kumbe lube mnyama." 
Matthew5:37 Kodwa ilizwi lenu kalibe ngelokuthi: Yebo yebo, hatshi hatshi; kodwa okudlula lokho kuvela komubi." 
Matthew5:38 Lizwile ukuthi kwathiwa: Ilihlo ngelihlo, lezinyo ngezinyo;" 
Matthew5:39 kodwa mina ngithi kini; 
Matthew5:40 lalowo ofuna ukukumangalela lokuthatha isigqoko sakho, mtshiyele lesembatho;" 
Matthew5:41 laloba ngubani okubamba ngamandla ukuthi uhambe imayili libe linye, hamba laye abe mabili." 
Matthew5:42 Mnike ocela kuwe. 
Matthew5:43 Lizwile ukuthi kwathiwa: Wothanda umakhelwane wakho; 
Matthew5:44 kodwa mina ngithi kini: Thandani izitha zenu, libabusise abaliqalekisayo, libaphathe kuhle abalizondayo;" 
Matthew5:45 ukuze libe ngabantwana bakaYihlo osemazulwini, ngoba yena uphumisa ilanga lakhe phezu kwababi labahle, anise izulu phezu kwabalungileyo labangalunganga." 
Matthew5:46 Ngoba aluba lithanda labo abalithandayo, lilomvuzo bani?" 
Matthew5:47 Futhi uba libingelela abafowenu bodwa, lenzani okukhulu okwedlula okwabanye? Kabenzi njalo labathelisi yini?" 
Matthew5:48 Ngakho lina banini ngabapheleleyo. 
Matthew6:1 Qaphelani ukuthi umsebenzi wenu womusa; nxa kunge njalo, alilamvuzo kuYihlo osemazulwini." 
Matthew6:2 Ngakho nxa usenza umsebenzi womusa, ungakhalisi uphondo phambi kwakho." 
Matthew6:3 Kodwa wena nxa usenza umsebenzi womusa isandlasakho sokhohlo kasingakwazi esikwenzayo esokunene sakho," 
Matthew6:4 ukuze umsebenzi wakho womusa ube sekusithekeni; njalo uYihlo obona ekusithekeni, yena uzakuvuza obala." 
Matthew6:5 Lalapho likhuleka, lingabi njengabazenzisi, ngoba bathanda ukukhuleka bemi emasinagogeni lemahlanganweni endlela, ukuze babonwe ngabantu; ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Sebewemukele umvuzo wabo." 
Matthew6:6 Kodwa wena nxa ukhuleka, ngena." 
Matthew6:7 Njalo uba likhuleka lingaphindaphindi. 
Matthew6:8 Ngakho lingafanani labo; ngoba uYihlo uyakwazi elikuswelayo, lingakaceli kuye." 
Matthew6:9 Ngakho lina khulekani ngokunje: Baba wethu osemazulwini; 
Matthew6:10 umbuso wakho kawuze; 
Matthew6:11 siphe lamuhla ukudla kwethu kwensuku zonke; 
Matthew6:12 njalo usithethelele amacala ethu, njengalokhu lathi sibathethelela abalamacala kithi;" 
Matthew6:13 njalo ungasingenisi ekulingweni. 
Matthew6:14 Ngoba uba lithethelela abantu iziphambeko zabo, uYihlo osezulwini uzalithethelela lani." 
Matthew6:15 Kodwa uba lingathetheleli abantu iziphambeko zabo, loYihlo kayikulithethelela iziphambeko zenu." 
Matthew6:16 Futhi nxa lizila ukudla. 
Matthew6:17 Kodwa wena nxa uzila ukudla gcoba ikhanda lakho, ugeze ubuso bakho," 
Matthew6:18 ukuze ungabonakali ebantwini ukuthi uzilile ukudla, kodwa kuYihlo osekusithekeni; njalo uYihlo obona ekusithekeni uzakuvuza obala." 
Matthew6:19 Lingazibekeli impahla eziligugu emhlabeni, lapho inundu lokuthomba okona khona, lalapho amasela afohlela khona ebe;" 
Matthew6:20 kodwa zibekeleni izinto eziligugu ezulwini, lapho inundu lokuthomba okungoni khona." 
Matthew6:21 Ngoba lapho okukhona impahla yenu eligugu, lenhliziyo yenu izakuba lapho." 
Matthew6:22 Isibane somzimba yilihlo; 
Matthew6:23 kodwa uba ilihlo lakho lilibi, umzimba wakho wonke uzakuba lobumnyama!" 
Matthew6:24 Kakho ongakhonza amakhosi amabili; ngoba uzazonda enye, athande enye; kumbe uzabambelela kwenye, adelele enye." 
Matthew6:25 Ngakho ngithi kini? 
Matthew6:26 Khangelani inyoni zezulu, ukuthi kazihlanyeli njalo kazivuni, kazibutheli eziphaleni; kanti uYihlo osezulwini uyazondla; lina kalizidluli kakhulu yini?" 
Matthew6:27 Njalo nguwuphi kini ngokuphisekela ongengezelela ingalo ibenye ebudeni bakhe? 
Matthew6:28 Langezembatho liphisekelani? Qaphelisani imiduze yeganga, ukuthi ikhula njani; kayitshikatshiki, kayiphothi;" 
Matthew6:29 kodwa ngithi kini: LoSolomoni ebucwazicwazini bakhe bonke wayengembathiswanga njengomunye wayo. 
Matthew6:30 Njalo uba uNkulunkulu esembathisa ngokunjalo utshani beganga, obukhona lamuhla, kuthi kusasa buphoswe eziko, kayikule mbathisakakhulu yini, lina abokholo oluncinyane?" 
Matthew6:31 Ngakho lingaphisekeli lutho, lisithi: Sizakudlani? Kumbe: Sizanathani? Loba: Sizakwembathani?" 
Matthew6:32 Ngoba zonke lezizinto izizwe ziyazidinga; ngoba uYihlo osezulwini uyazi ukuthi liyaziswela zonke lezizinto. 
Matthew6:33 Kodwa dingani kuqala umbuso kaNkulunkulu lokulunga kwakhe, njalo zonke lezizinto zizakwengezelelwa kini." 
Matthew6:34 Ngakho lingaphisekeli ikusasa; ngoba ikusasa izaziphisekela yona; bulwanele usuku obalo ububi. 
Matthew7:1 Lingehluleli, ukuze lingehlulelwa," 
Matthew7:2 ngoba lizakwahlulelwa ngokwehlulela elehlulela ngakho. 
Matthew7:3 Kanti ukhangelelani ucezwana oluselihlweni lomfowenu, kodwa ungalunanzeleli ugodo olukwelakho ilihlo?" 
Matthew7:4 Kumbe ungatsho njani kumfowenu ukuthi: Kahle ngikhuphe ucezwana oluselihlweni lakho; khangela kanti ugodo luselihlweni lakho? 
Matthew7:5 Mzenzisi, qala ukhuphe ugodo elihlweni lakho, khona-ke uzabona kuhle ukukhupha ucezwana elihlweni lomfowenu." 
Matthew7:6 Linganiki izinja okungcwele; lingaphoseli amapharele enu phambi kwezingulube, hlezi ziwanyathele ngenyawo zazo." 
Matthew7:7 Celani; dingani, lizathola; qoqodani, lizavulelwa." 
Matthew7:8 Ngoba wonke ocelayo uyemukela, loqoqodayo uzavulelwa." 
Matthew7:9 Kumbe nguwuphi kini ongathi, nxa indodana yakhe icela isinkwa, ayinike ilitshe?" 
Matthew7:10 Uba-ke icela inhlanzi, ayinike inyoka yini?" 
Matthew7:11 Ngakho uba lina, elingababi, likwazi ukupha abantwana benu izipho ezinhle, uYihlo osemazulwini uzabapha kakhulu kangakanani izinto ezinhle abacela kuye?" 
Matthew7:12 Ngakho konke elithanda ukuthi abantu bakwenze kini, kwenzeni lani ngokunjalo kubo." 
Matthew7:13 Ngenani ngesango elincinyane; ngoba isango likhulu, lendlela ibanzi eya ekubhujisweni, njalo banengi abangena ngalo;" 
Matthew7:14 ngoba isango lincinyane, lendlela ilukhonjwana eya empilweni, njalo balutshwana abayitholayo." 
Matthew7:15 Kodwa nanzelelani abaprofethi bamanga. 
Matthew7:16 Lizabazi ngezithelo zabo; bayazikha yini izithelo zevini emeveni, kumbe imikhiwa ekhuleni oluhlabayo?" 
Matthew7:17 Ngokunjalo sonke isihlahla esihle siyathela izithelo ezinhle; kodwa isihlahla esibi siyathela izithelo ezimbi; 
Matthew7:18 isihlahla esihle singethele izithelo ezimbi, lesihlahla esibi singethele izithelo ezinhle." 
Matthew7:19 Sonke isihlahla esingatheli isithelo esihle siyaganyulwa siphoselwe emlilweni. 
Matthew7:20 Ngakho-ke lizabazi ngezithelo zabo. 
Matthew7:21 Kakusibo bonke abatshoyo kimi ukuthi: Nkosi, Nkosi, abazangena embusweni wamazulu." 
Matthew7:22 Abanengi bazakuthi kimi ngalolosuku: Nkosi, Nkosi, kasiprofethanga yini ngelakho ibizo?" 
Matthew7:23 Njalo khona ngizakutsho obala kubo ukuthi: Angizanga ngilazi; sukani kimi lina benzi bobubi. 
Matthew7:24 Ngakho wonke owezwayo la amazwi ami njalo awenze; 
Matthew7:25 laselisina izulu, kwasekufika impophoma, kwasekuvunguza imimoya yayitshaya leyondlu; kodwa kayiwanga; ngoba yayisekelwe phezu kwedwala." 
Matthew7:26 Njalo wonke owezwayo la amazwi ami njalo angawenzi, uzafananiswa lendoda eyisithutha, eyakha indlu yayo phezu kwetshebetshebe;" 
Matthew7:27 laselisina izulu, kwasekufika impophoma, kwasekuvunguza imimoya yayitshaya leyondlu; yawa; kwaba kukhulu ukuwa kwayo." 
Matthew7:28 Kwasekusithi uJesu eseqedile lawomazwi amaxuku ababaza ngemfundiso yakhe; 
Matthew7:29 ngoba wabafundisa njengolamandla, njalo kungenjengababhali." 
Matthew8:1 Kwathi esehlile entabeni, amlandela amaxuku amakhulu;" 
Matthew8:2 njalo khangela, umlephero weza wamkhonza wathi." 
Matthew8:3 UJesu waseselula isandla, wamthinta, wathi: Ngiyathanda, hlambuluka. Njalo ubulephero bakhe bahle bahlanjululwa." 
Matthew8:4 UJesu wasesithi kuye: Khangela ungatsheli muntu. 
Matthew8:5 Kwathi uJesu esengenile eKapenawume, kweza kuye induna yekhulu imncenga," 
Matthew8:6 yasisithi: Nkosi, inceku yami ilele endlini iyisigoga, isebuhlungwini obukhulu." 
Matthew8:7 UJesu wasesithi kuye: Mina ngizakuza ngiyisilise. 
Matthew8:8 Induna yekhulu yasiphendula yathi: Nkosi, kangifanele ukuthi ungene ngaphansi kophahla lwami; kodwa kuphela khuluma ilizwi, njalo inceku yami izasiliswa." 
Matthew8:9 Ngoba lami ngingumuntu ongaphansi kwamandla, ngilamabutho ngaphansi kwami; njalo ngithi kuleli: Hamba, beselihamba; lakwelinye: Woza, beselisiza; lencekwini yami: Yenza lokhu, njalo ikwenze." 
Matthew8:10 Kwathi uJesu esezwile wamangala, wathi kwabalandelayo: Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Angitholanga ukholo olungaka ngitsho lakoIsrayeli." 
Matthew8:11 Njalo ngithi kini: Abanengi bazakuza bevela empumalanga lentshonalanga; 
Matthew8:12 kodwa abantwana bombuso. 
Matthew8:13 UJesu wasesithi enduneni yekhulu: Hamba, futhi kakube kuwe njengoba ukholiwe. Inceku yakhe yasisiliswa ngalelohola." 
Matthew8:14 Kwathi uJesu engene endlini kaPetro. 
Matthew8:15 Wasebamba isandla sakhe, njalo uqhuqho lwamyekela; wasesukuma, wabancedisa." 
Matthew8:16 Kwathi sekuhlwile baletha kuye abanengi ababengenwe ngamadimoni; wasekhupha omoya ngelizwi, wasilisa bonke abagulayo;" 
Matthew8:17 ukuze kugcwaliseke okwakhulunywa nguIsaya umprofethi ukuthi: Yena wathatha ubuthakathaka bethu, wazithwala izifo zethu." 
Matthew8:18 Kwathi uJesu ebona amaxuku amakhulu emhanqile, walaya ukuthi bachaphele ngaphetsheya." 
Matthew8:19 Kwasekusondela umbhali othile wathi kuye: Mfundisi, ngizakulandela loba kungaphi lapho oya khona." 
Matthew8:20 UJesu wasesithi kuye: Amakhanka alemilindi, lenyoni zezulu izidleke; kodwa iNdodana yomuntu kayila lapho engaqamelisa ikhanda khona." 
Matthew8:21 Omunye wabafundi bakhe wasesithi kuye: Nkosi, ngivumela ukuthi ngiqale ngiyengcwaba ubaba." 
Matthew8:22 Kodwa uJesu wathi kuye: Ngilandela, uyekele abafileyo bangcwabe ababo abafileyo." 
Matthew8:23 Kwathi esengenile emkhunjini, abafundi bakhe bamlandela." 
Matthew8:24 Njalo khangela, kwavuka isiphepho esikhulu olwandle, okungangokuthi umkhumbi wagutshuzelwa ngamagagasi; kodwa yena wayelele." 
Matthew8:25 Basebesondela abafundi bakhe bamvusa, besithi: Nkosi, sisindise, siyabhubha!" 
Matthew8:26 Wasesithi kubo: Lesabelani, lina abokholo oluncinyane." 
Matthew8:27 Kodwa abantu bamangala, besithi: Ngonjani lo, ukuthi lemimoya lolwandle kumlalele?" 
Matthew8:28 Kwathi esefikile ngaphetsheya elizweni lamaGergesi; 
Matthew8:29 njalo khangela, bamemeza besithi: Silani lawe? Uze lapha yini ukusihlupha kungakafiki isikhathi?" 
Matthew8:30 Kwakukhona khatshana labo umhlambi wengulube ezinengi usidla. 
Matthew8:31 Amadimoni asemncenga, esithi: Uba usikhupha, sivumela ukuthi sihambe singene emhlanjini wengulube." 
Matthew8:32 Wasesithi kuwo: Hambani. Esephumile angena emhlanjini wengulube; futhi khangela, umhlambi wonke wengulube waphaphatheka eliweni usiya olwandle, wafela emanzini." 
Matthew8:33 Abazelusayo basebebaleka, basebesiya emzini babika konke, lezin dabazababengenwe ngamadimoni." 
Matthew8:34 Njalo khangela, umuzi wonke waphuma ukumhlangabeza uJesu; bathi bembona, bancenga ukuthi asuke emikhawulweni yakibo." 
Matthew9:1 Wasengena emkhunjini. 
Matthew9:2 Futhi khangela, baletha kuye umuntu oyisigoga elele ehlakeni." 
Matthew9:3 Njalo khangela, abanye bababhali bakhulumela ngaphakathi bathi: Lo uyahlambaza." 
Matthew9:4 Njalo uJesu ebona imicabango yabo wathi: Linakanelani okubi enhliziyweni zenu? 
Matthew9:5 Ngoba yikuphi okulula, ukuthi: Uthethelelwe izono zakho; kumbe ukuthi: Sukuma uhambe?" 
Matthew9:6 Kodwa ukuze lazi ukuthi iNdodana yomuntu ilamandla emhlabeni okuthethelela izono (wasesithi koyisigoga): Sukuma uthathe uhlaka lwakho, uye endlini yakho." 
Matthew9:7 Wasesukuma waya endlini yakhe. 
Matthew9:8 Kwathi amaxuku esebonile, amangala, adumisa uNkulunkulu, onike abantu amandla anje." 
Matthew9:9 Esedlula lapho uJesu wabona umuntu, wathi kuye: Ngilandela. Wasesukuma wamlandela." 
Matthew9:10 Kwasekusithi ehlezi ekudleni endlini, khangela-ke, abathelisi abanengi lezoni beza bahlala ekudleni loJesu labafundi bakhe." 
Matthew9:11 AbaFarisi sebebonile bathi kubafundi bakhe: Kungani umfundisi wenu esidla labathelisi lezoni? 
Matthew9:12 Kwathi uJesu esizwa wathi kubo: Abaphilileyo kabadingi melaphi, kodwa abagulayo." 
Matthew9:13 Kodwa hambani lifunde ukuthi kutshoni. 
Matthew9:14 Khona kwafika kuye abafundi bakaJohane? 
Matthew9:15 UJesu wasesithi kubo. 
Matthew9:16 Futhi kakho obekela isichibi selembu elingakafinyeli esembathweni esidala; ngoba lokho okubekelwe kuso kuzadabuka esembathweni, besesiqhela isikhala." 
Matthew9:17 Njalo kabatheli iwayini elitsha emigodleni emidala; uba-ke kungenjalo imigodla iyadabuka, lewayini lichitheke, lemigodla yonakale; kodwa iwayini elitsha balifaka emigodleni emitsha, besekulondolozeka kokubili." 
Matthew9:18 Kwathi esakhuluma lezizinto kubo. 
Matthew9:19 Wasesukuma uJesu wamlandela, labafundi bakhe." 
Matthew9:20 Njalo khangela, owesifazana owayelomopho okweminyaka elitshumi lambili, wasondela ngemuva kwakhe, wathinta umphetho wesembatho sakhe." 
Matthew9:21 Ngoba wathi ngaphakathi kwakhe: Aluba ngithinta nje isembatho sakhe, ngizasindiswa." 
Matthew9:22 Kodwa uJesu etshibilika embona, wathi: Mana isibindi, ndodakazi; ukholo lwakho lukusindisile. Owesifazana wasesila kusukela ngalelohola." 
Matthew9:23 UJesu wasefika endlini yomphathi, wabona abakhalisa imihlanga lexuku liphithizela," 
Matthew9:24 wathi kubo: Dedani; ngoba intombazana kayifanga. 
Matthew9:25 Kodwa ixuku selikhutshiwe, wangena wabamba isandla sayo, intombazana yasivuka." 
Matthew9:26 Indumela yalokho yasiphumela kulelolizwe lonke. 
Matthew9:27 Kwathi uJesu esedlula lapho, iziphofu ezimbili zamlandela, zimemeza zisithi!" 
Matthew9:28 Esengenile endlini, iziphofu zeza kuye; uJesu wasesithi kuzo: Liyakholwa yini ukuthi ngingakwenza lokhu? Zathi kuye: Yebo, Nkosi." 
Matthew9:29 Wasethinta amehlo azo. 
Matthew9:30 Asevulwa amehlo azo; uJesu wasezilayisisa kakhulu wathi. 
Matthew9:31 Kodwa zaphuma. 
Matthew9:32 Kwathi ekuphumeni kwazo, khangela, baletha kuye umuntu oyisimungulu owayengenwe lidimoni;" 
Matthew9:33 kwathi idimoni selikhutshiwe, isimungulu sakhuluma; amaxuku asemangala, athi: Kakuzanga kubonwe okunje koIsrayeli." 
Matthew9:34 Kodwa abaFarisi bathi: Ukhupha amadimoni ngenkosi yamadimoni. 
Matthew9:35 UJesu wasebhoda emizini yonke lemizaneni. 
Matthew9:36 Kwathi ebona amaxuku, waba lesihelo ngawo." 
Matthew9:37 Wasesithi kubafundi bakhe: Isibili isivuno sikhulu, kodwa izisebenzi zinlutshwana;" 
Matthew9:38 ngakho ncengani iNkosi yesivuno. 
Matthew10:1 Wasebizela kuye abafundi bakhe abalitshumi lambili, wabanika amandla phezu kwabomoya abangcolileyo, ukuthi babakhuphe, lokuthi belaphe sonke isifo lobuthakathaka bonke." 
Matthew10:2 Njalo amabizo abaphostoli abalitshumi lambili yiwo la; 
Matthew10:3 uFiliphu, loBartolomewu; uTomasi, loMathewu umthelisi; uJakobe okaAlfewu, loLabewu othiwa njalo nguTadewu;" 
Matthew10:4 uSimoni umKhanani. 
Matthew10:5 Laba abalitshumi lambili uJesu wabathuma, wabalaya, esithi: Lingahambi ngendlela yabezizwe;" 
Matthew10:6 kodwa yanini ikakhulu. 
Matthew10:7 Futhi ekuhambeni kwenu tshumayelani, lisithi." 
Matthew10:8 Silisani abagulayo, lihlambulule amalephero, livuse abafileyo, likhuphe amadimoni. Lemukeliswe ngesihle, phanini ngesihle." 
Matthew10:9 Lingazithatheli igolide, loba isiliva," 
Matthew10:10 loba isikhwama sendlela, loba izigqoko ezimbili, loba amanyathela, loba udondolo." 
Matthew10:11 Lakuwuphi umuzi kumbe umzana elingena kuwo, buzani ukuthi ngubani ofaneleyo kuwo; lihlale khona, lize lisuke." 
Matthew10:12 Njalo nxa lingena endlini, liyibingelele." 
Matthew10:13 Njalo uba indlu ifanele, ukuthula kwenu kakube phezu kwayo; kodwa uba ingafanele." 
Matthew10:14 Njalo loba ngubani ongalemukeliyo kumbe ongalaleli amazwi enu, nxa liphuma kuleyondlu kumbe kulowomuzi, thintithani uthuli lwenyawo zenu." 
Matthew10:15 Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Kuzakuba ngcono kulizwe leSodoma leleGomora ngosuku lwesigwebo, kulakulowomuzi." 
Matthew10:16 Khangelani, mina ngiyalithuma njengezimvu phakathi kwezimpisi, libe msulwa njengamajuba." 
Matthew10:17 Kodwa limukani abantu; ngoba bazalinikela; 
Matthew10:18 njalo lizalethwa laphambi kwababusi lamakhosi ngenxa yami. 
Matthew10:19 Kodwa nxa belinikela, lingakhathaleli ukuthi lizakhuluma njani kumbe into bani;" 
Matthew10:20 ngoba kakusini elikhulumayo, kodwa ng uMoya kaYihlo okhuluma phakathi kwenu." 
Matthew10:21 Futhi umfowabo uzanikela umfowabo ekufeni, loyise umntwana; labantwana bazavukela abazali, bababulale." 
Matthew10:22 Njalo lizazondwa yibo bonke ngenxa yebizo lami. 
Matthew10:23 Kodwa nxa belizingela kulo umuzi. 
Matthew10:24 Umfundi kaphezu komfundisi, lenceku kayiphezu kwenkosi yayo." 
Matthew10:25 Kumanele umfundi ukuthi abe njengomfundisi wakhe, lenceku njengenkosi yayo, kakhulu kangakanani labo abendlu yakhe?" 
Matthew10:26 Ngakho lingabesabi; ngoba kakukho okufihliweyo, okungayikubonakaliswa; lokuthukuziweyo, okungayikwaziwa." 
Matthew10:27 Lokho engikutsho kini emnyameni, kukhulumeni ekukhanyeni; lalokho elikuzwa endlebeni, kumemezeleni phezu kwezimpahla." 
Matthew10:28 Njalo lingabesabi ababulala umzimba, kodwa bengelamandla okubulala umphefumulo." 
Matthew10:29 Kazithengiswa yini intaka ezimbili ngendibilitshi? Kodwa kakuyikuwa emhlabathini lanye yazo, ngaphandle kukaYihlo." 
Matthew10:30 Kodwa lezenu inwele zekhanda zibaliwe zonke. 
Matthew10:31 Ngakho lingesabi; lina liyazidlula intaka ezinengi. 
Matthew10:32 Ngakho wonke ozangivuma phambi kwabantu. 
Matthew10:33 Kodwa loba ngubani ongiphika phambi kwabantu. 
Matthew10:34 Lingacabangi ukuthi ngize ukuletha ukuthula emhlabeni; angizanga ukuletha ukuthula, kodwa inkemba." 
Matthew10:35 Ngoba ngize ukwehlukanisa umuntu loyise, lendodakazi lonina, lomalokazana loninazala;" 
Matthew10:36 lezitha zomuntu ngabendlu yakhe. 
Matthew10:37 Othanda uyise kumbe unina kulami kangifanele; lothanda indodana kumbe indodakazi kulami kangifanele; 
Matthew10:38 longathathi isiphambano sakhe njalo angilandele, kangifanele." 
Matthew10:39 Lowo othola impilo yakhe uzalahlekelwa yiyo; lolahlekelwa yimpilo yakhe ngenxa yami uzayithola. 
Matthew10:40 Owemukela lina wemukela mina. 
Matthew10:41 Owemukela umprofethi ebizweni lomprofethi uzazuza umvuzo womprofethi; lowemukela olungileyo ebizweni lolungileyo uzazuza umvuzo wolungileyo. 
Matthew10:42 Njalo loba ngubani ozanathisa omunye walababancinyane inkezo nje yamanziaqandayo ebizweni lomfundi, ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Kasoze alahlekelwa ngumvuzo wakhe." 
Matthew11:1 Kwasekusithi uJesu eseqedile ukulaya abafundi bakhe abalitshumi lambili, wasuka lapho ukuyafundisa lokutshumayela emizini yabo." 
Matthew11:2 Kwathi uJohane," 
Matthew11:3 wathi kuye: Wena unguye ozayo yini, kumbe silindele omunye?" 
Matthew11:4 UJesu wasephendula wathi kubo: Hambani limtshele uJohane izinto elizizwayo lelizibonayo: 
Matthew11:5 Iziphofu zibuye zibone; 
Matthew11:6 njalo ubusisiwe loba ngubani ongakhubekiyo ngami. 
Matthew11:7 Kwathi bona besuka uJesu waqala ukukhuluma emaxukwini ngoJohane wathi: Laphuma laya enkangala ukuyabonani? Umhlanga onyikinywa ngumoya yini? 
Matthew11:8 Kanti laphumela ukuyabonani? Umuntu owembethe izembatho ezibuthakathaka yini? Khangelani, abembethe ezibuthakathaka basezindlini zamakhosi." 
Matthew11:9 Pho laphumela ukuyabonani; 
Matthew11:10 ngoba lo nguye okulotshwe ngaye ukuthi: Khangela, mina ngiyathuma isithunywa sami phambi kobuso bakho, esizalungisa indlela yakho phambi kwakho." 
Matthew11:11 Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Kakuvelanga phakathi kwabazelwe ngabesifazana omkhulu kuloJohane uMbhabhathizi. Kodwa omncinyane embusweni wamazulu mkhulu kulaye. 
Matthew11:12 Njalo kusukela ensukwini zikaJohane uMbhabhathizi kuze kube khathesi umbuso wamazulu uphathwa ngodlakela, labalodlakela bawuthatha ngamandla." 
Matthew11:13 Ngoba abaprofethi bonke lomlayo baprofetha kwaze kwaba nguJohane; 
Matthew11:14 njalo uba livuma uku kw emukela, lo unguElija obezakuza." 
Matthew11:15 Olendlebe zokuzwa, akezwe." 
Matthew11:16 Kodwa ngizasifananisa lani lesisizukulwana? Sifanana labantwana abahlezi emamakethe," 
Matthew11:17 besithi: Salitshayela umhlanga, kodwa kalisinanga; salililela, kodwa kalikhalanga." 
Matthew11:18 Ngoba uJohane wafika engadli, basebesithi: Uledimoni." 
Matthew11:19 INdodana yomuntu yafika isidla inatha, basebesithi: Khangelani, umuntu oligovu lesinathi sewayini, umngane wabathelisi." 
Matthew11:20 Waseqala ukusola imizi okwakwenziwe phakathi kwayo ubunengi bemisebenzi yakhe yamandla, ngoba ingaphendukanga, wathi:" 
Matthew11:21 Maye kuwe, Korazini." 
Matthew11:22 Kodwa ngithi kini: Kuzakuba ngcono. 
Matthew11:23 Lawe, Kapenawume, ophakanyiselwe ezulwini." 
Matthew11:24 Kodwa ngithi kini: Kuzakuba ngcono kulizwe leSodoma ngosuku lwesigwebo, kulakuwe." 
Matthew11:25 Ngalesosikhathi uJesu, kodwa wazembulela izingane;" 
Matthew11:26 yebo Baba, ngoba ngokunjalo kwaba kuhle phambi kwakho." 
Matthew11:27 Konke kwanikelwa kimi nguBaba; njalo kakho oyaziyo iNdodana, ngaphandle kukaYise; kakho futhi omaziyo uYise ngaphandle kweNdodana, njalo loba ngubani iNdodana ethanda ukumembulela." 
Matthew11:28 Wozani kimi lonke elikhatheleyo. 
Matthew11:29 Thathani ijogwe lami lilibekephezu kwenu; 
Matthew11:30 ngoba ijogwe lami libutshelezi, lomthwalo wami ulula." 
Matthew12:1 Ngalesosikhathi uJesu wadabula emasimini amabele ngesabatha; futhi abafundi bakhe babelambile. 
Matthew12:2 Kodwa abaFarisi be ku bona bathi kuye: Khangela, abafundi bakho benza okungavunyelwanga ukwenziwa ngesabatha." 
Matthew12:3 Kodwa wathi kubo: Kalifundanga yini uDavida akwenzayo, mhla elambile yena lababelaye;" 
Matthew12:4 ukuthi wangena njani endlini kaNkulunkulu, wadla izinkwa zokubukiswa, ayengavunyelwa ukuzidla, ngitsho lababelaye?" 
Matthew12:5 Ingabe kalifundanga yini emlayweni, ukuthi ngamasabatha abapristi bayalona isabatha ethempelini, bangabi lacala?" 
Matthew12:6 Kodwa ngithi kini: Kukhona lapha omkhulu kulethempeli. 
Matthew12:7 Kodwa aluba belisazi ukuthi kutshoni ukuthi: Ngifisa isihawu hatshi umhlatshelo, ngabe kalibalahlanga abangelacala." 
Matthew12:8 Ngoba iNdodana yomuntu iyiNkosi leyesabatha. 
Matthew12:9 Futhi wasuka lapho wangena esinagogeni labo; 
Matthew12:10 njalo khangela, kwakukhona umuntu olesandla esitshwabheneyo; basebembuza besithi: Kuvunyelwe yini ukusilisa ngamasabatha? ukuze bambeke icala." 
Matthew12:11 Kodwa wathi kubo: Nguwuphi umuntu phakathi kwenu, elemvu eyodwa, futhi uba yona iwele emgodini ngesabatha, ongayikuyibamba a yi khuphule?" 
Matthew12:12 Umuntu uyedlula-ke kangakanani imvu! Ngakho kuvunyelwe ukwenza okuhle ngamasabatha. 
Matthew12:13 Wasesithi kumuntu: Yelula isandla sakho. Wase s elula, sasesisiliswa saphila njengesinye." 
Matthew12:14 Basebephuma abaFarisi becebisana ngaye, ukuthi bangambulala njani." 
Matthew12:15 Kodwa uJesu esekwazi wasuka lapho. 
Matthew12:16 Wasebalayisisa ukuthi bangamvezi; 
Matthew12:17 ukuze kugcwaliseke okwakhulunywa nguIsaya umprofethi, ukuthi:" 
Matthew12:18 Khangela, inceku yami engiyikhethileyo; othandekayo wami othokoza ngaye umphefumulo wami; ngizabeka uMoya wami phezu kwakhe, njalo uzatshumayela ukwahlulela kwabezizwe." 
Matthew12:19 Kayikubangisa, kayikumemeza, njalo kakho ozalizwa ilizwi lakhe ezindleleni." 
Matthew12:20 Umhlanga ofecekileyo kayikuwephula, lentambo yesibane ethunqayo kayikuyicitsha, aze aphumelelise ukwahlulela." 
Matthew12:21 Lezizwe zizathemba ebizweni lakhe. 
Matthew12:22 Kwasekulethwa kuye ongenwe lidimoni, ey isiphofu lesimungulu; wasemsilisa, kwaze kwathi isiphofu esiy isimungulu sakhuluma njalo sabona." 
Matthew12:23 Asemangala amaxuku wonke athi? 
Matthew12:24 Kodwa abaFarisi sebezwile bathi: Lumuntu kakhuphi amadimoni, ngaphandle ngoBhelezebhule inkosi yamadimoni." 
Matthew12:25 Kodwa uJesu, eseyazi imicabango yabo, wathi kubo: Wonke umbuso owehlukene umelene lawo ngokwawo uyachitheka; lawo wonke umuzi kumbe indlu eyehlukene imelene layo ngokwayo ingeze yema." 
Matthew12:26 Njalo uba uSathane ekhupha uSathane, wehlukene emelene laye ngokwakhe; pho umbuso wakhe uzakuma njani?" 
Matthew12:27 Futhi uba mina ngikhupha amadimoni ngoBhelezebhule, amadodana enu akhupha ngobani? Ngakho wona azakuba ngabagwebi benu." 
Matthew12:28 Kodwa uba mina ngikhupha amadimoni ngoMoya kaNkulunkulu, umbuso kaNkulunkulu usufikile kini." 
Matthew12:29 Kumbe umuntu angangena njani endlini yesiqhwaga aphange impahla yaso, ngaphandle kokuthi asibophe kuqala isiqhwaga." 
Matthew12:30 Ongelami, umelene lami, longabuthi lami, uyachithiza." 
Matthew12:31 Ngakho ngithi kini: Abantu bazathethelelwa sonke isono lokuhlambaza. 
Matthew12:32 Lalowo okhuluma ilizwi elimelana leNdodana yomuntu; kodwa lowo okhuluma emelana loMoya oyiNgcwele, kayikuthethelelwa, kungeyisikho kulesisikhathi loba kwesizayo." 
Matthew12:33 Loba yenzani isihlahla sibe ngesilungileyo, lesithelo saso sibe ngesilungileyo, kumbe lenze isihlahla sibe sibi, lesithelo saso sibe sibi." 
Matthew12:34 Nzalo yezinyoka, lingakhuluma njani izinto ezinhle, libabi? Ngoba umlomo ukhuluma ngokugcwala kwenhliziyo." 
Matthew12:35 Umuntu olungileyo ukhupha izinto ezilungileyo kokuligugu elilungileyo lenhliziyo; lomuntu omubi ukhupha izinto ezimbi kokuligugu elibi. 
Matthew12:36 Kodwa ngithi kini: Lonke ilizwi eliyize abalikhulumayo abantu, bazaziphendulela ngalo ngosuku lokwahlulela." 
Matthew12:37 Ngoba ngamazwi akho uzalungisiswa, langamazwi akho uzalahlwa." 
Matthew12:38 Abanye bababhali labaFarisi basebephendula, bathi: Mfundisi, sifuna ukubona isibonakaliso esivela kuwe." 
Matthew12:39 Kodwa waphendula wathi kubo: Isizukulwana esibi. 
Matthew12:40 Ngoba njengalokhu uJona waba sesiswini sensikabayitshiye insuku ezintathu lobusuku obuthathu, ngokunjalo iNdodana yomuntu izakuba semathunjini omhlaba insuku ezintathu lobusuku obuthathu." 
Matthew12:41 Amadoda eNineve. 
Matthew12:42 Indlovukazi yeningizimu izasukuma ekugwetshweni kanye lalesisizukulwana. 
Matthew12:43 Kodwa nxa umoya ongcolileyo esephumile emuntwini, uyahamba adabule indawo ezomileyo, edinga ukuphumula, kodwa enga ku tholi." 
Matthew12:44 Abesesithi: Ngizabuyela endlini yami engaphuma kuyo; njalo esefikile ayifice ize, ithanyelwe, njalo ilungisiwe." 
Matthew12:45 Abesehamba athathe kanye laye abanye omoya abayisikhombisa ababi kulaye uqobo, besebengena bahlale khona." 
Matthew12:46 Kwathi esakhuluma emaxukwini, khangela, unina labafowabo bema ngaphandle, bedinga ukukhuluma laye." 
Matthew12:47 Omunye wasesithi kuye: Khangela, unyoko labafowenu bemi phandle, badinga ukukhuluma lawe." 
Matthew12:48 Kodwa waphendula wathi komtshelileyo: Ngubani umama? Labafowethu ngobani? 
Matthew12:49 Waseselulela isandla sakhe kubafundi bakhe wathi: Khangelani, umama labafowethu." 
Matthew12:50 Ngoba loba ngubani owenza intando. 
Matthew13:1 Kwathi ngalolosuku uJesu waphuma endlini. 
Matthew13:2 Kwasekubuthana kuye amaxuku amakhulu. 
Matthew13:3 Wasekhuluma labo izinto ezinengi ngemifanekiso, wathi: Khangelani, kwaphuma umhlanyeli ukuyahlanyela." 
Matthew13:4 Kwathi ekuhlanyeleni kwakhe, enye inhlanyeloyawela eceleni kwendlela; kwasekufika inyoni, zayidla zayiqeda." 
Matthew13:5 Kodwa enye yawela emhlabathini olamatshe, lapho eyayingelamhlabathi omnengi khona; futhi yahle yamila, ngoba kwakungelakutshona komhlabathi;" 
Matthew13:6 kwathi ekuphumeni kwelanga yahangulwa; njalo ngoba yayingelampande yabuna. 
Matthew13:7 Kodwa enye yawela emeveni; ameva asekhula ayiminyanisa. 
Matthew13:8 Kodwa enye yawela emhlabathini omuhle, yathela isithelo." 
Matthew13:9 Olendlebe zokuzwa, akezwe." 
Matthew13:10 Kwasekufika abafundi bathi kuye: Ukhulumelani kubo ngemifanekiso? 
Matthew13:11 Wasephendula wathi kubo: Ngoba kuphiwe kini ukwazi imfihlo zombuso wamazulu, kodwa bona kabakunikwanga." 
Matthew13:12 Ngoba loba ngubani olakho uzaphiwa, abe lokwengezelelweyo; kodwa lowo ongelakho, uzakwemukwa." 
Matthew13:13 Ngakho ngikhuluma labo ngemifanekiso, ngoba bebona kababoni, njalo besizwa kabezwa, futhi kabaqedisisi." 
Matthew13:14 Kubo besekugcwaliseka isiprofetho sikaIsaya, esithi: Ukuzwa lizakuzwa, kodwa kalisoze liqedisise; lokubona lizabona, kodwa kalisoze libonisise;" 
Matthew13:15 ngoba inhliziyo yalababantu seyaba lukhuni. 
Matthew13:16 Kodwa abusisiwe amehlo enu. 
Matthew13:17 Ngoba ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Abaprofethi abanengi labalungileyo babethanda ukubona izinto elizibonayo, kodwa kaba zi bonanga; lokuzwa izinto elizizwayo kodwa kaba zi zwanga." 
Matthew13:18 Ngakho lina zwanini umfanekiso womhlanyeli. 
Matthew13:19 Kuthi wonke ozwayo ilizwi lombuso kodwa engaqedisisi. 
Matthew13:20 Kodwa ohlanyelwe emhlabathini olamatshe, nguye olizwayo ilizwi, ahle alemukele ngentokozo;" 
Matthew13:21 kodwa kalampande phakathi kwakhe. 
Matthew13:22 Lohlanyelwe emeveni, nguye olizwayo ilizwi, kodwa impisekelo yalumhlaba lenkohliso." 
Matthew13:23 Kodwa ohlanyelwe emhlabathini omuhle, nguye olizwayo ilizwi aliqedisise; athele izithelo, aveze, omunye ikhulu, lomunye amatshumi ayisithupha, lomunye amatshumi amathathu." 
Matthew13:24 Wabeka phambi kwabo omunye umfanekiso, esithi: Umbuso wamazulu ufananiswa lomuntu owahlanyela inhlanyelo enhle ensimini yakhe." 
Matthew13:25 Kodwa abantu besalele, kwafika isitha sakhe sahlanyela umfaba phakathi kwamabele, sahamba." 
Matthew13:26 Kodwa kwathi selumilile usungulo lwathela isithelo, lomfaba wasubonakala." 
Matthew13:27 Zasezisondela inceku zomninimuzi zathi kuye: Nkosi, kawuhlanyelanga yini inhlanyelo enhle ensimini yakho? Pho iwuthethe ngaphi umfaba?" 
Matthew13:28 Wasesithi kuzo: Umuntu oyisitha ukwenzile lokhu. Inceku zasezisithi kuye: Uthanda ukuthi siyewubutha yini? 
Matthew13:29 Kodwa wathi: Hatshi, hlezi, ekubutheni kwenu umfaba, lisiphune amabele kanye lawo." 
Matthew13:30 Yekelani kukhule kokubili ndawonye kuze kube yisivuno; langesikhathi sokuvuna ngizakuthi kwabavunayo: Buthani kuqala umfaba, liwubophe izinyanda ukuze liwutshise." 
Matthew13:31 Wasebabekela omunye umfanekiso, esithi: Umbuso wamazulu unjengohlamvu lwemasitedi, aluthatha umuntu waluhlanyela ensimini yakhe;" 
Matthew13:32 lona kambe luncinyane kulazo zonke inhlamvu; kodwa nxa selukhulile. 
Matthew13:33 Wabatshela omunye umfanekiso, wathi: Umbuso wamazulu unjengemvubelo." 
Matthew13:34 Lezizinto zonke uJesu wazikhuluma emaxukwini ngemifanekiso, futhi ngaphandle komfanekiso kakhulumanga kubo;" 
Matthew13:35 ukuze kugcwaliseke okwakhulunywa ngumprofethi. 
Matthew13:36 Kwathi uJesu esewayekele amaxuku ahamba wangena endlini. 
Matthew13:37 Wasephendula wathi kibo: Ohlanyela inhlanyelo enhle yiNdodana yomuntu; 
Matthew13:38 lensimu ngumhlaba; 
Matthew13:39 lesitha esawuhlanyelayo ngudiyabhola; labavunayo bazingilosi. 
Matthew13:40 Ngakho-ke njengalokhu umfaba uyabuthwa utshiswe emlilweni. 
Matthew13:41 INdodana yomuntu izathuma ingilosi zayo, besezibutha zikhuphe embusweni wayo konke okukhubekisayo lalabo abenza okubi," 
Matthew13:42 besezibaphosela. 
Matthew13:43 Khona abalungileyo bezakhanya njengelanga. 
Matthew13:44 Futhi umbuso wamazulu unjengempahla eligugu efihliweyo ensimini, okuthi umuntu eseyificile wa yi fihla." 
Matthew13:45 Futhi umbuso wamazulu unjengomuntu ongumthengi odinga amapharele amahle; 
Matthew13:46 esethole elinye ipharele eliligugu kakhulu. 
Matthew13:47 Futhi umbuso wamazulu unjengembule elaphoswa olwandle, laselibutha zonke inhlobo;" 
Matthew13:48 lona, lithe seligcwele, balidonsela ekhunjini, bahlala phansi, babuthela ezilungileyo ezitsheni, kodwa ezimbi bazilahlela ngaphandle." 
Matthew13:49 Kuzakuba njalo ekupheleni kwesikhathi," 
Matthew13:50 besezibaphosela esithandweni somlilo; lapho kuzakuba khona ukukhala lokugedla amazinyo. 
Matthew13:51 UJesu wathi kubo: Seliziqedisisile zonke lezizinto yini? Bathi kuye: Yebo, Nkosi." 
Matthew13:52 Wasesithi kubo: Ngakho wonke umbhali okutsha lokudala. 
Matthew13:53 Kwasekusithi uJesu eseqedile limifanekiso, wasuka lapho." 
Matthew13:54 Wathi esefikile? 
Matthew13:55 Lo kayisiyo yini oJakobe loJose loSimoni loJudasi? 
Matthew13:56 Labodadewabo kabakho yini bonke kithi? Pho, zivela ngaphi zonke lezizinto kuye?" 
Matthew13:57 Basebekhubeka ngaye. 
Matthew13:58 Njalo kenzanga lapho imisebenzi yamandla eminengi. 
Matthew14:1 Ngalesosikhathi uHerodi," 
Matthew14:2 wasesithi ezincekwini zakhe, kungakho-ke imisebenzi yamandla isebenza kuye." 
Matthew14:3 Ngoba uHerodi wayembambile uJohane wambopha wamfaka entolongweni; 
Matthew14:4 ngoba uJohane wayethe kuye: Kawuvunyelwa ukuba laye. 
Matthew14:5 Njalo efuna ukumbulala. 
Matthew14:6 Kodwa kwathi kugcinwa usuku lokuzalwa kukaHerodi, indodakazi kaHerodiyasi yagida phakathi kwabo, yamthokozisa uHerodi." 
Matthew14:7 Ngakho wathembisa ngesifungo ukuyinika loba yini ezayicela. 
Matthew14:8 Kodwa yona, isilayiwe ngunina, yathi ikhanda likaJohane uMbhabhathizi." 
Matthew14:9 Inkosi yasisiba losizi, kodwa ngenxa yezifungo langalabo ababehlezi layo ekudleni yalaya ukuthi inikwe." 
Matthew14:10 Yasithuma yamquma uJohane ikhanda entolongweni. 
Matthew14:11 Ikhanda lakhe laselilethwa ngomganu, lanikwa intombi; yona yasi l isa kunina." 
Matthew14:12 Kwasekusiza abafundi bakhe bathatha isidumbu, basingcwaba; basebesuka bambikela uJesu." 
Matthew14:13 UJesu esezwile. 
Matthew14:14 UJesu esephumile wabona ixuku elikhulu, waba lesihelo ngabo." 
Matthew14:15 Kwathi sekuhlwile abafundi bakhe beza kuye, bathi: Lindawo iyinkangala, lesikhathi sesihambile." 
Matthew14:16 Kodwa uJesu wathi kubo: Kakuswelekanga ukuthi bahambe; banikeni lina ukuthi badle. 
Matthew14:17 Kodwa bathi kuye: Kasila lapha ngaphandle kwezinkwa ezinhlanu lenhlanzi ezimbili. 
Matthew14:18 Wasesithi: Ziletheni lapha kimi. 
Matthew14:19 Waselaya amaxuku ukuthi ahlale phansi etshanini, wathatha izinkwa ezinhlanu lenhlanzi ezimbili." 
Matthew14:20 Basebesidla bonke, basutha; badobha imvuthu ezazisele, izitsha ezigcweleyo ezilitshumi lambili." 
Matthew14:21 Lalabo abasebedlile babengamadoda angaba zinkulungwane ezinhlanu, ngaphandle kwabesifazana labantwana." 
Matthew14:22 Njalo uJesu wahle wacindezela abafundi bakhe ukuthi bangene emkhunjini, njalo bamqalele ukuya ngaphetsheya, esayekela amaxuku ahambe." 
Matthew14:23 Kwathi eseyekele amaxuku ahamba, wenyukela entabeni eyedwa ukuze akhuleke; kwathi sekuhlwile, wayeyedwa lapho." 
Matthew14:24 Kodwa umkhumbi wawusuphakathi kolwandle, utshukunyiswa ngamagagasi; ngoba umoya wawuphambene labo." 
Matthew14:25 Kwathi ngesikhathi somlindo wesine wobusuku uJesu weza kubo, ehamba phezu kolwandle." 
Matthew14:26 Kodwa kwathi abafundi bembona ehamba phezu kolwandle bethuka, bathi: Lithonga. Basebekhala ngokwesaba." 
Matthew14:27 Kodwa uJesu wahle wakhuluma labo, wathi: Manini isibindi; yimi; lingesabi." 
Matthew14:28 UPetro wasemphendula wathi: Nkosi, uba kunguwe, ngilaya ukuthi ngize kuwe phezu kwamanzi." 
Matthew14:29 Wasesithi: Woza. UPetro wasesehla emkhunjini wahamba phezu kwamanzi, ukuze aye kuJesu." 
Matthew14:30 Kodwa ebona umoya olamandla wesaba; wathi eseqala ukutshona wakhala, wathi: Nkosi, ngisindisa!" 
Matthew14:31 Njalo uJesu wahle welula isandla, wambamba, wathi kuye: Wena olokukholwa okuncinyane, uthandabuzelani?" 
Matthew14:32 Sebengenile emkhunjini, umoya wathula." 
Matthew14:33 Abasemkhunjini basebesiza bamkhonza bathi. 
Matthew14:34 Kwathi sebechaphile bafika elizweni leGenesaretha. 
Matthew14:35 Esemazi amadoda akuleyondawo athumela ilizwikuso sonke lesosigaba esizingelezeleyo, aletha kuye bonke abagulayo." 
Matthew14:36 Basebemncenga, ukuthi bathinte nje umphetho wesembatho sakhe." 
Matthew15:1 Kwasekufika kuJesu ababhali labaFarisi ababevela eJerusalema, bathi:" 
Matthew15:2 Kungani abafundi bakho besephula isiko? Ngoba kabagezi izandla zabo, nxa besidla isinkwa." 
Matthew15:3 Kodwa waphendula wathi kubo: Lani-ke kungani lisephula umlayo kaNkulunkulu ngenxa yesiko lenu? 
Matthew15:4 Ngoba uNkulunkulu walaya, wathi: Hlonipha uyihlo lonyoko;" 
Matthew15:5 kodwa lina lithi: Loba ngubani othi kuyise kumbe kunina: Ku ngumnikelo, loba yini evela kimi ingakusiza," 
Matthew15:6 njalo engasoze amhloniphe uyise kumbe unina; ngalokho lenza umlayo kaNkulunkulu. 
Matthew15:7 Bazenzisi, uIsaya waprofetha kuhle ngani, esithi:" 
Matthew15:8 Lababantu basondela kimi ngomlomo wabo, langendebe bangidumise; kodwa inhliziyo yabo ikhatshana lami." 
Matthew15:9 Kodwa bangikhonza ngeze, befundisa izimfundiso eziy imilayo yabantu." 
Matthew15:10 Esebizele kuye ixuku, wathi kilo: Lalelani futhi liqedisise." 
Matthew15:11 Kakusikho okungena emlonyeni okungcolisa umuntu; kodwa okuphuma emlonyeni, yikho okungcolisa umuntu." 
Matthew15:12 Abafundi bakhe basebesondela bathi kuye: Uyazi yini ukuthi abaFarisi bathe ukulizwa lelilizwi bakhubeka? 
Matthew15:13 Kodwa waphendula wathi: Sonke isihlahlakazana, uBaba osezulwini angasihlanyelanga, sizasitshunwa." 
Matthew15:14 Bayekeleni; bangabakhokheli beziphofu abayiziphofu. 
Matthew15:15 UPetro wasephendula wathi kuye: Sichasisele lumfanekiso. 
Matthew15:16 UJesu wasesithi: Kanti lani lisengabangelakuqedisisa? 
Matthew15:17 Lilokhe lingaqedisisi yini, ukuthi konke okungena emlonyeni kuya esiswini, futhi kuyelahlelwa ngaphandle?" 
Matthew15:18 Kodwa izinto eziphuma emlonyeni zivela enhliziyweni. 
Matthew15:19 Ngoba enhliziyweni kuvela imicabango emibi, ukubulala, ubufebe, ukuphinga, ukweba, ukufakaza amanga, ukuhlambaza;" 
Matthew15:20 yizo lezozinto ezimngcolisayo umuntu. 
Matthew15:21 UJesu wasesuka lapho, waya kungxenye zeTire lezeSidoni." 
Matthew15:22 Njalo khangela, owesifazana ong umKhanani ovela kuleyomikhawulo, wakhala kuye esithi: Nkosi." 
Matthew15:23 Kodwa kamphendulanga nga lizwi. Basebesondela kuye abafundi bakhe bamncenga, bathi: Mxotshe, ngoba uyakhala ngemva kwethu." 
Matthew15:24 Kodwa waphendula wathi: Kangithunywanga, ngaphandle kuzo izimvu ezilahlekileyo zendlu yakoIsrayeli." 
Matthew15:25 Kodwa weza wamkhonza wathi: Nkosi, ngisize." 
Matthew15:26 Kodwa waphendula wathi: Kakukuhle ukuthatha isinkwa sabantwana, loku si phosela izinjana." 
Matthew15:27 Kodwa yena wathi: Yebo, Nkosi, kodwa lezinjana ziyadla okwemvuthuluka eziwa etafuleni labaninizo." 
Matthew15:28 UJesu wasephendula wathi kuye: O mama, lukhulu ukholo lwakho! Kakube kuwe njengokuthanda kwakho. Indodakazi yakhe yasisila kusukela kulelohola." 
Matthew15:29 UJesu wasesuka lapho weza eduzane kolwandle lweGalili; wenyukela entabeni wahlala phansi khona. 
Matthew15:30 Kwasekusiza kuye amaxuku amakhulu, izingini, labanye abanengi, basebebaphosela enyaweni zikaJesu, wasebasilisa;" 
Matthew15:31 aze amangala amaxuku. 
Matthew15:32 UJesu wasebizela kuye abafundi bakhe wathi: Ngilesihelo ngexuku, ngoba sebelami insuku ezintathu, bengelalutho lokudla; njalo kangithandi ukuthi ngibayekele bahambe bengadlanga, hlezi bayathe endleleni." 
Matthew15:33 Abafundi bakhe basebesithi kuye: Siza zuzangaphi enkangala izinkwa ezinengi kangaka, ukuthi zisuthise ixuku elikhulu kangaka?" 
Matthew15:34 UJesu wasesithi kubo: Lilezinkwa ezingaki? Basebesithi: Eziyisikhombisa, lenhlanzana ezinlutshwana." 
Matthew15:35 Waselaya amaxuku ukuthi ahlale phansi emhlabathini. 
Matthew15:36 Wasethatha izinkwa eziyisikhombisa lenhlanzi, esebongile wa zi hlephula, wa zi nika abafundi bakhe, labafundi ixuku." 
Matthew15:37 Basebesidla bonke basutha; basebedobha imvuthu ezazisele, izitsha eziyisikhombisa zigcwele." 
Matthew15:38 Lalabo abadlayo babengamadoda azinkulungwane ezine, ngaphandle kwabesifazana labantwana." 
Matthew15:39 Eseyekele amaxuku ahamba. 
Matthew16:1 AbaFarisi labaSadusi. 
Matthew16:2 Kodwa waphendula wathi kubo: Kusihlwa lithi: Umkhathi muhle; ngoba isibhakabhaka sibomvu; 
Matthew16:3 lekuseni lithi: Umkhathi mubi lamuhla; ngoba isibhakabhaka sibomvu sinyukubele. Bazenzisi, liyakwazi ukwehlukanisa umumo wesibhakabhaka; kodwa izibonakaliso zezikhathi lingeke yini?" 
Matthew16:4 Isizukulwana esibi lesifebayo sidinga isibonakaliso; kodwa kasiyikunikwa isibonakaliso, ngaphandle kwesibonakaliso sikaJona umprofethi. Wasebatshiya, wahamba." 
Matthew16:5 Sebefikile ngaphetsheya abafundi bakhe babekhohliwe ukuthatha izinkwa. 
Matthew16:6 UJesu wasesithi kubo: Nanzelelani liqaphele. 
Matthew16:7 Basebezindlisana besithi: Ngoba singathathanga izinkwa. 
Matthew16:8 UJesu esekwazi wathi kubo: Lina abokholo oluncinyane? 
Matthew16:9 Kalikaqedisisi yini, futhi kalikhumbuli izinkwa ezinhlanu zenkulungwane ezinhlanu?" 
Matthew16:10 Futhi lezinkwa eziyisikhombisa zenkulungwane ezine, lokuthi labutha izitsha ezingaki?" 
Matthew16:11 Kaliqedisisi njani, ukuthi bekungemayelana lesinkwa ebengi ku khuluma kini ukuthiliqaphele imvubelo yabaFarisi labaSadusi?" 
Matthew16:12 Basebeqedisisa ukuthi katshongo ukuthi baqaphele imvubelo yezinkwa. 
Matthew16:13 Kwathi uJesu esefikile kungxenye zeKesariya yeFiliphu wababuza abafundi bakhe, esithi: Abantu bathi, mina, iNdodana yomuntu, ngingubani?" 
Matthew16:14 Basebesithi: Abanye bathi: NguJohane uMbhabhathizi. 
Matthew16:15 Wathi kubo: Lina-ke lithi ngingubani? 
Matthew16:16 USimoni Petro wasephendula wathi: Wena unguKristu, iNdodana." 
Matthew16:17 UJesu wasephendula wathi kuye: Ubusisiwe. 
Matthew16:18 Lami-ke ngiyakutshela, ukuthi wena unguPetro." 
Matthew16:19 Futhi ngizakunika izihluthulelo zombuso wamazulu. 
Matthew16:20 Wasebalayisisa abafundi ukuthi bangatsheli muntu ukuthi yena unguJesu onguKristu. 
Matthew16:21 Kusukela kulesosikhathi uJesu waqala ukubatshengisa abafundi bakhe. 
Matthew16:22 UPetro wasesiya laye eceleni waqala ukumkhuza esithi: Kakungabi kuwe, Nkosi; lokhu kakusoze kwenziwa kuwe." 
Matthew16:23 Kodwa yena watshibilika wathi kuPetro: Suka ngemva kwami, Sathane." 
Matthew16:24 UJesu wasesithi kubafundi bakhe: Uba umuntu ethanda ukuza ngemva kwami, kazidele, athathe isiphambano sakhe, angilandele." 
Matthew16:25 Ngoba loba ngubani othanda ukusindisa impilo yakhe izamlahlekela; kodwa loba ngubani olahlekelwa yimpilo yakhe ngenxa yami uzayithola; 
Matthew16:26 ngoba kuzamsizani umuntu nxa ezuza umhlaba wonke? 
Matthew16:27 Ngoba iNdodana yomuntu izakuza ngenkazimulo kaYise. 
Matthew16:28 Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Bakhona abanye kwabemiyo lapha, abangasoze bezwe ukufa." 
Matthew17:1 Lemva kwensuku eziyisithupha uJesu wathatha. 
Matthew17:2 Waseguqulwa isimo phambi kwabo, njalo ubuso bakhe bakhanya njengelanga, lezembatho zakhe zaba mhlophe njengokukhanya." 
Matthew17:3 Futhi khangela, kwasekubonakala kubo uMozisi loElija, bekhuluma laye." 
Matthew17:4 UPetro wasephendula wathi kuJesu: Nkosi, kuhle ukuthi sibe lapha." 
Matthew17:5 Kwathi esakhuluma, khangela, iyezi elikhanyayo labasibekela; futhi khangela, ilizwi laphuma eyezini." 
Matthew17:6 Sebezwile abafundi. 
Matthew17:7 Kodwa uJesu weza wabathinta wathi. 
Matthew17:8 Sebephakamisile amehlo abo, kababonanga muntu, ngaphandle kukaJesu yedwa." 
Matthew17:9 Sebesehla entabeni. 
Matthew17:10 Abafundi bakhe basebembuza bathi: Pho batsholoni ababhali ukuthi uElija ufanele ukufika kuqala? 
Matthew17:11 UJesu wasephendula wathi kubo: UElija uzafika kuqala isibili, uzabuyisela zonke izinto;" 
Matthew17:12 kodwa ngitsho kini ukuthi uElija sewafika, kodwa kabamazanga." 
Matthew17:13 Abafundi basebeqedisisa ukuthi wakhuluma labo ngoJohane uMbhabhathizi. 
Matthew17:14 Kwathi sebefikile exukwini, kweza kuye umuntu:" 
Matthew17:15 Nkosi, akuhawukele indodana yami, ngoba ilesithuthwane iyahlupheka kakhulu; ngoba iwele kanengi emlilweni, futhi kanengi emanzini." 
Matthew17:16 Njalo ngiyilethe kubafundi bakho, kodwa bebengelakho ukuyisilisa." 
Matthew17:17 UJesu wasephendula wathi: O sizukulwana esingelakholo lesonakeleyo? Mletheni kimi lapha. 
Matthew17:18 UJesu waselikhuza, idimoni laseliphuma kuyo, umntwana wasesila kusukela kulelohola." 
Matthew17:19 Abafundi basebesiza kuJesu bebodwa bathi: Kungani thina sehlulekile ukulikhupha? 
Matthew17:20 UJesu wasesithi kubo: Kungenxa yokungakholwa kwenu. 
Matthew17:21 Kodwa loluhlobo kaluphumi. 
Matthew17:22 Besahlezi eGalili, uJesu wathi kubo: INdodana yomuntu izanikelwa ezandleni zabantu," 
Matthew17:23 njalo bazayibulala, kodwa ngosuku lwesithathu izavuswa." 
Matthew17:24 Kwathi sebefikile eKapenawume? 
Matthew17:25 Wathi: Yebo. Esengenile endlini, uJesu wamandulela wathi? Kumadodana abo yini, kumbe kwabezizwe?" 
Matthew17:26 UPetro wathi kuye: Kwabezizwe. UJesu wathi kuye: Ngakho-ke amadodana akhululekile. 
Matthew17:27 Kodwa-ke ukuze singabakhubekisi. 
Matthew18:1 Ngalesosikhathi abafundi beza kuJesu, bathi: Kanti ngubani omkhulu embusweni wamazulu?" 
Matthew18:2 UJesu wasebizela kuye umntwana omncane wammisa phakathi kwabo," 
Matthew18:3 wathi: Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Ngaphandle kokuthi liphenduke libe njengabantwana abancane, kalisoze lingene embusweni wamazulu." 
Matthew18:4 Ngakho lowo ozazithoba njengalumntwana omncane, nguye omkhulu embusweni wamazulu." 
Matthew18:5 Njalo loba ngubani owemukela abe munye umntwana omncane onje ebizweni lami, wemukela mina." 
Matthew18:6 Kodwa loba ngubani. 
Matthew18:7 Maye kuwo umhlaba ngenxa yezikhubekiso! 
Matthew18:8 Njalo. 
Matthew18:9 Futhi uba ilihlo lakho. 
Matthew18:10 Qaphelani lingadeleli omunye walaba abancinyane. 
Matthew18:11 Ngoba iNdodana yomuntu ize ukusindisa. 
Matthew18:12 Licabangani? Uba umuntu othile elezimvu ezilikhulu, besekulahleka enye yazo, kazitshiyi yini ezingamatshumi ayisificamunwemunye lasificamunwemunye, ahambe ezintabeni ukuyadinga elahlekileyo?" 
Matthew18:13 Futhi uba kungenzakala ukuthi ayithole, ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Uthokoza ngayo kakhulu kulalezo ezingamatshumi ayisificamunwemunye lasificamunwemunye ezingalahlekanga." 
Matthew18:14 Ngokunjalo kayisiyo intando kaYihlo osemazulwini. 
Matthew18:15 Kodwa nxa umfowenu ekona, hamba umsole phakathi kwakho laye lilodwa;" 
Matthew18:16 kodwa uba enga ku zwa, thatha abe munye kumbe babe babili kanye lawe futhi, ukuze lonke ilizwi liqiniswe ngomlomo wabafakazi ababili kumbe abathathu;" 
Matthew18:17 njalo nxa esala ukubezwa bona, tshela ibandla; uba esala ukuzwa lalo ibandla." 
Matthew18:18 Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Konke elizakubopha emhlabeni, kuzakuba kubotshiwe ezulwini; njalo konke elizakukhulula emhlabeni, kuzakuba kukhululiwe ezulwini." 
Matthew18:19 Njalo ngithi kini: Uba ababili benu bevumelana emhlabeni loba ngaluphi ulutho abalucelayo. 
Matthew18:20 Ngoba lapho ababili kumbe abathathu ababuthene khona ebizweni lami, ngikhona lapho phakathi kwabo." 
Matthew18:21 UPetro wasemsondelela wathi: Nkosi, umfowethu uzangona kangaki, njalo ngimthethelela?" 
Matthew18:22 UJesu wathi kuye: Kangitsho kuwe ukuthikuze kube kasikhombisa, kodwa kuze kube ngamatshumi ayisikhombisa aphindwe kasikhombisa." 
Matthew18:23 Ngakho umbuso wamazulu ufananiswa lomuntu oy inkosi, owayethanda ukulandiselana lenceku zakhe." 
Matthew18:24 Kwathi eseqalile ukulandisa, kwalethwa kuye enye elomlandu kuyo wamathalenta azinkulungwane ezilitshumi." 
Matthew18:25 Kodwa njengoba yayingelalutho lokuhlawula, inkosi yayo yalaya ukuthi ithengiswe." 
Matthew18:26 Ngakho inceku yawa phansi imkhothamela, yathi: Nkosi, ngibekezelela, futhi ngizakuhlawula konke." 
Matthew18:27 Inkosi yaleyonceku yasisiba lesihelo yayikhulula, yayixolela umlandu." 
Matthew18:28 Kodwa yaphuma leyonceku yathola omunye oyinceku kanye layo, olomlandu kuyo wabodenariyo abalikhulu, yambamba ya m khama, yathi: Ngihlawula okufaneleyo." 
Matthew18:29 Ngakho oyinceku kanye layo wawa phansi ezinyaweni zayo wayincenga, wathi: Ungibekezelele, futhi ngizakuhlawula konke." 
Matthew18:30 Kodwa yona kayivumanga, kodwa yasuka yayiphosela entolongweni, ize iwuhlawule umlandu." 
Matthew18:31 Kwathi abayizinceku kanye layo bebona izinto ezazenzakele badabuka kakhulu; beza babikela inkosi yabo konke okwakwenzekile. 
Matthew18:32 Inkosi yayo yasiyibizela kiyo yathi kiyo: Wena nceku embi, ngakuxolela wonke lowomlandu, ngoba wangincenga;" 
Matthew18:33 ngabe lawe kawumhawukelanga yini omunye oyinceku kanye lawe, njengoba lami ngakuhawukela?" 
Matthew18:34 Inkosi yayo yasithukuthela yayinikela kubahlukuluzi, ize ihlawule konke okufaneleyo kuyo." 
Matthew18:35 Uzakwenza njalo kini laye uBaba osezulwini, uba lingathetheleli lowo lalowo umfowenu iziphambeko zabo ngenhliziyo zenu." 
Matthew19:1 Kwasekusithi uJesu eseqedile lawomazwi. 
Matthew19:2 Amaxuku amakhulu asemlandela, wasewasilisa lapho." 
Matthew19:3 Basebesiza kuye abaFarisi bemlinga, bathi kuye: Kuvunyelwe yini endodeni ukuthi yale umkayo ngaso sonke isizatho?" 
Matthew19:4 Wasephendula wathi kubo: Kalifundanga yini ukuthi owa ba dabula kusukela ekuqaleni wabenza owesilisa lowesifazana? 
Matthew19:5 Wasesithi: Ngenxa yalokhu indoda izatshiya uyise lonina, inamathele kumkayo; labo ababili bazakuba nyamanye." 
Matthew19:6 Ngakho kabasebabili, kodwa sebe nyamanye. Ngakho lokho uNkulunkulu akuhlanganisileyo kakungabi lamuntu okwehlukanisayo." 
Matthew19:7 Bathi kuye: Pho uMozisi walayelani ukunika incwadi yesehlukaniso, lokumala?" 
Matthew19:8 Wathi kubo: Ngenxa yobulukhuni benhliziyo zenu uMozisi walivumela ukwala omkenu; kodwa kusukela ekuqaleni kwakungenjalo. 
Matthew19:9 Kodwa ngithi kini: Loba ngubani owala umkakhe, ngaphandle kokufeba, abesethatha omunye, uyafeba; futhi othatha owaliweyo uyafeba." 
Matthew19:10 Abafundi bathi kuye: Uba udaba lomuntu lomfazi lunjalo, akusizi ukuthatha." 
Matthew19:11 Kodwa wathi kubo: Kakusibo bonke. 
Matthew19:12 Ngoba kukhona abathenwa, abazalwa benjalo kusukela esiswini sikanina; njalo kukhona abathenwa, abathenwa ngabantu." 
Matthew19:13 Khona kwalethwa kuye abantwana abancane, ukuze abeke izandla zakhephezu kwabo, akhuleke; kodwa abafundi babakhuza." 
Matthew19:14 Kodwa uJesu wathi: Vumelani abantwana abancane, lingabenqabeli ukuza kimi; ngoba umbuso wamazulu ungowabanje." 
Matthew19:15 Wasebeka izandla phezu kwabo, wasuka lapho." 
Matthew19:16 Njalo khangela, kwasondela omunye wathi kuye: Mfundisi olungileyo, ngizakwenzani okulungileyo, ukuze ngibe lempilo elaphakade?" 
Matthew19:17 Wasesithi kuye: Ungibizelani ngokuthi olungileyo? Kakho olungileyo, ngaphandle koyedwa, uNkulunkulu." 
Matthew19:18 Wathi kuye: Yiyiphi? UJesu wasesithi: Ungabulali; ungafebi; ungebi; ungafakazi amanga; 
Matthew19:19 hlonipha uyihlo lonyoko. 
Matthew19:20 Ijaha lathi kuye: Konke lokhu ngikugcinile kusukela ebutsheni bami; ngisaswelani? 
Matthew19:21 UJesu wathi kulo: Uba uthanda ukuphelela; njalo uze lapha, ungilandele." 
Matthew19:22 Kodwa selizwile lelilizwi ijaha lasuka lidanile; ngoba lalilempahla ezinengi. 
Matthew19:23 UJesu wasesithi kubafundi bakhe: Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Onothileyo uzangena ngokulukhuni embusweni wamazulu. 
Matthew19:24 Njalo futhi ngithi kini: Kulula ukuthi. 
Matthew19:25 Sebezwile abafundi bakhe bamangala kakhulu, bathi: Pho kungasindiswa bani?" 
Matthew19:26 Kodwa uJesu wa ba khangela wathi kibo: Kubantu kakulakwenzeka. 
Matthew19:27 Khona uPetro waphendula wathi kuye: Khangela, thina sitshiye konke sakulandela; pho sizazuzani?" 
Matthew19:28 UJesu wasesithi kubo: Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Lina elingilandeleyo, ekuvuselelweni lapho iNdodana yomuntu isihlezi esihlalweni sobukhosi senkazimulo yayo." 
Matthew19:29 Laye wonke otshiye izindlu, kumbe abafowabo, kumbe odadewabo, kumbe uyise, kumbe unina, kumbe umkakhe, kumbe abantwana, kumbe amasimu, ngenxa yebizo lami, uzakwemukela ngekhulu, adle ilifa lempilo elaphakade." 
Matthew19:30 Kodwa abanengi abokuqala bazakuba ngabokucina. 
Matthew20:1 Ngoba umbuso wamazulu ufanana lomuntu ongumninindlu; 
Matthew20:2 esevumelene lezisebenzi ngodenariyo ngosuku, wazithuma esivinini sakhe." 
Matthew20:3 Wasephuma sekungaba lihola lesithathu, wabona abanye bemi emdangeni bengenzi lutho;" 
Matthew20:4 lakulabo wathi: Yanini lani esivinini; njalo loba yini efaneleyo ngizalinika yona. Bahamba-ke. 
Matthew20:5 Wabuya waphuma sekungaba lihola lesithupha langelesificamunwemunye, wenza njalo." 
Matthew20:6 Kwathi sekungaba lihola letshumi lanye waphuma, wathola abanye bemi bengenzi lutho, wathi kubo: Limeleni lapha usuku lonke lingenzi lutho?" 
Matthew20:7 Bathi kuye: Ngoba akulamuntu osiqatshileyo. Wathi kubo: Yanini lani esivinini, njalo lizakwemukela loba kuyini okufaneleyo." 
Matthew20:8 Kwathi sekuntambama umninisivini wathi enduneni yakhe. 
Matthew20:9 Kuthe befika aba qatshwangehola letshumi lanye ngulowo lalowo wemukela udenariyo. 
Matthew20:10 Njalo sebezile abokuqala bacabanga ukuthi bazakwemukela okungaphezulu; kodwa labo bemukela udenariyo ngamunye. 
Matthew20:11 Kwathi be ye mukela bamsola umninindlu," 
Matthew20:12 besithi: Labo abokucina basebenze ihola elilodwa, kodwa ubalinganise lathi." 
Matthew20:13 Kodwa ephendula wathi komunye wabo: Mngane, angikoni; kanti kawuvumelananga lami ngodenariyo?" 
Matthew20:14 Thatha okwakho uhambe; ngiyathanda ukumnika lowokucina njengawe. 
Matthew20:15 Kumbe angivunyelwa yini ukwenza engikuthandayo ngezinto zami? 
Matthew20:16 Kunjalo-ke abokucina bazakuba ngabokuqala, labokuqala ngabokucina." 
Matthew20:17 Kwathi uJesu: 
Matthew20:18 Khangelani, senyukela eJerusalema," 
Matthew20:19 bayinikele. 
Matthew20:20 Kwasekusiza kuye unina. 
Matthew20:21 Wasesithi kuye: Ufunani? Wathi kuye: Tshono ukuthi la amadodana ami amabili ahlale, lenye ngakwesokhohlo, embusweni wakho." 
Matthew20:22 Kodwa uJesu waphendula wathi: Kalikwazi elikucelayo. Linganatha yini inkezo engizayinatha mina? Bathi kuye: Singa kwenza. 
Matthew20:23 Wasesithi kubo: Ngeqiniso lizayinatha inkezo yami, libhabhathizwe ngobhabhathizo mina engizabhabhathizwa ngalo." 
Matthew20:24 Kwathi sebezwile abalitshumi, bathukuthela ngezelamani ezimbili." 
Matthew20:25 Kodwa uJesu wababizela kuye wathi: Liyazi ukuthi ababusi bezizwe. 
Matthew20:26 Kodwa akuyikuba njalo phakathi kwenu; kodwa loba ngubani othanda ukuba ngomkhulu phakathi kwenu; 
Matthew20:27 njalo loba ngubani othanda ukuba ngowokuqala phakathi kwenu kabe yisisebenzi senu; 
Matthew20:28 njengalokhu iNdodana yomuntu kayizanga ukukhonzwa, kodwa ukukhonza." 
Matthew20:29 Kwathi. 
Matthew20:30 Njalo khangela, iziphofu ezimbili zihlezi endleleni, sezizwile ukuthi uJesu uyadlula, zamemeza, zathi: Sihawukele, Nkosi, Ndodana kaDavida!" 
Matthew20:31 Ixuku laselizikhuza ukuthi zithule, kodwa zamemeza kakhulu, zisithi: Sihawukele, Nkosi, Ndodana kaDavida!" 
Matthew20:32 UJesu wasesima wazibiza, wathi: Lifuna ukuthi ngilenzeleni?" 
Matthew20:33 Zathi kuye: Nkosi, ukuthi amehlo ethu avuleke." 
Matthew20:34 UJesu esesiba lesihelo wathinta amehlo azo; njalo amehlo azo ahle abuya abona, zasezimlandela." 
Matthew21:1 Kwathi-ke sebesondele eJerusalema, khona uJesu wathuma abafundi ababili," 
Matthew21:2 esithi kubo: Hambani liye emzaneni okhangelene lani, lizahle libone ubabhemi ekhulekiwe, lethole lilaye; li ba khulule, li ba lethe kimi." 
Matthew21:3 Futhi uba umuntu ekhuluma ulutho kini, lizakuthi: INkosi iyabaswela; njalo uzahle abathumele." 
Matthew21:4 Njalo konke lokhu kwenzeka, ukuze kugcwaliseke okwakhulunywa ngumprofethi, ukuthi:" 
Matthew21:5 Tshelani indodakazi yeSiyoni ukuthi. 
Matthew21:6 Abafundi bahamba-ke, benza njengalokhu uJesu wayebalayile," 
Matthew21:7 baletha ubabhemi lethole, babeka izembatho zabo phezu kwabo, ba m hlalisa phezu kwazo." 
Matthew21:8 Lenengi lexuku lendlala ezalo izembatho endleleni. 
Matthew21:9 Lamaxuku ayehamba phambili lababelandela bamemeza, besithi: Hosana kuyo iNdodana kaDavida!" 
Matthew21:10 Esengenile eJerusalema? 
Matthew21:11 Amaxuku asesithi: Lo nguJesu umprofethi. 
Matthew21:12 UJesu wasengena ethempelini likaNkulunkulu, wabaxotsha bonke ababethengisa lababethenga ethempelini." 
Matthew21:13 Wasesithi kubo: Kulotshiwe ukuthi: Indlu yami izabizwa ngokuthi yindlu yomkhuleko. 
Matthew21:14 Kwasekufika kuye iziphofu leziqhuli ethempelini; wasezisilisa. 
Matthew21:15 Kodwa abapristi abakhulu lababhali sebebonile izimangaliso azenzayo, labantwana bememeza ethempelini, besithi: Hosana eNdodaneni kaDavida! bathukuthela," 
Matthew21:16 basebesithi kuye: Uyakuzwa lokhu yini abakutshoyo laba? UJesu wasesithi kubo: Yebo; alikaze lifunde yini ukuthi: Emlonyeni? 
Matthew21:17 Wasebatshiya waphuma phandle komuzi esiya eBethani, walala khona." 
Matthew21:18 Kwathi ebuyela emzini ekuseni, walamba;" 
Matthew21:19 kwathi ebona umkhiwa othile endleleni, wasondela kuwo, kodwa katholanga lutho kuwo ngaphandle kwamahlamvu wodwa; wathi kuwo: Kakungabe kusavela isithelo kuwe lanini. Njalo umkhiwa wahle wabuna." 
Matthew21:20 Kwathi bebona lokhuabafundi bakhe bamangala, besithi: Umkhiwa uhle wabuna njani?" 
Matthew21:21 UJesu wasephendula wathi kubo: Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Uba lilokholo. 
Matthew21:22 Njalo konke loba kuyini elikucelayo emkhulekweni, likholwa, lizakwemukela." 
Matthew21:23 Kwathi esengenile ethempelini, abapristi abakhulu labadala babantu basondela kuye esafundisa?" 
Matthew21:24 UJesu wasephendula wathi kubo: Lami ngizalibuza umbuzo ube munye; uba lingitshela lokhu, lami ngizalitshela ukuthi ngenza lezizinto ngaliphi igunya:" 
Matthew21:25 Ubhabhathizo lukaJohane lwavela ngaphi? Ezulwini kumbe ebantwini? Basebezindlisana, besithi: Uba sisithi: Ezulwini, uzakuthi kithi: Pho kalikholwanga kuye ngani?" 
Matthew21:26 Kodwa uba sisithi: Ebantwini, siyesaba ixuku." 
Matthew21:27 Basebemphendula uJesu bathi: Kasazi. Wasesithi kubo: Lami kangilitsheli ukuthi ngenza lezizinto ngaliphi igunya. 
Matthew21:28 Kanti licabangani. 
Matthew21:29 Kodwa yaphendula yathi: Angifuni. Kodwa emva kwalokho yaphenduka, yahamba." 
Matthew21:30 Wasesiya kweyesibili watsho ngokunjalo. Yona-ke yaphendula yathi: Ngiya hamba, nkosi. Kodwa kayiyanga." 
Matthew21:31 Yiyiphi kulawo amabili eyenza intando kayise? Bathi kuye: Eyokuqala. UJesu wathi kubo: Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Abathelisi. 
Matthew21:32 Ngoba uJohane wafika kini ngendlela yokulunga, kalikholwanga kuye." 
Matthew21:33 Zwanini omunye umfanekiso. Kwakukhona umuntu othile ongumninimuzi. 
Matthew21:34 Kwathi sekusondele isikhathi sezithelo, wathuma inceku zakhe kubalimi, ukuze zemukele izithelo zakhe." 
Matthew21:35 Abalimi basebezibamba inceku zakhe, enye bayitshaya." 
Matthew21:36 Wabuya wathuma ezinye inceku ezinengi kulezokuqala; basebesenza njalo kulezo. 
Matthew21:37 Ekucineni wasethuma indodana yakhe kubo, esithi: Bazayihlonipha indodana yami." 
Matthew21:38 Kodwa abalimi sebeyibonile indodana bakhulumisana besithi: Le yindlalifa. 
Matthew21:39 Basebeyibamba. 
Matthew21:40 Ngakho mhla kufika umninisivini, uzabenzani abalimi labo?" 
Matthew21:41 Bathi kuye: Uzababhubhisa kakubi labo ababi. 
Matthew21:42 UJesu wathi kubo: Alikaze lifunde yini emibhalweni ukuthi: Ilitshe abakhi abalalayo, yilo eseliyinhloko yengonsi; lokhu yikwenza kweNkosi; njalo kuyamangalisa emehlweni ethu?" 
Matthew21:43 Ngakho ngithi kini: Lizakwemukwa umbuso kaNkulunkulu, unikwe isizwe esithela izithelo zawo." 
Matthew21:44 Lalowo owela phezu kwalelilitshe uzaphahlazwa. 
Matthew21:45 Kwathi abapristi abakhulu labaFarisi sebezwile imifanekiso yakhe bazi ukuthi ubekhuluma ngabo. 
Matthew21:46 Kwathi sebedinga ukumbamba. 
Matthew22:1 UJesu wasephendula wabuya wakhuluma labo ngemifanekiso, wathi:" 
Matthew22:2 Umbuso wamazulu ufananiswa lomuntu oy inkosi; 
Matthew22:3 wasethuma inceku zakhe ukuthi zibize abanxusiweyo emtshadweni, kodwa kabavumanga ukubuya." 
Matthew22:4 Wabuya wathuma ezinye inceku, izinto zonke sezilungile; wozani emtshadweni." 
Matthew22:5 Kodwa kabananzanga, bazihambela, omunye ensimini yakhe, omunye ekuthengiselaneni kwakhe;" 
Matthew22:6 abaseleyo basebezibamba inceku zakhe ba zi phatha kubi ba zi bulala. 
Matthew22:7 Kodwa kwathi inkosi ikuzwa lokhoyathukuthela, yathuma amabutho ayo yabhubhisa labobabulali, yatshisa umuzi wabo." 
Matthew22:8 Yasisithi encekwini zayo: Umtshado usulungile, kodwa abanxusiweyo bebengafanelanga." 
Matthew22:9 Ngakho yanini emahlanganweni ezindlela, njalo bonke elingabathola, libabizele emtshadweni." 
Matthew22:10 Lezonceku zaseziphuma zaya ezindleleni zabutha bonke ezabatholayo, ababi kanye labalungileyo; indlu yomtshado yasigcwala ngabahleziyo." 
Matthew22:11 Kwathi inkosi ingena ukukhangela ababehlezi ekudleni yabona khona umuntu owayengembathanga; 
Matthew22:12 yasisithi kuye: Mngane, ungene njani lapha ungelasembatho somtshado." 
Matthew22:13 Inkosi yasisithi ezincekwini. 
Matthew22:14 Ngoba banengi ababiziweyo, kodwa balutshwana abakhethiweyo." 
Matthew22:15 Khona-ke abaFarisi basuka, bacebisana ngokuthi bangamthiya njani ekukhulumeni." 
Matthew22:16 Basebethuma kuye abafundi babo kanye labakaHerodi. 
Matthew22:17 Ngakho sitshele, wena ucabangani? Kuvunyelwe yini ukuthela?" 
Matthew22:18 Kodwa uJesu ebazi ububi babo wathi? 
Matthew22:19 Ngitshengisani imali yokuthela. Basebemlethela udenariyo. 
Matthew22:20 Wasesithi kubo: Ngokabani lumfanekiso lalumbhalo? 
Matthew22:21 Bathi: NgokaKesari. Wasesithi kubo: Ngakho mnikeni uKesari izinto zikaKesari; loNkulunkulu izinto zikaNkulunkulu. 
Matthew22:22 Kwathi sebezwile bamangala; bamtshiya bahamba. 
Matthew22:23 Ngalolosuku kweza kuye abaSadusi, basebembuza," 
Matthew22:24 besithi: Mfundisi, uMozisi wathi: Uba umuntu esifa engelabantwana, umfowabo uzamthatha umkakhe, amvusele umfowabo inzalo." 
Matthew22:25 Kwakukhona phakathi kwethu izelamani eziyisikhombisa; owokuqala wasethatha umfazi wafa; futhi engelanzalo, watshiya umkakhe kumfowabo." 
Matthew22:26 Kwaba njalo lowesibili, lowesithathu, kwaze kwaba kowesikhombisa." 
Matthew22:27 Kwathi emva kwabo bonke kwafa lomfazi. 
Matthew22:28 Ngakho ekuvukeni kwabafileyo, uzakuba ngumkabani kwabayisikhombisa? Ngoba bonke babelaye." 
Matthew22:29 Kodwa uJesu waphendula wathi kubo: Liduhile, lingayazi imibhalo;" 
Matthew22:30 ngoba ekuvukeni kwabafileyo kabathathani, kabendiswa, kodwa banjengengilosi zikaNkulunkulu ezulwini." 
Matthew22:31 Kodwa mayelana lokuvuka okwabafileyo, kalifundanga yini okwakhulunywa kini nguNkulunkulu, esithi:" 
Matthew22:32 Mina nginguNkulunkulu kaAbrahama, loNkulunkulu kaIsaka, loNkulunkulu kaJakobe? UNkulunkulu kayisuye uNkulunkulu wabafileyo, kodwa owabaphilayo." 
Matthew22:33 Kwathi amaxuku ekuzwa amangala kakhulu ngokufundisa kwakhe. 
Matthew22:34 Kwathi abaFarisi, sebezwile ukuthi uJesu ubaqume umlomo, babuthana ndawonye." 
Matthew22:35 Lomunye wabo, isazumthetho, wa m buza:" 
Matthew22:36 Mfundisi, yiwuphi umlayo omkhulu emthethweni?" 
Matthew22:37 UJesu wasesithi kuye: Wothanda iNkosi uNkulunkulu wakho, ngenhliziyo yakho yonke, langomphefumulo wakho wonke, langengqondo yakho yonke;" 
Matthew22:38 yiwo lowo umlayo owokuqala lomkhulu. 
Matthew22:39 Lowesibili ufanana lawo uthi: Wothanda umakhelwane wakho njengalokhu uzi thanda wena. 
Matthew22:40 Kuleyomilayo emibili kumisiwe umthetho wonke labaprofethi. 
Matthew22:41 Kwathi sebebuthene abaFarisi, uJesu wababuza," 
Matthew22:42 esithi: Licabangani ngoKristu? Uyindodana kabani. 
Matthew22:43 Wathi kubo: Pho uDavida wambiza njani ekuMoya ngokuthiyiNkosi, esithi:" 
Matthew22:44 INkosi yathi eNkosini yami: Hlala ngakwesokunene sami, ngize ngenze izitha zakho zibe yisenabelo senyawo zakho?" 
Matthew22:45 Ngakho uba uDavida embiza ngokuthi yiNkosi, uyiNdodana yakhe njani?" 
Matthew22:46 Njalo kwakungekho owayengamphendula ilizwi. 
Matthew23:1 Khona uJesu wakhuluma emaxukwini lakubafundi bakhe," 
Matthew23:2 esithi: Ababhali labaFarisi bahlezi esihlalweni sikaMozisi; 
Matthew23:3 ngakho konke lokhu abalitshela khona ukuthi likugcine, ku gcineni li kw enze; kodwa lingenzi njengokwemisebenzi yabo." 
Matthew23:4 Ngoba bayabopha imithwalo enzima njalo elukhuni ukuthwalwa, ba yi beke emahlombe abantu, kodwa kabafuni ukuyisusa ngomunwe wabo." 
Matthew23:5 Njalo imisebenzi yabo yonke bayenza ukuze babonwe ngabantu; 
Matthew23:6 bathanda izihlalo zabahloniphekayo ekudleni kwantambama," 
Matthew23:7 lokubingelelwa emidangeni. 
Matthew23:8 Kodwa lina kalingabizwa ngokuthiRabi; njalo lina lonke lingabazalwane. 
Matthew23:9 Futhi lingabizi muntu emhlabeni ngokuthinguyihlo; 
Matthew23:10 kalingabizwa ngokuthi ling abafundisi. 
Matthew23:11 Kodwa omkhulu kini. 
Matthew23:12 Lalowo oziphakamisayo, uzathotshiswa; lalowo ozithobayo, uzaphakanyiswa." 
Matthew23:13 Kodwa maye kini, babhali labaFarisi, bazenzisi." 
Matthew23:14 Maye kini, babhali labaFarisi, bazenzisi, ngoba lidla izindlu zabafelokazi, langokuzenzisa lenza imikhuleko emide; ngakho lizakwemukela ukulahlwa okukhulu." 
Matthew23:15 Maye kini, babhali labaFarisi, bazenzisi, ngoba libhoda ulwandle lomhlaba ukuthi lenze abe munye ophendukela kumaJuda." 
Matthew23:16 Maye kini, bakhokheli abayiziphofu." 
Matthew23:17 Zithutha leziphofu? 
Matthew23:18 Njalo: Loba ngubani ofunga ngelathi, akulutho; kodwa loba ngubani ofunga ngomnikelo ophezu kwalo, ulomlandu." 
Matthew23:19 Zithutha leziphofu! Ngoba yikuphi okukhulu? 
Matthew23:20 Ngakho ofunga ngelathi ufunga ngalo langakho konke okuphezu kwalo; 
Matthew23:21 lofunga ngethempeli ufunga ngalo langaye ohlala kulo; 
Matthew23:22 lofunga ngezulu ufunga ngesihlalo sobukhosi sikaNkulunkulu langaye ohlala phezu kwaso. 
Matthew23:23 Maye kini, babhali labaFarisi, bazenzisi, ngoba lithela okwetshumi kwetshwayi leganga ledile lekhumini." 
Matthew23:24 Bakhokheli abayiziphofu. 
Matthew23:25 Maye kini, babhali labaFarisi, bazenzisi, ngoba lihlambulula ingaphandle." 
Matthew23:26 MFarisi oyisiphofu! Hlambulula kuqala ingaphakathi yenkezo leyomganu, ukuze kuhlambuluke lengaphandle yakho." 
Matthew23:27 Maye kini, babhali labaFarisi, bazenzisi." 
Matthew23:28 Kunjalo lani ngaphandle libonakala ebantwini lilungile, kanti ngaphakathi ligcwele ukuzenzisa lobubi." 
Matthew23:29 Maye kini, babhali labaFarisi, bazenzisi, ngoba lakha amangcwaba abaprofethi," 
Matthew23:30 lithi: Uba besikhona ensukwini zabobaba bethu, besingayikuhlanganyela labo egazini labaprofethi." 
Matthew23:31 Kunjalo liyazifakazela lina ukuthi lingamadodana alabo ababulala abaprofethi; 
Matthew23:32 lina-ke gcwalisani! 
Matthew23:33 Zinyoka, nzalo yamabululu?" 
Matthew23:34 Ngakho, khangelani, mina ngithuma kini abaprofethi labahlakaniphileyo;" 
Matthew23:35 ukuze kwehlele phezu kwenu igazi lonke elilungileyo elachithwa emhlabeni. 
Matthew23:36 Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Zonke lezizinto zizakwehlela phezu kwalesisizukulwana. 
Matthew23:37 Jerusalema, Jerusalema." 
Matthew23:38 Khangelani, indlu yenu itshiyiwe kini ilunxiwa." 
Matthew23:39 Ngoba ngithi kini: Kalisoze langibona kusukela khathesi, lize lithi: Ubusisiwe ozayo ebizweni leNkosi." 
Matthew24:1 UJesu wasephuma; basebesondela abafundi bakhe ukumtshengisa izakhiwo zethempeli. 
Matthew24:2 UJesu wasesithi kubo: Kaliziboni yini zonke lezizinto? Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Akusoze kutshiywe lapha ilitshe elilodwa phezu kwelitshe, elingasoze lidilizelwe phansi." 
Matthew24:3 Kwathi esehlezi entabeni yeMihlwathi? 
Matthew24:4 UJesu wasephendula wathi kubo: Qaphelani, kungabi khona oliduhisayo;" 
Matthew24:5 ngoba abanengi bazakuza ngebizo lami, besithi: Mina nginguKristu." 
Matthew24:6 Njalo lizakuzwa ngezimpi lamahungahunga ezimpi; nanzelelani, lingethuki; ngoba konke lokhukufanele kwenzeke; kodwa ukuphela kakukabi khona." 
Matthew24:7 Ngoba isizwe sizavukela isizwe; 
Matthew24:8 kodwa zonke lezizinto ziyikuqala kwemihelo. 
Matthew24:9 Lapho-ke bazalinikela. 
Matthew24:10 Njalo ngalesosikhathi abanengi bazakhubeka, banikelane, bazondane." 
Matthew24:11 Futhi kuzavuka abaprofethi bamanga abanengi. 
Matthew24:12 Njalo ngenxa yokwanda kobubi, uthando lwabanengi luzaphola;" 
Matthew24:13 kodwa ophikelelayo kuze kube sekupheleni, nguye ozasindiswa." 
Matthew24:14 Njalo lelivangeli lombuso. 
Matthew24:15 Ngakho nxa libona amanyala encithakalo, akhulunywa nguDaniyeli umprofethi," 
Matthew24:16 khona labo abaseJudiya kababalekele ezintabeni; 
Matthew24:17 ophezu kophahla angehli ukuthatha ulutho endlini yakhe; 
Matthew24:18 losemasimini angabuyeli emuva uku ya thatha izembatho zakhe. 
Matthew24:19 Kodwa maye kwabakhulelweyo labamunyisayo ngalezonsuku! 
Matthew24:20 Kodwa khulekani ukuthi ukubaleka kwenu kungabi sebusika, loba ngesabatha." 
Matthew24:21 Ngoba ngalesosikhathi kuzakuba khona ukuhlupheka okukhulu. 
Matthew24:22 Uba-ke lezonsuku bezingafinyezwanga, bekungesindiswe nyama." 
Matthew24:23 Ngalesosikhathi nxa umuntu esithi kini: Khangelani, nangu uKristu, kumbe nanguya, lingakholwa." 
Matthew24:24 Ngoba kuzavuka okristu bamanga labaprofethi bamanga. 
Matthew24:25 Khangelani, sengilitshelile ngaphambili." 
Matthew24:26 Ngakho uba bengathi kini.
