Matthew24:27 Ngoba njengalokhu umbane ubaneka empumalanga ukhanye lentshonalanga, kuzakuba njalo lokufika kweNdodana yomuntu." 
Matthew24:28 Ngoba loba ngaphi lapho okukhona isidumbu. 
Matthew24:29 Njalo masinyane emva kokuhlupheka kwalezonsuku. 
Matthew24:30 Khona-ke sizabonakala. 
Matthew24:31 Njalo izathuma izingilosi zayo. 
Matthew24:32 Kodwa fundani umfanekiso emkhiweni; nxa khathesi ugatsha lwawo selusiba buthakathaka, njalo luhlume amahlamvu, liyazi ukuthi ihlobo seliseduze;" 
Matthew24:33 ngokunjalo lani, nxa libona lezizinto zonke, yazini ukuthi kuseduze kuseminyango." 
Matthew24:34 Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Lesisizukulwana asisoze sidlule, kuze kwenzeke zonke lezizinto." 
Matthew24:35 Kuzadlula izulu lomhlaba. 
Matthew24:36 Kodwa lolosuku lehola. 
Matthew24:37 Kodwa njengensuku zikaNowa, kuzakuba njalo ukufika kweNdodana yomuntu." 
Matthew24:38 Ngoba njengakulezonsuku ezaziphambili kukazamcolo," 
Matthew24:39 njalo babengazi, kwaze kwafika uzamcolo wasebasusa bonke, kuzakuba njalo lokufika kweNdodana yomuntu." 
Matthew24:40 Ngalesosikhathi kuzakuba khona ababili ensimini; omunye athathwe, lomunye atshiywe;" 
Matthew24:41 kuzakuthi abesifazanaababili bechola elitsheni; omunye athathwe, lomunye atshiywe." 
Matthew24:42 Ngakho lindani. 
Matthew24:43 Kodwa yazini lokhu. 
Matthew24:44 Ngakho lani hlalani lilungile. 
Matthew24:45 Pho ngubani? 
Matthew24:46 Ibusisiwe leyonceku, okuzakuthi inkosi yayo nxa ifika izayifica isenza njalo." 
Matthew24:47 Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Izayibeka phezu kwakho konke elakho. 
Matthew24:48 Kodwa nxa leyonceku embi isithi enhliziyweni yayo: Inkosi yami iphuzile ukubuya," 
Matthew24:49 njalo ibisiqala ukutshaya abayizinceku kanye layo, lokudla lokunatha lezidakwa," 
Matthew24:50 inkosi yaleyonceku izafika ngosuku enga yi lindele ngalo, langehola engalaziyo," 
Matthew24:51 izayiquma phakathi, izanika isabelo sayo labazenzisi." 
Matthew25:1 Ngalesosikhathi umbuso wamazulu uzafananiswa lentombi ezilitshumi. 
Matthew25:2 Njalo ezinhlanu zazo. 
Matthew25:3 Eziyizithutha zathatha izibane zazo, kazithathanga amafutha kanye lazo;" 
Matthew25:4 kodwa ezihlakaniphileyo zathatha amafutha ezitsheni kanye lezibane zazo. 
Matthew25:5 Kwathi umyeni esephuzile. 
Matthew25:6 Kodwa phakathi kobusuku kwamenyezwa: Khangelani, umyeni uyeza, phumani liyemhlangabeza!" 
Matthew25:7 Zasezivuka lezontombi zonke, zalungisa izibane zazo." 
Matthew25:8 Eziyizithutha zasezisithi: Sipheni okwamafutha enu, ngoba izibane zethu ziyacitsha." 
Matthew25:9 Kodwa ezihlakaniphileyo zaphendula. 
Matthew25:10 Kwathi zisiyathenga, weza umyeni. Ezasezilungile zasezingena laye." 
Matthew25:11 Kwathi emva kwalokho zafika lalezontombi ezinye, zathi: Nkosi, Nkosi, sivulele!" 
Matthew25:12 Kodwa yena waphendula wathi: Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Angilazi lina. 
Matthew25:13 Ngakho lindani. 
Matthew25:14 Ngoba; 
Matthew25:15 kwathi enye wayinika amathalenta amahlanu, lenye amabili, lenye lalinye, kwaba yileyo laleyo." 
Matthew25:16 Leyo eyayemukele amathalenta amahlanu yasihamba yathengiselana ngawo, yenza amanye amathalenta amahlanu." 
Matthew25:17 Ngokunjalo laleyo e la mabili, layo yazuza amanye amabili." 
Matthew25:18 Kodwa leyo eyayemukele elilodwa yasuka yagebha emhlabathini yayifihla imali yenkosi yayo. 
Matthew25:19 Kwathi emva kwesikhathi eside inkosi yalezozinceku yafika, yasilandiselana lazo." 
Matthew25:20 Kwasekusiza eyayemukele amathalenta amahlanu yaletha amanye amathalenta amahlanu, yathi: Nkosi, wanginika amathalenta amahlanu; khangela, ngizuzile amanye amathalenta amahlanu phezu kwawo." 
Matthew25:21 Inkosi yayo yasisithi kiyo: Kuhle, nceku elungileyo lethembekileyo, ubuthembekile ezintweni ezinlutshwana." 
Matthew25:22 Kwasekusiza laleyo eyayemukele amathalenta amabili yathi: Nkosi, wanginika amathalenta amabili; khangela, ngizuzile amanye amathalenta amabili phezu kwawo." 
Matthew25:23 Inkosi yayo yathi kiyo: Kuhle, nceku elungileyo lethembekileyo, ubuthembekile ezintweni ezinlutshwana, ngizakubeka phezu kwezinengi; ngena entokozweni yenkosi yakho." 
Matthew25:24 Kodwa kweza laleyo eyayemukele ithalenta elilodwa yathi: Nkosi, bengikwazi wena;" 
Matthew25:25 ngasengisesaba, ngasuka ngalifihla ithalenta lakho emhlabathini; khangela, ulokwakho." 
Matthew25:26 Kodwa inkosi yayo yaphendula yathi kiyo: Nceku embi lelivila, ubusazi ukuthi ngivuna lapho engingahlanyelanga khona, njalo ngibutha lapho engingahlakazanga khona;" 
Matthew25:27 ngakho ngabe ubekile imali yami ebhanga, njalo ekufikeni kwami ngabe ngemukele okwami lenzuzo." 
Matthew25:28 Ngakho mthatheleni ithalenta, li li nike yena olamathalenta alitshumi." 
Matthew25:29 Ngoba wonke olakho uzaphiwa, uzakwengezelelwa; kodwa ongelakho uzathathelwa lalokho alakho." 
Matthew25:30 Laleyonceku engasizi lutho iphoseleni emnyameni ongaphandle. 
Matthew25:31 Njalo nxa isiza iNdodana yomuntu ngobukhosi bayo," 
Matthew25:32 kuzabuthelwa phambi kwayo izizwe zonke; 
Matthew25:33 ibisibeka izimvu ngakwesokunene sayo, kodwa imbuzi ngakwesokhohlo." 
Matthew25:34 Khona-ke iNkosi. 
Matthew25:35 Ngoba ngangilambile, langinika ukudla; ngangomile, langinathisa;" 
Matthew25:36 ngangize, langigqokisa." 
Matthew25:37 Khona abalungileyo bezayiphendula, besithi: Nkosi, sakubona nini ulambile, njalo sa ku nika ukudla, kumbe womile, njalo sa ku nathisa?" 
Matthew25:38 Njalo sakubona nini ungowemzini, futhi sa kw emukela, kumbe uze, futhi sa ku gqokisa?" 
Matthew25:39 Njalo sakubona nini ugula, loba usentolongweni, njalo seza kuwe?" 
Matthew25:40 Futhi iNkosi izaphendula ithi kubo. 
Matthew25:41 Ngalesosikhathi izakuthi njalo kubo abangakwesokhohlo: Sukani kimi, lina eliqalekisiweyo." 
Matthew25:42 Ngoba ngangilambile, kodwa kalinginikanga ukudla; ngangomile, kodwa kalinginathisanga;" 
Matthew25:43 ngangingowemzini, kodwa kalingemukelanga; ngangi ze, kodwa kalingigqokisanga; ngangi gula, ngangi sentolongweni, kodwa kalizanga ukungibona." 
Matthew25:44 Khona lalaba bezamphendula, besithi: Nkosi, sakubona nini ulambile, loba womile, loba ungowemzini, loba uze, loba ugula, loba usentolongweni, kodwa kasakusiza?" 
Matthew25:45 Isizabaphendula, ithi: Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Njengoba linga kw enzanga komunye walaba abancinyane, kali kw enzanga lakimi." 
Matthew25:46 Lalaba bazakuya ekujezisweni okulaphakade. 
Matthew26:1 Kwasekusithi uJesu eseqedile wonke lamazwi, wathi kubafundi bakhe:" 
Matthew26:2 Liyazi ukuthi emva kwensuku ezimbili kuzakuba liphasika, leNdodana yomuntu izanikelwa ukuze ibethelwe." 
Matthew26:3 Kwasekubuthana abapristi abakhulu lababhali labadala babantu," 
Matthew26:4 basebecebisana ukuthi bambambe uJesu ngobuqili ba m bulale. 
Matthew26:5 Kodwa bathi: Kungabi ngomkhosi, hlezi kube khona isiphithiphithi ebantwini." 
Matthew26:6 Kwathi uJesu," 
Matthew26:7 kwafika kuye owesifazana ephethe umfuma we-alibasta ulamagcobo aligugu elikhulu. 
Matthew26:8 Kodwa abafundi bebona lokhubathukuthela, bathi: Ngokwani ukumotsha lokhu?" 
Matthew26:9 Ngoba la amagcobo angathengiswa ngokunengi, besekunikwa abayanga." 
Matthew26:10 Kodwa uJesu ekwazi wathi kubo: Limhluphelani owesifazana? Ngoba wenzile umsebenzi omuhle kimi; 
Matthew26:11 ngoba abayanga lihlala lilabo. 
Matthew26:12 Ngoba ngokuthululela la amagcobo emzimbeni wami, u kw enzele umngcwabo wami." 
Matthew26:13 Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Loba ngaphi emhlabeni wonke lapho okuzatshunyayelwa khona lelivangeli, lalokho akwenzileyo kuzakhulunywa ngakho, kube yisikhumbuzo ngaye." 
Matthew26:14 Omunye wabalitshumi lambili, wasesiya kubapristi abakhulu," 
Matthew26:15 wathi: Lizanginikani, mina-ke ngizamnikela kini? Basebevumelana laye." 
Matthew26:16 Njalo kusukela lapho wadinga ithuba elihle lokumnikela. 
Matthew26:17 Kwathi, besithi kuye: Uthanda ukuthi sikulungisele ngaphi ukuthi udle iphasika?" 
Matthew26:18 Wasesithi: Hambani liye emzini kusibanibani. 
Matthew26:19 Benza-ke abafundi njengoba uJesu ebalayile, basebelungisa iphasika." 
Matthew26:20 Kwathi ifika intambama. 
Matthew26:21 Bathi besidla wathi: Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Omunye wenu uzanginikela. 
Matthew26:22 Basebedabuka kakhulu baqala ukuthi kuye ngamunye wabo: Nkosi, yimi yini?" 
Matthew26:23 Wasephendula wathi: Ofaka isandla sakhekanye lami emganwini, nguye ozanginikela." 
Matthew26:24 Sibili iNdodana yomuntu. 
Matthew26:25 Wasephendula uJudasi owamnikelayo wathi: Rabi, yimi yini." 
Matthew26:26 Kwathi besidla, uJesu wathatha isinkwa." 
Matthew26:27 Wasethatha inkezo, wabonga, wabanika, esithi: Nathani lonke kuyo;" 
Matthew26:28 ngoba lokhu. 
Matthew26:29 Kodwa ngithi kini: Kusukela khathesi kangiyikunatha okwalesisithelo sevini, kuze kufikelolosuku lapho ngizasinatha lani sisitsha." 
Matthew26:30 Kwathi sebehlabele ingoma yokudumisa. 
Matthew26:31 UJesu wasesithi kubo: Lina lonke lizakhubeka ngami ngalobubusuku. 
Matthew26:32 Kodwa emva kokuvuswa kwami, ngizalandulela ukuya eGalili." 
Matthew26:33 Kodwa uPetro waphendula wathi kuye: Lanxa bonke bezakhubeka ngawe, mina angisoze ngikhubeke." 
Matthew26:34 UJesu wathi kuye: Ngiqinisile ngithi kuwe: Ngalobubusuku. 
Matthew26:35 UPetro wathi kuye: Loba kudingeka ngife lawe, angisoze ngikuphike. Basebesitsho njalo bonke abafundi." 
Matthew26:36 UJesu wasefika labo endaweni. 
Matthew26:37 Wasethatha kanye laye uPetro lamadodana amabili kaZebediya. 
Matthew26:38 Wasesithi kubo: Umphefumulo wami udabukile kakhulu kuze kube sekufeni. 
Matthew26:39 Waseqhubeka ibangana, wawa ngobuso bakhe wakhuleka wathi." 
Matthew26:40 Wasesiza kubafundi, wabafica belele?" 
Matthew26:41 Lindani likhuleke, ukuze lingangeni ekulingweni." 
Matthew26:42 Wabuya wasuka ngokwesibili wakhuleka, wathi: Baba." 
Matthew26:43 Wasebuya wabafica futhi belele, ngoba amehlo abo ayenzima." 
Matthew26:44 Wasebatshiya wahamba futhi wakhuleka ngokwesithathu, esitsho wona lawomazwi." 
Matthew26:45 Wasesiza kubafundi bakhe, wathi kubo: Qhubekani lilele liphumule; khangelani, isikhathi sesisondele, futhi iNdodana yomuntu iyanikelwa ezandleni zezoni." 
Matthew26:46 Sukumani, sihambe; khangelani, onginikelayo useduze." 
Matthew26:47 Kwathi esakhuluma, khangela, kwafika uJudasi, omunye wabalitshumi lambili." 
Matthew26:48 Laye omnikelayo wayebanike isiboniso, esithi: Lowo engizamanga, nguye; limbambe." 
Matthew26:49 Njalo wahle wasondela kuJesu wathi: Mpilo enhle, Rabi." 
Matthew26:50 UJesu wasesithi kuye: Mngane, ulandeni? Basebesondela bamdumela uJesu ngezandla, bambamba." 
Matthew26:51 Futhi khangela, omunye walabo ababeloJesu." 
Matthew26:52 UJesu wasesithi kuye: Buyisela inkemba yakho endaweni yayo; ngoba bonke ababamba inkemba bazabhubha ngenkemba. 
Matthew26:53 Kumbe ucabanga ukuthi ngingemcele uBaba yini khathesi, futhi anginike amabutho amakhulu ezingilosi?" 
Matthew26:54 Pho ingagcwaliseka njani imibhalo, ukuthi kumele ukuthi kube njalo?" 
Matthew26:55 Ngalelohola uJesu wathi emaxukwini: Liphume njengokuyamelana lomphangi. 
Matthew26:56 Kodwa konke lokhu kwenzakele, ukuze kugcwaliseke imibhalo yabaprofethi." 
Matthew26:57 Lababembambile uJesu ba m qhuba. 
Matthew26:58 Kodwa uPetro wamlandela ekhatshana, kwaze kwaba segumeni lompristi omkhulu." 
Matthew26:59 Njalo abapristi abakhulu labadala lomphakathi wonke badinga ubufakazi bamanga obumelana loJesu, ukuze bambulale," 
Matthew26:60 kodwa kaba bu tholanga; lanxa kwavela abafakazi abanengi bamanga," 
Matthew26:61 bathi: Lo wathi: Ngilakho ukudiliza ithempeli likaNkulunkulu. 
Matthew26:62 Kwasekusukuma umpristi omkhulu wathi kuye: Kawuphenduli lutho yini? Bafakazani laba okumelana lawe? 
Matthew26:63 Kodwa uJesu wathula. 
Matthew26:64 UJesu wathi kuye: Utshilo wena. 
Matthew26:65 Umpristi omkhulu wasedabula izembatho zakhe, wathi: Usehlambazile; sisadingelani abafakazi? Khangelani, khathesi seliyizwile inhlamba yakhe;" 
Matthew26:66 licabangani? Basebephendula besithi: Ulecala. 
Matthew26:67 Basebemkhafulela amathe ebusweni," 
Matthew26:68 bathi: Profetha kithi, Kristu, ngubani okutshayileyo?" 
Matthew26:69 UPetro wayesehlezi ngaphandle. 
Matthew26:70 Kodwa waphika phambi kwabo bonke, wathi: Kangikwazi lokho okutshoyo." 
Matthew26:71 Kwathi esephuma esiya esangweni. 
Matthew26:72 Wasebuya ephika ngesifungo esithi: Kangimazi lumuntu. 
Matthew26:73 Kwathi emva kwesikhatshana. 
Matthew26:74 Waseqala ukuqalekisa lokufunga esithi: Kangimazi lumuntu. Njalo lahle lakhala iqhude. 
Matthew26:75 UPetro wasekhumbula ilizwi likaJesu esithi kuye. 
Matthew27:1 Kwathi sekusile, bonke abapristi abakhulu labadala babantu;" 
Matthew27:2 sebembophile ba m qhuba. 
Matthew27:3 Kwathi uJudasi owamnikelayo esebonile ukuthi ulahliwe," 
Matthew27:4 wathi: Ngonile nginikele igazi elingelacala. Kodwa bona bathi: Kulani lathi? Zibonele wena. 
Matthew27:5 Wasephosela inhlamvu zesiliva ethempelini, wasuka; wayaziphanyeka." 
Matthew27:6 Abapristi abakhulu basebethatha inhlamvu zesiliva bathi: Kakuvunyelwa ukuzifaka emnikelweni, ngoba ziyintengo yegazi." 
Matthew27:7 Basebecebisana bathenga ngazo isiqinti sombumbi, sibe ngesokungcwaba abezizwe." 
Matthew27:8 Ngakho lesosiqinti sathiwa yisiqinti segazi. 
Matthew27:9 Kwasekugcwaliseka okwakhulunywa ngumprofethi uJeremiya, esithi: Basebethatha inhlamvu zesiliva ezingamatshumi amathathu, intengo yalowo owalinganiswayo, abantwana bakoIsrayeli abamlinganisayo;" 
Matthew27:10 basebebapha zona ngensimu yombumbi. 
Matthew27:11 UJesu wasesima phambi kombusi; umbusi wasembuza, wathi: Wena uyiNkosi yamaJuda yini." 
Matthew27:12 Kwathi nxa esemangalelwe ngabapristi abakhulu labadala, kaphendulanga lutho." 
Matthew27:13 UPilatu wasesithi kuye: Kawuzwa yini izinto ezingaka abazifakaza ngawe? 
Matthew27:14 Kodwa kamphendulanga lakwelilodwa ilizwi, waze wamangala kakhulu umbusi." 
Matthew27:15 Futhi ngomkhosi umbusi wayejwayele ukukhululela ixuku. 
Matthew27:16 Njalo ngalesosikhathi babelesibotshwa esidumileyo, esithiwa nguBarabasi." 
Matthew27:17 Ngakho sebebuthene, uPilatu wathi kubo: Lithanda ukuthi ngilikhululele bani, uBarabasi, kumbe uJesu othiwa nguKristu?" 
Matthew27:18 Ngoba wayekwazi ukuthi bamnikele ngomona. 
Matthew27:19 Kwathi esehlezi esihlalweni sokwahlulela. 
Matthew27:20 Kodwa abapristi abakhulu labadala bancengana lamaxuku ukuthi acele uBarabasi, ambhubhise uJesu." 
Matthew27:21 Wasephendula umbusi wathi kubo: Lithanda ukuthi ngilikhululele bani kulaba ababili? Basebesithi: UBarabasi. 
Matthew27:22 UPilatu wathi kubo: Pho ngimenzeni uJesu othiwa nguKristu? Bonke bathi kuye: Kabethelwe. 
Matthew27:23 Umbusi wasesithi: Ngoba wenze bubi bani? Kodwa bamemeza kakhulu, bathi: Kabethelwe!" 
Matthew27:24 Kwathi uPilatu esebonile ukuthi kakusizi lutho, kodwa kwasekuqala kulalokhu ukuba lesiphithiphithi." 
Matthew27:25 Bonke abantu basebephendula bathi: Igazi lakhe kalibephezu kwethu laphezu kwabantwana bethu. 
Matthew27:26 Wasebakhululela uBarabasi; kodwa esemtshaye ngesiswepu uJesu wa m nikela ukuthi abethelwe. 
Matthew27:27 Abebutho bombusi basebemngenisa uJesu endlini yombusi; 
Matthew27:28 bamhlubula, bamgqokisa isembatho esibomvu," 
Matthew27:29 sebelukile umqhele wameva, bamethesa wonaekhanda, bamphathisalomhlanga esandleni sakhe sokunene; baguqa phambi kwakhe!" 
Matthew27:30 Bamkhafulela amathe, bathatha umhlanga, batshaya ikhanda lakhe." 
Matthew27:31 Sebemklolodele. 
Matthew27:32 Kwathi sebephuma. 
Matthew27:33 Sebefikile endaweni ethiwa yiGolgotha," 
Matthew27:34 bamnika iviniga. 
Matthew27:35 Futhi sebembethele, babelana izembatho zakhe, benza inkatho yokuphosa." 
Matthew27:36 Njalo sebehlala phansi bamlinda khona. 
Matthew27:37 Babeka ngaphezu kwekhanda lakhe incwadiyecala lakhe ilotshiwe ukuthi. 
Matthew27:38 Kwasekubethelwa abaphangi ababili. 
Matthew27:39 Labadlulayo," 
Matthew27:40 besithi: Wena odiliza ithempeli ulakhe ngensuku ezintathu, zisindise." 
Matthew27:41 Langokunjalo labapristi abakhulu labo bekloloda kanye lababhali labadala bathi: 
Matthew27:42 Wasindisa abanye, yena angezisindise. Uba eyiNkosi yakoIsrayeli, kehle khathesi esiphambanweni, futhi sizamkholwa." 
Matthew27:43 Wathemba kuNkulunkulu; kamkhulule khathesi, uba emthanda." 
Matthew27:44 Labaphangi. 
Matthew27:45 Njalo kusukela ngehola lesithupha kwaba lobumnyama emhlabeni wonke kwaze kwaba lihola lesificamunwemunye; 
Matthew27:46 sekungaba lihola lesificamunwemunye? 
Matthew27:47 Njalo abanye kwababemi khona besizwa bathi: Lo ubiza uElija. 
Matthew27:48 Njalo omunye wabo wahle wagijima, wathatha uzipho, wa lu gcwalisa ngeviniga." 
Matthew27:49 Kodwa abanye bathi: Yekelani sibone ukuthi uElija uzakuza amsindise. 
Matthew27:50 UJesu wasebuya ememeza ngelizwi elikhulu. 
Matthew27:51 Futhi khangela, iveyili lethempeli ladatshulwa incezuezimbili laqala phezulu lisiya phansi;" 
Matthew27:52 lamangcwaba avuleka; lezidumbu ezinengi zabangcwele abasebelele zavuswa; 
Matthew27:53 sebephumile emangcwabeni emva kokuvuka kwakhe bangena emzini ongcwele, babonakala kwabanengi." 
Matthew27:54 Kwathi induna yekhulu lalabo ababelayo belinde uJesu. 
Matthew27:55 Kwakukhona lapho abesifazana abanengi bebukele; 
Matthew27:56 okwakukhona phakathi kwabo oMariya Magadalena. 
Matthew27:57 Kwathi sekuhlwile; 
Matthew27:58 yena waya kuPilatu, wacela isidumbu sikaJesu. UPilatu waselaya ukuthi isidumbu a sinikwe." 
Matthew27:59 UJosefa wasethatha isidumbu wasigoqela ngelembu elicolekileyo elihlambulukileyo," 
Matthew27:60 wasibeka engcwabeni lakhe elitsha. 
Matthew27:61 Futhi kwakukhona lapho uMariya Magadalena. 
Matthew27:62 Langosuku olulandelayo, olulandela olwamalungiselelo, abapristi abakhulu labaFarisi babuthana kuPilatu," 
Matthew27:63 besithi: Nkosi, siyakhumbula ukuthi lowomkhohlisi esaphila wathi." 
Matthew27:64 Ngakho laya ukuthi ingcwaba liqiniswe kuze kube lusuku lwesithathu; hlezi abafundi bakhe bafike ebusuku bamebe, besebesithi ebantwini: Uvukile kwabafileyo; kuthi inkohliso yokucina ibembi kuleyokuqala." 
Matthew27:65 UPilatu wasesithi kubo: Lilabalindi; hambani, li li qinise njengokubona kwenu." 
Matthew27:66 Bahamba-ke baliqinisa ingcwaba. 
Matthew28:1 Kwathi ekupheleni kwesabatha. 
Matthew28:2 Futhi khangela, kwaba khona ukuzamazama komhlaba okukhulu." 
Matthew28:3 Lokubonakala kwayo kwakunjengombane. 
Matthew28:4 Abalindi basebethuthumela ngokuyesaba, baba njengabafileyo." 
Matthew28:5 Kodwa ingilosi yaphendula yathi kwabesifazana: Lingesabi lina; ngoba ngiyazi ukuthi lidinga uJesu obebethelwe; 
Matthew28:6 kakho lapha; ngoba uvukile, njengokutsho kwakhe; wozani libone indawo lapho iNkosi ebilele khona." 
Matthew28:7 Hambani masinyane litshele abafundi bakhe ukuthi uvukile kwabafileyo; lizambona khona; khangelani, sengilitshelile." 
Matthew28:8 Basebephuma engcwabeni ngokuphangisa belokwesaba lentokozo enkulu. 
Matthew28:9 Kwathi besiyatshela abafundi bakhe, futhi khangela, uJesu wabahlangabeza, wathi: Mpilo enhle." 
Matthew28:10 UJesu wasesithi kubo: Lingesabi. 
Matthew28:11 Kwathi sebehamba, khangela, abanye kubalindi baya emzini babikela abapristi abakhulu konke okwenzakeleyo." 
Matthew28:12 Sebebuthene labadala, benza icebo, banika abebutho imali enengi," 
Matthew28:13 besithi: Kalibokuthi: Abafundi bakhe beze ebusuku bameba silele thina. 
Matthew28:14 Futhi uba lokhu kuzwakala kumbusi. 
Matthew28:15 Basebethatha imali benza njengalokhu ababekufundisiwe. Lalelilizwi landa phakathi kwamaJuda. 
Matthew28:16 Kwathi abafundi abalitshumi lanye baya eGalili, entabeni uJesu;" 
Matthew28:17 sebembonile bamkhonza. 
Matthew28:18 UJesu wasesondela wakhuluma labo, esithi: Wonke amandla aphiwe mina ezulwini lemhlabeni;" 
Matthew28:19 ngakho hambani; 
Matthew28:20 libafundise ukugcina konke engililaye khona; futhi khangelani, mina ngilani." 
Mark1:1 Ukuqala kwevangeli likaJesu Kristu, iNdodana kaNkulunkulu;" 
Mark1:2 njengokulotshiweyo kubaprofethi. 
Mark1:3 Ilizwi lomemezayo enkangala, lithi: Lungisani indlela yeNkosi; qondisani izindledlana zayo." 
Mark1:4 Kweza uJohane ebhabhathiza enkangala, etshumayela ubhabhathizo lokuphenduka kukho ukuthethelelwa kwezono," 
Mark1:5 kwaphumela kuye ilizwe lonke leJudiya, labo abeJerusalema, basebebhabhathizwa bonke nguye emfuleni iJodani, bevuma izono zabo." 
Mark1:6 Futhi uJohane wayembethe uboya bekamela, elozwezwe lwesikhumba ekhalweni lwakhe, wayesidla intethe loluju lweganga." 
Mark1:7 Watshumayela, esithi: Olamandla kulami uyeza emva kwami, engingafanele ukukhothama ngithukulule umchilo wamanyathela akhe." 
Mark1:8 Mina isibili ngilibhabhathize ngamanzi; kodwa yena uzalibhabhathiza ngoMoya oNgcwele. 
Mark1:9 Kwasekusithi ngalezonsuku, wabhabhathizwa nguJohane eJodani." 
Mark1:10 Wenela ukukhuphuka emanzini, wabona amazulu eqhekezeka, loMoya kungathi lijuba esehlela phezu kwakhe;" 
Mark1:11 kwasekusiza ilizwi livela emazulwini, lathi: Wena uyiNdodana yami ethandekayo, engithokoza ngayo." 
Mark1:12 Njalo uMoya. 
Mark1:13 Wayekhona-ke lapho enkangala insuku ezingamatshumi amane elingwa nguSathane, wayelezilo, ingilosi zasezimnceda." 
Mark1:14 Kwathi emva kokunikelwa kukaJohane," 
Mark1:15 wasesithi: Isikhathi sigcwalisekile. 
Mark1:16 Kwathi ehambahamba elwandle lweGalili wabona uSimoni loAndreya umfowabo, bephosela imbule olwandle; ngoba babengabagoli benhlanzi." 
Mark1:17 UJesu wasesithi kubo: Ngilandelani, ngizalenza libe ngabagoli babantu." 
Mark1:18 Njalo bahle batshiya amambule abo, bamlandela." 
Mark1:19 Eseqhubeke ibangana esuka lapho, wabona uJakobe okaZebediya, loJohane umfowabo, labo babesemkhunjini belungisa amambule abo." 
Mark1:20 Njalo wahle wababiza; basebetshiya uyise uZebediya emkhunjini leziqatshwa, basuka bamlandela." 
Mark1:21 Basebengena eKapenawume. 
Mark1:22 Basebebabaza ngemfundiso yakhe. 
Mark1:23 Futhi kwakukhona esinagogeni labo umuntu owayelomoya ongcolileyo, wasememeza," 
Mark1:24 wathi: Yekela, silani lawe, Jesu weNazaretha? Uze ukusibhubhisa yini." 
Mark1:25 UJesu wasemkhuza. 
Mark1:26 Futhi umoya ongcolileyo emhlukuluza ekhala ngelizwi elikhulu, waphuma kuye." 
Mark1:27 Basebemangala bonke, baze babuzana, bathi: Kuyini lokhu? Yimfundiso bani entsha le, ukuthi ngamandla uyalaya labomoya abangcolileyo, futhi bamlalele." 
Mark1:28 Njalo yahle yaphuma indumela yakhe esigabeni sonke seGalili esizingelezeleyo. 
Mark1:29 Njalo bahle baphuma. 
Mark1:30 Futhi uninazala kaSimoni wayelele eloqhuqho, njalo bahle bamtshela ngaye;" 
Mark1:31 wasesondela, wabamba isandla sakhe wamvusa; futhi uqhuqho lwahle lwamyekela, wabasebenzela." 
Mark1:32 Kwathi sekuhlwile, ilanga selitshona, baletha kuye bonke abagulayo lababengenwe ngamadimoni;" 
Mark1:33 njalo umuzi wonke wawubuthene emnyango. 
Mark1:34 Wasesilisa abanengi ababegula izifo ezitshiyeneyo, wakhupha amadimoni amanengi, ngoba ayemazi." 
Mark1:35 Njalo ekuseni kusesemnyama kakhulu wavuka waphuma. 
Mark1:36 USimoni lababelaye basebemdingisisa; 
Mark1:37 sebemtholile bathi kuye: Bonke bayakudinga. 
Mark1:38 Wasesithi kubo: Asiye emizini eseduze, ukuze ngitshumayele lakhona; ngoba ngiphumele lokhu." 
Mark1:39 Wasetshumayela emasinagogeni abo kulo lonke eleGalili, ekhupha amadimoni." 
Mark1:40 Kwasekufika kuye umlephero, emncenga, esithi kuye: Aluba uthanda, ungangihlambulula." 
Mark1:41 UJesu wasesiba lesihelo, welula isandla, wamthinta, wathi kuye: Ngiyathanda, hlambuluka;" 
Mark1:42 esekhulumile bahle basuka ubulephero kuye, wahlanjululwa." 
Mark1:43 Wasemlayisisa, wahle wamyekela wahamba," 
Mark1:44 esithi kuye: Khangela ungatsheli muntu ulutho; kodwa hamba, uziveze kumpristi, unikele ngokuhlanjululwa kwakho lokho uMozisi akulayayo, kube yibufakazi kubo." 
Mark1:45 Kodwa yena esephumile waqala ukutshumayela kakhulu. 
Mark2:1 Njalo wabuya wangena eKapenawume. 
Mark2:2 Njalo kwahle kwabuthana abanengi, akwazabe kusaba lendawo ya bo, ngitsho langasemnyango; wasekhuluma ilizwi kubo." 
Mark2:3 Basebesiza kuye, beletha oyisigoga, ethwelwe ngabane." 
Mark2:4 Babengelakusondela kuye ngenxa yexuku, bavula." 
Mark2:5 Njalo uJesu ebona ukholo lwabo wathi koyisigoga: Mntwana, izono zakho uzithethelelwe." 
Mark2:6 Kodwa abanye bababhali ababehlezi lapho, banakana enhliziyweni zabo, bathi:" 
Mark2:7 Ukhulumelani inhlamba enje lo? Ngubani ongathethelela izono ngaphandle koyedwa, uNkulunkulu?" 
Mark2:8 Njalo khonokho ekwazi uJesu emoyeni wakhe ukuthi babenakana njalo phakathi kwabo, wathi kubo: Linakanelani izinto lezi enhliziyweni zenu?" 
Mark2:9 Yikuphi okulula, ukuthi koyisigoga: Izono zakhouzithethelelwe, kumbe ukuthi: Sukuma, uthathe icansi lakho, uhambe?" 
Mark2:10 Kodwa ukuze lazi ukuthi iNdodana yomuntu ilamandla okuthethelela izono emhlabeni (wathi koyisigoga): 
Mark2:11 Ngithi kuwe: Sukuma uthathe icansi lakho, uye endlini yakho." 
Mark2:12 Njalo wahle wasukuma, wathatha icansi, waphuma phambi kwabo bonke; baze bamangala bonke, bamdumisa uNkulunkulu, besithi: Kasizange sikubone okunje." 
Mark2:13 Wasebuya esiya elwandle, ixuku lonke laselisiza kuye, wasebafundisa." 
Mark2:14 Esedlula wabona uLevi okaAlfewu ehlezi endlini yokuthelisela, wasesithi kuye: Ngilandela. Wasesukuma wamlandela." 
Mark2:15 Kwasekusithi ehlezi endlini yakhe, labathelisi abanengi lezoni bahlala ekudleni loJesu labafundi bakhe; ngoba babebanengi, njalo bemlandela." 
Mark2:16 Kwathi ababhali labaFarisi, bembona esidla labathelisi lezoni, bathi kubafundi bakhe: Kungani esidla enatha labathelisi lezoni?" 
Mark2:17 Kwathi uJesu esezwile wathi kubo: Abaphilileyo kabadingi melaphi, kodwa labo abagulayo. Kangizanga ukubiza abalungileyo, kodwa izoni zize ekuphendukeni." 
Mark2:18 Njalo abafundi bakaJohane lababaFarisi babezila ukudla; basebesiza bathi kuye: Kungani abafundi bakaJohane lababaFarisi bezila ukudla, kodwa abafundi bakho bengazili ukudla?" 
Mark2:19 UJesu wasesithi kubo: Amadodana endlu yomthimba angazila yini ukudla, umyeni eselawo? Angezile, ingqe ngesikhathi umyeni eselawo;" 
Mark2:20 kodwa zizafika insuku lapho umyeni azasuswa kuwo, njalo khona azazila ukudla ngalezonsuku." 
Mark2:21 Futhi kakho othungela isichibi selembu elingakafinyeli esembathweni esidala; uba-ke kungenjalo okubekelweyo kudabuke kiso, okutsha kwesidala, kuqhele ukudabuka." 
Mark2:22 Futhi kakho othela iwayini elitsha emigodleni emidala; uba-ke kungenjalo iwayini elitsha lidabula imigodla, lichitheke iwayini lemigodla yonakale; kodwa iwayini elitsha limele lifakwe emigodleni emitsha." 
Mark2:23 Kwasekusithi edabula emasimini amabele ngesabatha. 
Mark2:24 AbaFarisi basebesithi kuye: Khangela, kungani besenza lokho okungavunyelwayo ngesabatha?" 
Mark2:25 Yena wasesithi kubo: Kalizange libale yini uDavida akwenzayo, mhla eswele, elambile, yena lababelaye?" 
Mark2:26 Ukuthi wayangena njani endlini kaNkulunkulu esikhathini uAbhiyatha engumpristi omkhulu, wadla izinkwa zokubukiswa ezingavunyelwa ukudliwa ngaphandle kwabapristi, wabanika lababelaye?" 
Mark2:27 Wasesithi kubo: Isabatha lenziwa ngenxa yomuntu, njalo umuntu ke nzi wanga ngenxa yesabatha;" 
Mark2:28 ngakho iNdodana yomuntu iyiNkosi leyesabatha. 
Mark3:1 Wasebuya engena. 
Mark3:2 Basebemqaphela ukuthi uzamsilisa ngesabatha. 
Mark3:3 Wasesithi kumuntu olesandla esitshwabheneyo: Sukuma uye phakathi. 
Mark3:4 Wathi kubo: Kuvunyelwe yini ngamasabatha ukwenza okulungileyo, kumbe ukwenza okubi? Ukusindisa impilo, kumbe ukubulala? Kodwa bathula." 
Mark3:5 Wasebathalaza ngokuthukuthela, edabukile ngobulukhuni benhliziyo yabo, wathi kumuntu: Yelula isandla sakho. Waselula, isandla sakhe sasesisiliswa saphila njengesinye." 
Mark3:6 Basebephuma abaFarisi bahle bacebisana labakaHerodi bemelane laye, ukuthi bangambulala njani." 
Mark3:7 Kodwa uJesu wasuka wahamba labafundi bakhe ngaselwandle, leJudiya;" 
Mark3:8 leJerusalema, ixuku elikhulu, selizwile izinto ezinkulu abezenza, leza kuye." 
Mark3:9 Wasetshela abafundi bakhe ukuthi umkolo umlindele ngenxa yexuku, ukuze lingamcindezeli." 
Mark3:10 Ngoba wayesilisa abanengi, baze bawela phezu kwakhe bonke abalezifo." 
Mark3:11 Futhi omoya abangcolileyo, bembona, babesiwa phansi phambi kwakhe." 
Mark3:12 Wasebalayisisa kakhulu ukuthi bangamvezi. 
Mark3:13 Wasesenyukela entabeni, wabizela kuye labo ayebafuna yena; basebesiza kuye." 
Mark3:14 Wasemisa abalitshumi lambili, ukuze babe laye, lokuze abathume ukuyatshumayela," 
Mark3:15 futhi babe lamandla okwelapha imikhuhlane, lawokukhupha amadimoni." 
Mark3:16 LoSimoni wamutha ibizo lokuthinguPetro; 
Mark3:17 loJakobe okaZebediya, loJohane umfowabo kaJakobe; wabatha amabizo wathingoBowanegesi, okuyikuthi, amadodana omdumo;" 
Mark3:18 loAndreya, loFiliphu, loBartolomewu, loMathewu, loTomasi, loJakobe okaAlfewu, loTadewu, loSimoni umKhanani," 
Mark3:19 loJudasi uIskariyothi, laye owamnikelayo." 
Mark3:20 Ixuku laselibuthana futhi, kwaze kwathi bona abasazange benelise lokudla isinkwa." 
Mark3:21 Kwathi abakibo sebezwile lokhubaphuma ukuyambamba; ngoba bathi. 
Mark3:22 Lababhali abavela eJerusalema bathi. 
Mark3:23 Wasebabizela kuye, wathi kubo ngemifanekiso: USathane angakhupha njani uSathane?" 
Mark3:24 Futhi uba umbuso wehlukene umelene lawo ngokwawo, lowombuso ungeme." 
Mark3:25 Lendlu uba yehlukene imelana layo ngokwayo, leyondlu ingeme." 
Mark3:26 LoSathane uba ezivukela yena, ahlukane, angeme, kodwa uyaphela." 
Mark3:27 Kakho ongangena endlini yesiqhwaga, aphange impahla yaso, uba engasibophi isiqhwaga kuqala, abesephanga indlu yaso." 
Mark3:28 Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Zonke izono zizathethelelwa kubantwana babantu, lezinhlamba loba ziphi abahlambaza ngazo;" 
Mark3:29 kodwa loba ngubani ohlambaza emelene loMoya oyiNgcwele, kalakuthethelelwa lanini, kodwa ulecala lokulahlwa okulaphakade;" 
Mark3:30 ngoba bathi: Ulomoya ongcolileyo. 
Mark3:31 Kwasekufika. 
Mark3:32 Njalo ixuku lalihlezi limphahlile; basebesithi kuye: Khangela, unyoko labafowenu baphandle bayakudinga." 
Mark3:33 Wasebaphendula wathi: Ngubani umama kumbe abafowethu? 
Mark3:34 Wasethalaza labo ababehlezi bemphahlile, wathi: Khangelani umama labafowethu." 
Mark3:35 Ngoba loba ngubani owenza intando kaNkulunkulu, nguye ongumfowethu lodadewethu lomama." 
Mark4:1 Wasebuya waqala ukufundisa ngaselwandle; kwasekubuthana kuye ixuku elikhulu. 
Mark4:2 Wasebafundisa izinto ezinengi ngemifanekiso, lekufundiseni kwakhe wathi kubo:" 
Mark4:3 Lalelani; khangelani, kwaphuma umhlanyeli ukuyahlanyela." 
Mark4:4 Kwasekusithi ekuhlanyeleni, enye yawela eceleni kwendlela, kwasekufika inyoni zezulu zayidla zayiqeda." 
Mark4:5 Kodwa enye yawela emhlabathini olamatshe, lapho eyayingelamhlabathi omnengi khona; futhi yahle yamila, ngoba yayingelakutshona komhlabathi;" 
Mark4:6 kwathi ekuphumeni kwelanga yahangulwa yabuna ngoba yayingelampande. 
Mark4:7 Enye yasiwela emeveni, ameva asekhula, ayiminyanisa, futhi ayithelanga isithelo." 
Mark4:8 Njalo enye yawela emhlabathini omuhle; yathela isithelo esakhulayo sanda, yazala enye amatshumi amathathu, lenye amatshumi ayisithupha, lenye ikhulu." 
Mark4:9 Wasesithi kubo: Olendlebe zokuzwa, akezwe." 
Mark4:10 Kwathi eseyedwa, labo ababemphahlile kanye labalitshumi lambili bambuza ngomfanekiso." 
Mark4:11 Wasesithi kubo: Kuphiwe kini ukwazi imfihlo yombuso kaNkulunkulu; kodwa labo abangaphandle benzelwa izinto zonke ngemifanekiso; 
Mark4:12 ukuze bebona babone, bangabonisisi; njalo besizwa bezwe, bangaqedisisi; hlezi loba nini baphenduke, bathethelelwe izono zabo." 
Mark4:13 Wasesithi kubo: Kaliwazi lumfanekiso yini? Pho lizayazi njani imifanekiso yonke? 
Mark4:14 Umhlanyeli uhlanyela ilizwi. 
Mark4:15 Njalo abaseceleni kwendlela, yilabo lapho okuhlanyelwa khona ilizwi, futhi nxa belizwa, uSathane ahle afike alisuse ilizwi elihlanyelwe enhliziyweni zabo." 
Mark4:16 Lalabo ngokunjalo abahlanyelwe emhlabathini olamatshe, abathi, lapho besizwa ilizwi, bahle balemukele ngentokozo," 
Mark4:17 njalo kabalampande phakathi kwabo, kodwa bahlala okwesikhathi; kuthi sekufika inkathazo kumbe ukuzingelwa ngenxa yelizwi, bahle bakhubeke." 
Mark4:18 Lalaba yilabo abahlanyelwe emeveni, abalizwayo ilizwi," 
Mark4:19 kodwa impisekelo yalumhlaba, lenkohliso yenotho, lenkanuko yezinye izinto kungene kuminyanise ilizwi, futhi ibe ingasatheli." 
Mark4:20 Lalaba yilabo abahlanyelwe emhlabathini omuhle, abathi belizwile ilizwi, ba le mukele, bathele, enye amatshumi amathathu, lenye amatshumi ayisithupha, lenye ikhulu." 
Mark4:21 Wasesithi kubo: Kanti isibane silethwa ukuze sibekwe ngaphansi kwesitsha kumbe ngaphansi kombheda? Angithi ukuze sibekwe esiqobaneni sesibane? 
Mark4:22 Ngoba kakukho okufihliweyo okungayikubonakaliswa; akukho okwenzeka kube yimfihlo, kodwa ukuze kube sobala." 
Mark4:23 Nxa umuntu elendlebe zokuzwa akezwe. 
Mark4:24 Wasesithi kubo: Qaphelisani elikuzwayo. 
Mark4:25 Ngoba loba ngubani olakho, uzaphiwa; kodwa loba ngubani ongelakho, uzakwemukwa lalokho alakho." 
Mark4:26 Wasesithi: Unjalo umbuso kaNkulunkulu, njengokuba nxa umuntu ephosa inhlanyelo emhlabathini," 
Mark4:27 njalo alale abesevuka ebusuku lemini, lenhlanyelo imile njalo ikhule, yena kakwazi ukuthi njani." 
Mark4:28 Ngoba umhlabathi uyathela ngokwawo, kuqala usungulo, kulandele isikhwebu, kulandele amabele apheleleyo esikhwetshini." 
Mark4:29 Kodwa nxa sesivuthiwe isithelo, uhle athumeze isikela." 
Mark4:30 Wathi futhi: Sizawufananisa lani umbuso kaNkulunkulu? Kumbe sizawufananisa ngomfanekiso bani? 
Mark4:31 Unjengohlamvu lwemasitedi, oluthi nxa seluhlanyelwe emhlabathini, luncinyane kulazo zonke inhlamvu ezisemhlabeni;" 
Mark4:32 njalo nxa seluhlanyelwe, lukhule, lube lukhulu lwedlule izilimo zonke, lwenze ingatsha ezinkulu, kuze kuthi inyoni zezulu zingakhela ngaphansi komthunzi wazo." 
Mark4:33 Waselikhuluma kubo ilizwi ngemifanekiso eminengi enjalo; 
Mark4:34 kodwa ngaphandle komfanekiso kakhulumanga kubo. 
Mark4:35 Ngalolosuku sekuhlwile, wasesithi kubo: Asichapheleni ngaphetsheya." 
Mark4:36 Sebeyekele ixuku lahamba. Futhi leminye imikolo yayilaye. 
Mark4:37 Kwasekuvuka isiphepho esikhulu somoya; lamagagasi aphoseka emkhunjini, waze wagcwala khathesi." 
Mark4:38 Njalo yena wayengemuva emkhunjini elele emqamelweni; basebemvusa, bathi kuye: Mfundisi, kawukhathali yini ukuthi siyabhubha?" 
Mark4:39 Wasevuka wakhuza umoya, wathi kulo ulwandle: Thula, uthi zwi! Umoya wasuqamuka, kwasekusiba khona ukuthula okukhulu." 
Mark4:40 Wasesithi kubo: Kungani lisesaba kangaka? Kalilakholo ngani? 
Mark4:41 Basebesesaba ngokwesaba okukhulu, bathi omunye komunye: Kanti ungubani lo, ukuthi lomoya lolwandle kumlalele?" 
Mark5:1 Basebefika ngaphetsheya kolwandle, elizweni lamaGadarene." 
Mark5:2 Esephumile emkhunjini, wahle wamhlangabeza umuntu ovela emangcwabeni elomoya ongcolileyo," 
Mark5:3 owayehlala emangcwabeni; njalo kwakungelamuntu owayengambopha ngitsho langamaketane," 
Mark5:4 ngoba wayebotshiwe kanengi ngezibopho langamaketane, kodwa amaketane ayeqanyulwa nguye, lezibopho zaqanyuqanyulwa; njalo kwakungekho owayengamthambisa;" 
Mark5:5 langezikhathi zonke, ebusuku lemini, wayesezintabeni lemangcwabeni eklabalala ezisika ngamatshe." 
Mark5:6 Kwathi ebona uJesu ekhatshana, wagijima wamkhonza," 
Mark5:7 wamemeza ngelizwi elikhulu esithi: Ngilani lawe, Jesu, Ndodana kaNkulunkulu oPhezukonke." 
Mark5:8 Ngoba wathi kuye: Phuma emuntwini, moya ongcolileyo." 
Mark5:9 Wasembuza wathi: Ibizo lakho ungubani? Wasephendula, wathi: Ibizo lami nginguLegiyoni, ngoba sibanengi." 
Mark5:10 Wasemncenga kakhulu, ukuthi angabaxotsheli ngaphandle kwelizwe." 
Mark5:11 Kwakukhona lapho ngasezintabeni umhlambi omkhulu wengulube usidla; 
Mark5:12 lamadimoni wonke amncenga, athi: Sithume engulubeni, singene kuzo." 
Mark5:13 Njalo uJesu wahle wawavumela. Omoya abangcolileyo basebephuma bangena ezingulubeni; umhlambi wasuphaphatheka eliweni usiya olwandle; njalo zazingaba zinkulungwane ezimbili; zaminzwa olwandle. 
Mark5:14 Abazelusayo ingulube basebebaleka, bayabika emzini lemaphandleni. Basebephuma ukubona ukuthi kuyini okwenzakeleyo;" 
Mark5:15 bafika kuJesu, bambona obengenwe ngamadimoni ehlezi egqokile; basebesesaba." 
Mark5:16 Labo ababekubonile babatshela ukuthi kwenzeke njani kowayengenwe ngamadimoni, langengulube." 
Mark5:17 Basebeqala ukumncenga ukuthi asuke elizweni lakibo. 
Mark5:18 Wathi engena emkhunjini, owayengenwe ngamadimoni wamncenga, ukuthi abe laye." 
Mark5:19 Kodwa uJesu kamvumelanga, kodwa wathi kuye: Hamba uye ekhaya kwabakini, ubatshele ukuthi iNkosi ikwenzele okungakanani, ikuhawukele." 
Mark5:20 Wasesuka ehamba waqala ukutshumayela eDikapolisi ukuthi uJesu umenzele okungakanani; basebemangala bonke. 
Mark5:21 UJesu esebuye wachaphela ngaphetsheya ngomkhumbi, kwabuthana kuye ixuku elikhulu, futhi wayengasolwandle." 
Mark5:22 Njalo khangela, kwafika; embona, wawa phansi enyaweni zakhe," 
Mark5:23 wamncenga kakhulu, esithi: Indodakazi yami encane isiphela; ngiyakuncengaukuthi ubuye ubeke izandla phezu kwayo, ukuze isindiswe, njalo izaphila." 
Mark5:24 Wasehamba laye; ixuku elikhulu laselimlandela, lamminyezela." 
Mark5:25 Njalo owesifazana othile owayelomopho wegazi okweminyaka elitshumi lambili," 
Mark5:26 ehluphekile kakhulu kubelaphi abanengi, echithile konke ayelakho, engasizakalanga, kodwa kulokhu kumqinela," 
Mark5:27 esezwile ngoJesu, weza exukwini ngemuva, wathinta isembatho sakhe;" 
Mark5:28 ngoba wathi: Aluba ngithinta izembatho zakhe nje, ngizasindiswa." 
Mark5:29 Futhi wahle woma umthombo wegazi lakhe, wasesizwa emzimbeni ukuthi usilile esifweni." 
Mark5:30 Njalo uJesu wahle wazi phakathi kwakhe ukuthi amandla aphumile kuye, watshibilika esexukwini, wathi: Ngubani othinte izembatho zami?" 
Mark5:31 Abafundi bakhe basebesithi kuye: Uyabona ixuku likuminyezela, kodwa uthi: Ngubani ongithintileyo?" 
Mark5:32 Wasethalaza ukuthi ambone owenze lokhu. 
Mark5:33 Kodwa owesifazana esesaba ethuthumela, ekwazi okwenzekileyo kuye, weza wawa phambi kwakhe, wamtshela iqiniso lonke." 
Mark5:34 Wasesithi kuye: Ndodakazi, ukholo lwakho lukusindisile; hamba ngokuthula, siliswa esifweni sakho." 
Mark5:35 Esakhuluma, kwafika aba nyebomphathi wesinagoge?" 
Mark5:36 Kwahle kwathi uJesu esizwa ilizwi elikhulunywayo wathi kumphathi wesinagoge. 
Mark5:37 Futhi kavumelanga muntu ukuthi amlandele, ngaphandle kukaPetro loJakobe." 
Mark5:38 Bafika-ke endlini yomphathi wesinagoge, wabona isiphithiphithi, labakhalayo labalilayo kakhulu," 
Mark5:39 esengenile wathi kubo: Liphithizelelani, likhala? Umntwana omncane kafanga, kodwa ulele." 
Mark5:40 Basebemhleka usulu. Kodwa yena, esebakhuphile bonke, wathatha uyise womntwana omncane lonina lalabo ababelaye, wangena lapho okwakulele khona umntwana omncane." 
Mark5:41 Wabamba isandla somntwana omncane, wathi kuye: ""Thalitha, kumi""." 
Mark5:42 Njalo yahle yavuka intombazana encane, yahamba, ngoba yayileminyaka elitshumi lambili; basebesanganiseka ngokusanganiseka okukhulu." 
Mark5:43 Wasebalayisisa kakhulu ukuthi lokhu kungaziwa muntu; wathi kayinikwe ukudla. 
Mark6:1 Wasesuka lapho, waya emzini wakibo; abafundi bakhe basebemlandela." 
Mark6:2 Sekufike isabatha, waqala ukufundisa esinagogeni; labanengi aba mu zwayo bamangala, bathi: Zivela ngaphi lezizinto kuye? Njalo yinhlakanipho bani ayinikiweyo, ukuthi lalimisebenzi yamandla enje yenziwe ngezandla zakhe?" 
Mark6:3 Lo kayisuye umbazi yini, indodana kaMariya, lomfowabo kaJakobe loJose loJudasi loSimoni? Labodadewabo kabakho yini lapha kithi? Basebekhubeka ngaye." 
Mark6:4 Kodwa uJesu wathi kubo: Umprofethi kasweli ukudunyiswa, ngaphandle kwelizweni lakibo, lezihlotsheni zakhe lendlini yakwabo." 
Mark6:5 Futhi wayengelakho ukwenza lowodwa umsebenzi wamandla lapho. 
Mark6:6 Wasemangala ngokungakholwa kwabo. 
Mark6:7 Wasebizela kuye abalitshumi lambili. 
Mark6:8 Wabalaya ukuthi bangaphathi lutho lwendlela, ngaphandle kodondolo kuphela; lasikhwama, lasinkwa, lamali ezwezweni;" 
Mark6:9 kodwa bafake amanyathela; futhi bangembathi izembatho ezimbili. 
Mark6:10 Wasesithi kubo: Lapho elingena khona endlini, hlalani kiyo lize liphume khona." 
Mark6:11 Njalo loba ngobani abangayikulemukela, kumbe balizwe, nxa liphuma lapho, thintithani uthuli olungaphansi kwenyawo zenu kube yibufakazi kubo. Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Kuzakuba lula eSodoma kumbe laseGomora ngosuku lwesigwebo, kulakulowomuzi." 
Mark6:12 Sebephumile batshumayela ukuthi baphenduke; 
Mark6:13 bakhupha amadimoni amanengi, bagcoba abanengi abagulayo ngamagcobo." 
Mark6:14 Inkosi uHerodi, ngoba ibizo lakhe laba sobala, wasesithi: UJohane owabhabhathizayo uvukile kwabafileyo, futhi kungakho lamandla esebenza kuye." 
Mark6:15 Abanye bathi: UnguElija; labanye bathi: Ungumprofethi, kumbe u njengomunye wabaprofethi." 
Mark6:16 Kodwa uHerodi esizwa wathi: Lo nguJohane, mina engamquma ikhanda; yena uvukile kwabafileyo." 
Mark6:17 Ngoba yena uHerodi wayethumele wambamba uJohane, wambopha entolongweni, ngenxa kaHerodiyasi umkaFiliphu umfowabo, ngoba wayemthethe." 
Mark6:18 Ngoba uJohane wayethe kuHerodi: Kawuvunyelwa ukuba lomkamfowenu. 
Mark6:19 UHerodiyasi wasembambela inhliziyo, wafuna ukumbulala; kodwa kenelisanga;" 
Mark6:20 ngoba uHerodi wayemesaba uJohane, esazi ukuthi uyindoda elungileyo lengcwele, wamlondoloza; lalapho emuzwa, wenza izinto ezinengi." 
Mark6:21 Kwathi selufikile usuku oluhle, uHerodi ngelanga lakhe lokuzalwa wenzela izikhulu zakhe ukudla kwantambama," 
Mark6:22 kwathi indodakazi kaHerodiyasi lo isingenile yagida, yamkholisa uHerodi lalabo ababehlezi ekudleni laye, inkosi yathi entombini: Cela kimi loba kuyini okuthandayo, njalo ngizakupha;" 
Mark6:23 wafunga kuyo esithi: Loba kuyini ongakucela kimi, ngizakunika." 
Mark6:24 Yasiphuma isithi kunina: Ngizacelani? Yena wasesithi: Ikhanda likaJohane uMbhabhathizi. 
Mark6:25 Njalo yahle yangena enkosini ngokuphangisa, yacela, yathi: Ngifuna ukuthi unginike khathesinje emganwini ikhanda likaJohane uMbhabhathizi." 
Mark6:26 Inkosi yasidabuka kakhulu, kodwangenxa yezifungo langalabo ababehlezi layo ekudleni." 
Mark6:27 Njalo inkosi yahle yathuma ibutho yalaya ukuthi kulethwe ikhanda lakhe. Wasehamba wamquma ikhanda entolongweni," 
Mark6:28 waletha ikhanda lakhe ngomganu, walinika intombi; intombi yasilinika unina." 
Mark6:29 Kwathi abafundi bakhe sebezwile beza, bathatha isidumbu sakhe, basibeka engcwabeni." 
Mark6:30 Abaphostoli basebebuthana kuJesu, bambikela konke, lababekwenzile kanye lababekufundisile." 
Mark6:31 Wasesithi kubo: Wozani lina lodwa endaweni eyinkangala. 
Mark6:32 Bakhuphuka ngomkhumbi. 
Mark6:33 Amaxuku asebabona besuka, labanengi bamazi, bagijimela khona ndawonye ngenyawo bevela emizini yonke, basebebadlula, bahlangana kuye." 
Mark6:34 Kwathi uJesu esephuma wabona ixuku elikhulu, waba lesihelo ngabo." 
Mark6:35 Kwathi isikhathi sesihambile, abafundi bakhe beza kuye bathi: Lindawo iyinkangala, lesikhathi sesihambile;" 
Mark6:36 bayekele, ukuze baye ezigabeni ezizingelezeleyo lemizaneni bazithengele izinkwa. Ngoba bengelalutho abangaludla." 
Mark6:37 Wasephendula wathi kubo: Banikeni lina ukuthi badle. Basebesithi kuye? 
Mark6:38 Wasesithi kubo: Lilezinkwa ezingaki? Hambani liyebona. Sebesazi bathi: Zinhlanu, lenhlanzi ezimbili." 
Mark6:39 Wasebalaya ukuthi babahlalise bonke phansi ngezigaba ngezigaba etshanini obuluhlaza. 
Mark6:40 Basebehlala phansi ngamaviyo ngamaviyo, ngamakhulu langamatshumi amahlanu." 
Mark6:41 Wasethatha izinkwa ezinhlanu lenhlanzi ezimbili, ekhangela phezulu ezulwini, wabonga, wazihlephula izinkwa, wa zi nika abafundi bakhe ukuthi ba zi beke phambi kwabo; lenhlanzi ezimbili wazabela bonke." 
Mark6:42 Basebesidla bonke, basutha." 
Mark6:43 Basebedobha izitsha ezilitshumi lambili ezagcwala imvuthu ezazisele, l okuseleyokwenhlanzi." 
Mark6:44 Lalabo abadlayo izinkwa, babengaba ngamadoda azinkulungwane ezinhlanu." 
Mark6:45 Njalo wahle wacindezela abafundi bakhe, yena esayekela ixuku lihamba." 
Mark6:46 Esebavalelisile, wasuka waya entabeni." 
Mark6:47 Sekuhlwile, umkhumbi wawuphakathi kolwandle, futhi yena wayeyedwa emhlabathini." 
Mark6:48 Wababona behlupheka kakhulu ekugwedleni, ngoba umoya wawuphambene labo, wasesiza kubo sokungaba yisikhathi somlindo wesine wobusuku, ehamba phezu kolwandle; wasefuna ukubadlula." 
Mark6:49 Sebembonile ehamba phezu kolwandle, basebecabanga ukuthi lithonga, bakhala kakhulu;" 
Mark6:50 ngoba bambona bonke, bethuka. Kodwa wahle wakhuluma labo, wathi kubo: Manini isibindi; yimi, lingesabi." 
Mark6:51 Wasesenyukela kubo emkhunjini, umoya wasuthula; basebesanganiseka kakhulu okwedlula amalawulo ngaphakathi, bamangala." 
Mark6:52 Ngoba babengaqedisisanga ngezinkwa. 
Mark6:53 Kwathi sebechaphile bafika elizweni leGenesaretha, babophela umkhumbi ekhunjini." 
Mark6:54 Bathi sebephumile emkhunjini, bahle bamazi," 
Mark6:55 bagijimela kuso sonke lesosigaba esizingelezeleyo, baqala ukubhoda bethwala abagulayo ngamathala bebasa lapho abebesizwa ukuthi ukhona." 
Mark6:56 Njalo loba ngaphi angena khona emizaneni loba emizini, loba emaphandleni, babeka abagulayo emidangeni, bamncenga ukuthi bathinte umphetho wesembatho sakhe nje; njalo bonke abamthintayo basindiswa." 
Mark7:1 Kwasekubuthana kuye abaFarisi, labanye bababhali, ababevela eJerusalema;" 
Mark7:2 sebebonile ukuthi abanye babafundi bakhe badla izinkwa ngezandla ezingcolileyo, okuyikuthi ezingagezwanga, basola." 
Mark7:3 Ngoba abaFarisi lamaJuda bonke kabadli, ngaphandle kokuthi bagezisise izandla zabo, belondoloza isiko labadala." 
Mark7:4 Nxa be vela emdangeni, kabadli, ngaphandle kokuthi bageze." 
Mark7:5 Emva kwalokhu abaFarisi lababhali bambuza bathi: Kungani abafundi bakho bengahambi ngesiko labadala, kodwa badla isinkwa ngezandla ezingahlanjwanga?" 
Mark7:6 Kodwa waphendula wathi kubo: UIsaya waprofetha kuhle ngani lina bazenzisi, njengokulotshiweyo ukuthi: Lesisizwe singidumisa ngezindebe, kodwa inhliziyo yabo ikhatshana lami." 
Mark7:7 Kodwa zingikhonza ngeze, zifundisa izimfundiso eziy imilayo yabantu." 
Mark7:8 Ngoba liyekela umlayo kaNkulunkulu, ligcine isiko labantu, ukugezisa imbiza lenkezo." 
Mark7:9 Wasesithi kubo: Liyachitha kuhle umlayo kaNkulunkulu, ukuze lilondoloze isiko lenu." 
Mark7:10 Ngoba uMozisi wathi: Hlonipha uyihlo lonyoko; 
Mark7:11 kodwa lina lithi: Aluba umuntu esithi kuyise kumbe kunina: Lokho obungasizwa yimi ngakho, ""liKhobane"", okuyikuthi umnikelo kuNkulunkulu;" 
Mark7:12 kalisamvumeli ukwenzela uyise kumbe unina ulutho," 
Mark7:13 lilenza ize ilizwi likaNkulunkulu ngesiko lenu eliliqhubayo; lezinto ezinengi ezinjalo liyazenza. 
Mark7:14 Esebizile kuye ixuku lonke, wathi kilo: Ngilalelani lonke, liqedisise." 
Mark7:15 Kalukho ulutho olungaphandle komuntu olungamngcolisa lungena kuye; kodwa izinto eziphuma kuye, yizo lezo ezingcolisa umuntu." 
Mark7:16 Uba ekhona olendlebe zokuzwa akezwe. 
Mark7:17 Esengenile endlini evela exukwini. 
Mark7:18 Wasesithi kubo: Ngokunjalo lani lingabangelakuqedisisa yini? Kaliqedisisi yini ukuthi konke okungaphandle okungena emuntwini kungemngcolise? 
Mark7:19 Ngoba kakungeni enhliziyweni yakhe, kodwa esiswini; kuphumela ngaphandle, kuhlambulula ukudla konke." 
Mark7:20 Wasesithi: Okuphumayo emuntwini, yikho okungcolisa umuntu." 
Mark7:21 Ngoba kuphuma ngaphakathi enhliziyweni yabantu imicabango emibi, ukuphinga, ukufeba, ukubulala," 
Mark7:22 ukweba, ubuhwaba;" 
Mark7:23 zonke lezizinto ezimbi zivela ngaphakathi, zimngcolise umuntu." 
Mark7:24 Wasesukuma lapho waya emikhawulweni yeTire leSidoni. Wangena endlini, engathandi ukuthi umuntu akwazi, kodwa wayengelakufihlakala." 
Mark7:25 Ngoba owesifazana, olentombazana yakhe elomoya ongcolileyo, esezwile ngaye, weza wawa phansi enyaweni zakhe;" 
Mark7:26 njalo owesifazana wayengumGriki, engumSirofenike ngokuzalwa; wasemncenga ukuthi akhuphe idimoni endodakazini yakhe." 
Mark7:27 Kodwa uJesu wathi kuye: Ake kusuthe abantwana kuqala; ngoba kakukuhle ukuthatha isinkwa sabantwana sisiphosele izinjana. 
Mark7:28 Kodwa waphendula wathi kuye: Yebo, Nkosi; kodwa lezinjana ezingaphansi kwetafula ziyadla imvuthuluka yabantwana." 
Mark7:29 Wasesithi kuye: Ngenxa yalokhukutsho hamba-ke; idimoni liphumile endodakazini yakho. 
Mark7:30 Wasesuka waya endlini yakhe, wafica idimoni seliphumile, lendodakazi ilele embhedeni." 
Mark7:31 Wasebuya wasuka. 
Mark7:32 Basebeletha kuye isacuthe esigagasayo. 
Mark7:33 Wasesikhupha exukwini saba sodwa, wafaka iminwe yakhe endlebeni zaso," 
Mark7:34 ekhangela phezulu ezulwini! 
Mark7:35 Njalo zahle zavulwa indlebe zaso; yasithukululwa intambo yolimi lwaso, sasesikhuluma saqonda." 
Mark7:36 Wasebalaya ukuthi bangatsheli muntu. 
Mark7:37 Basebemangala kakhulukazi sibili, bathi: Uzenzile kuhle izinto zonke; wenza kokubili izacuthe ukuthi zizwe, lezimungulu ukuthi zikhulume." 
Mark8:1 Ngalezonsuku kwakukhona ixuku elikhulu kakhulu, njalo lalingelakho okokudla, uJesu wabizela kuye abafundi bakhe wathi kubo:" 
Mark8:2 Ngilesihelo ngexuku; ngoba sebehlezi lami insuku ezintathu, bengelalutho lokudla;" 
Mark8:3 njalo uba ngibayekela baye emakhaya abo bengadlanga, bazayatha endleleni; ngoba abanye babo bavela khatshana." 
Mark8:4 Abafundi bakhe basebemphendula bathi: Zingavela ngaphi izinkwa umuntu angasuthisa ngazo laba lapha enkangala? 
Mark8:5 Wasebabuza wathi: Lilezinkwa ezingaki? Basebesithi: Eziyisikhombisa. 
Mark8:6 Waselaya ixuku ukuthi lihlale phansi emhlabathini; wasethatha izinkwa eziyisikhombisa, esebongile wa zi hlephula wa zi nika abafundi bakhe, ukuthi babeke phambi kwabo; basebebeka phambi kwexuku." 
Mark8:7 Njalo babelenhlanzana ezinlutshwana; esebusisile wathi bazibeke lazo phambi kwabo. 
Mark8:8 Basebesidla, basutha; basebedobha imvuthu ezazisele, izitsha eziyisikhombisa." 
Mark8:9 Lababedlile babengaba zinkulungwane ezine; wasebayekela bahamba. 
Mark8:10 Njalo wahle wangena. 
Mark8:11 AbaFarisi basebephuma, baqala ukuphikisana laye, befunisisa kuye isibonakaliso esivela ezulwini, bemlinga." 
Mark8:12 Wasebubula kakhulu emoyeni wakhe wathi: Lesisizukulwana sidingelani isibonakaliso? Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Qiniso akulasibonakaliso esizanikwa kulesisizukulwana. 
Mark8:13 Wasebatshiya, wangena emkhunjini futhi, wasuka waya ngaphetsheya." 
Mark8:14 Njalo abafundi babekhohliwe ukuthatha izinkwa, bengela luthoemkhunjini ngaphandle kwesinkwa esisodwa." 
Mark8:15 Wasebalaya, wathi: Nanzelelani, liqaphele imvubelo yabaFarisi." 
Mark8:16 Basebezindlisana, besithi: Ngoba kasilazinkwa." 
Mark8:17 UJesu esekwazi wathi kubo: Kungani likhulumisana ngokuthi kalilazinkwa? Lokhe lilenhliziyo ezilukhuni yini? 
Mark8:18 Lilamehlo kaliboni yini? Futhi lilendlebe kalizwa yini? Njalo kalikhumbuli yini? 
Mark8:19 Mhla ngahlephulela abazinkulungwane ezinhlanu izinkwa ezinhlanu, ladobha izitsha ezingaki ezigcwele imvuthu? Bathi kuye: Ezilitshumi lambili." 
Mark8:20 Njalo mhla ziyisikhombisa kwabazinkulungwane ezine, ladobha izitsha ezingaki ezigcwele imvuthu? Basebesithi: Eziyisikhombisa." 
Mark8:21 Wasesithi kubo: Yinindaba lingaqedisisi? 
Mark8:22 Wasefika eBhethisayida. 
Mark8:23 Wasesibamba isiphofu ngesandla, wasikhuphela ngaphandle komzana, wasibuza ukuthi ngabe sibona ulutho." 
Mark8:24 Sasesikhangela phezulu sathi: Ngibona abantu behambahamba kungathi yizihlahla. 
Mark8:25 Emva kwalokhu wabuya wabeka izandla zakhephezu kwamehlo aso, wasenza sakhangela phezulu; sasesisiliswa, sabona bonke ngokucacileyo." 
Mark8:26 Wasesithuma endlini yaso, wathi: Ungangeni emzaneni." 
Mark8:27 UJesu wasephuma labafundi bakhe baya emizaneni yeKesariya yeFiliphu; besendleleni wababuza abafundi bakhe, wathi kubo: Abantu bathi ngingubani?" 
Mark8:28 Basebephendula bathi: UJohane uMbhabhathizi; labanye: UElija; labanye: Omunye wabaprofethi. 
Mark8:29 Yena wasesithi kubo: Lina-ke lithi ngingubani? UPetro wasephendula wathi kuye: Wena unguKristu. 
Mark8:30 Wasebalayisisa. 
Mark8:31 Waseqala ukubafundisa. 
Mark8:32 Waselikhuluma lelilizwi obala. UPetro wasemthatha waqala ukumkhuza. 
Mark8:33 Kodwa etshibilika, wabona abafundi bakhe, wamkhuza uPetro, wathi: Suka ngemva kwami, Sathane; ngoba kawucabangi ngezinto zikaNkulunkulu, kodwa ngezabantu." 
Mark8:34 Kwathi esebizele kuye ixuku kanye labafundi bakhe, wathi kubo: Uba umuntu ethanda ukuza ngemva kwami, kazidele, athathe isiphambano sakhe, angilandele." 
Mark8:35 Ngoba loba ngubani othanda ukusindisa impilo yakhe, izamlahlekela; kodwa loba ngubani olahlekelwa yimpilo yakhe ngenxa yami levangeli, yena uzayisindisa." 
Mark8:36 Ngoba kuzamsizani umuntu, nxa ezuza umhlaba wonke, kodwa alahlekelwe ngumphefumulo wakhe?" 
Mark8:37 Kumbe umuntu uzanikani kube lihlawulo lomphefumulo wakhe? 
Mark8:38 Ngoba loba ngubani olenhloni ngami langamazwi ami. 
Mark9:1 Wasesithi kubo: Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Bakhona abanye kwabemiyo lapha, abangasoze bezwe ukufa, baze babone umbuso kaNkulunkulu usufikile ngamandla." 
Mark9:2 Emva kwensuku eziyisithupha uJesu wasethatha uPetro loJakobe loJohane, wasebakhuphulela entabeni ende ebehlukanisa bodwa; waseguqulwa isimo phambi kwabo;" 
Mark9:3 lezembatho zakhe zacwazimula, zaba mhlophe nke njengeliqhwa elikhithikileyo, kakulamcoli welembu emhlabeni ongazenza zibe mhlophe kangako." 
Mark9:4 Kwasekubonakala kubo uElija eloMozisi, njalo bekhuluma loJesu." 
Mark9:5 UPetro wasephendula wathi kuJesu: Rabi, kuhle ukuthi sibe lapha; futhi asakhe amadumba amathathu, elinye ngelakho, lelinye ngelikaMozisi, lelinye ngelikaElija." 
Mark9:6 Ngoba wayengakwazi angakutsho; ngoba babesesaba kakhulu. 
Mark9:7 Kwasekufika iyezi labasibekela; kwaba lelizwi elivela eyezini, lisithi: Lo uyiNdodana yami ethandekayo; zwanini yona." 
Mark9:8 Njalo bahle bathalaza, kababe besabona muntu, kodwa uJesu yedwa elabo." 
Mark9:9 Kwathi besehla entabeni. 
Mark9:10 Njalo bazigcinela lelilizwi, bebuzana ukuthi kutshoni ukuvuka okwabafileyo." 
Mark9:11 Basebembuza, besithi: Batsholoni ababhali ukuthi uElija ufanele ukufika kuqala?" 
Mark9:12 Wasephendula, wathi kubo: UElija ufika kuqala isibili, abuyisele zonke izinto; njalo kubhalwe njani ngeNdodana yomuntu." 
Mark9:13 Kodwa ngitsho kini ukuthi uElija laye sewafika, basebesenza kuye konke abakuthandayo, njengokulotshiweyo ngaye." 
Mark9:14 Kwathi efika kubafundi, wabona ixuku elikhulu libahanqile." 
Mark9:15 Lahle lathi ukumbona ixuku lonke laselimangala, lagijimela ku yelambingelela." 
Mark9:16 Wasebabuza ababhali wathi: Liphikisana ngani labo? 
Mark9:17 Omunye wexuku wasephendula wathi: Mfundisi, ngilethe kuwe indodana yami, elomoya oyisimungulu;" 
Mark9:18 kuthi loba ngaphi oyibamba khona, uyidabule; ikhihlize amagwebu, igedle amazinyo ayo, yome qha; njalo ngikhulume labafundi bakho ukuthi bawukhuphe, kodwa behluleka." 
Mark9:19 Wasemphendula wathi: O sizukulwana esingelakholo, koze kube nini ngilani? Koze kube nini ngilibekezelela? Iletheni kimi." 
Mark9:20 Basebeyiletha kuye; kwathi umbona, umoya wahle wayihlukuza; yawela emhlabathini." 
Mark9:21 Wasebuza uyise wathi: Kulesikhathi esingakanani, lokhu kwenzeka kiyo? Wasesithi: Kusukela ebuntwaneni." 
Mark9:22 Futhi uyiphosele kanengi emlilweni lemanzini, ukuze uyibhubhise; kodwa nxa kukhona ongakwenza, sihawukele, usisize." 
Mark9:23 UJesu wasesithi kuye: Nxa usenelisa ukukholwa, zonke izinto ziyenzeka kokholwayo." 
Mark9:24 Njalo uyise womntwana wahle wamemeza ngezinyembezi wathi: Ngiyakholwa, Nkosi, siza ukungakholwa kwami." 
Mark9:25 Kwathi uJesu esebona ukuthi ixuku ligijima kanyekanye ndawonye, wakhuza umoya ongcolileyo, esithi kuwo: Wena moya oyisimungulu loyisacuthe, mina ngiyakulaya: Phuma kuye, ungabe usangena kuye." 
Mark9:26 Usumemezile, wayihlukuza kakhulu, waphuma; yasisiba njengofileyo, kwaze kwathi abanengi bathi isifile." 
Mark9:27 Kodwa uJesu wayibamba ngesandla, wayiphakamisa; yasisukuma." 
Mark9:28 Wathi esengenile endlini, abafundi bakhe bambuza bebodwa bathi: Kungani thina sehlulekile ukuwukhupha?" 
Mark9:29 Wasesithi kubo: Loluhlobo lungeke luphume ngalutho, ngaphandle komkhuleko lokuzila ukudla." 
Mark9:30 Basebesuka lapho badabula eGalili; wayengathandi ukuthi loba ngubani akwazi," 
Mark9:31 ngoba wayefundisa abafundi bakhe, esithi kubo: INdodana yomuntu izanikelwa ezandleni zabantu, njalo bazayibulala; isibulewe izavuka ngosuku lwesithathu." 
Mark9:32 Kodwa kabaqedisisanga lumutsho, besaba ukumbuza." 
Mark9:33 Wasefika eKapenawume? 
Mark9:34 Kodwa bathula; ngoba endleleni babephikisene ngokuthi ngubani omkhulu. 
Mark9:35 Wasehlala phansi wabiza abalitshumi lambili, wathi kubo: Uba umuntu ethanda ukuba ngowokuqala, uzakuba ngowokucina kubo bonke." 
Mark9:36 Wasethatha umntwana omncane, wammisa phakathi kwabo:" 
Mark9:37 Loba ngubani owemukela omunye wabantwana abancane abanje ebizweni lami, wemukela mina; njalo loba ngubani owemukela mina, kemukeli mina, kodwa yena ongithumileyo." 
Mark9:38 UJohane wasemphendula, wathi: Mfundisi, sabona omunye ongasilandeliyo." 
Mark9:39 Kodwa uJesu wathi: Lingamenqabeli; ngoba kakho owenza umsebenzi wamandla ebizweni lami, njalo olamandla okukhuluma kubi ngami masinyane;" 
Mark9:40 ngoba ongamelani lathi, ungowethu." 
Mark9:41 Ngoba loba ngubani ozalinathisa inkezo yamanzi ngebizo lami, ngoba lingabakaKristu, ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Kasoze alahlekelwa ngumvuzo wakhe." 
Mark9:42 Futhi loba ngubani okhubekisa omunye walaba abancinyane abakholwa kimi, kungcono kuye ukuthi ilitshe lokuchola ligaxwe entanyeni yakhe, abesephoselwa olwandle." 
Mark9:43 Njalo uba isandla sakho sikukhubekisa, siqume; kungcono kuwe ukungena ekuphileni uyingini," 
Mark9:44 lapho impethu yabo engafi khona, lomlilo ongacitshi khona." 
Mark9:45 Njalo uba unyawo lwakho lukukhubekisa, luqume," 
Mark9:46 lapho impethu yabo engafi khona, lomlilo ongacitshi khona." 
Mark9:47 Njalo uba ilihlo lakho likukhubekisa, likhuphe; kungcono kuwe ukungena embusweni kaNkulunkulu ulelihlo elilodwa," 
Mark9:48 lapho impethu yabo engafi khona, lomlilo ongacitshi khona." 
Mark9:49 Ngoba wonke uzatshwaywa ngomlilo. 
Mark9:50 Itshwayi lihle. 
Mark10:1 Wasesukuma lapho weza emingceleni yeJudiya edabula ngaphetsheya kweJodani; amaxuku asebuya abuthana kuye. 
Mark10:2 Kwasekusiza kuye abaFarisi bambuza ukuthi: Kuvunyelwe yini ukuthi indoda yale umka yo? bemlinga. 
Mark10:3 Wasephendula wathi kubo: UMozisi walilayani? 
Mark10:4 Basebesithi: UMozisi wavuma ukubhala incwadi yesehlukaniso, loku m ala." 
Mark10:5 UJesu wasephendula wathi kubo: Ngenxa yobulukhuni benhliziyo yenu walibhalela lumlayo; 
Mark10:6 kodwa kusukela ekuqaleni kokudaliweyo, uNkulunkulu wabenza owesilisa lowesifazana." 
Mark10:7 Ngenxa yalokhu indoda izatshiya uyise lonina, inamathele kumkayo," 
Mark10:8 njalo labo ababili bazakuba nyamanye. Ngakho kabasebabili, kodwa ba nyamanye." 
Mark10:9 Ngakho lokho uNkulunkulu akuhlanganisileyo, kakungabi lamuntu okwehlukanisayo." 
Mark10:10 Endlini abafundi bakhe basebebuya bembuza ngalokhu. 
Mark10:11 Wasesithi kubo: Loba ngubani owala umkakhe athathe omunye, uyafeba kuye;" 
Mark10:12 lomfazi uba esala indoda yakhe endele kwenye, uyafeba." 
Mark10:13 Basebeletha abantwana abancane kuye ukuze ababambe; kodwa abafundi bakhe babakhuza aba ba lethayo. 
Mark10:14 Kodwa uJesu e ku bona wathukuthela, wathi kubo: Vumelani abantwana abancane beze kimi." 
Mark10:15 Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Loba ngubani ongemukeli umbuso kaNkulunkulu njengomntwana omncane, kasoze angene kuwo." 
Mark10:16 Njalo ebagona, ebeka izandla zakhephezu kwabo, wababusisa." 
Mark10:17 Esephumele endleleni, omunye wa m gijimela?" 
Mark10:18 UJesu wasesithi kuye: Ungibizelani ngokuthi olungileyo? Kakho olungileyo, ngaphandle koyedwa, uNkulunkulu." 
Mark10:19 Uyayazi imilayo ethi: Ungafebi, ungabulali, ungebi, ungafakazi amanga." 
Mark10:20 Wasephendula wathi kuye: Mfundisi, lezizinto zonke ngizigcinile kusukela ebutsheni bami." 
Mark10:21 Njalo uJesu emkhangela wamthanda. 
Mark10:22 Kodwa edanile ngalelilizwi wasuka wahamba edabukile; ngoba wayelempahla ezinengi. 
Mark10:23 UJesu wasethalaza wathi kubafundi bakhe: Kuzakuba lukhuni kangakanani kwabalenotho ukungena embusweni kaNkulunkulu. 
Mark10:24 Abafundi basebemangala ngamazwi akhe. Kodwa uJesu ephendula futhi wathi kubo: Bantwana, kulukhuni kangakanani kwabathembela enothweni ukungena embusweni kaNkulunkulu;" 
Mark10:25 kulula ukuthi ikamela lithutshe entunjeni yenalithi, kulokuthi umuntu onothileyo angene embusweni kaNkulunkulu." 
Mark10:26 Basebemangala kakhulukazi, bekhulumisana bathi: Pho kungasindiswa bani?" 
Mark10:27 UJesu wasebakhangela wathi: Kubantu kakulakwenzeka, kodwa kaku njalokuNkulunkulu; ngoba zonke izinto ziyenzeka kuNkulunkulu." 
Mark10:28 UPetro waseqala ukuthi kuye: Khangela, thina sitshiye konke, sakulandela." 
Mark10:29 UJesu wasephendula wathi: Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Kakukho muntu otshiye indlu, kumbe abafowabo, kumbe odadewabo, kumbe uyise, kumbe unina, kumbe umka khe, kumbe abantwana, kumbe amasimu, ngenxa yami levangeli," 
Mark10:30 ongayikwemukela ngokwekhulu khathesi ngalesisikhathi, izindlu labafowabo labodadewabo labonina labantwana lamasimu." 
Mark10:31 Kodwa abanengi abokuqala bazakuba ngabokucina, labokucina ngabokuqala." 
Mark10:32 Njalo besendleleni benyukela eJerusalema. Wasethatha futhi abalitshumi lambili, waqala ukubatshela izinto ezazizakwenzakala kuye" 
Mark10:33 ukuthi: Khangelani, senyukela eJerusalema, futhi iNdodana yomuntu izanikelwa kubapristi abakhulu lakubabhali, njalo bazayigwebela ukufa, bayinikele kwabezizwe," 
Mark10:34 bazayiyangisa, bayitshaye ngesiswepu, bayikhafulele amathe, bayibulale; njalo ngosuku lwesithathu izabuya ivuke ekufeni." 
Mark10:35 Kwasekusiza kuye uJakobe loJohane, besithi: Mfundisi, sithanda ukuthi usenzele loba yini esizayicela." 
Mark10:36 Wasesithi kubo: Lithanda ukuthi ngilenzeleni? 
Mark10:37 Basebesithi kuye: Siphe ukuthi sihlale omunye ngakwesokunene sakho lomunye ngakwesokhohlo sakho ebukhosini bakho. 
Mark10:38 Kodwa uJesu wathi kubo: Kalikwazi elikucelayo. Linganatha yini inkezo engiyinathayo mina, njalo libhabhathizwe ngobhabhathizo engibhabhathizwa ngalo mina?" 
Mark10:39 Basebesithi kuye: Singa kwenza. Kodwa uJesu wathi kubo: Isibili inkezo engiyinathayo mina lizayinatha; lizabhabhathizwa ngobhabhathizo engibhabhathizwa ngalo mina; 
Mark10:40 kodwa ukuhlala ngakwesokunene sami langakwesokhohlo sami kayisikho okwami uku ku pha, kodwa kungo kwalabo abakulungiselweyo." 
Mark10:41 Kwathi sebezwile abalitshumi baqala ukuthukuthela ngoJakobe loJohane. 
Mark10:42 Kodwa uJesu wababizela kuye wathi kubo: Liyazi ukuthi labo okuthiwa babusa izizwe bazibusa ngobulukhuni; lezikhulu zazo zisebenzisa amandla phezu kwazo. 
Mark10:43 Kodwa akuyikuba njalo phakathi kwenu; kodwa loba ngubani othanda ukuba ngomkhulu phakathi kwenu, kabe yisisebenzi senu;" 
Mark10:44 njalo loba ngubani othanda ukuba ngowokuqala phakathi kwenu, kabe yisisebenzi sabo bonke." 
Mark10:45 Ngoba leNdodana yomuntu kayizanga ukukhonzwa, kodwa ukukhonza, lokunika impilo yayo ibe lihlawulo labanengi." 
Mark10:46 Basebefika eJeriko wayehlezi endleleni ephanza. 
Mark10:47 Kwathi esezwile ukuthi nguJesu weNazaretha, waqala ukumemeza lokuthi: Jesu Ndodana kaDavida, akungihawukele!" 
Mark10:48 Abanengi basebemkhuza ukuthi athule; kodwa wamemeza kakhulukazi, esithi: Ndodana kaDavida, akungihawukele!" 
Mark10:49 UJesu esima wasesithi kabizwe; basebesibiza isiphofu, besithi kuso: Mana isibindi; sukuma, uyakubiza." 
Mark10:50 Sasesilahla isembatho saso sasukuma seza kuJesu. 
Mark10:51 UJesu wasephendula wathi kuso: Ufuna ukuthi ngikwenzeleni? Isiphofu sasesisithi kuye: Raboni, ukuthi ngibuye ngibone." 
Mark10:52 UJesu wasesithi kuso: Hamba; ukholo lwakho. 
Mark11:1 Kwathi besondela eJerusalema, entabeni yeMihlwathi, wathuma ababili kubafundi bakhe," 
Mark11:2 wathi kubo: Hambani liye emzaneni okhangelene lani; lizahle lithi lingena kuwo lifice ithole likababhemi likhulekiwe. 
Mark11:3 Njalo uba umuntu esithi kini: Likwenzelani lokhu? Lithi: INkosi iyaliswela; njalo uzahle alithumele lapha. 
Mark11:4 Bahamba-ke bafica ithole likhulekiwe lisesangweni ngaphandle, endleleni; basebelikhulula." 
Mark11:5 Labanye kwababemi khona bathi kubo: Lenzani likhulula ithole? 
Mark11:6 Basebesitsho kubo njengoba uJesu elayile; basebebayekela bahamba. 
Mark11:7 Basebeliletha ithole kuJesu, baphosela izembatho zabo phezu kwalo, wasehlala phezu kwalo." 
Mark11:8 Labanengi bendlala izembatho zabo endleleni; labanye bagamula izingatsha lamahlamvu ezihlahleni, bakwendlala endleleni." 
Mark11:9 Lalabo ababehamba phambili lababelandela bamemeza, besithi: Hosana! Ubusisiwe ozayo ebizweni leNkosi;" 
Mark11:10 ubusisiwe umbuso kababa wethu uDavida, ozayo ebizweni leNkosi. Hosana kweliphezulu!" 
Mark11:11 UJesu wasengena eJerusalema, lethempelini." 
Mark11:12 Lakusisa. 
Mark11:13 Ebona umkhiwa ukhatshana, ulamahlamvu, wasondela ukuthi mhlawumbe angathola ulutho kuwo; njalo efika kuwo, katholanga lutho ngaphandle kwamahlamvu; ngoba kwakungesiso isikhathi somkhiwa." 
Mark11:14 UJesu ekhuluma wathi kuwo: Kakungabi kusadla muntu isithelo kuwe kuze kube nininini. Labafundi bakhe ba ku zwa. 
Mark11:15 Basebefika eJerusalema; uJesu wasengena ethempelini waqala ukuxotsha labo ababethengisa lababethenga ethempelini; wasegenqula amatafula ababentshintshelana imali, lezihlalo zalabo ababethengisa amajuba;" 
Mark11:16 wayengavumeli ukuthi umuntu athwale impahla adabule ethempelini. 
Mark11:17 Wasefundisa, wathi kubo: Kakulotshiwe yini ukuthi: Indlu yami izabizwa ngokuthi yindlu yomkhuleko yezizwe zonke." 
Mark11:18 Ababhali labapristi abakhulu basebe ku zwa, badinga ukuthi bangambulala njani." 
Mark11:19 Sekusihlwa, waphuma phandle komuzi." 
Mark11:20 Ekuseni kakhulu besedlula, babona umkhiwa womile kusukela empandeni." 
Mark11:21 UPetro wasekhumbula wathi kuye: Rabi, khangela, umkhiwa owuqalekisileyo womile." 
Mark11:22 UJesu wasephendula wathi kubo: Banini lokholo kuNkulunkulu. 
Mark11:23 Ngoba ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Loba ngubani ozakuthi kulintaba: Phakanyiswa, uphoselwe olwandle; njalo engathandabuzi enhliziyweni yakhe, kodwa ekholwa ukuthi akutshoyo kuyenzeka, kuzakwenzeka kuye loba yini akutshoyo." 
Mark11:24 Ngakho ngithi kini: Konke loba yini elikucelayo likhuleka, kholwani ukuthi liyakwemukela, njalo lizakuba layo." 
Mark11:25 Njalo nxa limi likhuleka. 
Mark11:26 Kodwa uba lina lingathetheleli, loYihlo osemazulwini kayikulithethelela iziphambeko zenu." 
Mark11:27 Basebebuya bafika eJerusalema; kwathi ehambahamba ethempelini, abapristi abakhulu lababhali labadala beza kuye," 
Mark11:28 bathi kuye: Izinto lezi uzenza ngaliphi igunya; njalo ngubani okunike leligunya lokuthi wenze lezizinto? 
Mark11:29 UJesu wasephendula wathi kubo: Lami ngizalibuza umbuzo ube munye, njalo lingiphendule, khona ngizalitshela ukuthi ngenza lezizinto ngaliphi igunya." 
Mark11:30 Ubhabhathizo lukaJohane lwavela ezulwini, kumbe ebantwini? Ngiphendulani." 
Mark11:31 Basebezindlisana, besithi: Uba sisithi: Ezulwini, uzakuthi: Pho kalikholwanga kuye ngani?" 
Mark11:32 Kodwa uba sisithi: Ebantwini; besaba abantu; ngoba bonke babemphatha uJohane, ngokuthi ungumprofethi ngeqiniso." 
Mark11:33 Basebephendula bathi kuJesu: Kasazi. UJesu wasephendula wathi kubo: Lami kangilitsheli ukuthi ngenza lezizinto ngaliphi igunya. 
Mark12:1 Waseqala ukukhuluma labo ngemifanekiso wathi: Umuntu wahlanyela isivini, wasibiyela ngothango, wagebha isikhamelo, wakha umphotshongo, wasiqatshisa kubalimi, waya kwelinye ilizwe." 
Mark12:2 Kwathi sekuyisikhathi esifaneleyo wathuma inceku kubalimi, ukuze yemukele kubalimi okwesithelo sesivini." 
Mark12:3 Kodwa ba yi bamba bayitshaya, ba yi mukisa ize." 
Mark12:4 Wasebuya ethuma kubo enye inceku; laleyo bayitshaya ngamatshe ba yi limaza ekhanda, ba yi xotsha isi thelwe inhloni." 
Mark12:5 Wasebuya ethuma enye; yona basebeyibulala; lezinye ezinengi, ezinye bazitshaya, lezinye bazibulala." 
Mark12:6 Ngakho eseselendodana eyodwa ethandekayo kuye, ekucineni wayithuma kubo layo, esithi: Bazayihlonipha indodana yami." 
Mark12:7 Kodwa labobalimi bakhulumisana besithi: Le yindlalifa; wozani, siyibulale, lelifa lizakuba ngelethu." 
Mark12:8 Basebe yi bamba bayibulala, ba yi phosela ngaphandle kwesivini." 
Mark12:9 Ngakho uzakwenzani umninisivini? Uzakuza ababhubhise abalimi, anikele isivini kwabanye." 
Mark12:10 Kalibalanga yini lumbhalo othi: Ilitshe abakhi abalalayo, yilo eseliyinhloko yengonsi;" 
Mark12:11 lokhu kwenziwe yiNkosi, njalo kuyisimanga emehlweni ethu?" 
Mark12:12 Basebedinga ukumbamba, kodwa besaba ixuku; ngoba babesazi ukuthi wayekhuluma lumfanekiso emelane labo." 
Mark12:13 Basebethuma kuye abanye babaFarisi labakaHerodi. 
Mark12:14 Basebesiza bathi kuye: Mfundisi, siyazi ukuthi wena uqotho, njalo kawukhathali ngomuntu; ngoba kawunanzi isimo somuntu, kodwa ufundisa indlela kaNkulunkulu ngeqiniso: Kuvunyelwe yini ukuthela kuKesari kumbe hatshi?" 
Mark12:15 Sithele, kumbe singatheli? Kodwa ekwazi ukuzenzisa kwabo wathi kubo: Lingilingelani? Lethani kimi udenariyo, ukuze ngibone." 
Mark12:16 Basebeletha. Wasesithi kubo: Ngokabani lumfanekiso lalumbhalo? Basebesithi kuye: NgokaKesari. 
Mark12:17 UJesu wasephendula wathi kubo: Mnikeni uKesari okukaKesari, loNkulunkulu okukaNkulunkulu. Basebemangala ngaye." 
Mark12:18 Basebesiza kuye abaSadusi, abathi kakukho ukuvuka kwabafileyo; bambuza, bathi:" 
Mark12:19 Mfundisi, uMozisi wasibhalela, ukuthi: Uba umfowabo womuntu esifa, atshiye umka khe, engatshiyi bantwana, umfowabo kamthathe umkakhe, amvusele umfowabo inzalo;" 
Mark12:20 kwakulezelamani eziyisikhombisa; owokuqala wasethatha umfazi, wafa engatshiyanga inzalo;" 
Mark12:21 lowesibili wamthatha, wafa, laye engatshiyanga inzalo; lowesithathu kwaba njalo;" 
Mark12:22 lalaba boyisikhombisa bamthatha, kabatshiyanga inzalo. Ekucineni kwabo bonke kwafa lomfazi." 
Mark12:23 Ngakho ekuvukeni kwabafileyo, mhla bevukayo, uzakuba ngumkabani kubo; lokhu abayisikhombisa babelaye engumkabo?" 
Mark12:24 UJesu wasephendula wathi kubo: Kaliduhanga yini ngalokhu, ngoba lingayazi imibhalo, loba amandla kaNkulunkulu?" 
Mark12:25 Ngoba mhla bevukayo ekufeni, kabathathani, njalo kabendiswa, kodwa banjengengilosi ezisemazulwini." 
Mark12:26 Kodwa mayelana labafileyo, ukuthi bayavuswa, kalifundanga yini egwalweni lukaMozisi, ukuthi uNkulunkulu esihlahleni wakhuluma njani kuye?" 
Mark12:27 Kayisuye uNkulunkulu wabafileyo, kodwa uNkulunkulu wabaphilayo; ngakho lina liduhile kakhulu." 
Mark12:28 Wasefika omunye wababhali, esezwile bebuzana, esebonile ukuthi ubaphendule kuhle, wambuza wathi: Yiwuphi umlayo wokuqala kuyo yonke?" 
Mark12:29 UJesu wasemphendula wathi: Owokuqala kuyo yonke imilayo ngowokuthi: Zwana, Israyeli: INkosi uNkulunkulu wethu, iNkosi yinye;" 
Mark12:30 njalo wothanda iNkosi uNkulunkulu wakho ngenhliziyo yakho yonke, langomphefumulo wakho wonke, langengqondo yakho yonke, langamandla akho wonke. Yilo umlayo owokuqala." 
Mark12:31 Lowesibili uyafanana, yilo: Wothanda umakhelwane wakho njengalokhu uzi thanda wena. Kawukho omunye umlayo omkhulu kulale." 
Mark12:32 Umbhali wasesithi kuye: Kuhle, Mfundisi, utsho okuqotho ukuthi kuloNkulunkulu oyedwa, langaphandle kwakhe kakho omunye;" 
Mark12:33 lokumthanda ngenhliziyo yonke. 
Mark12:34 UJesu esembona ukuthi uphendule ngenhlakanipho, wathi kuye: Kawukhatshana lombuso kaNkulunkulu." 
Mark12:35 UJesu, wasephendula wathi: Batsho njani ababhali ukuthi uKristu uyindodana kaDavida?" 
Mark12:36 Ngoba uDavida uqobo lwakhe ngoMoya oyiNgcwele wathi: INkosi yathi eNkosini yami: Hlala ngakwesokunene sami, ngize ngibeke izitha zakho zibe yisenabelo senyawo zakho." 
Mark12:37 Ngakho uDavida uqobo lwakhe umbiza ngokuthiyiNkosi; pho uyindodana yakhe njani? Lexuku elikhulu lamuzwa ngokuthokoza. 
Mark12:38 Wasesithi kubo ekufundiseni kwakhe," 
Mark12:39 lezihlalo eziqakathekileyo emasinagogeni; 
Mark12:40 abadla izindlu zabafelokazi, bekhuleka isikhathieside ngokuzenzisa; laba bazakwemukela ukulahlwa okukhulu." 
Mark12:41 UJesu wasehlala phansi; labanothileyo abanengi baphosela okunengi. 
Mark12:42 Kwasekufika umfelokazi othile ongumyanga waphosela inhlamvana ezimbili ezincane zemali, ezenza indibilitshi." 
Mark12:43 Wasebizela kuye abafundi bakhe, wathi kubo: Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Lumfelokazi ongumyanga uphosele okwedlula bonke;" 
Mark12:44 ngoba bonke baphosele kokunengi kwabo; kodwa yena ebuyangeni bakhe. 
Mark13:1 Kwathi ephuma ethempelini, omunye wabafundi bakhe wathi kuye: Mfundisi, khangela, amatshe anjani lezakhiwo ezinjani!" 
Mark13:2 UJesu wasephendula wathi kuye: Uyabona lezizakhiwo ezinkulu yini? Akusoze kutshiywe ilitshe phezu kwelitshe, elingasoze lidilizelwe phansi." 
Mark13:3 Esehlezi entabeni yeMihlwathi maqondana lethempeli, uPetro loJakobe loJohane loAndreya bambuza bebodwa," 
Mark13:4 bathi: Sitshele, lezizinto zizakuba nini? Lesibonakaliso siyini lapho sezizapheleliswa lezizinto zonke?" 
Mark13:5 UJesu ebaphendula waseqala ukuthi: Qaphelani kungabi khona oliduhisayo. 
Mark13:6 Ngoba abanengi bazakuza ngebizo lami, besithi: Mina ngingu ye; futhi baduhise abanengi." 
Mark13:7 Kodwa nxa lisizwa ngezimpi lamahungahunga ezimpi, lingethuki; ngoba kufanele kwenzeke; kodwa ukuphela kakukabi khona." 
Mark13:8 Ngoba isizwe sizavukela isizwe, lombuso u vuk ele umbuso; njalo kuzakuba khona ukuzamazama komhlaba indawo ngendawo, njalo kuzakuba khona indlala lezinhlupheko; lezizinto ziyikuqala kwemihelo." 
Mark13:9 Kodwa ziqapheleni lina. 
Mark13:10 Kodwa ivangeli limele ukutshunyayelwa kuqala kuzo zonke izizwe. 
Mark13:11 Kodwa nxa be li donsa belinikela, lingakhathaleli ngaphambili elizakukhuluma, linganakani; kodwa loba yini elizayinikwa ngalelohola, ikhulumeni; ngoba kakusini elikhulumayo, kodwa uMoya oyiNgcwele." 
Mark13:12 Futhi umfowabo uzanikela umfowabo ekufeni, loyise umntwana; labantwana bazavukela abazali, besebebabulala;" 
Mark13:13 njalo lizazondwa yibo bonke ngenxa yebizo lami; kodwa ophikelelayo kuze kube sekupheleni, nguye ozasindiswa." 
Mark13:14 Kodwa nxa libona amanyala encithakalo, akhulunywa nguDaniyeli umprofethi, emi lapho angafanele khona (ofundayo kaqedisise), khona labo abaseJudiya kababalekele ezintabeni;" 
Mark13:15 lophezu kophahla lwendlu angehleli endlini, angangeni ukuthatha ulutho endlini yakhe;" 
Mark13:16 losemasimini angabuyeli emuva, ukuyathatha isembatho sakhe." 
Mark13:17 Kodwa maye kwabakhulelweyo labamunyisayo ngalezonsuku! 
Mark13:18 Kodwa khulekani ukuthi ukubaleka kwenu kungabi sebusika. 
Mark13:19 Ngoba nga lezonsuku kuzakuba khona ukuhlupheka, okungazanga kube khona kusukela ekuqaleni kokudaliweyo uNkulunkulu akudalayo kuze kube khathesi, lokungasoze kwaba khona." 
Mark13:20 Njalo uba iNkosi ibingazifinyezanga lezonsuku, bekungesindiswe nyama; kodwa ngenxa yabakhethiweyo, ebakhethileyo, izifinyezile insuku." 
Mark13:21 Langalesosikhathi nxa umuntu esithi kini: Khangelani, nangu uKristu; kumbe: Khangelani, ulaphayana; lingakholwa;" 
Mark13:22 ngoba kuzavuka okristu bamanga labaprofethi bamanga, besebesenza izibonakaliso lezimangaliso, ukuduhisa, nxa kungenzeka, labakhethiweyo." 
Mark13:23 Kodwa qaphelani lina; khangelani, se ngilitshelile konke ngaphambili." 
Mark13:24 Kodwa ngalezonsuku, emva kwalokhokuhlupheka, ilanga lizafiphazwa, lenyanga kayiyikupha ukukhanya kwayo," 
Mark13:25 lenkanyezi zezulu zizabe zisiwa, lamandla asemazulwini azazanyazanyiswa." 
Mark13:26 Khona-ke bezabona iNdodana yomuntu isiza emayezini ilamandla amakhulu lenkazimulo," 
Mark13:27 khona-ke izathuma ingilosi zayo, ibisiqoqa abakhethiweyo bayo emimoyeni yomine, kusukela emkhawulweni womhlaba kuze kube semkhawulweni wezulu." 
Mark13:28 Fundani-ke umfanekiso emkhiweni; nxa ugatsha lwawo selusiba buthakathaka luhlume amahlamvu, liyazi ukuthi ihlobo seliseduze;" 
Mark13:29 ngokunjalo lani, nxa libona lezizinto zisenzeka, yazini ukuthi kuseduze kuseminyango." 
Mark13:30 Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Lesisizukulwana asisoze sidlule, zize zenzeke izinto zonke lezi." 
Mark13:31 Kuzadlula izulu lomhlaba; kodwa amazwi ami awasoze adlule. 
Mark13:32 Kodwa lolosuku lalelohola kakho owaziyo ngakho, ngitsho lengilosi ezisezulwini." 
Mark13:33 Qaphelani. 
Mark13:34 Njengomuntu owasuka elizweni lakibo watshiya indlu yakhe, wanika inceku zakhe amandla, kuleyo laleyo umsebenzi wayo." 
Mark13:35 Ngakho lindani; 
Mark13:36 hlezi ifike ilijume, ilifice lilele." 
Mark13:37 Lalokhu engikutsho kini ngikutsho kubo bonke: Lindani. 
Mark14:1 Kwathi emva kwensuku ezimbili kwaba khona iphasika l omkhosi wesinkwa esingelamvubelo; abapristi abakhulu lababhali basebedinga ukuthi bangambamba njani ngobuqili ba m bulale; 
Mark14:2 kodwa bathi: Kungabi ngomkhosi, hlezi kube lesiphithiphithi sabantu." 
Mark14:3 Kwathi eseBethani, endlini kaSimoni umlephero, ehlezi ekudleni, kwafika owesifazana ephethe umfuma we-alibasta wamagcobo awenadi uqobo aligugu elikhulu; wasephahlaza umfuma we-alibasta, wa wa thela ekhanda lakhe." 
Mark14:4 Kwakukhona abanye abathukuthelayo ngaphakathi kwabo, besithi: Kwenzelwani ukumotshwa kwalamagcobo?" 
Mark14:5 Ngoba la abengathengiswa ngemaliedlula odenariyo abangamakhulu amathathu, besekunikwa abayanga. Basebemsola." 
Mark14:6 Kodwa uJesu wathi: Myekeleni; limhluphelani? Wenze umsebenzi omuhle kimi. 
Mark14:7 Ngoba abayanga lihlala lilabo, futhi uba lithanda lingabenzela okuhle; kodwa mina kalihlali lilami." 
Mark14:8 Yena wenzile abengakwenza; uqalile ngaphambili ukuwugcobela ukungcwatshwa umzimba wami. 
Mark14:9 Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Loba ngaphi emhlabeni wonke lapho okuzatshunyayelwa khona lelivangeli, lalokhu akwenzileyo kuzakhulunywa ngakho kube yisikhumbuzo ngaye." 
Mark14:10 UJudasi Iskariyothi, omunye wabalitshumi lambili, wasesiya kubapristi abakhulu, ukuze amnikele kubo." 
Mark14:11 Futhi sebezwile bathokoza, bathembisa ukumnika imali; wasedinga ukuthi angamnikela njani kuhle." 
Mark14:12 Kwathi ngosuku lokuqala lwesinkwa esingelamvubelo, ababehlaba ngalo iphasika, abafundi bakhe bathi kuye: Uthanda ukuthi siyelungisa ngaphi ukuze udle iphasika?" 
Mark14:13 Wasethuma ababili kubafundi bakhe, wathi kubo: Hambani liye emzini, njalo umuntu uzahlangana lani ethwele imbiza yamanzi; limlandele," 
Mark14:14 njalo loba kungaphi azangena khona, kalibokuthi kumninindlu: UMfundisi uthi: Ingaphi indlu yezihambi, lapho engingadlela khona iphasika labafundi bami?" 
Mark14:15 Futhi yena uzalitshengisa indlu enkulu ephezulu eyendlelweyo elungisiweyo; silungiseleni khona. 
Mark14:16 Abafundi bakhe basebephuma, bangena emzini, bathola kunjengokutsho kwakhe kubo; basebelungisa iphasika." 
Mark14:17 Kwathi sekukusihlwa wafika labalitshumi lambili. 
Mark14:18 Sebehlezi besidla, uJesu wathi: Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Omunye wenu, odla lami, uzanginikela." 
Mark14:19 Basebeqala ukudabuka, bathi kuye ngamunye ngamunye: Yimi yini? Lomunye: Yimi yini?" 
Mark14:20 Kodwa waphendula wathi kubo: Ng omunye wabalitshumi lambili, otsheba kanye lami emganwini." 
Mark14:21 Sibili iNdodana yomuntu ihamba, njengokulotshiweyo ngayo; kodwa maye kulowomuntu enikelwa nguye iNdodana yomuntu! Bekungakuhle kuye aluba lowomuntu wayengazalwanga." 
Mark14:22 Kwathi besidla, uJesu wathatha isinkwa, wa si busisa wa si hlephula, wabanika, wathi: Thathani, lidle; lokhu kungumzimba wami." 
Mark14:23 Wasethatha inkezo, esebongile wabanika; basebenatha kuyo bonke." 
Mark14:24 Wasesithi kubo: Leli ligazi lami, elesivumelwano esitsha, elichithelwa abanengi." 
Mark14:25 Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Angisayikunatha okwesithelo sevini, kuze kufikelolosuku engizasinatha ngalo sisitsha embusweni kaNkulunkulu." 
Mark14:26 Kwathi sebehlabele ingoma yokudumisa baphuma baya entabeni yeMihlwathi. 
Mark14:27 UJesu wasesithi kubo: Lonke lizakhubeka ngami ngalobubusuku; ngoba kulotshiwe ukuthi: Ngizatshaya umelusi, izimvu besezihlakazeka." 
Mark14:28 Kodwa emva kokuvuswa kwami, ngizalandulela ukuya eGalili." 
Mark14:29 Kodwa uPetro wathi kuye: Lanxa bonke bezakhubeka, kodwa hatshi mina." 
Mark14:30 UJesu wasesithi kuye: Ngiqinisile ngithi kuwe: Lamuhla ngalobubusuku, lingakakhali kabili iqhude, uzangiphika kathathu." 
Mark14:31 Kodwa waqinisa ngamandla esithi: Loba kudingeka ngife lawe, angisoze ngikuphike. Basebesitsho njalo labo bonke." 
Mark14:32 Basebefika endaweni ebizo layo yiGetsemane; wasesithi kubafundi bakhe: Hlalani phansi lapha, ngisa ya khuleka." 
Mark14:33 Wasethatha kanye laye uPetro loJakobe loJohane, waseqala ukudatshulwa sibili lokukhathazeka kakhulu." 
Mark14:34 Wasesithi kubo: Umphefumulo wami udabukile kakhulu kuze kube sekufeni; hlalani lapha lilinde. 
Mark14:35 Waseqhubeka ibangana, wawela emhlabathini, wakhuleka ukuthi, uba kungenzeka, kudlule kuye lelihola." 
Mark14:36 Wasesithi: Abha, Baba." 
Mark14:37 Wasesiza, wabafica belele, wathi kuPetro: Simoni, ulele yini? Ubungelinde yini ihola libe linye?" 
Mark14:38 Lindani likhuleke, ukuze lingangeni ekulingweni. Umoya uyavuma-ke, kodwa inyama ibuthakathaka." 
Mark14:39 Wasebuya wahamba wa ya khuleka, esitsho wona lawomazwi." 
Mark14:40 Wasebuya wabafica futhi belele; ngoba amehlo abo ayenzima, kodwa babengazi ukuthi bazamphendula bathi ni." 
Mark14:41 Wasesiza ngokwesithathu, wathi kubo: Qhubekani lilele-ke liphumule. Kwanele; ihola selifikile; khangelani, iNdodana yomuntu iyanikelwa ezandleni zezoni." 
Mark14:42 Sukumani, sihambe; khangelani, onginikelayo useduze."
