Mark14:43 Kwathi esakhuluma, wahle wafika uJudasi, omunye wabalitshumi lambili, njalo elexuku elikhulu elilezinkemba lezinduku, livela kubapristi abakhulu lababhali labadala." 
Mark14:44 Lomnikelayo wayebanike isiboniso, esithi: Lowo engizamanga, nguye; limbambe, li m qhube li m qinise." 
Mark14:45 Esefikile, wahle wasondela kuye wathi: Rabi, Rabi! Wasemanga." 
Mark14:46 Basebemdumela, bambamba." 
Mark14:47 Lomunye kwababemi khona wakhokha inkemba wagadla inceku yompristi omkhulu, waquma indlebe yayo." 
Mark14:48 UJesu wasephendula wathi kubo: Liphume njengokuyamelana lomphangi yini lilezinkemba lezinduku ukuzangibamba? 
Mark14:49 Bengilani insuku ngensuku ethempelini ngifundisa, kodwa kalingibambanga; kodwa lokhu kwenzekeukuze kugcwaliseke imibhalo." 
Mark14:50 Bonke basebemtshiya babaleka. 
Mark14:51 Lejaha elithile lamlandela, lembethe ilembu elicolekileyo emzimbenionqunu. Aselibamba amajaha;" 
Mark14:52 laselitshiya ilembu elicolekileyo lababalekela linqunu. 
Mark14:53 Basebemqhuba uJesu bamusakumpristi omkhulu; basebebuthana kuye abapristi abakhulu bonke labadala lababhali. 
Mark14:54 UPetro wasemlandela ekhatshana waze waba phakathi kweguma lompristi omkhulu; wayehlezi kanye lezinceku, esotha umlilo." 
Mark14:55 Labapristi abakhulu lomphakathi wonke badinga ubufakazi ngoJesu, ukuze bambulale; kodwa kababutholanga." 
Mark14:56 Ngoba abanengi bafakaza amanga ngaye, kodwa lobubufakazi kabuvumelananga." 
Mark14:57 Kwasekusukuma abanye bafakaza amanga amelana laye besithi: 
Mark14:58 Thina samuzwa esithi: Mina ngizadiliza lelithempeli ngensuku ezintathu. 
Mark14:59 Loba kunjalo ubufakazi babo kabuvumelananga. 
Mark14:60 Kwasekusukuma umpristi omkhulu phakathi kwabowambuza uJesu, esithi: Kawuphenduli lutho yini? Bafakazani laba okumelana lawe?" 
Mark14:61 Kodwa wathula, kaphendulanga lutho. Umpristi omkhulu wabuya wambuza, wathi kuye: Wena unguKristu, iNdodana yoBusisiweyo yini?" 
Mark14:62 UJesu wasesithi: Mina nginguye. Njalo lizabona iNdodana yomuntu ihlezi ngakwesokunene samandla, isiza ngamayezi ezulu." 
Mark14:63 Umpristi omkhulu wasedabula izembatho zakhe wathi: Sisaswelelani abafakazi? 
Mark14:64 Liyizwile inhlamba; licabangani? Bonke basebemlahla ukuthi ulecala lokufa. 
Mark14:65 Abanye basebeqala ukumkhafulela amathe, lokumgubuzela ubuso, lokumdutshuza." 
Mark14:66 UPetro esegumeni ngaphansi; 
Mark14:67 isibona uPetro esotha, yamkhangela yathi: Lawe ubulomNazaretha, uJesu." 
Mark14:68 Kodwa waphika, wathi: Kangikwazi, futhi kangikuqedisisi okutshoyo. Wasephuma phandle, waya entubeni; laselikhala iqhude." 
Mark14:69 Njalo incekukazi encane imbona yabuya yaqala ukutsho kwababemi khona ukuthi: Lo ungo munyewabo. 
Mark14:70 Kodwa wabuya waphika. Kwathi emva kwesikhatshana futhi labo ababemi khona bathi kuPetro: Ngeqiniso ungo munyewabo; ngoba lawe ungumGalili. 
Mark14:71 Waseqala ukuqalekisa lokufunga esithi: Kangimazi lumuntu elimtshoyo. 
Mark14:72 Iqhude laselikhala ngokwesibili. UPetro wasekhumbula ilizwi uJesu ayelitshilo kuye lokuthi: Lingakakhali kabili iqhude, uzangiphika kathathu. Esenakane ngalokhu wakhala." 
Mark15:1 Kwathi khonokho ekuseni kakhulu abapristi abakhulu benza umhlangano kanye labadala lababhali. 
Mark15:2 UPilatu wasembuza wathi: Wena uyiNkosi yamaJuda yini? Wasemphendula wathi kuye: Uyatsho wena. 
Mark15:3 Abapristi abakhulu basebemmangalela ngezinto ezinengi; kodwa yena kaphendulanga lutho. 
Mark15:4 UPilatu wasebuya embuza, wathi: Kawuphenduli lutho yini? Khangela, zingaki izinto abazifakazayo ezimelana lawe." 
Mark15:5 Kodwa uJesu kabesaphendula lutho, waze wamangala uPilatu." 
Mark15:6 Langomkhosi wayebakhululela isibotshwa esisodwa, loba yisiphi abasicelayo." 
Mark15:7 Kwakukhona umuntuothiwa nguBarabasi, owayebotshiwe lalabo ababevukele umbuso laye, ababebulele ekuvukeleni umbuso." 
Mark15:8 Ixuku laselimemeza laqala ukucela ukuthi alenzele njengezikhathi zonke. 
Mark15:9 UPilatu wasebaphendula, wathi: Lithanda ukuthi ngilikhululele iNkosi yamaJuda yini?" 
Mark15:10 Ngoba wayekwazi ukuthi ngomona abapristi abakhulu bamnikele. 
Mark15:11 Kodwa abapristi abakhulu bavusa ixuku, ukuthi kungcono alikhululele uBarabasi." 
Mark15:12 UPilatu wasephendula wathi futhi kubo: Pho lifuna ngimenzeni lo elithi uyiNkosi yamaJuda? 
Mark15:13 Basebememeza futhi bathi: Mbethele! 
Mark15:14 Kodwa uPilatu wathi kubo: Ngoba wenze ububi bani? Kodwa bamemeza kakhulu bathi: Mbethele! 
Mark15:15 Khona uPilatu ethanda ukukholisa ixuku, wabakhululela uBarabasi; kodwa wamnikela uJesu, ese m tshaye ngesiswepu, ukuthi abethelwe." 
Mark15:16 Abebutho basebemngenisa," 
Mark15:17 bamgqokisa okuyibubende, sebeluke umqhele wameva bamethesa," 
Mark15:18 baqala ukumbingelela besithi: Bayethe, Nkosi yamaJuda!" 
Mark15:19 Batshaya ikhanda lakhe ngomhlanga, bamkhafulela amathe, baguqa ngamadolo bamkhonza." 
Mark15:20 Sebemklolodele, bamhlubula okuyibubende, bamgqokisa ezakhe izembatho. Basebemusa phandle ukuze bambethele." 
Mark15:21 Babamba ngamandla omunye owayesedlula othiwanguSimoni umKurene, evela emaphandleni, uyise kaAleksandro, ukuthi athwale isiphambano sakhe." 
Mark15:22 Basebemusa endaweni. 
Mark15:23 Basebemnika iwayini lixutshaniswe lenhlaka ukuthi alinathe; kodwa kalemukelanga. 
Mark15:24 Sebembethele, babelana izembatho zakhe, benza inkatho yokuphosa ngazo, ukuthi ngamunye uzathathani." 
Mark15:25 Kwakulihola lesithathu, njalo bambethela." 
Mark15:26 Futhi kwakulombhalo wecala lakhe elalibhalwe phezulu usithi: INKOSI YAMAJUDA. 
Mark15:27 Njalo babethela kanye laye abaphangi ababili, omunye ngakwesokunene lomunye ngakwesokhohlo sakhe." 
Mark15:28 Wasugcwaliseka umbhalo othi: Futhi wabalwa kanye lezoni. 
Mark15:29 Labedlulayo bamhlambaza, benikina amakhanda abo, besithi: Hiya, wena odiliza ithempeli, ulakhe ngensuku ezintathu," 
Mark15:30 zisindise, wehle esiphambanweni." 
Mark15:31 Langokunjalo abapristi abakhulu labo bakloloda kanye lababhali bathi omunye komunye: Wasindisa abanye, angezisindise yena." 
Mark15:32 UKristu iNkosi yakoIsrayeli kehle khathesi esiphambanweni, ukuze sibone sikholwe. Lababebethelwe kanye laye bamklolodela." 
Mark15:33 Kwathi sekufike ihola lesithupha, kwaba khona ubumnyama phezu komhlaba wonke kwaze kwaba lihola lesificamunwemunye." 
Mark15:34 Ngehola lesificamunwemunye uJesu wamemeza ngelizwi elikhulu, wathi, ""Eloyi, Eloyi, lama sabaktani?"" Okuyikuthi ngokuphendulelwa: Nkulunkulu wami, Nkulunkulu wami, ungitshiyeleni?" 
Mark15:35 Labanye kwababemi khona besizwa bathi: Khangelani, ubiza uElija." 
Mark15:36 Wasegijima omunye, wagcwalisa uzipho ngeviniga, waluhloma emhlangeni, wamnika ukuthi anathe, esithi: Yekelani, sibone uba uElija uzakuza amethule." 
Mark15:37 UJesu wasememeza ngelizwi elikhulu waphefumula okokucina. 
Mark15:38 Leveyili lethempeli ladatshulwa laba zincezuezimbili laqala phezulu lisiya phansi. 
Mark15:39 Kwathi induna yekhulu eyayimi maqondana laye ibona ukuthi ukhale njalo, waphefumula okokucina, yathi: Ngeqiniso lumuntu ubeyiNdodana kaNkulunkulu." 
Mark15:40 Kwakukhona labesifazana bebukele bekhatshana, okwakukhona phakathi kwabo loMariya Magadalena, loMariya unina kaJakobe omncinyane lokaJose, loSalome," 
Mark15:41 (labo ababemlandela, eseseGalili, bemncedisa), labanye abesifazana abanengi abenyukela eJerusalema laye." 
Mark15:42 Kwathi sekuhlwile," 
Mark15:43 wafika uJosefa owayevela eArimathiya, ilunga; wangena ngesibindi kuPilatu, wacela isidumbu sikaJesu." 
Mark15:44 UPilatu wasemangala ngokuthi usefile; wabizela kuye induna yekhulu, wayibuza ukuthi kambe sekuyisikhathi efile." 
Mark15:45 Esazisiwe yinduna yekhulu, wamnika uJosefa isidumbu." 
Mark15:46 Wasethenga ilembu elicolekileyo, wamethula, wamgoqela ngelembu elicolekileyo, wambeka engcwabeni elaligujwe edwaleni; wagiqela ilitshe emnyango wengcwaba." 
Mark15:47 Futhi uMariya Magadalena loMariya uninakaJose babona lapho ayebekwa khona. 
Mark16:1 Isabatha selidlulile. 
Mark16:2 Kwathi ekuseni kakhulu ngo sukulokuqala lweviki beza engcwabeni. 
Mark16:3 Basebekhulumisana besithi: Ngubani ozasigiqela ilitshe lisuke emnyango wengcwaba? 
Mark16:4 Futhi bathi ukukhangela babona ilitshe seligiqwe lasuswa; ngoba lalilikhulu kakhulu. 
Mark16:5 Kuthe bengena engcwabeni. 
Mark16:6 Kodwa lathi kubo: Lingesabi; lidinga uJesu umNazaretha obebethelwe; uvukile, kakho lapha; khangelani, indawo lapho abebembeke khona." 
Mark16:7 Kodwa hambani, litshele abafundi bakhe loPetro ukuthi uzalandulela ukuya eGalili." 
Mark16:8 Basebephuma ngokuphangisa babaleka engcwabeni; futhi ukuqhuqha lokwethuka kwababamba; futhi kabakhulumanga lutho emuntwini, ngoba babesesaba." 
Mark16:9 Kwathi uJesuesevukile ekuseni kakhulu ngolokuqala lweviki. 
Mark16:10 Yena wasuka wababikela labo ababelaye. 
Mark16:11 Labo sebezwile ukuthi uyaphila lokuthi ubonwe nguye, kabakholwanga." 
Mark16:12 Njalo emva kwalezizinto wabonakala ngesinye isimo. 
Mark16:13 Labo bahamba babikela abanye; lalabo kababakholwanga. 
Mark16:14 Emva kwalokhu wabonakala kwabalitshumi lanye. 
Mark16:15 Wasesithi kubo: Hambani liye emhlabeni wonke. 
Mark16:16 Lowo okholwayo. 
Mark16:17 Lalezizibonakaliso zizabalandela abakholwayo; 
Mark16:18 bazadobha izinyoka; uba benatha loba yikuphi okubulalayo. 
Mark16:19 Ngakho iNkosi, emva kokuthi isikhulumile labo." 
Mark16:20 Bona basebephuma batshumayela endaweni zonke, iNkosi isebenza la bo. Ameni." 
Luke1:1 Njengoba abanengi sebebeke izandla ukubeka ngendlela efaneleyo ukulandiswa kwezinto eziqiniseke ngokupheleleyo phakathi kwethu," 
Luke1:2 njengalokhu basinika," 
Luke1:3 kukhanye kukuhle lakimi," 
Luke1:4 ukuze wazi iqiniso ngalezozinto. 
Luke1:5 Ensukwini zikaHerodi inkosi yeJudiya kwakukhona umpristi othile othiwa nguZakariya; lomkakhe wayevela kumadodakazi kaAroni, lebizo lakhe linguElizabethi." 
Luke1:6 Njalo babelungile bobabili phambi kukaNkulunkulu. 
Luke1:7 Njalo babengelamntwana, ngoba uElizabethi wayeyinyumba." 
Luke1:8 Kwasekusithi esenza inkonzo yobupristi phambi kukaNkulunkulu esesimisweni seqembu lakibo," 
Luke1:9 ngomkhuba wenkonzo yobupristi. 
Luke1:10 Njalo ixuku lonke labantu. 
Luke1:11 Ingilosi yeNkosi yasibonakala kuye. 
Luke1:12 Kwathi uZakariya e yi bona waqhuqha, lokwesaba kwawela phezu kwakhe." 
Luke1:13 Kodwa ingilosi yathi kuye: Ungesabi Zakariya; ngoba umkhuleko wakho uzwakele, lomkakho uElizabethi uzakuzalela indodana, njalo uzakuthi ibizo layo nguJohane." 
Luke1:14 Futhi uzakuba lenjabulo lentokozo, labanengi bazakujabulela ukuzalwa kwakhe." 
Luke1:15 Ngoba uzakuba mkhulu phambi kweNkosi, iwayini kanye lokunathwayo okulamandla." 
Luke1:16 Labanengi kubantwana bakoIsrayeli uzabaphendulela eNkosini uNkulunkulu wabo; 
Luke1:17 njalo yena uzahamba phambi kwayo emoyeni lemandleni kaElija. 
Luke1:18 UZakariya wasesithi kuyo ingilosi: Ngizakwazi ngani lokhu. 
Luke1:19 Ingilosi yasiphendula yathi kuye: NginguGabriyeli. 
Luke1:20 Njalo khangela, uzakuba yisimungulu njalo wehluleke ukukhuluma, kuze kube lusuku okuzakwenzeka ngalolezizinto, ngenxa yokuthi ungakholwanga amazwi ami, azagcwaliseka ngesikhathi sawo." 
Luke1:21 Labantu babemlindele uZakariya; bamangala ngokuphuza kwakhe ethempelini. 
Luke1:22 Kuthe esephuma wehluleka ukukhuluma labo; njalo bazi ukuthi ubone umbono ethempelini. 
Luke1:23 Kwasekusithi seziphelile insuku. 
Luke1:24 Kwathi emva kwalezonsuku uElizabethi umkakhe wathatha isisu, wazifihla okwezinyanga ezinhlanu, esithi:" 
Luke1:25 Yenze kanje kimi iNkosi ensukwini eya ngi khangela ngazo. 
Luke1:26 Kwathi ngenyanga yesithupha," 
Luke1:27 entombini eyayigane indoda, ebizo layo lalinguJosefa; lebizo lentombi linguMariya." 
Luke1:28 Ingilosi yasingena kuye yathi: Ekuhle, wena othandiweyo." 
Luke1:29 Kwathi ese yi bonile wethuswa kakhulu yilizwi layo. 
Luke1:30 Ingilosi yasisithi kuye: Ungesabi, Mariya; ngoba uthole uthando kuNkulunkulu." 
Luke1:31 Njalo khangela, uzathatha isisu, uzale indodana." 
Luke1:32 Yena uzakuba mkhulu, uzabizwa ngokuthiyiNdodana yoPhezukonke," 
Luke1:33 njalo uzabusa phezu kwendlu kaJakobe kuze kube nininini, langombuso wakhe kawuzukuba lokuphela." 
Luke1:34 UMariya wasesithi kuyo ingilosi: Lokhu kungenzeka njani, njengoba ngingazi indoda?" 
Luke1:35 Ingilosi yasiphendula yathi kuye: UMoya oNgcwele uzakuza phezu kwakho. 
Luke1:36 Njalo khangela, isinini sakho uElizabethi, laye ukhulelwe yindodana ebudaleni bakhe." 
Luke1:37 Ngoba kuNkulunkulu kakulalutho oluzakwehlula. 
Luke1:38 UMariya wasesithi: Khangela, incekukazi yeNkosi; kakube kimi njengelizwi lakho. Ingilosi yasisuka kuye." 
Luke1:39 Ngalezonsuku uMariya wasesukuma waya ezintabeni," 
Luke1:40 wangena endlini kaZakariya, wabingelela uElizabethi." 
Luke1:41 Kwasekusithi uElizabethi ezwe ukubingelela kukaMariya, inkonyane yeqa esiswini sakhe; loElizabethi wagcwaliswa ngoMoya oNgcwele," 
Luke1:42 wamemeza ngelizwi elikhulu, wathi: Ubusisiwe wena phakathi kwabesifazana, njalo sibusisiwe isithelo sesizalo sakho!" 
Luke1:43 Kanti kuvela ngaphi lokhu kimi? 
Luke1:44 Ngoba khangela, kuthe ilizwi lokubingelela kwakho lifika endlebeni zami, umntwana weqa esiswini sami ngokuthokoza." 
Luke1:45 Futhi ubusisiwe. 
Luke1:46 UMariya wasesithi: Umphefumulo wami," 
Luke1:47 lomoya wami uyathokoza," 
Luke1:48 ngoba ukhangele ubuphansi bencekukazi yakhe. 
Luke1:49 Ngoba yena olamandla ungenzele," 
Luke1:50 lesihawu sakhe sikusizukulwana ngesizukulwana kulabo abamesabayo. 
Luke1:51 Wenzile amandla ngengalo yakhe. 
Luke1:52 Wehlisile. 
Luke1:53 Abalambileyo ubasuthise ngezinto ezinhle. 
Luke1:54 Umsizile uIsrayeli inceku yakhe," 
Luke1:55 njengoba watsho kubobaba bethu, kuAbrahama, lenzalweni yakhe kuze kube nininini." 
Luke1:56 UMariya wasehlala laye okungaba zinyanga ezintathu, wasebuyela endlini yakhe." 
Luke1:57 Isikhathi sikaElizabethi sokuthi abelethe sesiphelele, wasebeletha indodana." 
Luke1:58 Abakhelene laye. 
Luke1:59 Kwasekusithi ngosuku lwesificaminwembili, beza uku za soka usane." 
Luke1:60 Kodwa unina waphendula wathi: Hatshi bo, kodwa luzathiwa nguJohane." 
Luke1:61 Basebesithi kuye: Kakho ezihlotsheni zakho obizwa ngalelibizo. 
Luke1:62 Basebeqhweba uyise, ukuthi angathanda ukuthi lubizwe ngokuthini." 
Luke1:63 Wasecela into yokubhalela, wabhala, esithi: NguJohane ibizo lalo; basebemangala bonke." 
Luke1:64 Njalo wahle wavulwa umlomo wakhe. 
Luke1:65 Lokwesaba kwehlela phezu kwabo bonke abakhelene labo," 
Luke1:66 labo bonke aba zi zwayo ba zi londoloza ezinhliziyweni zabo. 
Luke1:67 LoZakariya uyise wagcwaliswa ngoMoya oNgcwele, waprofetha, esithi:" 
Luke1:68 Ibusisiwe iNkosi," 
Luke1:69 yasivusela uphondo losindiso endlini kaDavida inceku yayo," 
Luke1:70 njengalokho yakhuluma ngomlomo wabaprofethi bayo abangcwele," 
Luke1:71 isikhulula ezitheni zethu, lesandleni sabo bonke abasizondayo;" 
Luke1:72 ukwenzela obaba bethu," 
Luke1:73 isifungo eyasifunga kubaba wethu uAbrahama," 
Luke1:74 ukusinika, ukuthi sesikhululiwe esandleni sezitha zethu, siyikhonze si ngelakwesaba" 
Luke1:75 ngobungcwele langokulunga phambi kwayo. 
Luke1:76 Lawe-ke, sane, uzabizwa ngokuthiu ngumprofethi;" 
Luke1:77 lokunika isizwe sayo ulwazi losindiso ngothethelelo lwezono zabo," 
Luke1:78 ngesihelo sikaNkulunkulu wethu, okuthi ngaso ukusa kwaphezulu kusethekelele," 
Luke1:79 ukubakhanyisela. 
Luke1:80 Wakhula-ke umntwana omncane, waqina emoyeni." 
Luke2:1 Kwasekusithi ngalezonsuku, isimiso saphuma kuKesari uAgastasi." 
Luke2:2 Lokhukubhalwa kwakungokokuqala. 
Luke2:3 Bonke basebesiya ukuze ba ye bhalwa, ngulowo lalowo emzini wakibo." 
Luke2:4 LoJosefa laye wenyuka," 
Luke2:5 uku ya bhalwa kanye loMariya umkakhe ayemganile, owayezithwele." 
Luke2:6 Kwasekusithi belapho, zaseziphelela insuku zokubeletha kwakhe." 
Luke2:7 Wasebeletha indodana yakhe eyingqabutho. 
Luke2:8 Njalo kwakukhona kulelolizwe abelusi ababehlala egangeni futhi belinde umhlambi wabo ebusuku. 
Luke2:9 Njalo khangela, ingilosi yeNkosi yema eduze kwabo." 
Luke2:10 Ingilosi yasisithi kubo: Lingesabi; ngoba khangelani, ngitshumayela indaba ezinhle kini ezentokozo enkulu, ezakuba kubantu bonke;" 
Luke2:11 ngoba lizalelwe lamuhla. 
Luke2:12 Njalo lokhu kuzakuba yisibonakaliso kini. 
Luke2:13 Njalo kwahle kwaba khona kanye lengilosi ixuku, lisithi:" 
Luke2:14 Udumo kalube kuNkulunkulu. 
Luke2:15 Kwasekusithi, ingilosi sezisukile kubo zisiya ezulwini, abantu, abangabelusi, bakhulumisana besithi: Ake siye eBhethelehema, sibone leyonto eyenzakeleyo, iNkosi esazise yona." 
Luke2:16 Basebesiza ngokuphangisa, bathola oMariya loJosefa, losane lulele emkolweni." 
Luke2:17 Sebebonile basebesazisa indawoezizingelezeleyo ngelizwi ababelitshelwe mayelana lalo umntwana omncane. 
Luke2:18 Labo bonke aba ku zwayo bamangala ngezinto ezazikhulunywe ngabelusi kubo. 
Luke2:19 Kodwa uMariya. 
Luke2:20 Basebebuyela abelusi, bemdumisa." 
Luke2:21 Kwathi seziphelile insuku eziyisificaminwembili zokuthi umntwana omncane asokwe. 
Luke2:22 Kwathi seziphelele insuku zokuhlanjululwa kwakhe ngokomlayo kaMozisi 
Luke2:23 (njengokulotshiweyo emlayweni weNkosi ukuthi konke okwesilisa okuvula isibeletho kuzathiwa kungcwele eNkosini) 
Luke2:24 lokuthi banikele umhlatshelo njengokutshiwo emlayweni weNkosi, amajuba amabili kumbe amaphuphu amabili enkwilimba." 
Luke2:25 Njalo khangela, kwakukhona eJerusalema umuntu, obizo lakhe linguSimeyoni, njalo lumuntu wayelungile ekhuthele ekukhonzeni, loMoya oNgcwele wayephezu kwakhe." 
Luke2:26 Futhi kwakubonakalisiwe kuye nguMoya oyiNgcwele. 
Luke2:27 Wasengena ethempelini ngoMoya," 
Luke2:28 yena wasemthatha wamphatha engalweni zakhe, wabonga uNkulunkulu, wathi:" 
Luke2:29 Nkosi; 
Luke2:30 ngoba amehlo ami alubonile usindiso lwakho 
Luke2:31 olulungisileyo phambi kobuso babantu bonke; 
Luke2:32 ukukhanya kokwembulela abezizwe. 
Luke2:33 UJosefa lonina basebemangala ngezinto ezatshiwo ngaye. 
Luke2:34 USimeyoni wasebabusisa, wathi kuMariya unina: Khangela, lo umiselwe;" 
Luke2:35 futhi lawe, inkemba izadabula owakho umphefumulo." 
Luke2:36 Njalo kwakukhona uAna umprofethikazi, indodakazi kaFanuweli, owesizwe sikaAsheri, ebehlale lendoda iminyaka eyisikhombisa kusukela ebuntombini bakhe," 
Luke2:37 njalo wayengumfelokazi owayengaba leminyaka engamatshumi ayisificaminwembili lane, engasuki ethempelini, ekhonza." 
Luke2:38 Laye efika ngalelohola wadumisa uNkulunkulu, wakhuluma ngaye kubo bonke ababelindele." 
Luke2:39 Kwathi sebeqedile konke okungokomlayo weNkosi, babuyela eGalili." 
Luke2:40 Lomntwana omncane wakhula, waqina emoyeni, wagcwala inhlakanipho; lomusa kaNkulunkulu wawuphezu kwakhe." 
Luke2:41 Njalo abazali bakhe babesiya eJerusalema iminyaka yonke. 
Luke2:42 Kwathi eseleminyaka elitshumi lambili, sebenyukele eJerusalema njengomkhuba womkhosi," 
Luke2:43 njalo seziphelile insuku, ekubuyeleni kwabo, umntwana uJesu wasala eJerusalema; njalo uJosefa lonina bengazi;" 
Luke2:44 kodwa becabanga ukuthi wayesexukwini endleleni, bahamba uhambo losuku, bamdinga phakathi kwezinini;" 
Luke2:45 kodwa bengamtholi, babuyela eJerusalema, bemdinga." 
Luke2:46 Kwasekusithi emva kwensuku ezintathu, bamthola ethempelini, ehlezi phakathi." 
Luke2:47 Njalo bonke ababemuzwa. 
Luke2:48 Kwathi bembona bamangala. 
Luke2:49 Wasesithi kubo: Ku ngani lingidinga? Belingakwazi yini ukuthi kumele ukuthi ngibe sezintweni zikaBaba? 
Luke2:50 Kodwa bona kabaliqedisisanga ilizwi alikhuluma kibo. 
Luke2:51 Wasesehla labo, weza eNazaretha." 
Luke2:52 UJesu waseqhubeka enhlakanipheni. 
Luke3:1 Kwathi ngomnyaka wetshumi lanhlanu wokubusa kukaTiberiyosi uKesari," 
Luke3:2 uAnasi. 
Luke3:3 Wasesiza esigabeni sonke seJodani esizingelezeleyo, etshumayela ubhabhathizo lokuphenduka kube yikuthethelelwa kwezono;" 
Luke3:4 njengokulotshiweyo egwalweni lwamazwi kaIsaya umprofethi, ukuthi: Ilizwi lomemezayo enkangala lithi: Lungisani indlela yeNkosi; qondisani indledlana zayo." 
Luke3:5 Sonke isigodi sizagqitshwa, layo yonke intaba loqaqa kuzakwehliswa; njalo kuzaqondiswa amazombazombe, lamaxhakaxhaka ezindlela azalungiswa;" 
Luke3:6 layo yonke inyama. 
Luke3:7 Ngakho wathi emaxukwini aphumela ukubhabhathizwa nguye: Nzalo yezinyoka, ngubani olixwayise ukubalekela ulaka oluzayo?" 
Luke3:8 Ngakho thelani izithelo ezifanele ukuphenduka; njalo lingaqali ukuthi phakathi kwenu. 
Luke3:9 Lakhathesi lehloka selibekiwe empandeni zezihlahla; ngakho sonke isihlahla esingatheli isithelo esihle siyaganyulwa siphoselwe emlilweni. 
Luke3:10 Amaxuku asembuza, athi: Pho thina sizakwenzani?" 
Luke3:11 Wasephendula wathi kubo: Olezembatho ezimbili, kamuphe ongelaso; lolokudla kenze njalo." 
Luke3:12 Kwasekufika labathelisi ukuze babhabhathizwe? 
Luke3:13 Wasesithi kubo: Lingabizi okwedlula elikumiselweyo. 
Luke3:14 Lamabutho lawo ambuza, athi: Thina-ke sizakwenzani." 
Luke3:15 Kwathi abantu belindile, futhi bonke bezibuza enhliziyweni zabo ngoJohane, ukuthi kambe yena angaba enguKristu," 
Luke3:16 uJohane waphendula, esithi kubo bonke: Mina-ke ngilibhabhathiza ngamanzi; kodwa uyeza olamandla kulami, engingafanele ukuthukulula umchilo wamanyathela akhe; yena uzalibhabhathiza ngoMoya oNgcwele langomlilo;" 
Luke3:17 okhomane lwakhe lokwela lusesandleni sakhe, njalo uzahlambululisisa isibuya sakhe, abesebuthela amabele esiphaleni sakhe, kodwa amakhoba uzawatshisa ngomlilo ongacitshekiyo." 
Luke3:18 Langokulaya ngezinye izinto ezinengi, watshumayela ivangeli ebantwini." 
Luke3:19 Kodwa, langakho konke okubi ayekwenzile uHerodi," 
Luke3:20 wengezelela lalokhu phezu kwakho konke, ukuthi wamvalela uJohane entolongweni." 
Luke3:21 Kwasekusithi sebebhabhathiziwe bonke abantu, laye uJesu esebhabhathiziwe, izulu lavulwa," 
Luke3:22 uMoya oyiNgcwele wasesehlela phezu kwakhe elesimo somzimba onjengowejuba, lelizwi lavela ezulwini, lisithi: Wena uyiNdodana yami ethandekayo, ngithokoza ngawe." 
Luke3:23 Yena uJesu waseqala ukuba leminyaka engaba ngamatshumi amathathu, kaEli," 
Luke3:24 kaMathati, kaLevi, kaMeliki, kaJanayi, kaJosefa," 
Luke3:25 kaMatathiya, kaAmosi, kaNahume, kaEseli, kaNagayi," 
Luke3:26 kaMahati, kaMatathiya, kaSemeyini, kaJosefa, kaJuda," 
Luke3:27 kaJohana, kaResa, kaNeri," 
Luke3:28 kaMeliki, kaAdi, kaKosamu, kaElimodamu, kaEri," 
Luke3:29 kaJose, kaEliyezeri, kaJorima, kaMathati, kaLevi," 
Luke3:30 kaSimeyoni, kaJuda, kaJosefa, kaJonanu, kaEliyakhimi," 
Luke3:31 kaMeleya, kaMena, kaMathata, kaNathani," 
Luke3:32 kaJese, kaObedi, kaBowosi, kaSalimoni, kaNashoni," 
Luke3:33 kaAminadaba, kaAramu, kaEsiromu, kaFaresi, kaJuda," 
Luke3:34 kaJakobe, kaIsaka, kaAbrahama, kaThara, kaNahori," 
Luke3:35 kaSarugi, kaRagawu, kaFaleki, kaEberi, kaSala," 
Luke3:36 kaKayinani, kaArpakishadi, kaShemu, kaNowe, kaLameki," 
Luke3:37 kaMethusala, kaEnoki, kaJaredi, kaMaleleyeli, kaKayinani," 
Luke3:38 kaEnosi, kaSeti, kaAdamu." 
Luke4:1 Kwathi uJesu egcwele uMoya oNgcwele," 
Luke4:2 walingwa ngudiyabhola insuku ezingamatshumi amane. Njalo kadlanga lutho ngalezonsuku; kwathi seziphelile, ekucineni walamba." 
Luke4:3 Udiyabhola wasesithi kuye: Uba uyiNdodana kaNkulunkulu, tshono kulelilitshe ukuthi libe yisinkwa." 
Luke4:4 UJesu wasemphendula, wathi: Kulotshiwe, ukuthi umuntu kayikuphila ngesinkwa sodwa, kodwa ngalo lonke ilizwi likaNkulunkulu." 
Luke4:5 Udiyabhola wasemkhokhelela entabeni ende. 
Luke4:6 Udiyabhola wasesithi kuye: Amandla wonke la lobukhosi bayo ngizakunika. 
Luke4:7 Ngakho wena uba ukhonza phambi kwami, konke kuzakuba ngokwakho." 
Luke4:8 UJesu wasemphendula wathi: Suka ngemva kwami, Sathane; ngoba kulotshiwe ukuthi: Uzakhothamela eNkosini uNkulunkulu wakho, njalo umkhonze yena yedwa." 
Luke4:9 Wasemkhokhelela eJerusalema, wammisa engqongeni yethempeli, wasesithi kuye: Uba uyiNdodana kaNkulunkulu, ziwisele phansi usuka lapha;" 
Luke4:10 ngoba kulotshiwe ukuthi: Uzalaya ingilosi zakhe ngawe, ukukulondoloza;" 
Luke4:11 lokuthi: Zizakuphatha ngezandla, hlezi loba nini ukhube unyawo lwakho elitsheni." 
Luke4:12 UJesu wasephendula wathi kuye: Kuthiwa: Ungayilingi iNkosi uNkulunkulu wakho. 
Luke4:13 Udiyabhola eseqedile ukulinga konke, wasuka kuye kwaze kwaba ngesinyeisikhathi." 
Luke4:14 UJesu wasebuyela. 
Luke4:15 Yena wasefundisa emasinagogeni abo. 
Luke4:16 Wasefika. 
Luke4:17 Wasenikwa ugwalo lomprofethi uIsaya, wayithola indawo okubhalwe kuyo ukuthi:" 
Luke4:18 UMoya weNkosi uphezu kwami, ngakho ingigcobile ukuthi ngitshumayele ivangeli kubayanga; ingithumile ukusilisa abadabukileyo enhliziyweni; ukumemezela ukukhululwa kwabathunjiweyo," 
Luke4:19 ukumemezela. 
Luke4:20 Waselugoqa ugwalo. 
Luke4:21 Waseqala ukuthi kubo: Lamuhla lumbhalo ugcwalisekile endlebeni zenu. 
Luke4:22 Labo bonke bafakaza ngaye, bamangala ngamazwi omusa aphuma emlonyeni wakhe?" 
Luke4:23 Wasesithi kubo: Isibili lizakutsho kimi lesisaga: Melaphi, zelaphe wena." 
Luke4:24 Wathi-ke: Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Kakho umprofethi. 
Luke4:25 Kodwa ngeqiniso ngithi kini: Abafelokazi abanengi; 
Luke4:26 kodwa uElija kathunyelwanga lakomunye wabo, ngaphandle kweSarepita." 
Luke4:27 Futhi amalephero amanengi. 
Luke4:28 Kwathi bonke ababesesinagogeni bagcwala ulaka, bezizwa lezizinto," 
Luke4:29 basebesukuma, bamkhuphela ngaphandle komuzi, bamqhubela eliweni lentaba umuzi wabo owawakhiwe phezu kwayo, ukuze bamphosele phansi eliweni." 
Luke4:30 Kodwa yena edabula phakathi kwabo wahamba. 
Luke4:31 Wasesehlela eKapenawume umuzi weGalili; njalo wayebafundisa ngamasabatha. 
Luke4:32 Basebebabaza ngemfundiso yakhe. 
Luke4:33 Futhi kwakukhona esinagogeni umuntu owayelomoya wedimoni ongcolileyo, wasememeza ngelizwi elikhulu" 
Luke4:34 wathi: Yekela! Silani lawe, Jesu mNazaretha? Uze ukusibhubhisa yini? Ngiyakwazi wena ukuthi ungubani: ONgcwele kaNkulunkulu." 
Luke4:35 UJesu wasemkhuza, esithi: Thula, uphume kuye! Ledimoni selimwisele phakathi laphuma kuye, lingamlimazanga." 
Luke4:36 Kwasekubafikela bonke ukumangala, bakhulumisana, besithi: Yilizwi bani leli, ukuthi ngegunya langamandla uyalaya omoya abangcolileyo, baphume?" 
Luke4:37 Yasiphuma indumela yakhe kuyo yonke indawo yesigaba esizingelezeleyo. 
Luke4:38 Wasesukuma; njalo uninazala kaSimoni wayebanjwe luqhuqho olukhulu; basebemcelela kuye. 
Luke4:39 Wasemengama, wakhuza uqhuqho, khona lwamyekela; njalo wahle wasukuma wabasebenzela." 
Luke4:40 Kwathi ekutshoneni kwelanga, bonke ababelababegula izifo ezitshiyeneyo babaletha kuye." 
Luke4:41 Kwasekuphuma lamadimoni kwabanengi ukuthi akhulume, ngoba ayemazi ukuthi unguKristu." 
Luke4:42 Kwathi sekusile, waphuma waya endaweni eyinkangala." 
Luke4:43 Kodwa wathi kuwo: Ngimele ukutshumayela ivangeli lombuso kaNkulunkulu lakweminye imizi; ngoba ngithunyelwe lokho. 
Luke4:44 Wayesetshumayela emasinagogeni eGalili. 
Luke5:1 Kwasekusithi ixuku selimminyezele ukuzwa ilizwi likaNkulunkulu; 
Luke5:2 wabona imikhumbi emibili imi eceleni kwechibi; kodwa abagoli benhlanzi babephumile kiyo behlambulula amambule. 
Luke5:3 Wasengena komunye wemikhumbi, ongokaSimoni, wamcela ukuthi asuke kancinyane emhlabathini." 
Luke5:4 Kwathi eseqedile ukukhuluma, wathi kuSimoni: Ngena enzikini, lehlise amambule enu ukuze libambe." 
Luke5:5 USimoni wasephendula wathi kuye: Nkosi. 
Luke5:6 Kwathi sebekwenzile lokho, babamba inkithinkithi enkulu yenhlanzi. Laselidabuka imbule labo." 
Luke5:7 Basebeqhweba ababehlanganyele labo. 
Luke5:8 Kuthe uSimoni Petro ebona, wawela emadolweni kaJesu." 
Luke5:9 Ngoba ukumangala kwakumbambile, labo bonke ababelaye, ngokubanjwa kwenhlanzi ababezibambile;" 
Luke5:10 ngokufananayo-ke loJakobe loJohane, amadodana kaZebediya, ababehlanganyele loSimoni. UJesu wasesithi kuSimoni: Ungesabi; kusukela khathesi uzagola abantu." 
Luke5:11 Kwathi sebeyifikisile imikhumbi emhlabathini, batshiya konke, bamlandela." 
Luke5:12 Kwasekusithi, esekomunye wemizi, khangela-ke, indoda egcwele ubulephero; yathi ibona uJesu, yawa ngobuso, yamncenga, isithi: Nkosi, aluba uthanda, ungangihlambulula." 
Luke5:13 Waseselula isandla, wayithinta, esithi: Ngiyathanda, hlambuluka. Njalo bahle basuka ubulephero kuyo." 
Luke5:14 Yena waseyilaya ukuthi ingatsheli muntu; wathi: Kodwa hamba uziveze kumpristi, unikelele ukuhlanjululwa kwakho, njengoba uMozisi walaya, kube yibufakazi kubo." 
Luke5:15 Kodwa kwayilapho ukukhuluma ngaye kwanda kakhulu; lamaxuku amanengi abuthana ukulalela, lokusiliswa nguye ezifweni zawo." 
Luke5:16 Kodwa yena waphumela enkangala. 
Luke5:17 Kwasekusithi ngolunye lwezinsuku, yena wayefundisa; njalo kwakuhlezi abaFarisi labafundisi bomlayo, abavela kuyo yonke imizana yeGalili leJudiya leJerusalema; lamandla eNkosi aye khonaukubasilisa." 
Luke5:18 Njalo khangela, amadoda ethwele ngohlaka umuntu owayeyisigoga; njalo adinga ukumngenisa a m beke phambi kwakhe;" 
Luke5:19 kodwa engatholi indlela yokumngenisa ngenxa yexuku. 
Luke5:20 Kwathi ebona ukholo lwawo, wathi kuye: Ndoda, izono zakho uzithethelelwe." 
Luke5:21 Ababhali labaFarisi basebeqala ukunakana, besithi: Ungubani lo okhuluma inhlamba?" 
Luke5:22 Kwathi uJesu esazi ukunakana kwabo waphendula wathi kubo: Linakanani enhliziyweni zenu? 
Luke5:23 Yikuphi okulula, ukuthi: Izono zakho uzithethelelwe; kumbe ukuthi: Sukuma uhambe?" 
Luke5:24 Kodwa ukuze lazi ukuthi iNdodana yomuntu ilamandla okuthethelela izono emhlabeni (wathi koyisigoga): Ngithi kuwe: Sukuma, uthathe ithala lakho, uye endlini yakho." 
Luke5:25 Njalo wahle wasukuma phambi kwabo, wathatha lokhu ayelele kukho, wasuka waya endlini yakhe." 
Luke5:26 Lokusanganiseka kwababamba bonke, basebedumisa uNkulunkulu, besithi: Sibone izimanga lamuhla." 
Luke5:27 Njalo emva kwalezizinto waphuma, wabona umthelisi, uLevi ngebizo, ehlezi endlini yokuthelisela, wathi kuye: Ngilandela." 
Luke5:28 Wasetshiya konke, wasukuma wamlandela." 
Luke5:29 ULevi wasemenzela. 
Luke5:30 Ababhali babo labaFarisi basebesola kubafundi bakhe, besithi: Kungani lisidla linatha labathelisi lezoni?" 
Luke5:31 UJesu wasephendula wathi kubo: Abaphilayo kabasweli melaphi, kodwa abagulayo." 
Luke5:32 Kangizanga ukubiza abalungileyo, kodwa izoni zize ekuphendukeni." 
Luke5:33 Basebesithi; kodwa abakho bayadla banathe? 
Luke5:34 Kodwa wathi kubo: Kambe, lingabazilisa ukudla yini abantwana bendlu yomthimba, umyeni eselabo?" 
Luke5:35 Kodwa zizafika insuku, lapho umyeni ezasuswa kubo, khona bezazila ukudla ngalezonsuku." 
Luke5:36 Wasebatshela futhi umfanekiso wokuthi: Kakho obekela isichibi sesembatho esitsha esembathweni esidala; uba kungenjalo, esitsha laso siyadabula, lesichibi sesitsha asihambelani lesidala." 
Luke5:37 Futhi kakho ofaka iwayini elitsha emigodleni emidala; uba-ke kungenjalo, iwayini elitsha lizadabula imigodla, lichitheke lona, lemigodla yonakale." 
Luke5:38 Kodwa iwayini elitsha limele lifakwe emigodleni emitsha, njalo kokubili kulondolozeke." 
Luke5:39 Njalo kakho othi esenathe iwayinielidala ahle afise elitsha; ngoba uthi: Elidala lingcono. 
Luke6:1 Kwasekusithi, abafundi bakhe bakha izikhwebu, badla, be zi hlikihla ngezandla." 
Luke6:2 Kodwa abathile babaFarisi bathi kubo: Lenzelani okungavunyelwa ukwenziwa ngensuku zesabatha? 
Luke6:3 UJesu wasebaphendula, wathi: Alifundanga lalokho yini, uDavida akwenzayo, mhla elambile yena lababelaye," 
Luke6:4 ukuthi wayangena njani endlini kaNkulunkulu, wathatha izinkwa zokubukiswa, wasesidla, wanika lalabo ababelaye; ezingavunyelwa ukudliwa ngaphandle kwabapristi bodwa?" 
Luke6:5 Wasesithi kubo: INdodana yomuntu iyiNkosi leyesabatha. 
Luke6:6 Kwasekusithi langelinye isabatha wangena esinagogeni, wafundisa." 
Luke6:7 Ababhali labaFarisi basebemqaphela, ukuthi uzasilisa ngesabatha yini; ukuze bathole oko kumbeka icala." 
Luke6:8 Kodwa wayazi imicabango yabo, wathi kumuntu olesandla esitshwabheneyo: Sukuma, ume phakathi. Wasukuma-ke wema." 
Luke6:9 UJesu wasesithi kubo: Ngizalibuza ulutho: Kuvunyelwe yini ngamasabatha ukwenza okulungileyo kumbe ukwenza okubi? Ukusindisa impilo kumbe ukuchitha? 
Luke6:10 Wasebathalaza bonke, wathi kumuntu: Yelula isandla sakho. Wasesenza njalo. Isandla sakhe sasesisiliswa saphila njengesinye." 
Luke6:11 Basebegcwala ubuhlanya. 
Luke6:12 Kwasekusithi ngalezonsuku waphuma waya entabeni ukuyakhuleka. 
Luke6:13 Kwathi sekusile, wabizela kuye abafundi bakhe;" 
Luke6:14 uSimoni laye ambiza ngokuthi nguPetro, loAndreya umfowabo, uJakobe loJohane, uFiliphu loBartolomewu," 
Luke6:15 uMathewu loTomasi, uJakobe okaAlfewu, loSimoni owayethiwa ngumZelothi," 
Luke6:16 uJudasi. 
Luke6:17 Wasesehla labo, wema esigcawini, lexuku labafundi bakhe, ababezile ukumuzwa, lokusiliswa ezifweni zabo;" 
Luke6:18 lalabo ababekhathazwa ngomoya abangcolileyo, basebesiliswa." 
Luke6:19 Lexuku lonke ladinga ukumthinta. 
Luke6:20 Yena wasephakamisela amehlo akhe kubafundi bakhe wathi: Libusisiwe, bayanga, ngoba umbuso kaNkulunkulu ungowenu." 
Luke6:21 Libusisiwe, lina elilambileyo khathesi, ngoba lizasuthiswa. Libusisiwe, lina elikhalayo khathesi, ngoba lizahleka." 
Luke6:22 Libusisiwe, nxa abantu belizonda, njalo nxa belehlukanisa, belithuka, belahla ibizo lenu ngokungathi libi, ngenxa yeNdodana yomuntu." 
Luke6:23 Thokozani ngalolosuku leqe ngokuthokoza; ngoba khangelani, umvuzo wenu mkhulu ezulwini; ngoba oyise benza njalo kubaprofethi." 
Luke6:24 Kodwa maye kini. 
Luke6:25 Maye kini, lina elisuthiyo! Ngoba lizalamba." 
Luke6:26 Maye kini, nxa abantu bonke bekhuluma kuhle ngani." 
Luke6:27 Kodwa ngithi kini elizwayo: Thandani izitha zenu, lenze okuhle kwabalizondayo," 
Luke6:28 libusise abaliqalekisayo, libakhulekele abaliphatha kubi." 
Luke6:29 Okutshaya esihlathini, mnike lesinye; lokwemuka isembatho sakho, ungali lesigqoko sakho." 
Luke6:30 Kodwa mnike wonke ocela kuwe; lokwemuka okwakho, ungabuyi u ku bize kuye." 
Luke6:31 Njalo njengalokho lithanda ukuthi abantu benze kini, lani yenzani njalo kubo." 
Luke6:32 Njalo uba lithanda labo abalithandayo. 
Luke6:33 Njalo uba lisenza okuhle kulabo abenza okuhle kini, yikubongwa bani elilakho? Ngoba lezoni zenza okufananayo." 
Luke6:34 Futhi uba liseboleka labo elithemba ukwemukela kubo, yikubongwa bani elilakho? Ngoba lezoni zeboleka izoni, ukuze zemukele izinto ezifananayo." 
Luke6:35 Kodwa thandani izitha zenu. 
Luke6:36 Ngakho banini lesihawu. 
Luke6:37 Lingahluleli, njalo alisoze lahlulelwe;" 
Luke6:38 phanini, lani lizaphiwa. Ngoba ngalesosilinganiso elilinganisa ngaso lizalinganiselwa ngaso futhi." 
Luke6:39 Wasebatshela umfanekiso wokuthi: Kambe isiphofu singakhokhela isiphofu yini? Kabayikuwela bobabili emgodini yini? 
Luke6:40 Umfundi kamkhulu kulomfundisi wakhe. 
Luke6:41 Njalo ukhangelelani ucezwana oluselihlweni lomfowenu, kodwa ungalunanzeleli ugodo olukwelakho ilihlo?" 
Luke6:42 Kumbe ungatsho njani kumfowenu ukuthi: Mfowethu, kahle ngikhuphe ucezwana oluselihlweni lakho, wena ungaluboni ugodo oluselihlweni lakho? Mzenzisi, qala ukhuphe ugodo elihlweni lakho, khona-ke uzabona kuhle ukukhupha ucezwana oluselihlweni lomfowenu." 
Luke6:43 Ngoba kayisiso isihlahla esihle esithela isithelo esibi; futhi kayisiso isihlahla esibi esithela isithelo esihle. 
Luke6:44 Ngoba yileso laleso isihlahla saziwa ngesaso isithelo. Ngoba kabaseli imikhiwa emeveni, futhi kakukhiwa isithelo sevini evikaneni." 
Luke6:45 Umuntu olungileyo uveza okulungileyo kokuligugu elilungileyo lenhliziyo yakhe, lomuntu omubi uveza okubi kokuligugu elibi lenhliziyo yakhe." 
Luke6:46 Kodwa lingibizelani ngokuthi: Nkosi, Nkosi, kodwa lingazenzi izinto engizitshoyo?" 
Luke6:47 Wonke oza kimi awezwe amazwi ami njalo awenze, ngizalitshengisa ukuthi ufanana lobani;" 
Luke6:48 ufanana lomuntu owakha indlu, wagebha watshonisa, wabeka isisekelo phezu kwedwala; kwathi ekufikeni kwempophoma, umfula watshaya kuleyondlu, kodwa wawungelamandla okuyinyikinya; ngoba yayisekelwe phezu kwedwala." 
Luke6:49 Kodwa owezwayo njalo angawenzi unjengomuntu owakha indlu emhlabathini ingelasisekelo. 
Luke7:1 Kwathi eseqedile amazwi akhe wonke endlebeni zabantu, wangena eKapenawume." 
Luke7:2 Njalo inceku yenduna yekhulu ethile, eyayiligugu kuyo, yayigula isizakufa." 
Luke7:3 Kwathi isizwile ngoJesu, yathuma kuye abadala bamaJuda." 
Luke7:4 Kwathi bona, sebefikile kuJesu, bamncenga kakhulu, besithi: Yona kufanele ukuthi uyenzele lokhu;" 
Luke7:5 ngoba iyasithanda isizwe sakithi, njalo yiyo eyasakhela isinagoge." 
Luke7:6 UJesu wasehamba labo. Kwathi engasekhatshana lendlu, induna yekhulu yathuma abangane kuye, isithi kuye: Nkosi, ungazikhathazi; ngoba kangifanele ukuthi ungene ngaphansi kophahla lwami;" 
Luke7:7 yikho kangizibonanga ngifanele ukuza kuwe; kodwa khuluma ngelizwi, njalo inceku yami izasiliswa." 
Luke7:8 Ngoba lami ngingumuntu obekwe ngaphansi kwamandla, ngilamabutho ngaphansi kwami, njalo ngithi kuleli: Hamba, njalo lihambe; lakwelinye: Woza, njalo lize; lencekwini yami: Yenza lokhu, njalo ikwenze." 
Luke7:9 Kwathi uJesu ezizwa lezizinto wamangala ngayo, watshibilika, wathi exukwini elimlandelayo: Ngithi kini, angitholanga ukholo olungaka ngitsho lakoIsrayeli." 
Luke7:10 Kwathi ababethunyiwe sebebuyele endlini bafica inceku eyayigula isisilile. 
Luke7:11 Kwasekusithi nge langaelilandelayo, waya emzini othiwa yiNayini; abafundi bakhe abanengi basebehamba laye, lexuku elikhulu." 
Luke7:12 Kwathi esesondela esangweni lomuzi, njalo khangela, kwakulofileyo ethwelwe kuphunywa, indodana engeyodwa kanina, futhi yena engumfelokazi; lexuku elikhulu lomuzi lalilaye." 
Luke7:13 INkosi imbona, yasisiba lesihelo ngaye, yathi kuye: Ungakhali." 
Luke7:14 Yasondela yathinta ithala; aba li thweleyo basebesima! 
Luke7:15 Ofileyo wasevuka wahlala waqala ukukhuluma. Yasimnika unina. 
Luke7:16 Ukwesaba kwasekubabamba bonke. 
Luke7:17 Le indumela ngaye yasiphumela kuyo yonke iJudiya, lakuso sonke isigaba esizingelezeleyo." 
Luke7:18 Abafundi bakaJohane basebembikela ngazo zonke lezizinto. 
Luke7:19 UJohane wasebizela kuye ababili abathile kubafundi bakhe wa ba thuma kuJesu, esithi: Wena unguye ozayo yini, kumbe silindele omunye?" 
Luke7:20 Lamadoda esefikile kuye athi: UJohane uMbhabhathizi usithumile kuwe, esithi: Wena unguye ozayo yini, kumbe silindele omunye?" 
Luke7:21 Langalelohola wasilisa abanengi ezifweni lemikhuhlaneni lakubomoya ababi. 
Luke7:22 UJesu wasephendula wathi kubo: Hambani limtshele uJohane izinto elizibonileyo lelizizwileyo: Ukuthi iziphofu zibuye zibone, iziqhuli ziyahamba, amalephero ayahlanjululwa, izacuthe ziyezwa, abafileyo bayavuswa, abayanga bayatshunyayezwa ivangeli;" 
Luke7:23 njalo ubusisiwe loba ngubani ongakhubekiyo ngami. 
Luke7:24 Kwathi sezihambile izithunywa zikaJohane, waqala ukukhuluma lamaxuku ngoJohane esithi: Laphuma laya enkangala ukuyabonani? Umhlanga onyikinywa ngumoya yini?" 
Luke7:25 Kanti laphumela ukuyabonani? Umuntu owembethe izembatho ezicolekileyo yini? Khangelani, abe mbetheezikhazimulayo baphila mnandi basezindlini zamakhosi." 
Luke7:26 Pho laphumela ukuyabonani? Umprofethi yini? Yebo, ngithi kini: Loba odlula kakhulu umprofethi." 
Luke7:27 Lo nguye okubhalwe ngaye ukuthi: Khangela, mina ngiyathuma isithunywa sami phambi kobuso bakho, esizalungisa indlela yakho phambi kwakho." 
Luke7:28 Ngoba ngithi kini: Phakathi kwabazelwe ngabesifazana kakho umprofethi omkhulu kuloJohane uMbhabhathizi; kodwa omncinyane embusweni kaNkulunkulu mkhulu kulaye. 
Luke7:29 Labantu bonke bekuzwa, labathelisi, bathi ulungile uNkulunkulu;" 
Luke7:30 kodwa abaFarisi lezazumthetho bemelene labo, ngoba bengabhabhathizwanga nguye." 
Luke7:31 Yasisithi iNkosi: Pho-ke abantu balesisizukulwana ngizabafananisa lani? Kanti bafanana lani? 
Luke7:32 Banjengabantwana abancane abahlezi emakethe bememezana besithi: Silitshayele umhlanga, kodwa kalisinanga; silililele, kodwa kalikhalanga." 
Luke7:33 Ngoba uJohane uMbhabhathizi wafika engadli isinkwa njalo enganathi iwayini, laselisithi: Uledimoni;" 
Luke7:34 iNdodana yomuntu ifikile isidla, inatha, laselisithi: Khangelani, umuntu oligovu lesinathi sewayini, umngane wabathelisi lezoni." 
Luke7:35 Kodwa inhlakanipho ithiwa ilungile ngabantwana bayo bonke. 
Luke7:36 Omunye wabaFarisi wasemcela ukuthi adle laye; esengenile endlini yomFarisi wahlala ekudleni. 
Luke7:37 Njalo khangela, owesifazana kulowomuzi, owayeyisoni, esekwazi ukuthi uJesu uhlezi ekudleni endlini yomFarisi, waletha umfuma we-alibasta owamagcobo," 
Luke7:38 wasesima eceleni kwenyawo zakhe ngemva kwakheekhala, waqala ukuthambisa inyawo zakhe ngenyembezi, wa ze sula ngenwele zekhanda lakhe, wanga inyawo zakhe, wa zi gcoba ngamagcobo." 
Luke7:39 Kuthe umFarisi obemnxusile e ku bona wakhulumela ngaphakathi kwakhe wathi: Lo, ngabe uyamazi ukuthi ungubani lokuthi unjani lo owesifazana omthintayo, ngoba uyisoni." 
Luke7:40 UJesu wasephendula wathi kuye: Simoni, ngilengizakukhuluma lawe. Yena wasesithi: Khuluma, Mfundisi." 
Luke7:41 Kwakukhona ababili ababelezikwelede kumkweledisi othile; omunye wayelomlandu wabodenariyo abangamakhulu amahlanu, lomunye abangamatshumi amahlanu." 
Luke7:42 Kwathi bengelakho okokuhlawula ngakho, wabaxolela bobabili. Kambe nguwuphi kubo, tshono, ozamthanda okwedlulisileyo?" 
Luke7:43 USimoni wasephendula wathi: Ngicabanga ngulowo amxolela okwedlulisileyo. Wathi kuye: Wahlulele ngokuqonda. 
Luke7:44 Wasetshibilikela kowesifazana, wathi kuSimoni: Uyambona lo owesifazana yini? Ngingene endlini yakho, amanzi enyaweni zami kawu ngi nikanga." 
Luke7:45 Kawunganganga; kodwa yena, lokhu ngingenile, kayekelanga ukwanga inyawo zami." 
Luke7:46 Ngamagcobo ikhanda lami kawuligcobanga; kodwa yena ugcobile inyawo zami ngamakha. 
Luke7:47 Ngenxa yalokhu, ngithi kuwe: Izono zakhe ezinengi zithethelelwe, ngoba uthandile kakhulu; kodwa lowo othethelelwa kancinyane, uthanda kancinyane." 
Luke7:48 Wasesithi kuye: Zithethelelwe izono zakho. 
Luke7:49 Ababehlezi laye ekudleni basebeqala ukukhulumisana bodwa besithi: Ngubani lo othethelela lezono? 
Luke7:50 Wasesithi kowesifazana: Ukholo. 
Luke8:1 Kwasekusithi emva kwalokho, yena wadabula imizi lemizana, ememezela lokutshumayela indaba ezinhle zombuso kaNkulunkulu; labalitshumi lambili babelaye," 
Luke8:2 labesifazana abathile ababesiliswe kubomoya ababi lemikhuhlaneni," 
Luke8:3 loJowana umkaKuza. 
Luke8:4 Kwathi sekubuthene ixuku elikhulu, njalo bevela emizini ngemizi besiza kuye, wakhuluma ngomfanekiso" 
Luke8:5 wathi: Umhlanyeli waphuma ukuyahlanyela inhlanyelo yakhe; kwathi ekuhlanyeleni kwakhe, enye yawela eceleni kwendlela; yasinyathelwa ngenyawo, lenyoni zezulu zayidla zayiqeda." 
Luke8:6 Lenye yawela edwaleni, kwathi ekukhuleni yabuna, ngoba yaswela ubumanzi." 
Luke8:7 Lenye yawela phakathi kwameva, ameva asemila layo ayiminyanisa." 
Luke8:8 Lenye yawela emhlabathini omuhle, yakhula yathela ikhulu. Esetshilo lezizinto wamemeza wathi: Olendlebe zokuzwa akezwe." 
Luke8:9 Abafundi bakhe basebembuza besithi: Ungaba yini lumfanekiso? 
Luke8:10 Wasesithi: Kuphiwe kini ukwazi imfihlo zombuso kaNkulunkulu; kodwa kwabanye ngemifanekiso, ukuze bebona bangaboni, njalo besizwa bangaqedisisi." 
Luke8:11 Lomfanekiso uyilokhu: Inhlanyelo iyilizwi likaNkulunkulu. 
Luke8:12 Labaseceleni kwendlela yilabo abathi sebezwile, besekufika udiyabhola alisuse ilizwi enhliziyweni zabo, ukuze bangakholwa basindiswe." 
Luke8:13 Labasedwaleni yilabo, abathi belizwile, balemukele ilizwi ngentokozo, kodwa laba kabalampande, abakholwa okwesikhathi, kuthi ngesikhathi sokulingwa bawe." 
Luke8:14 Lewele phakathi kwameva, yilabo abathi sebezwile, bahambe baminyaniswe yikukhathalela lenotho lenkanuko yempilo, njalo bangatheli izithelo ezivuthiweyo." 
Luke8:15 Kodwa esemhlabathini omuhle, yilabo abathi belizwile ilizwi ba li londoloze enhliziyweni enhle lelungileyo, bathela izithelo ngokubekezela." 
Luke8:16 Njalo kakho othi eselumathise isibane, kumbe asibeke ngaphansi kombheda, kodwa usibeka esiqobaneni sesibane, ukuze abangenayo babone ukukhanya." 
Luke8:17 Ngoba kakukho okufihliweyo, okungasoze kube sobala; lokuthukuziweyo, okungayikwaziwa lokungayikulethwa obala." 
Luke8:18 Ngakho qaphelisani ukuthi lizwa njani. 
Luke8:19 Kwasekufika kuye unina labafowabo, kodwa abazange bamfinyelele ngenxa yexuku." 
Luke8:20 Wasebikelwa ngabanyeabathi: Unyoko labafowenu bemi phandle, bafuna ukukubona." 
Luke8:21 Kodwa waphendula wathi kubo: Umama labafowethu yilabo, abalizwayo ilizwi likaNkulunkulu balenze." 
Luke8:22 Kwasekusithi ngolunye lwezinsuku, wangena emkhunjini yena labafundi bakhe; basuka-ke." 
Luke8:23 Kwathi behamba ngomkhumbi, walala ubuthongo; isiphepho esikhulu somoya sasesisehlela phansi echibini." 
Luke8:24 Basebesondela bamvusa, besithi: Nkosi, nkosi, siyabhubha." 
Luke8:25 Wasesithi kubo: Lungaphi ukholo lwenu? Basebesesaba bamangala, bakhulumisana besithi: Kambe ungubani lo, ukuthi alaye ngitsho imimoya lamanzi, njalo kumlalele?" 
Luke8:26 Basebesiya ngomkhumbi elizweni lamaGadarene, eliqondene leGalili." 
Luke8:27 Kwathi esephumele emhlabathini, yamhlangabeza indoda ethile ivela emzini, njalo ingembathi isembatho, ingahlali endlini, kodwa emangcwabeni." 
Luke8:28 Yathi imbona uJesu, yamemeza, yawa phansi phambi kwakhe, yathi ngelizwi elikhulu: Ngilani lawe, Jesu, Ndodana kaNkulunkulu oPhezukonke? Ngiyakuncenga, ungangihluphi." 
Luke8:29 Ngoba walaya umoya ongcolileyo ukuthi aphume ku lowo muntu; ngoba wayesembambe okwezikhathi ezinengi, walindwa ebotshiwe ngamaketane lezibopho, kodwa eseqamule izibopho waqhutshelwa enkangala lidimoni." 
Luke8:30 UJesu wasembuza, wathi: Ungubani ibizo lakho? Wasesithi: NguLegiyoni; ngoba amadimoni amanengi ayengene kuye." 
Luke8:31 Asemncenga ukuthi angawalayi ukuya emgodini ongelamkhawulo. 
Luke8:32 Kwakukhona lapho umhlambi wengulube ezinengi usidla entabeni; asemncenga ukuthi awavumele angene kuzo. Wasewavumela. 
Luke8:33 Kwathi amadimoni esephumile kulowomuntu angena engulubeni; umhlambi wasuphaphatheka usuka eliweni usiya echibini, waminzwa." 
Luke8:34 Kwathi ababe z elusile bebona okwenzakeleyo babaleka, basuka bayabika emzini, lemaphandleni." 
Luke8:35 Basebephuma ukuyabona okwenzakeleyo; bafika kuJesu, bamfica umuntu okwakuphume kuye amadimoni; basebesesaba." 
Luke8:36 Basebebatshela lalabo ababebonile ukuthi usindiswe njani owayengenwe ngamadimoni. 
Luke8:37 Ixuku lonke lesigaba samaGadarene waphindela emuva. 
Luke8:38 Kodwa indoda. Kodwa uJesu wayiyekela yahamba, esithi:" 
Luke8:39 Buyela endlini yakho, ulandise ukuthi kungakanani uNkulunkulu akwenze kuwe. Wasesuka wahamba, etshumayela phakathi komuzi wonke ukuthi kungakanani uJesu ayekwenzile kuye." 
Luke8:40 Kwasekusithi ekubuyeni kukaJesu. 
Luke8:41 Njalo khangela, kwafika indoda, uJayirosi ngebizo, yona ingumphathi wesinagoge, yasisiwa phansi enyaweni zikaJesu yamncenga ukuthi angene endlini yayo;" 
Luke8:42 ngoba yayilendodakazi eyodwa ezelweyo eyayingaba leminyaka elitshumi lambili, njalo yona yayisisifa. Kwathi esahamba amaxuku amcindezela." 
Luke8:43 Lowesifazana owayelomopho wegazi okweminyaka elitshumi lambili, echithe konke okwempilo yakhe kubelaphi engelakusiliswa langubani," 
Luke8:44 wasondela ngemva kwakhe, wathinta umphetho wesembatho sakhe; njalo wahle wakhawula umopho wegazi lakhe." 
Luke8:45 UJesu wasesithi: Ngubani ongithintileyo? Kwathi lapho bephika bonke, uPetro wathi lababelaye: Nkosi, ixuku likuminyanisile li ku cindezele, kodwa uthi: Ngubani ongithintileyo?" 
Luke8:46 Kodwa uJesu wathi: Ukhona ongithintileyo; ngoba mina ngazile ukuthi amandla aphumile kimi. 
Luke8:47 Kwathi owesifazana ebona ukuthi kafihlakalanga, weza ethuthumela, wawa phambi kwakhe, walandisa phambi kwabantu bonke ukuthi umthinte ngesizatho bani, lokuthi uhle wasila njani." 
Luke8:48 Wasesithi kuye: Mana isibindi, ndodakazi, ukholo lwakho lukusindisile." 
Luke8:49 Esakhuluma, kwafika umuntu evela endliniyomphathi wesinagoge, wathi kuye: Indodakazi yakho isifile; ungamhluphi uMfundisi." 
Luke8:50 Kodwa uJesu esizwa, wamphendula, wathi: Ungesabi; kholwa kuphela, njalo izasindiswa." 
Luke8:51 Futhi esengenile endlini, kavumanga ukuthi kungene muntu, ngaphandle kukaPetro loJakobe loJohane, loyise wendodakazi lonina." 
Luke8:52 Njalo bakhala bonke, beyililela. Kodwa wathi: Lingakhali; kayifanga, kodwa ilele." 
Luke8:53 Basebemhleka usulu, besazi ukuthi ifile." 
Luke8:54 Kodwa yena esebakhuphele phandle bonke, wabamba isandla sayo, wamemeza, esithi: Ndodakazi, vuka!" 
Luke8:55 Wasubuya umoya wayo, yasivuka khona lapho; waselaya ukuthi kayiphiwe ukudla." 
Luke8:56 Abazali bayo basebemangala kakhulu. 
Luke9:1 Wasebizela ndawonye abafundi bakhe abalitshumi lambili. 
Luke9:2 Wasebathuma uku ya tshumayela umbuso kaNkulunkulu, lokusilisa abagulayo," 
Luke9:3 wasesithi kubo: Lingaphathi lutho lwendlela; lodondolo, lesikhwama, lomphako, lemali, njalo lingabi lezigqoko ezimbili ngamunye." 
Luke9:4 Lakuyiphi indlu elingena kuyo, hlalani lapho, lalapho lisuke." 
Luke9:5 Labo bonke abangalemukeliyo, nxa lisuka kulowomuzi, thintithani ngitsho uthuli enyaweni zenu kube yibufakazi obumelana labo." 
Luke9:6 Basuka-ke bahamba bedabula imizana, betshumayela ivangeli besilisa endaweni zonke." 
Luke9:7 UHerodi umtetrarki, ngoba kwatshiwo ngabanye ukuthi uJohane uvukile kwabafileyo;" 
Luke9:8 langabanye ukuthi uElija ubonakele; langabanye ukuthi kuvukile omunye wabaprofethi abadala. 
Luke9:9 Kodwa uHerodi wathi: UJohane ngamquma ikhanda mina; kodwa ngubani lo, mina engizwa ngaye izinto ezinje? Wasefunisisa ukumbona." 
Luke9:10 Abaphostoli. 
Luke9:11 Kwathi amaxuku esekwazi, amlandela; wasewemukela, wakhuluma lawo ngombuso kaNkulunkulu." 
Luke9:12 Ilanga laseliqala ukutshona; ngoba lapha sisendaweni eyinkangala. 
Luke9:13 Kodwa wathi kubo: Banikeni lina bona ukuthi badle. Bathi-ke: Asilakho okwedlula izinkwa ezinhlanu lenhlanzi ezimbili, ngaphandle kokuthi thina siyebathengela ukudla bonke lababantu." 
Luke9:14 Ngoba kwakukhona amadoda angaba zinkulungwane ezinhlanu. Wasesithi kubafundi bakhe: Bahlaliseni phansi ngezigaba ngamatshumi amahlanu. 
Luke9:15 Basebesenza njalo, babahlalisa phansi bonke." 
Luke9:16 Wasezithatha izinkwa ezinhlanu lenhlanzi ezimbili, wakhangela phezulu ezulwini, wazibusisa, wa zi hlephula, wa zi nika abafundi ukuthi babeke phambi kwexuku." 
Luke9:17 Basebesidla basutha bonke; kwadojwa imvuthu ezazisele kubo, izitsha ezilitshumi lambili." 
Luke9:18 Kwasekusithi ekhuleka yedwa, abafundi babelaye; wasebabuza, esithi: Amaxuku athi ngingubani?" 
Luke9:19 Basebephendula bathi: UJohane uMbhabhathizi; kodwa abanye bathi: UElija; kodwa abanye bathi: Kuvukile umprofethi othile wabadala. 
Luke9:20 Wasesithi kubo: Lina-ke lithi ngingubani? UPetro wasephendula wathi: UKristu kaNkulunkulu. 
Luke9:21 Esebaxwayisisile," 
Luke9:22 esithi. 
Luke9:23 Wasesithi kubo bonke: Uba umuntu ethanda ukuza ngemva kwami, kazidele, athathe isiphambano sakhe." 
Luke9:24 Ngoba loba ngubani othanda ukusindisa impilo yakhe, izamlahlekela; kodwa loba ngubani olahlekelwa yimpilo yakhe ngenxa yami, yena uzayisindisa." 
Luke9:25 Ngoba kuzamsizani umuntu, uba ezuza umhlaba wonke, kodwa yena uqobo lwakhe azone kumbe alahleke?" 
Luke9:26 Ngoba loba ngubani olenhloni ngami langamazwi ami, iNdodana yomuntu izakuba lenhloni ngaye, nxa isiza enkazimulweni yayo lekaBaba leyengilosi ezingcwele." 
Luke9:27 Kodwa ngilitshela ngeqiniso: Bakhona abanye kwabemiyo lapha, abangasoze bezwe ukufa, baze babone umbuso kaNkulunkulu." 
Luke9:28 Kwasekusithi. 
Luke9:29 Kwasekusithi ekukhulekeni kwakhe, isimo sobuso bakhe saphenduka, lesembatho sakhe saba mhlophe, sacwazimula." 
Luke9:30 Njalo khangela, akhuluma laye amadoda amabili, ayengoMozisi loElija;" 
Luke9:31 abonakala ngenkazimulo. 
Luke9:32 Kodwa uPetro lababelaye babesindwe yibuthongo, lamadoda amabili ayemi laye." 
Luke9:33 Kwasekusithi, ekwehlukaneni kwawo laye." 
Luke9:34 Kwathi ekhuluma lezizinto, kwafika iyezi labasibekela; basebesesaba ekungeneni kwabo eyezini." 
Luke9:35 Kwasekuphuma ilizwi eyezini, lisithi: Lo uyiNdodana yami ethandekayo; zwanini yona." 
Luke9:36 Kwathi ilizwi selifikile, uJesu waficwa eyedwa. Kodwa bona bathula, kabaze batshela muntu ngalezonsuku okunye kwalezozinto abazibonileyo." 
Luke9:37 Kwasekusithi ngelanga elilandelayo, sebehlile." 
Luke9:38 Njalo khangela, indoda exukwini yamemeza, isithi: Mfundisi, ngiyakuncenga, bona indodana yami;" 
Luke9:39 njalo khangela, umoya uyayibamba, futhi ihle iklabalale." 
Luke9:40 Njalo ngincenge abafundi bakho ukuthi bawukhuphe, kodwa abenelisanga." 
Luke9:41 UJesu wasephendula wathi: O sizukulwana esingelakholo lesonakeleyo, kuzaze kube nini ngilani, ngilibekezelela? Ilethe lapha indodana yakho." 
Luke9:42 Kuthe iseza, idimoni layidabula la yi hlukuza; kodwa uJesu wawukhuza umoya ongcolileyo, wamsilisa umntwana, wambuyisela kuyise." 
Luke9:43 Bonke basebemangaliswa kakhulu yibukhulu bukaNkulunkulu. Kwathi bemangele bonke ngazo zonke izinto uJesu azenzileyo, wathi kubafundi bakhe:" 
Luke9:44 Fakani lina endlebeni zenu lamazwi: Ngoba iNdodana yomuntu izanikelwa ezandleni zabantu. 
Luke9:45 Kodwa kabaqedisisanga lumutsho, njalo wawufihlakele kubo, ukuze bangawuzwisisi; basebesesaba ukumbuza ngalumutsho." 
Luke9:46 Kwasekungena. 
Luke9:47 Kwathi uJesu ebona ukunakana kwenhliziyo yabo, wathatha umntwana omncane, wammisa phansi kwakhe," 
Luke9:48 wasesithi kubo: Loba ngubani owemukela lumntwana omncane ebizweni lami wemukela mina; njalo loba ngubani owemukela mina wemukela ongithumileyo. 
Luke9:49 UJohane wasephendula wathi: Nkosi, sabona omunye ekhupha amadimoni ngebizo lakho, sasesimenqabela, ngoba engalandeli kanye lathi." 
Luke9:50 Kodwa uJesu wathi kuye: Linga m enqabeli, ngoba ongamelani lathi ungakithi." 
Luke9:51 Kwathi seziphelelisiwe insuku," 
Luke9:52 wasethuma izithunywa phambi kobuso bakhe, ukuze zimlungisele." 
Luke9:53 Kodwa kawamemukelanga. 
Luke9:54 Kwathi abafundi bakhe uJakobe loJohane? 
Luke9:55 Kodwa watshibilika wabakhuza, esithi: Alazi ukuthi lina lingabomoya onjani." 
Luke9:56 Ngoba iNdodana yomuntu kayizanga ukuthi ibhubhise imiphefumulo yabantu, kodwa uku yi sindisa. Basebesedlulela komunye umzana." 
Luke9:57 Kwasekusithi behamba endleleni, umuntuothile wathi kuye: Nkosi, ngizakulandela loba ngaphi lapho oya khona." 
Luke9:58 UJesu wasesithi kuye: Amakhanka alemilindi, lenyoni zezulu zile zidleke; kodwa iNdodana yomuntu kayilalapho engaqamelisa ikhanda khona." 
Luke9:59 Wasesithi komunye: Ngilandela. Kodwa yena wathi: Nkosi, ngivumela ukuthi ngiyengcwaba ubaba kuqala." 
Luke9:60 Kodwa uJesu wathi kuye: Yekela abafileyo bangcwabe ababo abafileyo; kodwa wena hamba utshumayele umbuso kaNkulunkulu. 
Luke9:61 Lomunye wasesithi: Ngizakulandela, Nkosi." 
Luke9:62 Kodwa uJesu wathi kuye: Kakho othi esebeke isandla sakhe ekhubeni, akhangele kokusemuva." 
Luke10:1 Njalo emva kwalezizinto iNkosi yamisa njalo abanye. 
Luke10:2 Ngakho yathi kubo: Isibili isivuno sikhulu, kodwa izisebenzi zinlutshwana. Ngakho ncengani eNkosini yesivuno, ukuze ithume izisebenzi esivunweni sayo." 
Luke10:3 Hambani; khangelani, mina ngiyalithuma linjengezimvana phakathi kwezimpisi." 
Luke10:4 Lingaphathi. 
Luke10:5 Njalo lakuyiphi indlu elingena kuyo, qalani lithi: Ukuthula kakubekulindlu." 
Luke10:6 Njalo uba kukhona lapho indodana yokuthula, ukuthula kwenu kuzahlala phezu kwayo; kodwa uba kunge njalo, kuzabuyela kini." 
Luke10:7 Hlalani-ke kuleyondlu, lidle linathe izinto ezivela kibo; ngoba isisebenzi sifanele umvuzo waso. Lingayi endlini lendlini." 
Luke10:8 Lakuwuphi umuzi elingena kuwo, besebelemukela, dlanini okubekwa phambi kwenu," 
Luke10:9 lisilise abagulayo abakuwo. 
Luke10:10 Kodwa lakuwuphi umuzi elingena kuwo, futhi bengalemukeli, phumelani endleleni zawo, lithi:" 
Luke10:11 Lothuli lomuzi wenu olusinamatheleyo siyaluthintithela kini. 
Luke10:12 Njalo ngithi kini: Kuzakuba lula eSodoma ngalolosuku, kulakulowomuzi." 
Luke10:13 Maye kuwe, Korazini! Maye kuwe, Bhethisayida! Ngoba uba kwakwenziwe eTire leSidoni imisebenzi yamandla eyenziwe kini." 
Luke10:14 Kodwa kuzakuba lula eTire leSidoni ekugwetshweni, kulakini." 
Luke10:15 Lawe, Kapenawume, ophakanyiselwe ezulwini, uzaphoselwa phansi esihogweni." 
Luke10:16 Olizwayo lina uyangizwa mina. 
Luke10:17 Babuya-ke abangamatshumi ayisikhombisa ngentokozo. 
Luke10:18 Wasesithi kubo: Ngabona uSathane njengombane. 
Luke10:19 Khangelani, ngilinika amandla okunyathela phezu kwezinyoka labofezela, laphezu kwamandla wonke esitha; njalo akusoze kube lalutho olungalilimaza." 
Luke10:20 Kodwa lingathokozi ngalokho ukuthi omoya bayazehlisela ngaphansi kwenu. 
Luke10:21 Ngalelohola uJesu. 
Luke10:22 Konke kwanikelwa kimi nguBaba; njalo kakho owaziyo ukuthi iNdodana ingubani, ngaphandle kukaBaba, lokuthi uBaba ungubani, ngaphandle kweNdodana, njalo loba ngubani iNdodana ethanda ukumembulela." 
Luke10:23 Wasephendukela kubafundi bebodwa wathi: Abusisiwe amehlo abona elikubonayo. 
Luke10:24 Ngoba ngithi kini: Abaprofethi abanengi lamakhosi babethanda ukubona izinto elizibonayo lina, kodwa kaba zi bonanga; lokuzwa izinto elizizwayo, kodwa kaba zi zwanga." 
Luke10:25 Njalo khangela, isazumthetho esithile?" 
Luke10:26 Wasesithi kuso: Kubhalweni emlayweni? Uwubala njani? 
Luke10:27 Sasesiphendula sathi: Wothanda iNkosi uNkulunkulu wakho, ngenhliziyo yakho yonke, langomphefumulo wakho wonke, langamandla akho wonke, langengqondo yakho yonke." 
Luke10:28 Wasesithi kuso: Uphendule ngokuqonda; yenza lokhu, futhi uzaphila." 
Luke10:29 Kodwa sona sithanda ukuzilungisisa sathi kuJesu: Kanti ngubani umakhelwane wami? 
Luke10:30 UJesu wasephendula wathi: Umuntu othile wehla evela eJerusalema, njalo bamhlubula impahla ba m tshaya imivimvinya basuka bahamba, ba m tshiya ephosukufa." 
Luke10:31 Umpristi othile waseqabuka esehla ngaleyondlela. 
Luke10:32 Langokunjalo lomLevi nxa wayesekulindawo, wafika e m bona, wadlula eceleni." 
Luke10:33 Kodwa umSamariya othile owayehamba wafika lapho ayekhona, njalo kwathi embona waba lesihelo," 
Luke10:34 waya kuyewabopha amanxeba akhe; wamkhweza phezu kweyakhe inyamazana, wamusa endlini yezihambi, wamlondoloza." 
Luke10:35 Kusisa esehamba, wakhupha odenariyo ababili wa ba nika umninindlu, wathi kuye: Umlondoloze; njalo loba yini ozakuchitha okwedlula lokhu, mina ngizabuyisela kuwe ekubuyeni kwami." 
Luke10:36 Pho, nguwuphi kulaba abathathu ocabanga ukuthi wayengumakhelwane walowo owatheleka phakathi kwabaphangi?" 
Luke10:37 Wasesithi: Ngulowo owamenzela isihawu. Ngakho uJesu wathi kuye: Hamba, lawe wenze njalo." 
Luke10:38 Kwasekusithi ekuhambeni kwabo, yena wangena emzaneni othile; lowesifazana othile, uMarta." 
Luke10:39 Njalo lo wayelodadewabo othiwa nguMariya, walizwa ilizwi lakhe." 
Luke10:40 Kodwa uMarta wayephazanyiswa yikusebenza okunengi; weza eduze wasesithi: Nkosi, kawukhathali yini ukuthi udadewethu ungitshiye ukuthi ngisebenze ngedwa? Ngakho umtshele ukuthi angisize." 
Luke10:41 Kodwa uJesu waphendula wathi kuye: Marta, Marta;" 
Luke10:42 kodwa yinye into edingekayo. 
Luke11:1 Kwasekusithi ekhuleka endaweni ethile, eseqedile, omunye wabafundi bakhe wathi kuye: Nkosi, sifundise ukukhuleka, njengoJohane laye wafundisa abafundi bakhe." 
Luke11:2 Wasesithi kubo: Nxa likhuleka, libokuthi: Baba wethu osemazulwini, kalihlonitshwe ibizo lakho. Umbuso wakho kawuze. Intando yakho kayenziwe, lemhlabeni njengezulwini." 
Luke11:3 Siphe usuku ngosuku ukudla kwethu kwensuku zonke. 
Luke11:4 Njalo usithethelele amacala ethu, ngoba lathi sibathethelela bonke abalamacala kithi. Njalo ungasingenisi ekulingweni, kodwa usikhulule ebubini." 
Luke11:5 Wasesithi kubo: Nguwuphi kini olomngane, futhi aye kuye phakathi kobusuku, athi kuye: Mngane, ngeboleka izinkwa ezintathu," 
Luke11:6 ngoba kufike kimi umngane wami evela ekuhambeni, kodwa kangilalutho engingalubeka phambi kwakhe;" 
Luke11:7 longaphakathi aphendule athi: Ungangihluphi; umnyango usuvaliwe, labantwana bami abancane balami embhedeni; kangingeke ngivuke ngikunike." 
Luke11:8 Ngithi kini: Loba engazukuvuka amnike, ngoba engumngane wakhe, kodwa ngenxa yokuphikelela kwakhe uzavuka amnike konke akuswelayo." 
Luke11:9 Mina-ke ngithi kini: Celani, lizaphiwa; dingani, lizathola; qoqodani, lizavulelwa." 
Luke11:10 Ngoba wonke ocelayo uyemukela; lodingayo uyathola; loqoqodayo uyavulelwa. 
Luke11:11 Kambe, nguwuphi kini onguyise ongathi indodana icela isinkwa, ayinike ilitshe? Loba-ke inhlanzi, ayinike inyoka endaweni yenhlanzi yini?" 
Luke11:12 Uba-ke icela iqanda, ayinike ufezela yini?" 
Luke11:13 Ngakho uba lina elingababi likwazi ukupha abantwana benu izipho ezinhle, kakhulu kangakanani uBaba osezulwini." 
Luke11:14 Wayesekhupha idimoni, elaliyisimungulu. Kwasekusithi, seliphumile idimoni, wakhuluma oyisimungulu; amaxuku asemangala." 
Luke11:15 Kodwa abanye babo bathi: Ukhupha amadimoni ngoBhelezebhule inkosi yamadimoni. 
Luke11:16 Labanye be m linga. 
Luke11:17 Kodwa yena eyazi imicabango yabo wathi kubo: Wonke umbuso owehlukene umelene lawo ngokwawo uyachitheka; njalo indlu emelene lendlu iyadilika. 
Luke11:18 Njalo uba uSathane laye ehlukene emelane laye ngokwakhe, umbuso wakhe uzakuma njani? Ngoba lithi, ngikhupha amadimoni ngoBhelezebhule." 
Luke11:19 Njalo uba mina ngikhupha amadimoni ngoBhelezebhule, amadodana enu akhupha ngobani? Ngakho wona azakuba ngabagwebi benu." 
Luke11:20 Kodwa uba ngikhupha amadimoni ngomunwe kaNkulunkulu, isibili umbuso kaNkulunkulu usufikile kini." 
Luke11:21 Uba isiqhwaga sihlomile silinda owaso umuzi, impahla yaso isekuthuleni;" 
Luke11:22 kodwa nxa olamandla kulaso e si sukela asinqobe, uyasemuka izikhali zaso ebesithembele kuzo, abesesaba impango yaso." 
Luke11:23 Ongelami umelene lami. 
Luke11:24 Nxa umoya ongcolileyo esephumile emuntwini, uyahamba adabule indawo ezomileyo, edinga ukuphumula; kodwa engakutholi athi: Ngizabuyela endlini yami engaphuma kuyo;" 
Luke11:25 njalo esefikile ayifice ithanyelwe njalo ilungisiwe. 
Luke11:26 Abesehamba azithathele abanye omoya abayisikhombisa ababi kulaye uqobo, bangene bahlale lapho; njalo ukucina kwalowomuntu kube kubi kulokuqala." 
Luke11:27 Kwasekusithi ekhuluma lezizinto, owesifazana othile exukwini waphakamisa ilizwi, wathi kuye." 
Luke11:28 Kodwa yena wathi: Kodwa ikakhulu. 
Luke11:29 Kwathi sekubuthene amaxuku eminyene, waqala ukuthi: Lesi isizukulwana sibi; sidinga isibonakaliso, kodwa kasiyikunikwa isibonakaliso, ngaphandle kwesibonakaliso sikaJona umprofethi." 
Luke11:30 Ngoba njengalokhu uJona waba yisibonakaliso kwabeNineve, leNdodana yomuntu izakuba njalo kulesisizukulwana." 
Luke11:31 Indlovukazi yeningizimu izasukuma ekugwetshweni kanye lamadoda alesisizukulwana, iwalahle; ngoba yavela emikhawulweni yomhlaba uku zaku zwa inhlakanipho kaSolomoni, njalo khangelani, omkhulu kuloSolomoni ulapha." 
Luke11:32 Amadoda eNineve azasukuma ekugwetshweni kanye lalesisizukulwana, asilahle; ngoba aphenduka ngokutshumayela kukaJona, njalo khangelani, omkhulu kuloJona ulapha." 
Luke11:33 Futhi kakho othi eselumathise isibane asibeke ekusithekeni, loba ngaphansi kwesitsha, kodwa phezu kwesiqobane sesibane." 
Luke11:34 Isibane somzimba yilihlo; ngakho nxa ilihlo lakho liphilile, lomzimba wakho wonke ugcwele ukukhanya." 
Luke11:35 Ngakho qaphela ukuthi ukukhanya okukuwe kungabi ngumnyama. 
Luke11:36 Ngakho uba umzimba wakho wonke ugcwele ukukhanya, ungelandawo emnyama, uzakhanya wonke, njengesibane sikukhanyisa ngokukhanya." 
Luke11:37 Kwathi esakhuluma, umFarisi othile wamcela ukuthi adle laye; wasengena wahlala ekudleni." 
Luke11:38 Kwathi umFarisi ebona lokhuwamangala ukuthi kazange aqale ageze. 
Luke11:39 Yasisithi iNkosi kuye: Khathesi lina baFarisi lihlambulula ingaphandle yenkezo leyesitsha. 
Luke11:40 Zithutha, yena owenza ingaphandle kayenzanga yini lengaphakathi?" 
Luke11:41 Kodwa phanini zibe yizipho lezozinto ezingaphakathi. 
Luke11:42 Kodwa maye kini baFarisi. 
Luke11:43 Maye kini baFarisi! Ngoba lithanda izihlalo zabahloniphekayo emasinagogeni. 
Luke11:44 Maye kini, babhali labaFarisi, bazenzisi! Ngoba lifanana lamangcwaba angabonakaliyo, labantu abahamba phezu kwawo bengawazi." 
Luke11:45 Omunye wezazumthetho wasephendula wathi kuye: Mfundisi, ngokutsho lezizinto uyasithuka lathi." 
Luke11:46 Kodwa wathi: Maye lakini zazumthetho. 
Luke11:47 Maye kini! Ngoba lakha amangcwaba abaprofethi, njalo oyihlo bababulala." 
Luke11:48 Ngalokhu-ke lifakaza. 
Luke11:49 Ngalokhu-ke inhlakanipho kaNkulunkulu yathi; 
Luke11:50 ukuze kubizwe kulesisizukulwana igazi labaprofethi bonke elachithwa kusukela ekusekelweni komhlaba," 
Luke11:51 kusukela egazini likaAbela kuze kufike egazini likaZakariya owabulawa phakathi laphakathi kwelathi lendlu kaNkulunkulu; yebo, ngithi kini: Lizabizwa kulesisizukulwana." 
Luke11:52 Maye kini zazumthetho, labangenayo labavimbela." 
Luke11:53 Kwathi ekhuluma lezizinto kubo, ababhali labaFarisi baqala uku m ngxamela kakhulukazi, lokumbuzisisa ngezinto ezinengi," 
Luke11:54 bemthiya. 
Luke12:1 Kusenjalo sezibuthene izigidi zexuku, baze banyathelana, waqala ukukhuluma labafundi bakhe kuqala." 
Luke12:2 Njalo kakukho okumbomboziweyo, okungayikwembulwa, lokufihliweyo, okungayikwaziwa." 
Luke12:3 Ngakho loba yini eliyikhuluma emnyameni izazwakala ekukhanyeni; lelikukhulume endlebeni ezindlini zensitha. 
Luke12:4 Njalo ngithi kini bangane bami: Lingabesabi ababulala umzimba, njalo emva kwalokho bengelakho ukwenza olunye ulutho." 
Luke12:5 Kodwa ngizalitshengisa elifanele ukumesaba: Mesabeni lowo othi esebulele abe lamandla okuphosela esihogweni; yebo, ngithi kini: Mesabeni yena." 
Luke12:6 Kazithengiswa yini intaka ezinhlanu ngendibilitshi ezimbili? Kakukhohlakali lanye yazo phambi kukaNkulunkulu. 
Luke12:7 Kanti lenwele zekhanda lenu zibaliwe zonke. Ngakho lingesabi; liyazedlula intaka ezinengi. 
Luke12:8 Njalo ngithi kini: Wonke loba ngubani ongivuma phambi kwabantu, iNdodana yomuntu layo izamvuma phambi kwengilosi zikaNkulunkulu;" 
Luke12:9 kodwa ongiphika phambi kwabantu uzaphikwa phambi kwengilosi zikaNkulunkulu. 
Luke12:10 Laye wonke okhuluma ilizwi elimelana leNdodana yomuntu, uzathethelelwa; kodwa lowo ohlambaza uMoya oNgcwele kayikuthethelelwa." 
Luke12:11 Njalo nxa belisa emasinagogeni; 
Luke12:12 ngoba uMoya oNgcwele uzalifundisa ngalelohola izinto e li fanele ukuzikhuluma. 
Luke12:13 Futhi omunye wexuku wathi kuye: Mfundisi, akutshele umfowethu abelane lami ilifa." 
Luke12:14 Kodwa wathi kuye: Ndoda? 
Luke12:15 Wasesithi kubo: Nanzelelani liqaphele ubuhwaba, ngoba impilo yomuntu kayikho ebunengini bezinto alazo." 
Luke12:16 Wasebatshela umfanekiso, esithi: Insimu yomuntu othile onothileyo yathela kakhulu;" 
Luke12:17 wasenakana ngaphakathi kwakhe? 
Luke12:18 Wasesithi: Ngizakwenza lokhu; ngizadiliza iziphala zami, ngakhe ezinkulu," 
Luke12:19 besengisithi kumphefumulo wami: Mphefumulo, ulempahla ezinengi ezibekelwe iminyaka eminengi; phumula, udle, unathe." 
Luke12:20 Kodwa uNkulunkulu wathi kuye: Siphukuphuku? 
Luke12:21 Kunjalo-ke kozibekela inotho. 
Luke12:22 Wasesithi kubafundi bakhe: Ngakho ngithi kini: Lingakhathaleli impilo yenu, ukuthi lizakudlani; loba umzimba, ukuthi lizakwembathani." 
Luke12:23 Impilo yedlula ukudla, lomzimba isembatho." 
Luke12:24 Qaphelisisani amawabayi, ukuthi kawahlanyeli, njalo kawavuni inyoni?" 
Luke12:25 Njalo nguwuphi kini ongathingokuphiseka engezelele ingalo ibenye? 
Luke12:26 Ngakho nxa lingelamandla okwenza into encinyane, liphisekelani ngokunye?" 
Luke12:27 Qaphelisani imiduze ukuthi ikhula njani; kayitshikatshiki, kayiphothi, kodwa ngithi kini: LoSolomoni ebucwazicwazini bakhe bonke wayengembathiswanga njengomunye wayo." 
Luke12:28 Njalo uba uNkulunkulu esembathisa ngokunjalo utshani obukhona lamuhla egangeni, kuthi kusasa buphoswa eziko, uza l embathisangokukhulu kangakanani, lina abokholo oluncinyane?" 
Luke12:29 Lani-ke lingadingi elizakudla lelizakunatha; njalo lingakhathazeki. 
Luke12:30 Ngoba konke lokhu izizwe zomhlaba ziyakudinga; kodwa uYihlo uyazi ukuthi liyaziswela lezizinto. 
Luke12:31 Kodwa dingani umbuso kaNkulunkulu, njalo zonke lezizinto zizakwengezelelwa kini." 
Luke12:32 Lingesabi. 
Luke12:33 Thengisani impahla zenu; 
Luke12:34 ngoba lapho okukhona impahla yenu eligugu, izakuba khona lapho lenhliziyo yenu." 
Luke12:35 Inkalo zenu kazihlale zibotshiwe; 
Luke12:36 lani libe njengabantu abalindele inkosi yabo, lapho izabuya ivela emtshadweni, ukuze, nxa ifika iqoqoda, bahle bayivulele." 
Luke12:37 Zibusisiwe lezozinceku. 
Luke12:38 Njalo nxa ifika ngomlindo wesibili, zibusisiwe lezozinceku." 
Luke12:39 Kodwa yazini lokhu, ukuthi uba umninindlu ebelazi ihola isela elizafika ngalo, futhi ubengayikuvuma ukuthi indlu yakhe ifohlelwe." 
Luke12:40 Ngakho lani-ke hlalani lilungile. 
Luke12:41 UPetro wasesithi kuye: Nkosi, uwutshela thina lumfanekiso?" 
Luke12:42 INkosi yasisithi: Pho ngubani umphathi wezinceku othembekileyo lohlakaniphileyo, inkosi ezambeka phezu kwabendlu yayo, ukuze a ba nike isabelo sabosokudla ngesikhathi esifaneleyo?" 
Luke12:43 Ibusisiwe leyonceku, okuzakuthi inkosi yayo nxa ifika iyifice isenza njalo." 
Luke12:44 Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Izayibeka phezu kwakho konke elakho. 
Luke12:45 Kodwa nxa leyonceku isithi enhliziyweni yayo: Inkosi yami iphuzile ukubuya; njalo ibisiqala ukutshaya izinceku lezincekukazi, lokudla lokunatha lokudakwa," 
Luke12:46 inkosi yaleyonceku izafika ngosuku enga yi lindele ngalo, langehola engalaziyo; izayiquma phakathi, izanika isabelo sayo lalabo abangathembekanga." 
Luke12:47 Laleyonceku ebisazi intando yenkosi yayo. 
Luke12:48 Kodwa leyo. 
Luke12:49 Ngize ukuphosela umlilo emhlabeni? 
Luke12:50 Kodwa ngilobhabhathizo engizabhabhathizwa ngalo. 
Luke12:51 Licabanga ukuthi ngize ukunika ukuthula emhlabeni yini. 
Luke12:52 Ngoba kusukela khathesi abahlanu endlini yinye bazakwehlukana, abathathu bamelane lababili, lababili bamelane labathathu," 
Luke12:53 bazakwehlukana, uyise amelane lendodana, lendodana imelane loyise; unina amelane lendodakazi, lendodakazi imelane lonina; uninazala amelane lomalokazana wakhe, lomalokazana amelane loninazala." 
Luke12:54 Wasesithi lemaxukwini: Nxa libona iyezi, lihle lithi: Izulu liyabuya; futhi kube njalo." 
Luke12:55 Njalo nxa libonaumoya weningizimu uphephetha, lithi: Lizatshisa; besekusenzakala." 
Luke12:56 Bazenzisi! Liyakwazi ukuhlola umumo wesibhakabhaka lowomhlaba; kodwa lesisikhathi kungani lingasihloli? 
Luke12:57 Pho, kungani ukuthi lingahluleli lani lina uqobo lwenu okulungileyo?" 
Luke12:58 Ngoba nxa usiya, endleleni yenza ubungcono ukuthi ukhululwe kuye; hlezi akudonsele kumahluleli, lomahluleli akunikele epholiseni, lepholisa likuphosele entolongweni." 
Luke12:59 Ngithi kuwe, kawusoze waphuma khona, uze ubhadale lenhlamvu encane yemali yokucina." 
Luke13:1 Njalo ngalesosikhathi kwaba khona abathile abamtshela ngamaGalili, igazi lawo uPilatu alixubanisa lemihlatshelo yawo." 
Luke13:2 UJesu wasephendula wathi kubo: Licabanga ukuthi amaGalili la ayeyizoni yini kulawo wonke amaGalili, ngoba ahlupheka izinto ezinje?" 
Luke13:3 Hatshi bo, ngithi kini: Kodwa uba lingaphenduki, lizabhubha ngokunjalo lonke." 
Luke13:4 Lalabo abalitshumi lesificaminwembili, owawela phezu kwabo umphotshongo eSilowama wababulala, licabanga ukuthi bona babebabi yini kulabantu bonke ababehlala eJerusalema?" 
Luke13:5 Hatshi bo, ngithi kini: Kodwa uba lingaphenduki, lizabhubha ngokunjalo lonke." 
Luke13:6 Wasekhuluma lumfanekiso wathi: Umuntuothile wayelomkhiwa owawuhlanyelwe esivinini sakhe; wafika edinga isithelo kuwo, kodwa ka si tholanga." 
Luke13:7 Wasesithi kuso isisebenzi sesivini: Khangela, sekuyiminyaka emithathu ngisiza ngidinga isithelo emkhiweni, kodwa nginga si tholi; ugamule; yini ukuthi wone ngitsho umhlabathi?" 
Luke13:8 Sasesiphendula sathi kuye: Nkosi, ake uwuyekele langalumnyaka, ngize ngigebhe ngiwugombolozele, ngithele umquba;" 
Luke13:9 njalo uba uthela isithelo, kuhle." 
Luke13:10 Futhi wayefundisa kwelinye lamasinagoge ngesabatha; 
Luke13:11 njalo khangela, kwakukhona owesifazana owayelomoya wobuthakathaka iminyaka elitshumi leyisificaminwembili." 
Luke13:12 Kwathi uJesu embona wa m bizela kuye, wathi kuye: Mama, ukhululwe ebuthakathakeni bakho." 
Luke13:13 Wasebeka izandla phezu kwakhe. 
Luke13:14 Kodwa umphathi wesinagoge. 
Luke13:15 Ngakho iNkosi yamphendula, yathi: Mzenzisi?" 
Luke13:16 Lalo, oyindodakazi kaAbrahama?" 
Luke13:17 Kwathi esitsho lezizinto, bayangeka bonke ababephikisana laye; lexuku lonke lathokoza ngezinto zonke ezilodumo ezenziwe nguye." 
Luke13:18 Wasesithi: Umbuso kaNkulunkulu unjengani? Futhi ngizawufananisa lani? 
Luke13:19 Unjengohlamvu lwemasitedi, umuntu aluthatha wa lu phosa esivandeni sakhe; lwaselumila, lwaba yisihlahla esikhulu, lenyoni zezulu zakhele engatsheni zaso." 
Luke13:20 Wasebuya wathi: Ngizawufananisa lani umbuso kaNkulunkulu? 
Luke13:21 Unjengemvubelo, ayithathayo owesifazana wayifaka ezilinganisweni ezintathu zempuphu, kwaze kwabila konke." 
Luke13:22 Wasehamba edabula imizi lemizana efundisa. 
Luke13:23 Omunye wasesithi kuye: Nkosi, balutshwana yini abasindiswayo? Wasesithi kubo:" 
Luke13:24 Zamani kakhulu ukungena ngesango elincinyane; ngoba abanengi, ngithi kini, bazadinga ukungena, kodwa bazakwehluleka." 
Luke13:25 Emva kokuthi umninindlu; 
Luke13:26 lapho lizaqala ukuthi: Sadla sanatha phambi kwakho. 
Luke13:27 Kodwa uzakuthi: Ngithi kini: Kangilazi lapho elivela khona. 
Luke13:28 Lapho kuzakuba khona ukukhala lokugedla amazinyo. 
Luke13:29 Futhi bazakuza. 
Luke13:30 Njalo khangelani, bakhona abokucina abazakuba ngabokuqala, njalo bakhona abokuqala abazakuba ngabokucina." 
Luke13:31 Ngelanga elifananayo kwafika abaFarisi abathile, bathi kuye: Phuma usuke lapha." 
Luke13:32 Wasesithi kubo: Hambani lilitshele lelokhanka: Khangela, ngiyakhupha amadimoni ngenza izelapho lamuhla lakusasa, langelesithathu ngipheleliswe." 
Luke13:33 Kodwa kumele ukuthi ngihambe lamuhla lakusasa. 
Luke13:34 Jerusalema, Jerusalema, wena obulala abaprofethi, lobakhanda ngamatshe labo abathunywe kuwe! Bengithanda kangakanani ukubuthela ndawonye abantwana bakho." 
Luke13:35 Khangelani, indlu yenu itshiywe kini ilunxiwa." 
Luke14:1 Kwasekusithi ekungeneni kwakhe ngesabatha endlini yomunye wabakhulu kubaFarisi ukuthi adle isinkwa. 
Luke14:2 Njalo khangela, kwakukhona umuntu othile phambi kwakhe owayelombizankulu." 
Luke14:3 UJesu wasephendula? 
Luke14:4 Kodwa bathula. Wase m bamba wamsilisa wa m yekela ukuthi ahambe. 
Luke14:5 Wasebaphendula esithi? 
Luke14:6 Abasazange babuyisele impendulo kuye ngalezizinto. 
Luke14:7 Wasekhuluma umfanekiso kubo abanxusiweyo, wathi kubo:" 
Luke14:8 Nxa unxusiwe ngumuntu emtshadweni; hlezi kukhona omkhulu kulawe onxusiweyo nguye," 
Luke14:9 futhi okunxusileyo wena laye eze athi kuwe: Mxekele lo; khona uzaqala ukuhlala endaweni esekucineni usulenhloni. 
Luke14:10 Kodwa nxa unxusiwe, hamba uhlale endaweni esekucineni." 
Luke14:11 Ngoba wonke oziphakamisayo uzathotshiswa, lozithobayo uzaphakanyiswa." 
Luke14:12 Wasesithi lakulowo owayemnxusile: Nxa usenza ukudla kwemini loba ukudla kwantambama, unganxusi abangane bakho, loba abafowenu, loba izihlobo zakho, loba omakhelwane abanothileyo; hlezi labo babuye bakunxuse, futhi ukwenananiswa kwenziwe kuwe." 
Luke14:13 Kodwa nxa usenza idili, nxusa abayanga, izilima, iziqhuli, iziphofu;" 
Luke14:14 njalo uzabusiswa, ngoba abalalutho lokukwenanisa." 
Luke14:15 Kwathi omunye kwababehlezi laye ekudleni esezwile lezizinto wathi kuye: Ubusisiwe lowo ozakudla isinkwa embusweni kaNkulunkulu. 
Luke14:16 Kodwa wathi kuye: Umuntu othile wenza ukudla kwantambama okukhulu, wanxusa abanengi." 
Luke14:17 Ngesikhathi sokudla kwantambama wasethuma inceku yakhe ukuthi ithi kwabanxusiweyo: Wozani, ngoba sekulungisiwe konke." 
Luke14:18 Kodwa bonke baqala omunye lomunye ukuzixolisela. 
Luke14:19 Lomunye wathi: Sengithenge izipane ezinhlanu zenkabi, ngiya ukuzilinga; ngiyakuncenga, akungixolisele." 
Luke14:20 Lomunye wathi: Sengithethe umfazi, ngakho ngingeze ngeza." 
Luke14:21 Isibuyile leyonceku yayibikela lezizinto inkosi yayo. Wasethukuthela umninindlu wathi encekwini yakhe: Phuma ngokuphangisa uye emigwaqweni lendleleni zomuzi, ulethe abayanga lezilima leziqhuli leziphofu ubangenise lapha." 
Luke14:22 Inceku yasisithi: Nkosi, sekwenziwe njengokulaya kwakho, njalo indawo isesekhona." 
Luke14:23 Yasisithi inkosi encekwini: Phuma uye ezindleleni lezintangweni u ba cindezele ba ngene, ukuze igcwaliswe indlu yami." 
Luke14:24 Ngoba ngithi kini: Kakho kulamadoda ayenxusiwe ozakuzwa ukudla kwami kwantambama. 
Luke14:25 Kwakuhamba laye amaxuku amanengi; wasetshibilika wathi kuwo: 
Luke14:26 Uba umuntu esiza kimi. 
Luke14:27 Njalo loba ngubani. 
Luke14:28 Ngoba nguwuphi kini, othi efuna ukwakha umphotshongo, ongaqali ahlale phansi, abale indleko, ukuthi ulakho yini okokuqedisa?" 
Luke14:29 Ukuze hlezi, kuthi esebekile isisekelo kodwa angabi lamandla okuqeda, bonke abakubonayo baqale ukumhleka," 
Luke14:30 besithi: Lumuntu waqala ukwakha, kodwa kabanga lamandla okuqeda." 
Luke14:31 Loba yiyiphi inkosi ezakuya empini imelene lenye inkosi engaqali ihlale phansi inakane ngokuthi ilamandla yini ngenkulungwane ezilitshumi okuhlangabezana laleyo? 
Luke14:32 Kodwa uba kunge njalo, ingathi isekhatshana leyo, ithume amanxusa icele okokuthula." 
Luke14:33 Ngakho kunjalo wonke kini ongadeli konke alakho, angeke aba ngumfundi wami." 
Luke14:34 Itshwayi lihle? 
Luke14:35 Kalifanele lamhlabathi ledundulu lomquba. 
Luke15:1 Kwasekusondela kuye bonke. 
Luke15:2 AbaFarisi lababhali basebesola besithi: Lo wemukela izoni, adle lazo." 
Luke15:3 Wasebatshela lumfanekiso, esithi:" 
Luke15:4 Nguwuphi umuntu kini ongathi elezimvu ezilikhulu? 
Luke15:5 Njalo athi ese yi tholile a ye tshate ethokoza. 
Luke15:6 Esefikile ekhaya, abizele ndawonye abangane labomakhelwane, esithi kubo: Thokozani lami, ngoba ngithole imvu yami ebilahlekile." 
Luke15:7 Ngithi kini: Ngokunjalo kuzakuba khona intokozo ezulwini ngesoni esisodwa esiphendukayo, kulabalungileyo abangamatshumi ayisificamunwemunye lasificamunwemunye, abangasweli ukuphenduka." 
Luke15:8 Loba nguwuphi umfazi othi elenhlamvu zesiliva ezilitshumi, uba elahlekelwa luhlamvu olulodwa lwesiliva, angalumathisi isibane, athanyele indlu, adingisise aze a lu thole?" 
Luke15:9 Njalo nxa ese lu tholile ubizela ndawonye abangane labomakhelwane, athi: Thokozani lami, ngoba sengilutholile uhlamvu lwesiliva ebengilahlekelwe yilo." 
Luke15:10 Ngokunjalo, ngithi kini, ikhona intokozo phambi kwezingilosi zikaNkulunkulu ngesoni esisodwa esiphendukayo." 
Luke15:11 Wasesithi: Umuntu othile wayelamadodana amabili; 
Luke15:12 encinyane yawo yasisithi kuyise: Baba, nginika isabelo sempahla." 
Luke15:13 Njalo kungelansuku ezinengi emva kwalokhu indodana encinyane yabutha konke yasuka yahamba yaya elizweni elikhatshana, njalo lapho yachitha khona impahla yayo, iphila okobuhlanya." 
Luke15:14 Yathi isichithile konke, kwavela indlala enkulu kulelolizwe, yona yasiqala ukuswela." 
Luke15:15 Yasisuka yazihlanganisa lesinye sezakhamizi zalelolizwe; njalo sayithuma emasimini aso ukuze yeluse izingulube. 
Luke15:16 Yasifisa ukugcwalisa isisu sayo ngamakhasi ingulube eziwadlayo; njalo kwakungelamuntu oyinika ulutho. 
Luke15:17 Kwathi ingqondoyayo isibuyile yathi: Zingaki izisebenzi zikababa eziqatshiweyo ezilezinkwa ezinengi kakhulu, kanti mina ngiyafa yindlala;" 
Luke15:18 ngizasukuma ngiye kubaba, ngithi kuye: Baba, ngonile ezulwini, laphambi kwakho;" 
Luke15:19 njalo; ngenza ngibe njengomunye wezisebenzi zakho eziqatshiweyo. 
Luke15:20 Yasisukuma yaya kuyise. Kodwa kuthe isesekhatshana, uyise wayibona, waba lesihelo." 
Luke15:21 Indodana yasisithi kuye: Baba, ngonile ezulwini." 
Luke15:22 Kodwa uyise wathi ezincekwini zakhe: Khuphani lilethe isembatho esihle kakhulu liyigqokise; 
Luke15:23 lilethe ithole elinonisiweyo; 
Luke15:24 ngoba indodana yami le ibifile, isibuye yaphila; ibilahlekile, itholiwe." 
Luke15:25 Kodwa indodana yakhe endala yayisensimini; yathi isiza isondela endlini, yezwa ukuhlabelela lokusina." 
Luke15:26 Yasibizela kuyo omunye wezinceku, yabuza ukuthi zitshoni lezizinto." 
Luke15:27 Yasisithi kuyo: Umfowenu ufikile; loyihlo uhlabile ithole elinonisiweyo, ngoba ememukele ephila." 
Luke15:28 Kodwa yathukuthela, ayizange ifune ukungena; ngakho uyise waphuma wayincenga." 
Luke15:29 Kodwa yaphendula yathi kuyise: Khangela, iminyaka engaka ngikusebenzela, kangizange ngeqe umlayo wakho, kodwa kawuzange unginike lazinyane lembuzi." 
Luke15:30 Kodwa kuthe isifikile lindodana yakho eyachitha impahla yakho lezifebe, wayihlabela." 
Luke15:31 Wasesithi kuyo: Ndodana, wena uhlezi ulami." 
Luke15:32 Kodwa bekufanele ukuthi sijabule sithokoze. 
Luke16:1 Wasekhuluma futhi kubafundi bakhe esithi: Kwakukhona umuntu othile onothileyo, owayelomphathi; lalo wayemangalelwe kuye njengochitha impahla yakhe." 
Luke16:2 Wasembiza wathi kuye: Kuyini lokhu engikuzwayo ngawe? Landisa ngobuphathi bakho; ngoba ungebe usaba ngumphathi. 
Luke16:3 Umphathi wasesithi ngaphakathi kwakhe: Ngizakwenzani, lokhu inkosi yami isingemuka ubuphathi? Kangilamandla okugebha, ngilenhloni zokuphanza." 
Luke16:4 Ngiyakwazi engizakwenza, ukuze nxa sengikhutshiwe ebuphathini, bangemukele ezindlini zabo."
