Luke16:5 Wasebabizela kuye ngamunye abalemilandu enkosini yakhe, wathi kowokuqala: Ulomlandu ongakanani enkosini yami?" 
Luke16:6 Wasesithi yena: Izilinganiso ezilikhulu zamagcobo. Wasesithi kuye: Thatha incwadi yakho, uhlale phansi ubhale masinya amatshumi amahlanu." 
Luke16:7 Wasesithi komunye: Wena-ke ulomlandu ongakanani? Wasesithi: Izilinganiso ezilikhulu zamabele. Wasesithi kuye: Thatha incwadi yakho, ubhale amatshumi ayisificaminwembili." 
Luke16:8 Inkosi yasimbabaza umphathi. 
Luke16:9 Lami ngithi kini: Zenzeleni lina abangane. 
Luke16:10 Othembekileyo kokuncinyanyana uthembekile lakokukhulu, longathembekanga kokuncinyanyana kathembekanga lakokukhulu." 
Luke16:11 Ngakho uba lingathembekanga kuMamona ongalunganga, ngubani ozaliphathisa into eqotho?" 
Luke16:12 Futhi uba lingathembekanga kokomunye, ngubani ozalinika okungokwenu?" 
Luke16:13 Kayikho inceku engakhonza amakhosi amabili. 
Luke16:14 Njalo labaFarisi ababethanda imali bazizwa zonke lezizinto. 
Luke16:15 Kodwa wathi kubo: Lina yini elizilungisisayo phambi kwabantu. 
Luke16:16 Umlayo labaprofethi kukhonakuze kube nguJohane; kusukela lapho ivangeli lombuso kaNkulunkulu liyatshunyayelwa. 
Luke16:17 Kodwa kulula ukuthi kudlule izulu lomhlaba, kulokuthi kuwe ichatshana elilodwa lomlayo." 
Luke16:18 Wonke owala umkakhe athathe omunye uyafeba; njalo wonke othatha owaliwe yindoda uyafeba. 
Luke16:19 Kwakukhona umuntu othile onothileyo, owayegqoka eziyibubende." 
Luke16:20 Kwakukhona futhi umuntu othile ongumyanga othiwa nguLazaro," 
Luke16:21 wafisa ukusuthiswa; kanti lezinja zazisiza zikhothe izilonda zakhe. 
Luke16:22 Kwasekusithi ongumyanga wafa, wathwalelwa zingilosi; lesinothi laso safa, sangcwatshwa." 
Luke16:23 Sisesihogweni. 
Luke16:24 Sona sasesimemeza sisithi: Baba Abrahama, ngihawukela." 
Luke16:25 Kodwa uAbrahama wathi: Ndodana, khumbula ukuthi wemukela okuhle, njalo wena uyahlupheka." 
Luke16:26 Langaphezu kwakho konke lokhu, kubekiwe phakathi kwethu lani igebe elikhulu, ukuze kuthi abafuna ukuchapha besuka ngapha beze ngakini bangekwenze, labangapho bangechaphele ngakithi." 
Luke16:27 Sasesisithi: Ngakho ngiyakuncenga, baba, ukuthi umthume endlini kababa," 
Luke16:28 ngoba ngilabafowethu abahlanu, ukuze abaxwayise." 
Luke16:29 UAbrahama wathi: BaloMozisi labaprofethi; kabezwe bona. 
Luke16:30 Sona sasesisithi: Hatshi bo, baba Abrahama; kodwa uba omunye kwabafileyo esiya kubo, bazaphenduka." 
Luke16:31 Kodwa wathi kuso: Uba bengalaleli. 
Luke17:1 Wasesithi kubafundi! 
Luke17:2 Kungaba ngcono kuye ukuthi ilitshe lokuchola elikhulu ligaxwe entanyeni yakhe, abesephoselwa olwandle." 
Luke17:3 Zinanzeleleni lina; futhi nxa ephenduka, mthethelele." 
Luke17:4 Njalo loba ekona kuze kube kasikhombisa ngosuku, abesebuya kuwe kasikhombisa ngosuku, esithi: Ngiyaphenduka; uzamthethelela." 
Luke17:5 Abaphostoli basebesithi eNkosini. 
Luke17:6 INkosi yasisithi: Uba lilokholo olungangohlamvu lwemasitedi. 
Luke17:7 Kodwa nguwuphi kini olenceku elimayo kumbe eyelusayo, ohle athi kiyo ingena ivela ensimini: Sondela, uhlale ekudleni?" 
Luke17:8 Kodwa kazukutsho yini kuyo ukuthi: Lungisa engingakudla? 
Luke17:9 Uyayibonga yini leyonceku, ngoba yenze izinto ezilayiweyo? Angicabangi." 
Luke17:10 Kunjalo-ke lani, nxa selikwenzile konke elikulayiweyo, kalibokuthi: Sizinceku ezingasizi lutho, ngoba senze lokhu ebesifanele ukukwenza." 
Luke17:11 Kwasekusithi esahamba esiya eJerusalema. 
Luke17:12 Esangena emzaneni othile, amadoda alitshumi alobulephero amhlangabeza, ema khatshana;" 
Luke17:13 wona asephakamisa ilizwi, esithi: Jesu, Nkosi, sihawukele!" 
Luke17:14 Futhi kuthe e wa bona wathi kuwo: Hambani liyeziveza kubapristi. Kwasekusithi ekusukeni kwawo, ahlanjululwa." 
Luke17:15 Futhi omunye wawo, esebonile ukuthi usilisiwe, wabuyela, edumisa uNkulunkulu ngelizwi elikhulu;" 
Luke17:16 wasesiwa ngobuso enyaweni zakhe. 
Luke17:17 Kodwa uJesu waphendula wathi: Kakuhlanjululwanga yini abalitshumi? Bangaphi pho abayisificamunwemunye? 
Luke17:18 Akuficakalanga ababuya ukunika uNkulunkulu udumo, ngaphandle kwalo owezizweni." 
Luke17:19 Wasesithi kuye: Sukuma uhambe; ukholo lwakho. 
Luke17:20 Kwathi ebuzwa ngabaFarisi, ukuthi umbuso kaNkulunkulu uzakuza nini;" 
Luke17:21 njalo kabayikutsho ukuthi: Khangelani nanku, kumbe: Khangelani nankuya. Ngoba khangelani, umbuso kaNkulunkulu uphakathi kwenu." 
Luke17:22 Wasesithi kubafundi: Kuzafika insuku lapho elizafisa. 
Luke17:23 Njalo bazakuthi kini. 
Luke17:24 Ngoba njengombane ophazimayo ukhanyisa kusukela kokunye ukucinangaphansi kwezulu kusiya kokunye ukucinangaphansi kwezulu. 
Luke17:25 Kodwa kuqala imele ihlupheke izinto ezinengi njalo ilahlwe yilesisizukulwana. 
Luke17:26 Futhi njengoba kwenzeka ensukwini zikaNowa, kuzakuba njalo lensukwini zeNdodana yomuntu." 
Luke17:27 Babesidla, benatha, bethatha, besendiswa, kwaze kwaba lusuku uNowa angena ngalo emkhunjini, kwasekufika uzamcolo, wababhubhisa bonke." 
Luke17:28 Ngokufananayo futhi njengoba kwenzeka ensukwini zikaLothi; babesidla, benatha, bethenga, bethengisa, behlanyela, besakha;" 
Luke17:29 kodwa ngosuku uLothi aphuma ngalo eSodoma, kwana umlilo lesibabule kuvela ezulwini, kwababhubhisa bonke;" 
Luke17:30 kuzakuba njalo ngosuku ezakwembulwa ngalo iNdodana yomuntu. 
Luke17:31 Ngalolosuku, lowo ophezu kophahla lwendlu, lempahla zakhe zisendlini, angehli uku ya zithatha; losensimini ngokunjalo angabuyeli ezintweni ezisemuva." 
Luke17:32 Khumbulani umkaLothi. 
Luke17:33 Loba ngubani odinga ukusindisa impilo yakhe izamlahlekela. 
Luke17:34 Ngithi kini: Ngalobobusuku kuzakuba khona ababili embhedeni munye; omunye uzasuswa, lomunye atshiywe." 
Luke17:35 Kuzakuba khona abesifazanaababili bechola ndawonye; omunye uzasuswa, lomunye atshiywe." 
Luke17:36 Kuzakuba khona ababili ensimini; omunye uzasuswa, lomunye atshiywe." 
Luke17:37 Basebephendula bathi kuye: Ngaphi, Nkosi? Wasesithi kubo: Lapho okukhona isidumbu, ku lapho amanqe azabuthana khona." 
Luke18:1 Wasebatshela lomfanekiso esenzela ukuthi bafanele ukukhuleka isikhathi sonke," 
Luke18:2 wathi: Kwakukhona emzini othile umahluleli othile, owayengesabi uNkulunkulu, njalo engahloniphi muntu;" 
Luke18:3 kwakukhona futhi kulowomuzi umfelokazi othile, njalo wayefika kuye, esithi: Ngiphindiselele esitheni sami." 
Luke18:4 Kodwa kavumanga okwesikhathi; kodwa emva kwalezizinto wathi ngaphakathi kwakhe: Lanxa ngingamesabi uNkulunkulu, ngingahloniphi muntu," 
Luke18:5 kodwa ngoba lumfelokazi engikhathaza, ngizamphindiselela." 
Luke18:6 INkosi yasisithi: Zwanini umahluleli ongalunganga akutshoyo. 
Luke18:7 Kanti uNkulunkulu? 
Luke18:8 Ngithi kini, uzahle enze. Kodwa-ke nxa iNdodana yomuntu ifika, izathola ukholo yini emhlabeni?" 
Luke18:9 Wasekhuluma lumfanekiso lakwabathile ukuthi balungile, futhi bedelela abanye, wathi:" 
Luke18:10 Abantu ababili benyukela ethempelini ukuyakhuleka; omunye engumFarisi. 
Luke18:11 UmFarisi wema wazikhulekela kanje wathi: Nkulunkulu, ngiyakubonga ukuthi kanginjengabanye abantu." 
Luke18:12 Ngizila ukudla kabili ngeviki. 
Luke18:13 Kodwa umthelisi emi khatshana. 
Luke18:14 Ngithi kini: Lo wehlela endlini yakhe. 
Luke18:15 Basebeletha kuye lensane, ukuze azibambe; kodwa abafundi be ku bona babakhuza." 
Luke18:16 Kodwa uJesu wazibizela kuye wathi: Vumelani abantwana abancane beze kimi, lingabenqabeli, ngoba umbuso kaNkulunkulu ungowabanje." 
Luke18:17 Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Loba ngubani ongemukeli umbuso kaNkulunkulu njengomntwana omncane, kasoze angene kuwo." 
Luke18:18 Umbusi wasembuza, esithi: Mfundisi olungileyo, ngenzeni ukuze ngidle ilifa lempilo elaphakade?" 
Luke18:19 Kodwa uJesu wathi kuye: Ungibizelani ngokuthiolungileyo? Kakho olungileyo, ngaphandle koyedwa, uNkulunkulu." 
Luke18:20 Uyayazi imilayo ethi: Ungafebi, ungabulali, ungebi, ungafakazi amanga, hlonipha uyihlo lonyoko." 
Luke18:21 Yena wasesithi: Konke lokhu ngikugcinile kusukela ebutsheni bami. 
Luke18:22 Kodwa uJesu esizwa lezizinto wathi kuye: Usaswele ulutho olulodwa; thengisa konke olakho, wabele abayanga, njalo uzakuba lempahla eligugu ezulwini; njalo uze lapha ungilandele." 
Luke18:23 Kodwa yena esizwa lezizinto wadana kakhulu; ngoba wayenothile kakhulu. 
Luke18:24 Kwathi uJesu ebona ukuthi usedane kakhulu wathi: Abalenotho bazangena ngokulukhuni kangakanani embusweni kaNkulunkulu. 
Luke18:25 Ngoba kulula ukuthi ikamela lingene ngentunja yenalithi, kulokuthi umuntu onothileyo angene embusweni kaNkulunkulu." 
Luke18:26 Aba ku zwayo basebesithi: Pho kungasindiswa bani? 
Luke18:27 Kodwa yena wathi: Izinto ezingenzekiyo ebantwini ziyenzeka kuNkulunkulu. 
Luke18:28 UPetro wasesithi: Khangela, thina sitshiye konke, sakulandela." 
Luke18:29 Wasesithi kubo: Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Kakho umuntu otshiye indlu, kumbe abazali, kumbe abafowabo, kumbe umka khe, kumbe abantwana, ngenxa yombuso kaNkulunkulu," 
Luke18:30 ongayikwemukela okuphindwe kanengi. 
Luke18:31 Wasezithathela abalitshumi lambili, wathi kubo: Khangelani, senyukela eJerusalema." 
Luke18:32 Ngoba izanikelwa kwabezizwe, iyangiswe," 
Luke18:33 ba yi tshaye ngesiswepu bayibulale; njalo ngosuku lwesithathu izabuya ivuke. 
Luke18:34 Kodwa bona kabaqedisisanga lutho ngalezizinto. 
Luke18:35 Kwasekusithi esesondela siphanza; 
Luke18:36 sathi sisizwa ixuku lisedlula, sabuza ukuthi kuyini lokho." 
Luke18:37 Basebesitshela bathi: UJesu weNazaretha uyedlula. 
Luke18:38 Sasesimemeza, sisithi: Jesu, Ndodana kaDavida, ngihawukela!" 
Luke18:39 Ababehamba phambili basebesikhuza ukuthi sithule; kodwa samemeza kakhulukazi, sisithi: Ndodana kaDavida, ngihawukele!" 
Luke18:40 UJesu wema-ke walaya ukuthi silethwe kuye; sathi sesisondele wasibuza," 
Luke18:41 esithi: Ufuna ukuthi ngikwenzeleni? Sasesisithi: Nkosi, ukuthi ngibuye ngibone." 
Luke18:42 UJesu wasesithi kuso: Buya ubone! Ukholo lwakho lukusindisile. 
Luke18:43 Njalo sahle sabuya sabona, samlandela, sidumisa uNkulunkulu." 
Luke19:1 Wathi uJesuengena, wadabula eJeriko." 
Luke19:2 Njalo khangela, kwakukhona indoda eyayithiwa nguZakewu ngebizo; owayeyinduna yabathelisi, njalo wayenothile;" 
Luke19:3 wadinga ukubona uJesu ukuthi ungubani. 
Luke19:4 Wasegijimela phambili wakhwela emkhiweni wesikhamore ukuze ambone; ngoba wayezadlula ngaleyo ndlela. 
Luke19:5 Kwathi uJesu efika kuleyondawo, wakhangela phezulu wambona, wathi kuye: Zakewu, phangisa wehle; ngoba lamuhla ngimele ukuhlala endlini yakho." 
Luke19:6 Wasephangisa wehla, wamemukela ethokoza." 
Luke19:7 Futhi bonke be ku bona basola. 
Luke19:8 Kodwa uZakewu wema wathi eNkosini: Khangela, ingxenye yempahla yami, Nkosi, ngiyipha abayanga; kuthi uba ngimthathele umuntu." 
Luke19:9 UJesu wasesithi kuye: Lamuhla usindiso lufikile kulindlu, ngoba." 
Luke19:10 Ngoba iNdodana yomuntu. 
Luke19:11 Kwathi besizwa lezizinto, wengezelela watsho umfanekiso, ngoba wayeseduze leJerusalema." 
Luke19:12 Wasesithi-ke: Umuntu. 
Luke19:13 Wasebiza inceku zakhe ezilitshumi, wazinika impondo ezilitshumi, wathi kuzo: Sebenzani ngemali ngize ngibuye." 
Luke19:14 Kodwa izakhamizi zakhe zamzonda, zathuma amanxusa emva kwakhe, zisithi: Kasithandi ukuthi lo asibuse." 
Luke19:15 Kwasekusithi esebuyile esewemukele umbuso, wathi azibizelwe kuye lezozinceku, ayezinike imali, ukuze azi ukuthi yileyo laleyo izuzeni ngokuthengiselana." 
Luke19:16 Kweza-ke eyokuqala, yathi: Nkosi, impondo yakho izuze impondo ezilitshumi." 
Luke19:17 Wasesithi kuyo: Kuhle, nceku elungileyo." 
Luke19:18 Kwasekusiza eyesibili, yathi: Nkosi, impondo yakho yenze impondo ezinhlanu." 
Luke19:19 Wasesithi lakuyo: Lawe woba phezu kwemizi emihlanu. 
Luke19:20 Kwasekusiza enye, isithi: Nkosi, khangela impondo yakho, engayibeka elenjini;" 
Luke19:21 ngoba bengikwesaba, ngoba ungumuntu olukhuni; uthatha lokho ongakubekanga, futhi uvune lokho ongakuhlanyelanga." 
Luke19:22 Wasesithi kuyo: Ngizakugweba ngoku vela emlonyeni wakho, nceku embi ukuthi mina ngingumuntu olukhuni, othatha lokho engingakubekanga, futhi avune lokho engingakuhlanyelanga;" 
Luke19:23 ngakho kungani ungafakanga imali yami ebhanga? 
Luke19:24 Wasesithi kulabo ababemi khona: Memukeni impondo, li yi nike lowo olempondo ezilitshumi." 
Luke19:25 Kodwa bathi kuye: Nkosi, lowo ulempondo ezilitshumi." 
Luke19:26 Ngoba ngithi kini: Wonke olakho uzaphiwa; kodwa lowo ongelakho, uzakwemukwa lalokho alakho." 
Luke19:27 Kodwa lezozitha zami, ebezingathandi ukuthi ngizibuse." 
Luke19:28 Esetshilo lezizinto, wahamba phambili." 
Luke19:29 Kwasekusithi esondela eBetfage leBethani entabeni okuthiwa ngeyeMihlwathi, wathuma ababili kubafundi bakhe," 
Luke19:30 esithi: Hambani liye emzaneni okhangelene lani; lizakuthi lingena kuwo lifice ithole likababhemi libotshiwe, okungazanga kuhlale kulo muntu; lilikhulule li li lethe." 
Luke19:31 Uba umuntu elibuza esithi: Li li khululelani? Lizakutsho njalo kuye ukuthi: INkosi iyaliswela. 
Luke19:32 Ababethunyiwe bahamba-ke bafica kunjengoba ebatshelile. 
Luke19:33 Kuthe besalikhulula ithole, abaninilo bathi kubo: Lilikhululelani ithole?" 
Luke19:34 Bona basebesithi: INkosi iyaliswela. 
Luke19:35 Basebeliletha kuJesu; baphosela izembatho zabo phezu kwethole likababhemi, bamkhweza uJesu kulo." 
Luke19:36 Kwathi ehamba, bendlala izembatho zabo phansi endleleni." 
Luke19:37 Kwathi khathesi esesondela ekwehleni kwentaba yeMihlwathi, ixuku lonke labafundi laqala ukuthokoza lokudumisa uNkulunkulu ngelizwi elikhulu," 
Luke19:38 lisithi: Ibusisiwe inkosi ezayo ebizweni leNkosi. 
Luke19:39 Labanye babaFarisi ababesexukwini bathi kuye: Mfundisi, khuza abafundi bakho." 
Luke19:40 Wasephendula wathi kubo: Ngithi kini, uba bethula laba, amatshe azamemeza." 
Luke19:41 Kwathi esondela, ewubona umuzi," 
Luke19:42 esithi: Kungathi ngabe wazi lawe, ngitsho ngalolusuku lwakho, izinto zokuthula kwakho; kodwa-ke khathesi zifihlakele emehlweni akho." 
Luke19:43 Ngoba insuku zizakwehlela phezu kwakho, lapho izitha zakho zizakwakhela umthangala," 
Luke19:44 zikudilizele phansi wena labantwana bakho. 
Luke19:45 Wasengena ethempelini, waqala ukuxotsha abathengisayo kulo, labathengayo," 
Luke19:46 esithi kubo: Kulotshiwe ukuthi: Indlu yami yindlu yomkhuleko. 
Luke19:47 Njalo wayefundisa ethempelini insuku zonke lenduna zabantu badinga ukumbulala; 
Luke19:48 kodwa kabatholanga abangakwenza, ngoba abantu bonke banamathela kuye be m lalela." 
Luke20:1 Kwasekusithi ngolunye lwalezonsuku, efundisa abantu ethempelini etshumayela ivangeli, ba m fikela abapristi abakhulu lababhali kanye labadala," 
Luke20:2 basebekhuluma laye, besithi: Sitshele, ukuthi izinto lezi uzenza ngaliphi igunya, kumbe ngubani okunike leligunya?" 
Luke20:3 Wasephendula wathi kubo: Lami ngizalibuza umbuzo ube munye, njalo lingitshele:" 
Luke20:4 Ubhabhathizo lukaJohane lwavela ezulwini, kumbe ebantwini?" 
Luke20:5 Basebezindlisana, besithi: Uba sisithi: Ezulwini; uzakuthi: Kungani-ke lingamkholwanga?" 
Luke20:6 Kodwa uba sisithi: Ebantwini; abantu bonke bazasikhanda ngamatshe. 
Luke20:7 Basebephendula ngokuthikabazi lapho o lwa vela khona. 
Luke20:8 UJesu wasesithi kubo: Lami kangilitsheli ukuthi ngenza lezizinto ngaliphi igunya. 
Luke20:9 Waseqala ukutshela abantu lumfanekiso, esithi: Umuntu othile wahlanyela isivini, wasiqatshisa kubalimi;" 
Luke20:10 kwathi ngesikhathi esifaneleyo wathuma inceku kubalimi, ukuze bayinike okwesithelo sesivini; kodwa abalimi bayitshaya ba yi thumeza ize." 
Luke20:11 Wasethuma njalo enye inceku; layo bayitshaya ba yi yangisa, ba yi thumeza ize." 
Luke20:12 Wasephinda ethuma leyesithathu; layo leyo ba yi limaza ba yi phosela ngaphandle. 
Luke20:13 Umninisivini wasesithi: Ngizakwenza njani? Ngizathuma indodana yami ethandekayo; mhlawumbe bebona yona baza yi hlonipha. 
Luke20:14 Kodwa abalimi beyibona bazindlisana, besithi: Le yindlalifa; wozani, siyibulale, ukuze ilifa libe ngelethu." 
Luke20:15 Bayiphosela ngaphandle kwesivini, ba yi bulala. Kambe uzakwenzani kubo umninisivini?" 
Luke20:16 Uzakuza, ababhubhise labobalimi, anikele isivini kwabanye. Be ku zwa basebesithi: Akungabi njalo!" 
Luke20:17 Kodwa wabakhangela wathi? 
Luke20:18 Wonke owela phezu kwalelolitshe, uzaphahlazwa; kodwa loba ngubani eliwela phezu kwakhe, lizamchoboza." 
Luke20:19 Abapristi abakhulu lababhali basebedinga ukumbamba ngezandla ngalelohola, kodwa besaba abantu; ngoba baqedisisa ukuthi wayekhuluma lumfanekiso emelane labo." 
Luke20:20 Basebe m qaphela. 
Luke20:21 Bambuza-ke, besithi: Mfundisi, siyazi ukuthi wena ukhuluma ufundise ngokuqondileyo, kawemukeli buso, kodwa ufundisa indlela kaNkulunkulu ngeqiniso." 
Luke20:22 Sivunyelwe yini ukuthela kuKesari, kumbe hatshi?" 
Luke20:23 Kodwa wabubona ubuqili babo, wathi kubo: Lingilingelani?" 
Luke20:24 Ngitshengisani udenariyo; ulomfanekiso lombhalo kabani? Basebephendula besithi: OkaKesari. 
Luke20:25 Wasesithi kubo: Ngakho nikani uKesari okukaKesari, loNkulunkulu okukaNkulunkulu." 
Luke20:26 Basebesehluleka ukumbamba ngelizwi lakhephambi kwabantu; basebemangaliswa yimpendulo yakhe, bathula." 
Luke20:27 Kwasekusiza kuye abathile babaSadusi, abaphika besithi kakukho ukuvuka kwabafileyo, bambuza," 
Luke20:28 besithi: Mfundisi, uMozisi wasibhalela ukuthi: Uba kusifa umfowabo womuntu elomkakhe, lo abesesifa engelamntwana, umfowabo kamthathe umfazi, abesemvusela inzalo umfowabo." 
Luke20:29 Ngakho kwakulezelamani eziyisikhombisa; owokuqala wasethatha umfazi, wafa engelamntwana;" 
Luke20:30 lowesibili wamthatha umfazi, laye lo wafa engelamntwana;" 
Luke20:31 lowesithathu wamthatha. Kwaba njalo-ke lakwabayisikhombisa; abatshiyanga abantwana, bafa." 
Luke20:32 Ekucineni kwabo bonke kwafa lomfazi. 
Luke20:33 Ngakho ekuvukeni kwabafileyo, uzafika abe ngumkabani kubo? Ngoba abayisikhombisa babelaye engumkabo." 
Luke20:34 UJesu wasephendula wathi kubo: Abantwana balumhlaba bayathatha, bendiswe;" 
Luke20:35 kodwa labo okuzathiwa bafanele ukuzuza lowomhlaba lokuvuka okwabafileyo kabathathani, kabendiswa;" 
Luke20:36 ngoba bengelakuphinda bafe; ngoba banjengezingilosi, njalo bangabantwana bakaNkulunkulu, bengabantwana bokuvuka." 
Luke20:37 Kodwa ukuthi abafileyo bayavuswa, loMozisi wakutshengisa esihlahleni." 
Luke20:38 Futhi kayisuye uNkulunkulu wabafileyo, kodwa owabaphilayo; ngoba bonke baphilela yena." 
Luke20:39 Abathile bababhali basebephendula bathi: Mfundisi, ukhulume kuhle." 
Luke20:40 Njalo kababanga lesibindi sokuphinda bambuze ulutho. 
Luke20:41 Wasesithi kubo: Batsho njani ukuthi uKristu uyiNdodana kaDavida? 
Luke20:42 Ngoba uDavida uqobo lwakhe uthi encwadini yeziHlabelelo: INkosi yathi eNkosini yami: Hlala ngakwesokunene sami," 
Luke20:43 ngize ngenze izitha zakho zibe yisenabelo senyawo zakho. 
Luke20:44 Ngakho uDavida umbiza ngokuthi yiNkosi, pho uyindodana yakhe njani?" 
Luke20:45 Kwathi besalalele abantu bonke, wathi kubafundi bakhe:" 
Luke20:46 Xwayani ababhali abathanda ukuhamba bembethe izembatho ezinde, njalo bethanda ukubingelelwa emidangeni, lezihlalo zabahloniphekayo ezilayelweni;" 
Luke20:47 abadla izindlu zabafelokazi, bekhuleka isikhathieside ngokuzenzisa. Laba bazakwemukela ukulahlwa okukhulu." 
Luke21:1 Wathi ephakamisa amehlo wabona abanothileyo. 
Luke21:2 Wabona lomfelokazi othile ongumyanga ephosela khona inhlamvana ezincane ezimbili zemali. 
Luke21:3 Wathi: Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Lumfelokazi ongumyanga uphosele okwedlula okwabo bonke; 
Luke21:4 ngoba bonke laba baphosele kokunengi kwabo eminikelweni kaNkulunkulu, kodwa yena ebuyangeni bakhe uphosele konke alakho abephila ngakho." 
Luke21:5 Abanye besakhuluma ngethempeli, ukuthi liceciswe ngamatshe amahle langezipho, wathi:" 
Luke21:6 Lezizinto elizibonayo, kuzafika insuku okungayikutshiywa ngazo ilitshe phezu kwelitshe, elingayikudilizelwa phansi." 
Luke21:7 Basebembuza, besithi: Mfundisi, pho lezizinto zizakuba nini? Lesibonakaliso siyini, lapho sekuzakwenzeka lezizinto?" 
Luke21:8 Wasesithi: Qaphelani ukuthi lingaduhiswa; ngoba abanengi bazakuza ebizweni lami. 
Luke21:9 Njalo nxa lisizwa ngezimpi langeziphithiphithi. 
Luke21:10 Wasesithi kubo: Isizwe sizavukela isizwe, lombuso u vuk ele umbuso;" 
Luke21:11 njalo kuzakuba khona ukuzamazama komhlaba okukhulu indawo ngendawo lezindlala labomatshayabhuqe bezifo; kube khona lezinto ezesabekayo lezibonakaliso ezinkulu ezivela ezulwini. 
Luke21:12 Kodwa ngaphambi kwakho konke lokhu bazalibamba ngezandla zabo, ba li zingele." 
Luke21:13 Njalo lokhukuzaphenduka kini kube yibufakazi. 
Luke21:14 Ngakho kubekeni enhliziyweni zenu; 
Luke21:15 ngoba mina ngizalinika umlomo lenhlakanipho, abangekuphike, bamelane lakho, bonke abayizitha zenu." 
Luke21:16 Njalo lizanikelwa langabazali labafowenu lezihlobo labangane, njalo bazabulala abanyebenu." 
Luke21:17 Njalo lizazondwa yibo bonke ngenxa yebizo lami. 
Luke21:18 Kodwa kakuyikulahleka ngitsho unwele lwekhanda lenu. 
Luke21:19 Ekubekezeleni kwenu. 
Luke21:20 Kodwa nxa libona iJerusalema ihanqwe ngamabutho. 
Luke21:21 Ngalesosikhathi abaseJudiya kababalekele ezintabeni; labaphakathi kwayo baphume; labasemaphandleni. 
Luke21:22 Ngoba lezi zinsuku zempindiselo. 
Luke21:23 Kodwa maye kwabakhulelweyo labamunyisayo ngalezonsuku! Ngoba kuzakuba khona ukuhlupheka okukhulu emhlabeni, lolaka kulesisizwe." 
Luke21:24 Njalo bazakuwa ngobukhali benkemba, bathunjelwe ezizweni zonke." 
Luke21:25 Kuzakuba khona izibonakaliso elangeni lenyangeni lezinkanyezini; lemhlabeni usizi lwezizwe ngokudideka; kudume ulwandle lamagagasi," 
Luke21:26 abantu baphele amandla ngenxa yokwesaba langokubona lokho okuzayo emhlabeni; ngoba amandla amazulu azazanyazanyiswa. 
Luke21:27 Khona-ke bezayibona iNdodana yomuntu isiza eyezini ilamandla lenkazimulo enkulu. 
Luke21:28 Njalo nxa kuqala ukwenzeka lezizinto, manini liqonde njalo liphakamise amakhanda enu." 
Luke21:29 Wasebatshela umfanekiso: Khangelani umkhiwa lazo zonke izihlahla; 
Luke21:30 nxa sezihluma, liyazibonela lani likwazi ukuthi ihlobo selisondele." 
Luke21:31 Ngokunjalo lani, nxa libona lezizinto zisenzeka, yazini ukuthi umbuso kaNkulunkulu useduze." 
Luke21:32 Ngiqinisile ngithi kini: Lesisizukulwana asisoze sidlule, kuze kwenzeke zonke izinto." 
Luke21:33 Kuzadlula izulu lomhlaba, kodwa amazwi ami kawasoze adlule." 
Luke21:34 Njalo ziqapheleni; 
Luke21:35 ngoba luzafika njengomjibila phezu kwabo bonke abahlezi ebusweni bomhlaba wonke. 
Luke21:36 Ngakho lindani ngezikhathi zonke. 
Luke21:37 Njalo wayefundisa. 
Luke21:38 Lekuseni kakhulu abantu bonke babesiza kuye. 
Luke22:1 Kwasekusondela umkhosi wesinkwa esingelamvubelo, othiwa liphasika." 
Luke22:2 Abapristi abakhulu lababhali basebedinga ukuthi bangambulala njani; ngoba babesesaba abantu. 
Luke22:3 USathane, owayengowenani labalitshumi lambili." 
Luke22:4 Wasesuka wayakhuluma labapristi abakhulu lezinduna ngokuthi angamnikela njani kubo. 
Luke22:5 Basebethokoza, basebevumelana ukumnika imali." 
Luke22:6 Yena wasevuma, njalo wadinga ithuba elihle lokumnikela kubo lingekho ixuku." 
Luke22:7 Lwaselufika usuku lwesinkwa esingelamvubelo, okwakumele kuhlatshwe ngalo iphasika." 
Luke22:8 Wasethuma uPetro loJohane, esithi: Hambani li ye silungisela iphasika, ukuze sidle." 
Luke22:9 Basebesithi kuye: Uthanda ukuthi silungise ngaphi? 
Luke22:10 Wasesithi kubo: Khangelani, kuzakuthi selingenile emzini, umuntu uzahlangana lani ethwele imbiza yamanzi; limlandele endlini azangena kuyo." 
Luke22:11 Beselisithi kumninindlu: Uthi uMfundisi kuwe: Ingaphi indlu yezihambi, lapho engingadlela khona iphasika labafundi bami?" 
Luke22:12 Yena-ke uzalitshengisa indlu enkulu ephezulu eyendlelweyo; lilungise khona. 
Luke22:13 Bahamba-ke bafica njengokutsho kwakhe kubo; basebelungisa iphasika. 
Luke22:14 Kwathi selifikile ihola, wahlala phansi." 
Luke22:15 Wasesithi kubo: Ngokunxwanela nginxwanele ukudla lani leliphasika ngingakahlupheki; 
Luke22:16 ngoba ngithi kini: Kangisoze ngidle futhi kulo, lize ligcwaliseke." 
Luke22:17 Wasethatha inkezo, esebongile wathi: Thathani lokhu, beselisabelana;" 
Luke22:18 ngoba ngithi kini: Kangisoze nginathe okwesithelo sevini, kuze kufike umbuso kaNkulunkulu." 
Luke22:19 Wasethatha isinkwa. 
Luke22:20 Ngokunjalo lenkezo emva kokudla, esithi: Inkezo le iyisivumelwano esitsha egazini lami, elichithelwa lina." 
Luke22:21 Kodwa khangelani, isandla songinikelayo silami etafuleni." 
Luke22:22 Ngoba isibili iNdodana yomuntu ihamba; kodwa maye kulowomuntu enikelwa nguye! 
Luke22:23 Bona basebeqala ukubuzana ukuthi kambe ngubani kubo ozakwenza lokho. 
Luke22:24 Kwavela lokuphikisana phakathi kwabo. 
Luke22:25 Wasesithi kubo: Amakhosi abezizwe azibusa ngobulukhuni, leziphathamandla zazo zithiwa ngabasizi." 
Luke22:26 Kodwa lina kakungabi njalo; kodwa omkhulu phakathi kwenu, longumkhokheli njengosebenzayo." 
Luke22:27 Ngoba nguwuphi omkhulu. 
Luke22:28 Lina-ke liyibo ababehlezi lami ezilingweni zami; 
Luke22:29 njalo mina ngilimisele," 
Luke22:30 ukuthi lidle linathe etafuleni lami embusweni wami. 
Luke22:31 INkosi yasisithi: Simoni, Simoni, khangela, uSathane ulifunisisile;" 
Luke22:32 kodwa mina ngikukhulekele. 
Luke22:33 Kodwa wathi kuye: Nkosi, lentolongweni." 
Luke22:34 Kodwa yena wathi: Ngiyakutshela, Petro, iqhude kaliyikukhala lamuhla, ungakaphiki kathathu ukuthi uyangazi." 
Luke22:35 Wasesithi kubo: Mhla ngilithuma, laswela yini ulutho? Basebesithi: Kakulalutho." 
Luke22:36 Wasesithi kubo: Kodwa khathesi lowo olomxhaka ka wu thathe, ngokunjalo lesikhwama; lalowo ongelakho, athengise isembatho sakhe, athenge inkemba." 
Luke22:37 Ngoba ngithi kini, kusamele kugcwaliseke kimi lokhu okulotshiweyo, ukuthi: Wabalwa kanye lezoni." 
Luke22:38 Basebesithi: Nkosi, khangela, nanzi inkemba ezimbili. Wasesithi kubo: Kwanele." 
Luke22:39 Wasephuma; labafundi bakhe bamlandela. 
Luke22:40 Esefikile kuleyondawo, wathi kubo." 
Luke22:41 Yena wasemonyuka kubo okungaba libangalokuphosa ilitshe, waguqa phansi ngamadolo wakhuleka," 
Luke22:42 esithi: Baba, uba uthanda, susa linkezo kimi; kodwa-ke kungenziwa intando yami, kodwa eyakho." 
Luke22:43 Kwabonakala kuye ingilosi evela ezulwini imqinisa. 
Luke22:44 Esesesizini olunzima, wakhuleka kakhulu. Njalo izithukuthuku zakhe zaba njengamathonsi egazi zawela emhlabathini." 
Luke22:45 Esesukumile emkhulekweni, weza kubafundi bakhe, wabafica belele ngenxa yokudabuka," 
Luke22:46 wasesithi kubo: Lilaleleni? Vukani likhuleke, ukuze lingangeni ekulingweni." 
Luke22:47 Kwathi esakhuluma, khangela, ixuku, lalowo okuthiwa nguJudasi, omunye wabalitshumi lambili, ehamba phambi kwabo, wasesondela kuJesu ukumanga." 
Luke22:48 Kodwa uJesu wathi kuye: Judasi, uyayinikela yini iNdodana yomuntu ngokuyanga?" 
Luke22:49 Kwathi labo ababengakuye sebebona okuzakwenzeka bathi kuye: Nkosi, sigadle yini ngenkemba?" 
Luke22:50 Omunye wabo wasegadla inceku yompristi omkhulu, waquma indlebe yayo yokunene." 
Luke22:51 Kodwa uJesu waphendula wathi: Yekelani kuze kube yilokhu. Wasethinta indlebe yayo, wayisilisa." 
Luke22:52 UJesu wasesithi kubapristi abakhulu lezinduna zethempeli labadala ababeze kuye: Liphume njengokuyamelana lomphangi yini lilezinkemba lezinduku? 
Luke22:53 Nxa bengilani insuku ngensuku ethempelini, kalelulanga izandla ukumelana lami; kodwa leli lihola lenu." 
Luke22:54 Sebembambile ba m qhuba, bamusa endlini yompristi omkhulu." 
Luke22:55 Sebebasile umlilo, sebehlezi phansi ndawonye, uPetro wahlala phakathi kwabo." 
Luke22:56 Kodwa incekukazi ethile imbona ehlezi emlilweni, yamjolozela, yathi: Lumuntu laye ube laye." 
Luke22:57 Kodwa wamphika, wathi: Mama, kangimazi." 
Luke22:58 Emva kwesikhatshana omunye: Lawe ungomunye wabo. Kodwa uPetro wathi: Ndoda, kangisu ye." 
Luke22:59 Sekungaba kwedlule ihola elilodwa, omunye waqinisa, esithi: Isibili laye ube laye; ngoba futhi ungumGalili." 
Luke22:60 Kodwa uPetro wathi: Ndoda, kangazi ukuthi uthini. Njalo khonokho esakhuluma lakhala iqhude." 
Luke22:61 INkosi yasiphenduka yamkhangela uPetro. 
Luke22:62 UPetro wasephuma phandle wakhala ngokubabayo. 
Luke22:63 Lamadoda ayembambile uJesu. 
Luke22:64 Amembesa, amtshaya ubuso, asembuza, esithi: Profetha! Ngubani okutshayileyo?" 
Luke22:65 Akhuluma lezinye izinto ezinengi kuye ehlambaza. 
Luke22:66 Kwathi sekusile, bathi:" 
Luke22:67 Uba unguKristu, sitshele. Wasesithi kubo: Uba ngilitshela, kalisoze likholwe;" 
Luke22:68 njalo uba lami ngilibuza, kalisoze lingiphendule, loba li ngi khulule." 
Luke22:69 Kusukela khathesi iNdodana yomuntu izahlala ngakwesokunene samandla kaNkulunkulu. 
Luke22:70 Basebesithi bonke: Kanti uyiNdodana kaNkulunkulu. 
Luke22:71 Basebesithi: Pho sisafunelani ubufakazi? Ngoba sesizizwele uqobo lwethu emlonyeni wakhe. 
Luke23:1 Kwasekusukuma ixuku labo lonke, lamusa kuPilatu." 
Luke23:2 Baqala ukummangalela, besithi: Simficile lo eduhisa isizwe." 
Luke23:3 UPilatu wasembuza? Wasemphendula wathi: Uyatsho wena. 
Luke23:4 Wasesithi uPilatu kubapristi abakhulu lemaxukwini: Kangitholi cala kulumuntu. 
Luke23:5 Kodwa baqinisa, besithi: Udunga abantu, efundisa kuyo yonke iJudiya." 
Luke23:6 Lapho uPilatu esizwa kuthiwaiGalili wabuza ukuthi lumuntu ungumGalili yini. 
Luke23:7 Kwathi esezwile ukuthi ungowombuso kaHerodi. 
Luke23:8 Kwathi uHerodi embona uJesu wathokoza kakhulu; ngoba wayekade ethanda ukumbona. 
Luke23:9 Wambuza ngamazwi amanengi; kodwa yena kamphendulanga lutho. 
Luke23:10 Abapristi abakhulu lababhali babemi, bemmangalela ngamandla." 
Luke23:11 UHerodi lamabutho akhe. 
Luke23:12 Ngalolosuku uHerodi kanye loPilatu baba ngabangane omunye komunye; ngoba ngaphambi kwalokhu babelobutha phakathi kwabo. 
Luke23:13 UPilatu wasebizela ndawonye abapristi abakhulu lababusi labantu," 
Luke23:14 wathi kubo: Limlethile kimi lumuntu; 
Luke23:15 hatshi ngitsho loHerodi; ngoba ngilithumeze kuye, njalo khangelani, kakulalutho olufanele ukufa olwenziwe nguye." 
Luke23:16 Ngakho ngizamtshaya ngi m khulule. 
Luke23:17 Kwakufanele ukuthi abakhululele abe munye ngomkhosi. 
Luke23:18 Bamemeza bonke kanyekanye besithi: Msuse lo, usikhululele uBarabasi" 
Luke23:19 (owayephoselwe entolongweni ngenxa yomvukela othile owenzeka phakathi komuzi langenxa yokubulala). 
Luke23:20 Ngakho uPilatu wabuya wakhuluma labo, efuna ukumkhulula uJesu." 
Luke23:21 Kodwa bamemeza, besithi: Bethela, mbethele!" 
Luke23:22 Wasesithi kubo ngokwesithathu: Ngoba lo enze bubi bani. 
Luke23:23 Kodwa baqinisa ngamazwi amakhulu, befuna ukuthi abethelwe; lamazwi abo lawabapristi abakhulu aphumelela." 
Luke23:24 UPilatu wasequma ukuthi kwenziwe isicelo sabo. 
Luke23:25 Wasebakhululela lowo ababemcelile owayephoselwe entolongweni ngenxa yomvukela lokubulala. 
Luke23:26 Kwathi sebemqhuba, babamba uSimoni othile umKurene owayevela emaphandleni, bamethesa isiphambano, ukuthi asi thwale ngemva kukaJesu." 
Luke23:27 Laselimlandela ixuku elikhulu labantu, labesifazana labo ababekhala bemlilela." 
Luke23:28 Kodwa uJesu ephendukela kubo wathi: Madodakazi eJerusalema, lingangikhaleli mina, kodwa zikhaleleni lina labantwana benu," 
Luke23:29 ngoba khangelani, ziyeza insuku abazakutsho ngazo ukuthi: Zibusisiwe inyumba, lezizalo ezingazalanga, lamabele angamunyisanga." 
Luke23:30 Khona bezaqalisa ukuthi ezintabeni: Welani phezu kwethu; lemaqaqeni: Sisibekeleni. 
Luke23:31 Ngoba uba besenza lezizinto esihlahleni esimanzi? 
Luke23:32 Kwaqhutshwa labanye abenzi bobubi ababili. 
Luke23:33 Sebefikile endaweni ethiwa luKhakhayi, bambethela khona." 
Luke23:34 UJesu wasesithi: Baba. 
Luke23:35 Labantu bema babukela. 
Luke23:36 Labebutho bamklolodela," 
Luke23:37 besithi: Uba wena uyiNkosi yamaJuda, zisindise wena." 
Luke23:38 Kwakukhona lombhalo ngaphezu kwakhe. 
Luke23:39 Lomunye wabenzi bobubi ababelengisiwe. 
Luke23:40 Kodwa omunye waphendula emkhuza, esithi: Wena kawumesabi yini uNkulunkulu, lokhu lawe ukulokhukulahlwa?" 
Luke23:41 Thina kambe kusilungele, ngoba semukela okulingene ukwenza kwethu; kodwa lo kenzanga lutho olungafanelanga." 
Luke23:42 Wasesithi kuJesu: Ungikhumbule, Nkosi, lapha ufika embusweni wakho." 
Luke23:43 UJesu wasesithi kuye: Ngiqinisile ngithi kuwe: Lamuhla uzakuba lami eParadise. 
Luke23:44 Kwakungaba lihola lesithupha, kwaba khona ubumnyama phezu komhlaba wonke kwaze kwaba lihola lesificamunwemunye," 
Luke23:45 futhi ilanga lalifiphaziwe. 
Luke23:46 UJesu wasememeza ngelizwi elikhulu esithi. 
Luke23:47 Kwathi induna yekhulu isibonile okwenzekileyo, isithi: Isibili lumuntu ubelungile." 
Luke23:48 Lamaxuku wonke ayebuthene ukubukela lokho, sebebonile izinto ezenzekileyo, babuyela bezitshaya izifuba." 
Luke23:49 Bonke abazana laye, bema khatshana, bebona lezizinto." 
Luke23:50 Njalo khangela, indoda ethiwa nguJosefa;" 
Luke23:51 yena wayengavumelananga lecebo lesenzo sabo; waye vela eArimathiya umuzi wamaJuda, laye ngokwakhe;" 
Luke23:52 lowo wasuka waya kuPilatu wacela isidumbu sikaJesu. 
Luke23:53 Wasesethula wasigoqela ngelembu elicolekileyo, wasibeka engcwabeni elaligujwe edwaleni, lapho okwakungazanga kubekwe khona umuntu." 
Luke23:54 Kwakulusuku lwamalungiselelo, lesabatha." 
Luke23:55 Labesifazana, ababeze laye bevela eGalili." 
Luke23:56 Basebebuyela emuva balungisa amakha lamagcobo. 
Luke24:1 Kodwa ngo sukulokuqala lweviki. 
Luke24:2 Bafica ilitshe ligiqiwe lasuswa engcwabeni. 
Luke24:3 Kuthe bengena kabasitholanga isidumbu seNkosi uJesu. 
Luke24:4 Kwasekusithi bedidekile kakhulu ngalokhu; 
Luke24:5 njalo besesaba, bakhothamisa ubuso emhlabathini, athi kubo: Lidingelani ophilayo kwabafileyo?" 
Luke24:6 Kakho lapha, kodwa uvukile; khumbulani ukuthi wakhuluma njani kini, eseseGalili," 
Luke24:7 esithi: INdodana yomuntu imele ukunikelwa ezandleni zabantu abayizoni, ibethelwe." 
Luke24:8 Basebewakhumbula amazwi akhe. 
Luke24:9 Sebebuyile bevela engcwabeni, babika konke lokhu kwabalitshumi lanye lakubo bonke abanye." 
Luke24:10 KwakunguMariya Magadalena. 
Luke24:11 Kodwa amazwi abo akhanya kibo njengokukhuluma okuyize, futhi kabaze bawakholwa." 
Luke24:12 Kodwa uPetro wasukuma wagijimela engcwabeni. 
Luke24:13 Futhi khangela, ngalona lolosuku ababili babo babehamba besiya emzaneni, obizo lawo yiEmawusi." 
Luke24:14 Njalo bona babekhulumisana ngazo zonke lezizinto ezenzekileyo. 
Luke24:15 Kwasekusithi bekhulumisana bebuzana, uJesu uqobo wasondela wahamba kanye labo," 
Luke24:16 kodwa amehlo abo ayebanjiwe ukuze bangamazi. 
Luke24:17 Wasesithi kubo: Ngamazwi bani la elikhulumisana ngawo lihamba, lidanile?" 
Luke24:18 Omunye, obizo lakhe linguKleyopha, wasephendula wathi kuye: Wena nguwe wedwa isihambi eJerusalema, njalo esingaziyo yini izinto ezenzekileyo phakathi kwayo kulezinsuku?" 
Luke24:19 Wasesithi kubo: Yizinto bani? Basebesithi kuye: Ezimayelana loJesu weNazaretha, obeyindoda umprofethi;" 
Luke24:20 lokuthi abapristi abakhulu. 
Luke24:21 Kodwa thina besithemba ukuthi nguye obezakhulula uIsrayeli. Kodwa-ke phezu kwakho konke lokhu lamuhla lusuku lwesithathu selokhu lezizinto zenzakele. 
Luke24:22 Kodwa njalo abesifazana abathile abangakithi basimangalisile; 
Luke24:23 kuthe bengasitholi isidumbu sakhe. 
Luke24:24 Labathile abebelathi baya engcwabeni, bafica kunjalo njengokutsho kwabesifazana labo; kodwa yena kabambonanga." 
Luke24:25 Yena wasesithi kubo: O lina elingelakuqedisisa elilenhliziyo ezivilaphela ukukholwa konke lokho abaprofethi abalitshela khona! 
Luke24:26 UKristu ubengamele yini ukuthi ahlupheke ngalezizinto, abesengena ebukhosini bakhe?" 
Luke24:27 Esesusela. 
Luke24:28 Basebesondela emzaneni ababesiya kuwo; yena wasesenza angathi uyedlula. 
Luke24:29 Kodwa bamcindezela, besithi: Hlala lathi, ngoba sekuzakuhlwa. Wangena-ke ukuze ahlale labo." 
Luke24:30 Kwasekusithi ehlezi ekudleni labo, wathatha isinkwa wa si busisa, wa si hlephuna wabanika." 
Luke24:31 Amehlo abo asevuleka. 
Luke24:32 Basebekhulumisana besithi: Kambe inhliziyo zethu bezingavuthi yini phakathi kwethu? 
Luke24:33 Basebesukuma ngalelohola, babuyela eJerusalema, bafica abalitshumi lanye bebuthene ndawonye," 
Luke24:34 besithi: Isibili iNkosi ivukile, ibonwe nguSimoni." 
Luke24:35 Basebelandisa okw enzekileyoendleleni, lokuthi yaziwa njani yibo ekuhlephuneni isinkwa." 
Luke24:36 Besakhuluma lezizinto. 
Luke24:37 Kodwa batshaywa luvalo besaba. 
Luke24:38 Wasesithi kubo: Likhathazekelani, njalo kuvukelani imicabango enhliziyweni zenu?" 
Luke24:39 Khangelani izandla zami lenyawo zami, ukuthi yimi uqobo; ngibambani libone." 
Luke24:40 Esekutshilo lokho wabatshengisa izandla lenyawo zakhe. 
Luke24:41 Kodwa belokhu bengakholwa? 
Luke24:42 Bamnika iqatha lenhlanzi eyosiweyo, lohlanga lwenyosi." 
Luke24:43 Wase ku thatha wa ku dla phambi kwabo. 
Luke24:44 Wasesithi kubo: Yila amazwi, engawakhuluma kini ngiseselani okuthi." 
Luke24:45 Wasevula ingqondo yabo, ukuze baqedisise imibhalo;" 
Luke24:46 wasesithi kubo: Kulotshiwe kanje, njalo uKristu kumele ahlupheke kanje," 
Luke24:47 njalo kutshunyayelwe ebizweni lakhe ukuphenduka lothethelelo lwezono. 
Luke24:48 Lina-ke lingabafakazi balezizinto. 
Luke24:49 Futhi khangelani, mina ngiyathumela kini isithembiso sikaBaba; kodwa lina hlalani emzini weJerusalema." 
Luke24:50 Wasebakhokhela ephuma phandle baze bafika eBethani; ephakamisa izandla zakhe wababusisa. 
Luke24:51 Kwasekusithi esababusisa, wehlukana labo, wenyukiselwa ezulwini." 
Luke24:52 Basebemkhonza; 
Luke24:53 baqhubeka besethempelini. Ameni. 
John1:1 Ekuqaleni. 
John1:2 Yena lo wayeloNkulunkulu ekuqaleni. 
John1:3 Zonke izinto zenziwa ngaye, njalo ngaphandle kwakhe kakulalutho lolulodwa olwenziwayo lolo olwenziweyo." 
John1:4 Impilo yayikuye," 
John1:5 lokukhanya kukhanya. 
John1:6 Kwavela umuntu ethunywe nguNkulunkulu; 
John1:7 yena lo wezela ubufakazi, ukuze afakaze ngokukhanya, ukuze bonke bakholwe ngaye." 
John1:8 Yena wayengayisikho ukukhanya, kodwa ukuze afakaze ngokukhanya." 
John1:9 Kwakuyikukhanya okuqotho. 
John1:10 Wayekhona emhlabeni, njalo umhlaba wenziwa ngaye, kodwa umhlaba kawumazanga." 
John1:11 Weza kokwakhe. 
John1:12 Kodwa bonke abamemukelayo, wabapha amandla okuthi babe ngabantwana bakaNkulunkulu, labo abakholwa ebizweni lakhe;" 
John1:13 abazalwa kungeyisikho ngegazi, langentando yenyama." 
John1:14 ULizwi. 
John1:15 UJohane wafakaza ngaye. 
John1:16 Lekugcwaleni kwakhe thina semukele sonke, futhi umusa ngomusa;" 
John1:17 ngoba umlayo wanikwa ngoMozisi. 
John1:18 Kakho. 
John1:19 Njalo lobu yibufakazi bukaJohane? 
John1:20 Wasevuma, kaphikanga; futhi wavuma wathi: Kangisuye uKristu mina." 
John1:21 Bambuza futhi bathi: Kuyini pho? Wena unguElija yini? Wasephendula wathi: Hatshi. 
John1:22 Basebesithi kuye: Ungubani? Ukuze sibaphe impendulo abasithumileyo; uthini ngawe? 
John1:23 Wathi: Mina ngiyilizwi lomemezayo enkangala. 
John1:24 Lalabo ababethunyiwe babevela kubaFarisi. 
John1:25 Basebembuza, bathi kuye: Ubhabhathizelani pho?" 
John1:26 UJohane wabaphendula, wathi: Mina ngibhabhathiza ngamanzi;" 
John1:27 nguye ozayo emva kwami, ophambi kwami." 
John1:28 Lezizinto zenzeka eBethabara. 
John1:29 Kusisa uJohane wabona uJesu esiza kuye, wathi: Khangelani iWundlu likaNkulunkulu." 
John1:30 Nguye lo mina ebengi li tshela ngaye ukuthi: Emva kwami kuza indoda, eyayikhona phambi kwami." 
John1:31 Lami bengingamazi; kodwa ukuze abonakaliswe kuIsrayeli. 
John1:32 UJohane wasefakaza. 
John1:33 Lami bengingamazi; kodwa owangithumayo ukubhabhathiza ngamanzi, yena wathi kimi: Lowo ozabona uMoya esehlela phezu kwakhe ahlale kuye, nguye obhabhathiza ngoMoya oNgcwele." 
John1:34 Mina ngibonile, ngafakaza." 
John1:35 Kusisa futhi uJohane wayemi, lababili kubafundi bakhe;" 
John1:36 wasekhangela uJesu ehambahamba. 
John1:37 Abafundi ababili bamuzwa ekhuluma, basebemlandela uJesu." 
John1:38 Kwathi uJesu enyemukula ebabona belandela, wathi kibo: Lidingani?" 
John1:39 Wathi kibo: Wozani libone. Beza babona lapho ayehlala khona; bahlala laye ngalolosuku; kwakungaba lihola letshumi. 
John1:40 UAndreya umfowabo kaSimoni Petro wayengomunye wababili ababe ku zwe ngoJohane bamlandela. 
John1:41 Yena wathola kuqala umfowabo uqobo uSimoni. 
John1:42 Wasemletha kuJesu. UJesu esemkhangele wathi. 
John1:43 Kusisa, wathola uFiliphu, wathi kuye: Ngilandela." 
John1:44 UFiliphu-ke, emzini wakibo kaAndreya loPetro." 
John1:45 UFiliphu wathola uNathaniyeli. 
John1:46 UNathaniyeli wasesithi kuye: Kambe kungavela okuhle eNazaretha? UFiliphu wathi kuye: Woza ubone. 
John1:47 UJesu wabona uNathaniyeli esiza kuye, wathi ngaye: Khangelani umIsrayeli uqobo." 
John1:48 UNathaniyeli wathi kuye: Ungazela ngaphi? UJesu waphendula wathi kuye: UFiliphu engakakubizi, ungaphansi komkhiwa, ngakubona." 
John1:49 UNathaniyeli waphendula wathi kuye: Rabi. 
John1:50 UJesu waphendula wathi kuye: Uyakholwa ngoba ngithe kuwe, bengikubona ungaphansi komkhiwa. Uzabona izinto ezinkulu kulalezi." 
John1:51 Wasesithi kuye: Ngiqinisile, ngiqinisile, ngithi kini: Kusukela khathesi." 
John2:1 Kwathi ngosuku lwesithathu kwaba khona umtshado; lonina kaJesu wayekhona lapho; 
John2:2 njalo uJesu laye wayenxusiwe labafundi bakhe. 
John2:3 Kwathi iwayini selisweleka, unina kaJesu wathi kuye: Kabalalo iwayini." 
John2:4 UJesu wathi kuye: Mama. 
John2:5 Unina wathi kuzinceku: Yenzani loba yikuphi azalitshela khona. 
John2:6 Kwakukhona lapho imbiza zamanzi ezamatshe zimiswe njengokokuhlambulula kwamaJuda. 
John2:7 UJesu wathi kuzo: Gcwalisani imbiza zamanzi ngamanzi. Zasezizigcwalisa zathi kliki. 
John2:8 Wasesithi kuzo: Khanini khathesi, lise kumphathi wokudla. Zasezikusa." 
John2:9 Umphathi wokudla, engazi ukuthi livela ngaphi (kodwa inceku ezaziwakhile amanzi zazisazi), umphathi wokudla wabiza umyeni," 
John2:10 wasesithi kuye: Wonke umuntu uletha iwayini elimnandi kuqala, kuthi lapho sebenathile kakhulu, abese lethaelibi; wena ugcinile iwayini elimnandi kwaze kwaba khathesi." 
John2:11 Lokho kuyikuqala kwezibonakaliso uJesu akwenza eKana yeGalili; labafundi bakhe bakholwa kuye. 
John2:12 Emva kwalokho wehlela eKapenawume, labafundi bakhe; njalo bahlala khona kungeyisikho okwensuku ezinengi." 
John2:13 Iphasika lamaJuda laselisondele. 
John2:14 Wafica ethempelini labo abathengisa inkabi lezimvu lamajuba, labantshintshi bemali behlezi." 
John2:15 Esenze isiswepu sezintambo wabaxotsha bonke ethempelini, izimvu kanye lenkabi; wachitha imali yabantshintshisayo, wagenqula amatafula;" 
John2:16 wasesithi kwabathengisa amajuba: Susani lezizinto lapha; lingayenzi indlu kaBaba indlu yokuthengisela. 
John2:17 Abafundi bakhe basebekhumbula ukuthi kulotshiwe ukuthi: Ukutshisekela indlu yakho kungidlile. 
John2:18 Ngakho amaJuda aphendula athi kuye? 
John2:19 UJesu waphendula wathi kuwo: Dilizani. 
John2:20 AmaJuda asesithi: Okweminyaka engamatshumi amane lesithupha lelithempeli lakhiwa, wena-ke uzalivusa ngensuku ezintathu yini?" 
John2:21 Kodwa yena wayekhuluma ngethempeli lomzimba wakhe. 
John2:22 Ngakho, kwathi esevukile kwabafileyo, abafundi bakhe bakhumbula ukuthi wayekutshilo lokhu kubo." 
John2:23 Njalo kwathi eseJerusalema ngephasika, emkhosini, abanengi bakholwa ebizweni lakhe, bebona izibonakaliso zakhe azenzayo;" 
John2:24 kodwa uJesu ngokwakhe kazinikelanga yena kubo, ngoba yena wayebazi bonke," 
John2:25 langenxa yokuthi wayengasweli ukuthi loba ngubani afakaze ngomuntu; ngoba yena wayekwazi okusemuntwini. 
John3:1 Kwakukhona-ke umuntu wakubaFarisi, nguNikodima ibizo lakhe;" 
John3:2 lo weza kuJesu. 
John3:3 UJesu waphendula wathi kuye: Ngiqinisile, ngiqinisile, ngithi kuwe: Ngaphandle kokuthi umuntu azalwe, angewubone umbuso kaNkulunkulu." 
John3:4 UNikodima wathi kuye: Umuntu angazalwa njani esemdala? Angangena yini ngokwesibili esiswini sikanina azalwe? 
John3:5 UJesu waphendula wathi: Ngiqinisile, ngiqinisile, ngithi kuwe: Uba umuntu engazalwanga ngamanzi, angengene embusweni kaNkulunkulu." 
John3:6 Lokho okuzelwe yinyama kuyinyama; lalokho okuzelwe nguMoya kungumoya. 
John3:7 Ungamangali ukuthi ngithe kuwe: Kufanele ukuthi lizalwe ngokutsha. 
John3:8 Umoya uphephethela lapho othanda khona, uyawuzwa umdumo wawo, kodwa kawazi lapho ovela khona lalapho oya khona; unjalo wonke ozelwe nguMoya." 
John3:9 UNikodima waphendula wathi kuye: Lezizinto zingenzeka njani? 
John3:10 UJesu waphendula wathi kuye: Wena ungumfundisi wakoIsrayeli, kodwa kawuzazi lezizinto yini?" 
John3:11 Ngiqinisile, ngiqinisile, ngithi kuwe: Sikhuluma esikwaziyo, sifakaze esikubonileyo." 
John3:12 Nxa ngilitshelile izinto zomhlaba njalo lingakholwa, lizakholwa njani, uba ngilitshela izinto zezulwini?" 
John3:13 Njalo kakho owake wenyukela ezulwini. 
John3:14 Futhi njengoba uMozisi waphakamisa inyoka enkangala; 
John3:15 ukuze wonke okholwa kuyo angabhubhi. 
John3:16 Ngoba uNkulunkulu wawuthanda umhlaba ngokunjalo. 
John3:17 Ngoba uNkulunkulu kayithumanga iNdodana yakhe emhlabeni. 
John3:18 Okholwa kiyo kalahlwa. 
John3:19 Ukulahlwa kuyilokhu, ukuthi ukukhanya kufikile emhlabeni." 
John3:20 Ngoba wonke. 
John3:21 Kodwa owenza iqiniso uyeza ekukhanyeni, ukuze imisebenzi yakhe ibonakale, ukuthi yenziwe kuNkulunkulu." 
John3:22 Emva kwalezizinto uJesu weza elizweni leJudiya. 
John3:23 UJohane laye wayebhabhathiza eEnoni. 
John3:24 Ngoba uJohane wayengakaphoselwa entolongweni. 
John3:25 Kwasekusiba khona ukuphikisana phakathi kwabafundi bakaJohane lamaJuda ngokuhlambulula. 
John3:26 Basebesiza kuJohane bathi kuye: Rabi, khangela yena uyabhabhathiza, njalo bayeza kuye bonke." 
John3:27 UJohane waphendula wathi: Umuntu angemukele ulutho. 
John3:28 Lina ngokwenu liyangifakazela ukuthi ngathi: Kangisuye uKristu mina. 
John3:29 Olomakoti ungumyeni; ngakho lintokozo yami isiphelele. 
John3:30 Umele ukukhula yena, kodwa mina nginciphe." 
John3:31 Ovela. 
John3:32 Lalokho akubonileyo. 
John3:33 Owemukele ubufakazi bakhe uphawulile. 
John3:34 Ngoba lowo uNkulunkulu amthumileyo, ukhuluma amazwi kaNkulunkulu." 
John3:35 UYise uyayithanda iNdodana. 
John3:36 Yena okholwa eNdodaneni ulempilo elaphakade; kodwa yena ongakholwayo eNdodaneni, kayikubona impilo, kodwa ulaka lukaNkulunkulu luhlezi phezu kwakhe." 
John4:1 Kwathi-ke iNkosi isisazi ukuthi abaFarisi sebezwile ukuthi uJesu wenza wabhabhathiza abafundi abanengi kuloJohane," 
John4:2 lanxa uJesu ngokwakhe wayengabhabhathizi, kodwa abafundi bakhe," 
John4:3 wasuka eJudiya. 
John4:4 Kodwa kwakumele. 
John4:5 Wafika-ke emzini weSamariya okuthiwa yiSikari; 
John4:6 lomthombo kaJakobe wawulapho. Ngakho uJesu ekhathele ngohambo. 
John4:7 Kwafika owesifazana evela eSamariya ukuzakukha amanzi; uJesu wathi kuye: Nginathisa 
John4:8 (ngoba abafundi bakhe babehambile baya emzini, ukuze bathenge ukudla)." 
John4:9 Ngakho owesifazana umSamariya wathi kuye: Kungani wena ungumJuda ucela ukunatha kimi, owesifazana ongumSamariya? Ngoba amaJuda awalabudlelwano lamaSamariya." 
John4:10 UJesu waphendula wathi kuye: Aluba ubusazi isipho sikaNkulunkulu, lokuthi ungubani othi kuwe: Nginathisa; ubuzacela kuye, njalo ubezakunika amanzi aphilayo." 
John4:11 Owesifazana wathi kuye: Nkosi, kawulalutho lokukha, lomgodi uyatshona; uwathethe ngaphi pho amanzi aphilayo?" 
John4:12 Wena umkhulu yini kulobaba wethu uJakobe, owasinika umgodi, wanatha kuwo yena, labantwana bakhe, lemihlambi yakhe?" 
John4:13 UJesu waphendula wathi kuye: Wonke onatha lamanzi, uzakoma futhi;" 
John4:14 kodwa loba ngubani onatha amanzi mina engizamnika wona, kasoze ome kuze kube laphakade." 
John4:15 Owesifazana wathi kuye: Nkosi, ngipha lawomanzi, ukuze ngingomi, ngingabe ngiseza lapha ukukha." 
John4:16 UJesu wathi kuye: Hamba, ubize umkakho, uze lapha." 
John4:17 Owesifazana waphendula wathi: Kangilandoda. UJesu wathi kuye: Utsho kuhle ukuthi: Kangilandoda; 
John4:18 ngoba usuke waba lamadoda amahlanu, le olayo khathesi kayisiyo indoda yakho; lokhu ukutsho uqinisile." 
John4:19 Owesifazana wathi kuye: Nkosi, ngiyabona ukuthi wena ungumprofethi." 
John4:20 Obaba bethu babekhonza kulintaba. 
John4:21 UJesu wathi kuye: Mama, kholwa kimi, ukuthi ihola liyeza." 
John4:22 Lina likhonza elingakwaziyo. 
John4:23 Kodwa ihola liyeza njalo seliyilo. 
John4:24 UNkulunkulu unguMoya. 
John4:25 Owesifazana wathi kuye: Ngiyazi ukuthi uMesiya uyeza okuthiwa nguKristu. 
John4:26 UJesu wathi kuye: Mina nginguye, okhuluma lawe." 
John4:27 Kwathi ngalesosikhathi bafika abafundi bakhe, bamangala ukuthi wayekhuluma lowesifazana; kodwa kakho owathi: Udingani? Kumbe: Ukhulumani laye?" 
John4:28 Ngakho owesifazana wasetshiya inkonxa yakhe, wasesuka waya emzini, wathi ebantwini:" 
John4:29 Wozani, libone umuntu, ongitshele konke engakwenzayo?" 
John4:30 Ngakho baphuma emzini, beza kuye." 
John4:31 Kusenjalo abafundi bamncenga besithi: Rabi. 
John4:32 Kodwa wathi kubo: Mina ngilokudla engikudlayo lina elingakwaziyo. 
John4:33 Basebekhulumisana abafundi besithi: Kambe ukhona omlethele ukudla? 
John4:34 UJesu wathi kubo: Ukudla kwami. 
John4:35 Kalitsho yini ukuthi: Kuseselenyanga ezine ukuthi kufike ukuvuna? Khangelani, ngithi kini: Phakamisani amehlo enu." 
John4:36 Njalo ovunayo wemukela umvuzo. 
John4:37 Ngoba kulokhu ilizwi liqinisile elokuthi: Omunye ngohlanyelayo, lomunye ngovunayo." 
John4:38 Mina ngalithuma ukuvuna. 
John4:39 Njalo amaSamariya amanengi akulowomuzi akholwa kuye ngenxa yelizwi lowesifazana. 
John4:40 Kwathi esefikile kuye amaSamariya, amncenga ukuthi ahlale lawo." 
John4:41 Abanengi bengezelelwa bakholwa ngenxa yelizwi lakhe. 
John4:42 Basebesithi kowesifazana: Kasisakholwa ngenxa yokutsho kwakho; ngoba sesizizwele thina, siyazi ukuthi oqotho lo unguMsindisi womhlaba, uKristu." 
John4:43 Kwathi emva kwensuku ezimbili wasuka lapho; 
John4:44 ngoba uJesu ngokwakhe wafakaza ukuthi umprofethi kaladumo elizweni lakibo. 
John4:45 Wathi esefikile eGalili, amaGalili amemukela." 
John4:46 UJesu wafika-ke futhi eKana yeGalili. 
John4:47 Esezwile ukuthi uJesu u se fikile eGalili evela eJudiya, ngoba yayisizaphela." 
John4:48 Ngakho uJesu wathi kuye: Ngaphandle kokuthi, kalisoze likholwe." 
John4:49 Owesikhosini wathi kuye: Nkosi, yehla." 
John4:50 UJesu wathi kuye: Hamba; indodana yakho iyaphila. Umuntu wasekholwa ilizwi uJesu alikhuluma laye, wasuka wahamba." 
John4:51 Kwathi esesehla, inceku zakhe zamhlangabeza, zabika zathi: Umntanakho uyaphila." 
John4:52 Wasezibuza ihola aqale ngalo ukuba ngcono. Zasezisithi kuye: Izolo ngehola lesikhombisa uqhuqho lumyekele. 
John4:53 Ngakho uyise wazi ukuthi kwaku ngalelohola uJesu athi ngalo kuye: Indodana yakho iyaphila; wasekholwa yena lendlu yakhe yonke. 
John4:54 UJesu waphinda wakwenza lokhu kwaba yisibonakaliso sesibili. 
John5:1 Emva kwalezizinto kwaba khona umkhosi wamaJuda. 
John5:2 Kwakukhona-ke lapho eJerusalema eduze lesangolezimvu ichibi, elithiwa ngesiHebheru iBethesda, lilamakhulusi amahlanu." 
John5:3 Kwakulele kuwo ixuku elikhulu labagulayo, eleziphofu, eleziqhuli, elabatshwabheneyo, belindele ukuzanyanzanyiswa kwamanzi." 
John5:4 Ngoba ingilosi yayisehlela echibini ngezikhathi ezithile, izamazamise amanzi; kuthi lowo ongene kuqala emva kokuzanyazanyiswa kwamanzi, asiliswe, loba yisiphi isifo ebesimbambile." 
John5:5 Njalo kwakukhona lapho umuntu othile owayelesifo okweminyaka engamatshumi amathathu leyisificaminwembili. 
John5:6 Kwathi uJesu embona elele, esazi ukuthi ulesikhathi eside enjalo, wathi kuye: Uyafuna ukuthi uphile yini?" 
John5:7 Ogulayo wamphendula wathi: Nkosi, kangilamuntu wokungifaka echibini, nxa amanzi ezanyazanyiswa; kuthi nxa ngizayo mina, kwehle omunye phambi kwami." 
John5:8 UJesu wathi kuye: Sukuma, uthathe icansi lakho, uhambe." 
John5:9 Lowomuntu wahle waphila, wathatha icansi lakhe wahamba. Njalo kwakulisabatha mhlalokho." 
John5:10 Ngakho amaJuda athi kosilisiweyo: Kulisabatha. 
John5:11 Wawaphendula wathi: Ongiphilisileyo, yena uthe kimi: Thatha icansi lakho uhambe." 
John5:12 Ngakho ambuza: Ngubani umuntu othe kuwe: Thatha icansi lakho uhambe? 
John5:13 Kodwa osilisiweyo wayengamazi ukuthi ungubani; ngoba uJesu wayesesithele, ngoba kukhona ixuku kuleyondawo." 
John5:14 Emva kwalezizinto uJesu wamfica ethempelini, wasesithi kuye: Khangela usuphilile; ungabe usona futhi." 
John5:15 Umuntu wasuka, watshela amaJuda ukuthi nguJesu owayemenze waphila." 
John5:16 Njalo ngenxa yalokhu amaJuda amzingela uJesu. 
John5:17 Kodwa uJesu wawaphendula wathi. 
John5:18 Ngenxa yalokhu-ke amaJuda. 
John5:19 UJesu wasephendula wathi kubo. 
John5:20 Ngoba uYise uyayithanda iNdodana, uyayitshengisa konke akwenzayo yena." 
John5:21 Ngoba njengalokhu uYise evusa abafileyo abaphilise ukubaphilisa. 
John5:22 Ngoba loYise kahluleli muntu, kodwa unike iNdodana konke;" 
John5:23 ukuze bonke badumise iNdodana, njengalokhu bedumisa uYise." 
John5:24 Ngiqinisile, ngiqinisile, ngithi kini: Olizwayo ilizwi lami, akholwe kuye ongithumileyo, ulempilo elaphakade; njalo kangeni ekulahlweni." 
John5:25 Ngiqinisile, ngiqinisile, ngithi kini: Ihola liyeza, njalo selikhona." 
John5:26 Ngoba njengoba uYise elempilo ngokwakhe, kunjalo uyinikile layo iNdodana ukuthi ibe lempilo ngokwayo;" 
John5:27 njalo uyiphile. 
John5:28 Lingamangali ngalokhu," 
John5:29 babesebephuma. 
John5:30 Mina ngingenze lutho ngokwami. 
John5:31 Aluba ngizifakazela mina, ubufakazi bami abusiloqiniso." 
John5:32 Ukhona omunye ongifakazelayo mina. 
John5:33 Lina lathumela kuJohane. 
John5:34 Kodwa mina kangibemukeli ubufakazi obuvela emuntwini, kodwa ngitsho lezizinto ukuze lina lisindiswe." 
John5:35 Yena wayeyisibane. 
John5:36 Kodwa mina ngilobufakazi obukhulu kulo buka Johane. 
John5:37 Laye uBaba ongithumileyo," 
John5:38 njalo kalilalizwi lakhe elihlala phakathi kwenu, ngoba amthumileyo yena, lowo lina kalimkholwa." 
John5:39 Hlolani imibhalo, ngoba lina licabanga ukuthi lilempilo elaphakade kiyo;" 
John5:40 kodwa kalivumi ukuza kimi, ukuze libe lempilo." 
John5:41 Angemukeli udumo ebantwini; 
John5:42 kodwa ngiyalazi lina. 
John5:43 Mina ngizile ebizweni likaBaba, kodwa kalingemukeli." 
John5:44 Lingakholwa njani lina, nxa lisemukela udumo omunye komunye?" 
John5:45 Lingacabangi ukuthi mina ngizalimangalela kuBaba. 
John5:46 Ngoba uba belikholwa uMozisi, belizakholwa mina; ngoba yena wabhala ngami." 
John5:47 Kodwa uba lingakholwa imibhalo yakhe? 
John6:1 Emva kwalezizinto uJesu wasuka waya. 
John6:2 Laselimlandela ixuku elikhulu, ngoba babebone izibonakaliso zakhe azenza kulabo abagulayo." 
John6:3 UJesu wasesenyukela entabeni. 
John6:4 Iphasika, umkhosi wamaJuda, laselisondele." 
John6:5 Kwathi uJesu ephakamisa amehlo, wasebona ixuku elikhulu lisiza kuye: Sizathenga ngaphi izinkwa, ukuze laba badle?" 
John6:6 Njalo watsho lokhu emhlola, ngoba yena wayekwazi azakwenza." 
John6:7 UFiliphu wamphendula wathi: Izinkwa zabodenariyo abangamakhulu amabili zingebanele, ukuthi wonke ngamunye wabo azuze ingcosana." 
John6:8 Omunye wabafundi bakhe, uAndreya umfowabo kaSimoni Petro, wathi kuye:" 
John6:9 Kukhona umfanyana lapha, olezinkwa ezinhlanu zebhali lenhlanzana ezimbili; kodwa ziyini kwabanengi kangaka?" 
John6:10 Kodwa uJesu wathi: Hlalisani abantu phansi. Kwakukhona utshani obunengi ku leyo ndawo. 
John6:11 UJesu wasezithatha izinkwa, esebongile wazinika abafundi." 
John6:12 Bathi sebesuthi, wathi kubafundi bakhe: Buthani imvuthu eziseleyo, ukuze kungachitheki lutho." 
John6:13 Basebebutha, bagcwalisa izitsha ezilitshumi lambili ngemvuthu zezinkwa ezinhlanu zebhali, ezasalayo kulabo abadlayo." 
John6:14 Kwathi lababantu bebona isimangaliso asenzileyo uJesu, bathi: Ngeqiniso lo nguye umProfethi." 
John6:15 Kwathi uJesu esazi ukuthi bazakuza bambambe ngamandla. 
John6:16 Sekuhlwile, abafundi bakhe behlela elwandle," 
John6:17 sebengenile emkhunjini. Kwasekumnyama, uJesu wayengafikanga kubo." 
John6:18 Lwaseluvuka ulwandle ngoba umoya olamandla wawuvunguza. 
John6:19 Sebegwedlile amastadiyu angaba ngamatshumi amabili lanhlanu, babona uJesu ehamba phezu kolwandle, esondela emkhunjini; basebesethuka." 
John6:20 Kodwa wathi kubo: Yimi, lingesabi." 
John6:21 Basebevuma ukumemukela emkhunjini; njalo wahle wafika umkhumbi elizweni ababesiya kilo. 
John6:22 Kusisa ixuku elalimi ngaphetsheya kolwandle, kodwa abafundi bakhe babehambe bodwa," 
John6:23 kodwa imikolo evela eTiberiyasi; 
John6:24 ngakho ixuku selibonile ukuthi uJesu wayengekho lapho loba abafundi bakhe, bangena labo emikhunjini, bafika eKapenawume, bedinga uJesu." 
John6:25 Bathi sebemtholile ngaphetsheya kolwandle, ufike nini lapha?" 
John6:26 UJesu wabaphendula wathi: Ngiqinisile, ngiqinisile, ngithi kini: Liyangidinga, kungeyisikho ukuthi labona izibonakaliso, kodwa ngoba ladla izinkwa lasutha." 
John6:27 Lingasebenz el i ukudla okuphelayo. 
John6:28 Basebesithi kuye: Sizakwenzani, ukuze senze imisebenzi kaNkulunkulu?" 
John6:29 UJesu waphendula wathi kubo: Lo ngumsebenzi kaNkulunkulu. 
John6:30 Ngakho bathi kuye: Pho wena wenza isibonakaliso bani, ukuze sibone sikholwe kuwe? Usebenzani?" 
John6:31 Obaba bethu badla imana enkangala. 
John6:32 UJesu wasesithi kubo: Ngiqinisile, ngiqinisile, ngithi kini: UMozisi kalinikanga isinkwa esivela ezulwini; kodwa uBaba ulinika isinkwa soqobo esivela ezulwini." 
John6:33 Ngoba isinkwa sikaNkulunkulu singuye owehla evela ezulwini esinika impilo emhlabeni. 
John6:34 Basebesithi kuye: Nkosi, sinike lesosinkwa njalonjalo." 
John6:35 UJesu wasesithi kubo: Mina. 
John6:36 Kodwa ngithe kini: Lani lingibonile, kodwa kalikholwa." 
John6:37 Bonke uBaba anginika bona bazakuza kimi. 
John6:38 Ngoba ngehlile ezulwini. 
John6:39 Lalokhu kuyintando kaBaba ongithumileyo, ukuze konke anginike khona." 
John6:40 Lalokhu kuyintando yongithumileyo, ukuthi wonke obona iNdodana." 
John6:41 Ngalokho amaJuda akhonona ngaye. 
John6:42 Athi-ke: Lo kayisuye yini uJesu indodana kaJosefa? 
John6:43 UJesu wasephendula wathi kuwo: Lingakhononi phakathi kwenu. 
John6:44 Kakho ongeza kimi, ngaphandle kokuthi uBaba ongithumileyo amdonse." 
John6:45 Kulotshiwe kubaprofethi. 
John6:46 Kayisikho ukuthi ukhona obone uBaba, yena umbonile uBaba." 
John6:47 Ngiqinisile, ngiqinisile, ngithi kini: Okholwayo kimi, ulempilo elaphakade." 
John6:48 Mina ngiyisinkwa sempilo. 
John6:49 Oyihlo badla imana enkangala, futhi bafa;" 
John6:50 lesi yisinkwa esehla sivela ezulwini. 
John6:51 Mina ngiyisinkwa esiphilayo. 
John6:52 AmaJuda? 
John6:53 Ngakho uJesu wathi kuwo: Ngiqinisile, ngiqinisile, ngithi kini: Ngaphandle kokuthi lidle inyama yeNdodana yomuntu." 
John6:54 Odla inyama yami anathe igazi lami, ulempilo elaphakade." 
John6:55 Ngoba inyama yami iyikudla oqotho, legazi lami lingokunathwayo oqotho." 
John6:56 Odla inyama yami anathe igazi lami, uhlala kimi, lami kuye." 
John6:57 Njengalokhu uBaba ophilayo engithumile, lami ngiphila ngoBaba." 
John6:58 Lesi yisinkwa. 
John6:59 Watsho lezizinto esinagogeni efundisa eKapenawume. 
John6:60 Kwathi abanengi kubafundi bakhe besizwa bathi? 
John6:61 Kodwa uJesu esazi phakathi kwakhe ukuthi abafundi bakhe bayasola ngalokhu? 
John6:62 Pho, lizathiniuba libona iNdodana yomuntu?" 
John6:63 KunguMoya ophilisayo, inyama kayisizi lutho." 
John6:64 Kodwa bakhona abanye kini abangakholwayo. 
John6:65 Wasesithi: Kungenxa yalokhu ngithe kini: Kakho ongeza kimi, ngaphandle kokuthi ekunikwe nguBaba." 
John6:66 Kusukela lapho abanengi babafundi bakhe babuyela emuva, kababe besahamba laye." 
John6:67 UJesu wasesithi kwabalitshumi lambili: Lani lithanda ukuzihambela yini? 
John6:68 USimoni Petro wasemphendula wathi: Nkosi, sizakuya kubani," 
John6:69 njalo thina siyakholwa, sesisazi ukuthi wena unguKristu iNdodana." 
John6:70 UJesu wabaphendula wathi: Mina kangilikhethanga yini? 
John6:71 Wayekhuluma ngoJudasi Iskariyothi kaSimoni. 
John7:1 Njalo emva kwalezizinto uJesu wabhoda eGalili; ngoba wayengathandi ukubhoda eJudiya. 
John7:2 Wawusondele umkhosi wamaJuda wokwakha amadumba. 
John7:3 Ngakho abafowabo bathi kuye: Suka lapha, uye eJudiya." 
John7:4 Ngoba kakho owenza ulutho ensitha, kodwa yena ngokwakhe edinga ukuba sobala. Uba uzenza lezizinto, ziveze wena emhlabeni." 
John7:5 Ngoba labafowabo. 
John7:6 Ngakho uJesu wathi kubo: Isikhathi sami kasikafiki, kodwa esenu isikhathi sihlala silungile." 
John7:7 Ungelizonde umhlaba lina; kodwa uyangizonda, ngoba mina ngifakaza ngawo." 
John7:8 Yenyukelani lina emkhosini lo; mina angikenyukeli kulumkhosi. 
John7:9 Esetshilo lezizinto kubo, wahlala eGalili." 
John7:10 Kodwa sebenyukile, laye wasesenyukela emkhosini, kungeyisikho obala, kodwa kungathi ku sensitha." 
John7:11 AmaJuda, athi: Ungaphi yena?" 
John7:12 Kwakukhona ukukhonona okukhulu ngaye phakathi kwamaxuku. 
John7:13 Loba kunjalo kwakungekho muntu owakhuluma obala ngaye ngokwesaba. 
John7:14 Kuthe sekuphakathi komkhosi, uJesu wenyukela." 
John7:15 AmaJuda: Lo uyazi njani imibhalo, engafundanga?" 
John7:16 UJesu wawaphendula wathi: Imfundiso yami kayisiyo eyami kodwa ngeyalowo ongithumileyo. 
John7:17 Uba umuntu ethanda ukwenza intando yakhe, uzakwazi ngemfundiso, ukuthi ivela kuNkulunkulu, kumbe ngizikhulumela mina ngokwami." 
John7:18 Ozikhulumela ngokwakhe, uzidingela udumo lwakhe." 
John7:19 Kalinikanga yini uMozisi umlayo? 
John7:20 Ixuku laphendula lathi: Uledimoni? 
John7:21 UJesu waphendula wathi kubo: Ngenze umsebenzi owodwa, njalo lonke liyamangala." 
John7:22 Ngakho uMozisi walinika ukusoka (kungeyisikho ukuthi kwavela kuMozisi. 
John7:23 Uba ngesabatha umuntu esemukela ukusoka, ukuze kungephulwa umlayo kaMozisi?" 
John7:24 Lingahluleli ngokubona, kodwa yahlulelani ukwahlulela okuqondileyo." 
John7:25 Abanye kwabeJerusalema basebesithi: Lo kayisuye yini abadinga ukumbulala? 
John7:26 Kodwa khangela ukhuluma obala, kodwa kabatsho lutho kuye. Kungaba yikuthi ababusi sebesazi oqotho ukuthi lo unguKristu uqobo yini?" 
John7:27 Kodwa. 
John7:28 Ngakho uJesu efundisa ethempelini wamemeza. 
John7:29 Kodwa ngiyamazi mina. 
John7:30 Ngakho badinga ukumbamba. 
John7:31 Kodwa abanengi bexuku bakholwa kuye? 
John7:32 AbaFarisi bezwa ixuku likhonona lezizinto ngaye; abapristi abakhulu labaFarisi basebethuma abancedisi ukuze bambambe. 
John7:33 UJesu wasesithi kubo: Ngiselani okwesikhatshana. 
John7:34 Lizangidinga, linga ngit holi." 
John7:35 Ngakho amaJuda akhulumisana athi: Uzakuya ngaphi lo ukuthi thina singayikumthola? 
John7:36 Yilizwi bani leli alitshoyo elokuthi: Lizangidinga, aliyiku ngi thola; lelo kuthi: Lapho engikhona mina, lina lingeze leza?" 
John7:37 Kwathi ngosuku lokucina olukhulu lomkhosi. 
John7:38 Okholwa kimi, njengokutsho kombhalo." 
John7:39 Lalokhu wakutsho. 
John7:40 Ngakho abanengi bexuku besizwa lelilizwi bathi: Oqotho lo ungulowomProfethi. 
John7:41 Abanye bathi: Lo unguKristu? 
John7:42 Kawutsho yini umbhalo ukuthi uKristu uzavela enzalweni kaDavida? 
John7:43 Ngakho kwaba khona ukwehlukana ngaye phakathi kwexuku. 
John7:44 Abanye babo bafuna ukumbamba. 
John7:45 Khona abancedisi baya kubapristi abakhulu lakubaFarisi? 
John7:46 Abancedisi baphendula bathi. 
John7:47 AbaFarisi basebebaphendula bathi: Lani seliduhisiwe yini? 
John7:48 Ukhona yini? 
John7:49 Kodwa lelixuku elingawaziyo umlayo liqalekisiwe. 
John7:50 UNikodima, wathi kubo:" 
John7:51 Kanti umlayo wakithi uyamgweba umuntu ukwazi akwenzayo? 
John7:52 Baphendula bathi kuye: Kanti lawe ungoweGalili? Hlolisisa ubone ukuthi kakuvukanga umprofethi eGalili. 
John7:53 Ngulowo lalowo wasesuka waya ekhaya. 
John8:1 Kodwa uJesu waya entabeni yeMihlwathi. 
John8:2 Kwathi ekuseni kakhulu wabuya weza. 
John8:3 Ababhali labaFarisi basebeletha kuye owesifazana owayebanjwe efeba, bammisa phakathi," 
John8:4 bathi kuye: Mfundisi, lo owesifazana ubanjwe eseqotsheni lo kuphinga;" 
John8:5 lemlayweni uMozisi; ngakho wena uthini? 
John8:6 Kodwa batsho lokhu bemlinga, wenza angathi ka bezwa." 
John8:7 Kwathi bephikelela ukumbuza, walulama wathi kubo." 
John8:8 Wasebuya ekhothamela phansi wabhala emhlabathini. 
John8:9 Kodwa bona, bekuzwa, balahlwa; uJesu wasesala yedwa, lowesifazana emi phakathi." 
John8:10 UJesu waseselulama, engaboni muntu ngaphandle kowesifazana, wathi kuye: Mama, bangaphi labo abakumangalelayo? Kakho okulahlayo yini?" 
John8:11 Wasesithi: Kakho, Nkosi. UJesu wasesithi kuye: Lami kangikulahli." 
John8:12 Ngakho uJesu wakhuluma labo futhi wathi: Mina ngiyikukhanya komhlaba. 
John8:13 Ngakho abaFarisi bathi kuye: Wena uyazifakazela; ubufakazi bakho kabulaqiniso. 
John8:14 UJesu waphendula wathi kubo: Lanxa ngizifakazela mina. 
John8:15 Lina lahlulela ngokwenyama. 
John8:16 Kodwa uba lami ngisahlulela, ukwahlulela kwami kuqinisile." 
John8:17 Njalo emlayweni wenu kulotshiwe ukuthi ubufakazi babantu ababili bungobuqinisileyo. 
John8:18 Mina ngingozifakazelayo, loBaba ongithumileyo ufakaza ngami." 
John8:19 Ngakho bathi kuye: Ungaphi uYihlo? UJesu waphendula wathi: Kalingazi mina, loba uBaba." 
John8:20 UJesu wakhuluma la amazwi endlini yomnikelo. 
John8:21 Ngakho uJesu wathi kubo futhi: Ngiyahamba mina, njalo lizangidinga." 
John8:22 Ngakho amaJuda athi. 
John8:23 Wasesithi kuwo: Lina livela phansi. 
John8:24 Ngakho ngithe kini, lizafela ezonweni zenu." 
John8:25 Ngakho athi kuye: Wena ungubani? UJesu wasesithi kuwo: Lokho engalitshela khona futhi ekuqaleni. 
John8:26 Ngilezinto ezinengi engilokuzikhuluma ngani lokwahlulela ngazo; kodwa ongithumileyo uqinisile. 
John8:27 Kawaqedisisanga ukuthi ukhuluma lawo ngoYise. 
John8:28 Ngakho uJesu wathi kuwo: Nxa seliyiphakamisile iNdodana yomuntu; 
John8:29 njalo yena ongithumileyo ulami. 
John8:30 Esakhuluma lezizinto abanengi bakholwa kuye. 
John8:31 Ngakho uJesu wathi kumaJuda akholwe kuye: Uba lina lihlala elizwini lami; 
John8:32 lizalazi iqiniso. 
John8:33 Amphendula athi: Siyinzalo kaAbrahama, kasizanga sibe yizigqili zamuntu?" 
John8:34 UJesu wawaphendula wathi: Ngiqinisile, ngiqinisile, ngithi kini: Wonke owenza isono uyisigqili sesono." 
John8:35 Njalo isigqili kasihlali phakade ekhaya. 
John8:36 Ngakho uba iNdodana. 
John8:37 Ngiyazi ukuthi liyinzalo. 
John8:38 Mina ngikhuluma lokho engikubonileyo kuBaba. 
John8:39 Aphendula athi kuye: Ubaba wethu nguAbrahama. 
John8:40 Kodwa khathesi lidinga ukungibulala, umuntu olitshele iqiniso; lokho uAbrahama kakwenzanga." 
John8:41 Lina lenza imisebenzi kayihlo. Ngakho athi kuye: Kasizalwanga ngobufebe thina. 
John8:42 UJesu wathi kuwo: Uba uNkulunkulu ubenguyihlo, belizangithanda." 
John8:43 Kungani lingaqedisisi inkulumo yami? Ngoba lingeke lilizwe ilizwi lami. 
John8:44 Lina; ngoba engumqambimanga loyise wawo. 
John8:45 Mina-ke ngoba ngikhuluma iqiniso, kalingikholwa." 
John8:46 Nguwuphi kini? Njalo uba ngilitshela iqiniso, lina kalingikholwa ngani?" 
John8:47 Yena ongokaNkulunkulu. 
John8:48 Ngakho amaJuda aphendula athi kuye? 
John8:49 UJesu waphendula wathi: Mina kangiladimoni, kodwa ngiyadumisa uBaba; kodwa lina liyangigcona." 
John8:50 Mina-ke kangizidingeli udumo lwami; ukhona odingayo lowahlulelayo. 
John8:51 Ngiqinisile, ngiqinisile, ngithi kini: Uba umuntu elondoloza ilizwi lami." 
John8:52 Ngakho amaJuda athi kuye: Khathesi sesisazi ukuthi uledimoni. 
John8:53 Wena umkhulu yini kulobaba wethu uAbrahama, owafayo? Labaprofethi bafa; uzenza bani wena?" 
John8:54 UJesu waphendula wathi: Uba ngizidumisa mina, udumo lwami luyize," 
John8:55 njalo kalimazanga. 
John8:56 Uyihlo uAbrahama wajabula kakhulu ukubona. 
John8:57 Ngakho amaJuda athi kuye: Kawukabi leminyaka engamatshumi amahlanu, njalo wena wambona uAbrahama yini?" 
John8:58 UJesu wathi kuwo: Ngiqinisile, ngiqinisile, ngithi kini: UAbrahama engakabi khona, mina ngikhona." 
John8:59 Asedobha amatshe ukuze amjikijele. 
John9:1 Wathi esedlula wabona umuntu oyisiphofu kusukela ekuzalweni. 
John9:2 Abafundi bakhe basebembuza bathi: Rabi? 
John9:3 UJesu waphendula wathi: Konanga lo loba abazali bakhe; kodwa ukuze kubonakaliswe imisebenzi kaNkulunkulu kuye. 
John9:4 Kufanele ngisebenze imisebenzi yongithumileyo; ubusuku buyeza, lapho okungekho olakho ukusebenza khona." 
John9:5 Ngisekhona emhlabeni, ngiyikukhanya komhlaba." 
John9:6 Esetshilo lezizinto, wakhafulela emhlabathini, wenza udaka ngamathe, waninda loludaka emehlweni esiphofu," 
John9:7 wasesithi kuso: Hamba uyegeza echibini leSilowama. 
John9:8 Ngakho abakhelene laso lalabo ababesibonile ngaphambili ukuthi sasiyisiphofu? 
John9:9 Abanye bathi: Lo nguye; kodwa abanye bathi: Unjengaye. Yena wathi: Ngingu ye. 
John9:10 Ngakho bathi kuye: Avulwe njani amehlo akho? 
John9:11 Yena waphendula wathi: Umuntu othiwa nguJesu wenze udaka, waninda amehlo ami, wathi kimi: Hamba uye echibini leSilowama, ugeze. Njalo ngahamba ngageza, ngabuye ngabona." 
John9:12 Ngakho bathi kuye: Ungaphi yena? Wathi: Kangazi. 
John9:13 Basebemletha kubaFarisi, lowo owayekade eyisiphofu." 
John9:14 Njalo kwakulisabatha mhla uJesu esenza udaka, evula amehlo akhe." 
John9:15 AbaFarisi labo basebembuza futhi, ukuthi wemukele njani ukubona. Wasesithi kubo: Ufake udaka emehlweni ami, ngasengigeza, sengibona." 
John9:16 Ngakho abanye babaFarisi bathi: Lumuntu kaveli kuNkulunkulu. 
John9:17 Baphinda bathi kuso isiphofu: Wena uthini ngaye, lokhu evule amehlo akho? Wasesithi: Ungumprofethi." 
John9:18 AmaJuda-ke kawakholwanga ngaye, ukuthi wayeyisiphofu usemukele ukubona, aze abiza abazali bakhe osebuye wabona," 
John9:19 asebabuza athi: Lo uyindodana yenu, lina elithi yazalwa iyisiphofu yini? Pho isibona njani khathesi?" 
John9:20 Abazali bakhe bawaphendula bathi: Siyazi ukuthi lo uyindodana yethu, lokuthi wazalwa eyisiphofu;" 
John9:21 kodwa ukuthi ubona njani khathesi, kasikwazi; kumbe ngubani ovule amehlo akhe, thina kasikwazi; yena usekhulile; mbuzeni, uzazikhulumela yena." 
John9:22 Abazali bakhe batsho lezizinto, ngoba besesaba." 
John9:23 Kungakho abazali bakhe bathi: Usekhulile, mbuzeni." 
John9:24 Ambiza-ke ngokwesibili lowomuntu owayeyisiphofu, athi kuye: Phana uNkulunkulu udumo." 
John9:25 Yena wasephendula esithi: Loba eyisoni kangazi, kunye engikwaziyo, ukuthi bengiyisiphofu, khathesi sengibona." 
John9:26 Asesithi kuye futhi: Wenzeni kuwe? Uwavule njani amehlo akho? 
John9:27 Wawaphendula wathi: Sengilitshelile, kodwa kalizwanga, lifunelani ukuzwa futhi? Liyafisa lani ukuba ngabafundi bakhe yini?" 
John9:28 Ngakho amthuka, esithi: Nguwe ongumfundi wakhe; kodwa thina singabafundi bakaMozisi." 
John9:29 Thina siyazi ukuthi uNkulunkulu wakhuluma loMozisi; kodwa lo kasimazi lapho avela khona. 
John9:30 Umuntu waphendula wathi kuwo: Ngoba kulokhu kuyisimanga ukuthi lina kalimazi lapho avela khona, kanti uvule amehlo ami." 
John9:31 Njalo siyazi ukuthi uNkulunkulu kazizwa izoni. 
John9:32 Loba nini kakukaze kuzwakale ukuthi kukhona umuntu owavula amehlo owazalwa eyisiphofu. 
John9:33 Uba lo. 
John9:34 Aphendula athi kuye: Wena wazalelwa esonweni ngokupheleleyo, njalo wena uyasifundisa yini." 
John9:35 UJesu wezwa ukuthi amxotshele phandle? 
John9:36 Yena waphendula wathi: Ingubani, Nkosi, ukuze ngikholwe kuyo?" 
John9:37 UJesu wasesithi kuye: Lawe usuyibonile. 
John9:38 Wasesithi: Nkosi, ngiyakholwa; wasemkhonza." 
John9:39 UJesu wasesithi: Mina ngizele ukwahlulela kulumhlaba, ukuze abangaboniyo babone." 
John9:40 Lalabo kubaFarisi ababelaye bezwa lezizinto, bathi kuye: Lathi siyiziphofu yini?" 
John9:41 UJesu wathi kubo: Uba beliyiziphofu, ngabe kalilasono." 
John10:1 Ngiqinisile, ngiqinisile, ngithi kini: Ongangeni ngesango esibayeni sezimvu, kodwa akhwele kwenye indawo, lowo ulisela lomphangi;" 
John10:2 kodwa ongena ngesango ungumelusi wezimvu. 
John10:3 Umlindi wesango uyamvulela, lezimvu ziyalizwa ilizwi lakhe, njalo uyazibiza ezakhe izimvu ngebizo, azikhokhelele phandle." 
John10:4 Nxa esezikhuphile ezakhe izimvu, uhamba phambi kwazo; lezimvu zimlandele, ngoba ziyalazi ilizwi lakhe." 
John10:5 Kodwa owemzini kazisoze zimlandele, kodwa zizambalekela; ngoba kazilazi ilizwi labemzini." 
John10:6 UJesu wakhuluma lumfanekiso kubo. 
John10:7 Ngakho uJesu waphinda wathi kubo: Ngiqinisile, ngiqinisile, ngithi kini: Mina ngilisango lezimvu;" 
John10:8 bonke abake bafika phambi kwami bangamasela labaphangi; kodwa izimvu kazibezwanga. 
John10:9 Mina ngilisango; uba umuntu engena ngami, uzasindiswa." 
John10:10 Isela kalizi ngaphandle kokuzakweba lokubulala lokubhubhisa; mina ngizile ukuze babe lempilo, babe layoiphuphume." 
John10:11 Mina ngingumelusi olungileyo. 
John10:12 Kodwa oqatshiweyo. 
John10:13 Oqatshiweyo uyabaleka-ke, ngoba engoqatshiweyo, njalo engazikhathaleli izimvu." 
John10:14 Mina ngingumelusi olungileyo, ngiyazazi ezami, ngiyaziwa ngezami," 
John10:15 njengalokhu uBaba engazi, lami ngiyamazi uBaba." 
John10:16 Njalo ngilezinye izimvu. 
John10:17 Ngenxa yalokhu uBaba uyangithanda. 
John10:18 Kakho ongemuka yona, kodwa mina ngiyibeka phansi ngokwami. Ngilamandla okuyibeka phansi." 
John10:19 Ngakho kwaba khona futhi ukwehlukana. 
John10:20 Labanengi bawo bathi: Uledimoni? 
John10:21 Amanye athi: Lamazwi kawasiwo wongenwe lidimoni? 
John10:22 Kwakukhona umkhosi wokuvuselela eJerusalema, kwakusebusika;" 
John10:23 uJesu wasehambahamba ethempelini ekhulusini likaSolomoni. 
John10:24 AmaJuda asemhanqa, athi kuye: Koze kube nini usilibazisa? Uba wena unguKristu, sitshele ngokucacileyo." 
John10:25 UJesu wawaphendula wathi: Ngalitshela, kodwa kalikholwanga;" 
John10:26 kodwa lina kalikholwa; ngoba kalisibo abezimvu zami, njengokutsho kwami kini." 
John10:27 Izimvu zami ziyalizwa ilizwi lami, lami ngiyazazi, futhi ziyangilandela;" 
John10:28 njalo mina ngizinika impilo elaphakade. 
John10:29 UBaba; kungekho njalo ongazihluthuna esandleni sikaBaba. 
John10:30 Mina loBaba simunye. 
John10:31 Ngakho amaJuda. 
John10:32 UJesu wawaphendula wathi: Ngilitshengise imisebenzi eminengi emihle evela kuBaba; yiwuphi umsebenzi kuyo elingikhandela wona ngamatshe? 
John10:33 AmaJuda amphendula athi: Kasikukhandi ngamatshe ngenxa yomsebenzi omuhle. 
John10:34 UJesu wawaphendula wathi: Kakulotshiwe yini emlayweni wenu? 
John10:35 Uba wababiza bona ngokuthi ngonkulunkulu, eleza kubo ilizwi likaNkulunkulu, njalo umbhalo ungephulwe," 
John10:36 lowo uBaba amehlukanisileyo? 
John10:37 Uba ngingenzi imisebenzi kaBaba, kalingakholwa kimi." 
John10:38 Kodwa uba ngi y enza, lanxa lingakholwa kimi, kholwani imisebenzi." 
John10:39 Ngakho adinga futhi ukumbamba. 
John10:40 Wasebuya wasuka waya ngaphetsheya kweJodani; wasehlala khona. 
John10:41 Labanengi beza kuye, bathi: UJohane kenzanga sibonakaliso." 
John10:42 Abanengi basebekholwa kuye lapho. 
John11:1 Kwakukhona-ke othile owayegula othiwanguLazaro. 
John11:2 Kwakunguye uMariya owagcoba iNkosi ngamagcobo, wesula inyawo zayo ngenwele zakhe, omnewabo uLazaro wayegula." 
John11:3 Ngakho odadewabo bathumela kuye besithi: Nkosi. 
John11:4 UJesu esezwile wathi: Lokhu ukugula kakusikho okokufa, kodwa kungokodumo lukaNkulunkulu ukuze iNdodana kaNkulunkulu idunyiswe ngakho." 
John11:5 UJesu wayebathanda-ke oMarta lodadewabo loLazaro. 
John11:6 Ngakho esezwile ukuthi uyagula, wasehlala insuku ezimbili endaweni lapho ayekhona." 
John11:7 Emva kwalokhu wasesithi kubafundi: Asiphinde siye eJudiya. 
John11:8 Abafundi bathi kuye: Rabi? 
John11:9 UJesu waphendula wathi: Kawakho amahola alitshumi lambili emini yini. 
John11:10 Kodwa uba umuntu ehamba ebusuku, uyakhubeka, ngoba ukukhanya kakukho kuye." 
John11:11 Wakhuluma lezizinto, emva kwalokhu wasesithi kubo: Umngane wethu uLazaro." 
John11:12 Ngakho abafundi bakhe bathi kuye: Nkosi, uba elele, uzaphila." 
John11:13 Kodwa uJesu wakhuluma ngokufa kwakhe; kodwa bona bacabanga ukuthi wakhuluma ngokuphumula kobuthongo. 
John11:14 Ngakho uJesu wasebatshela ngokucacileyo: ULazaro ufile. 
John11:15 Njalo ngiyathokoza ngenxa yenu ukuthi bengingekho lapho, ukuze likholwe; kodwa asiye kuye." 
John11:16 Ngakho uTomasi. 
John11:17 Kwathi esefika uJesu, wamfica eselensuku ezine engcwabeni." 
John11:18 LeBethani yayiseduze leJerusalema, okungaba ngamastadiyu alitshumi lanhlanu ukusuka lapho;" 
John11:19 labanengi kumaJuda babefikile kuMarta loMariya, ukuze babaduduze ngomnewabo." 
John11:20 Ngakho uMarta, esezwile ukuthi uJesu uyeza, wayakumhlangabeza." 
John11:21 UMarta wasesithi kuJesu: Nkosi, aluba ubukhona lapha, umnewethu ngabe kafanga;" 
John11:22 kodwa lakhathesi ngiyazi ukuthi loba yini ongayicela kuNkulunkulu, uNkulunkulu uzakunika yona." 
John11:23 UJesu wathi kuye: Umnewenu uzabuya avuke. 
John11:24 UMarta wathi kuye: Ngiyazi ukuthi uzabuya avuke ekuvukeni ngosuku lokucina. 
John11:25 UJesu wathi kuye: Mina ngiyikuvuka; 
John11:26 njalo wonke ophilayo ekholwa kimi, kasoze afe laphakade. Uyakukholwa lokhu yini?" 
John11:27 Wathi kuye: Yebo, Nkosi; mina ngiyakholwa ukuthi wena unguKristu." 
John11:28 Esetshilo lokhu uMarta wasuka, wayabiza udadewabo uMariya ensitha, wathi: UMfundisi ulapha uyakubiza." 
John11:29 Yena-ke esezwile lokhu, wahle wasukuma waya kuye." 
John11:30 Kodwa uJesu wayengakafiki emzaneni, kodwa wayesendaweni lapho uMarta amhlangabeza khona." 
John11:31 Ngakho amaJuda ayesendlini laye emduduza. 
John11:32 Kwathi uMariya, esefike lapho uJesu akhona, embona, wawela enyaweni zakhe." 
John11:33 Ngakho uJesu wathi embona ekhala, lamaJuda afika laye ekhala, wabubula emoyeni, wazikhathaza," 
John11:34 wathi: Limbeke ngaphi? Bathi kuye: Nkosi, woza ubone." 
John11:35 UJesu walila. 
John11:36 Ngakho amaJuda athi: Khangelani ukuthi ubemthanda njani. 
John11:37 Kodwa amanye awo athi: Lo, owavula amehlo esiphofu, ubengekwenze yini ukuthi lalo angafi?" 
John11:38 Ngakho uJesu ebubula futhi phakathi kwakhe wafika engcwabeni. 
John11:39 UJesu wathi: Susani ilitshe. 
John11:40 UJesu wathi kuye: Kangitshongo yini kuwe? 
John11:41 Balisusa-ke ilitshe, lapho okwakulele khona ofileyo, wathi: Baba, ngiyakubonga ngoba wena ungizwile." 
John11:42 Kodwa mina bengisazi ukuthi uyangizwa njalonjalo. 
John11:43 Esetshilo lezizinto, wamemeza ngelizwi elikhulu wathi: Lazaro, phuma!" 
John11:44 Wasephuma owayefile, ebotshiwe izandla lenyawo ngamalembu." 
John11:45 Ngakho abanengi kumaJuda, ababeze kuMariya." 
John11:46 Kodwa abanye babo baya kubaFarisi, babatshela izinto azenzileyo uJesu." 
John11:47 Ngakho abapristi abakhulu labaFarisi, bathi: Sizakwenzani? Ngoba umuntu lo wenza izibonakaliso ezinengi;" 
John11:48 uba simyekele njalo, bonke bazakholwa kuye." 
John11:49 Kodwa omunye wabo, uKayafasi, wathi kubo: Kalazi lutho lina," 
John11:50 futhi kalinakani ukuthi kusilungele ukuthi umuntu oyedwa afele abantu, lokuthi isizwe sonke singabhubhi." 
John11:51 Kodwa kazitsholongo lokhu ngokwakhe," 
John11:52 njalo. 
John11:53 Ngakho kusukela kulolosuku benza ndawonye icebo ukuze bambulale. 
John11:54 Ngakho uJesu kabesahamba obala phakathi kwamaJuda, wasehlala khona labafundi bakhe." 
John11:55 Laselisondele iphasika lamaJuda. 
John11:56 Ngakho bamdinga uJesu, bekhulumisana bemi ethempelini besithi: Licabangani? Lithi isibili kayikuza emkhosini yini?" 
John11:57 Kodwa bonke abapristi abakhulu labaFarisi babekhuphe umlayo wokuthi uba ekhona owaziyo lapho akhona, akubike ukuze bambambe." 
John12:1 Kwathi kuselensuku eziyisithupha lingakafiki. 
John12:2 Basebemenzela ukudla kwantambama lapho; njalo uLazaro wayengomunye walabo ababehlezi ekudleni laye. 
John12:3 UMariya, wesula inyawo zakhe ngenwele zakhe; lendlu yagcwala iphunga lamagcobo." 
John12:4 Ngakho omunye wabafundi bakhe, uJudasi Iskariyothi kaSimoni, owayezamnikela, wathi:" 
John12:5 Kungani amafutha la engathengiswanga ngabodenariyo abangamakhulu amathathu, kwasekunikwa abayanga?" 
John12:6 Wakutsho-ke lokhu, kungeyisikho ukuthi ekhathalele abayanga, kodwa ngoba wayelisela, wayelesikhwama." 
John12:7 UJesu wasesithi: Myekeleni; uwalondolozele usuku lokungcwatshwa kwami. 
John12:8 Ngoba abayanga lihlala lilabo, kodwa mina kalihlali lilami." 
John12:9 Ngakho ixuku elikhulu lamaJuda lakwazi ukuthi ulapho; laselisiza kungesikuthi ngenxa kaJesu kuphela, kodwa lokuthi babone loLazaro." 
John12:10 Abapristi abakhulu; 
John12:11 ngoba ngenxa yakhe. 
John12:12 Kusisa ixuku elikhulu, lezwa ukuthi uJesu uyeza eJerusalema," 
John12:13 bathatha ingatsha zezihlahla zelala, baphuma uku ya mhlangabeza, bamemeza besithi: Hosana! Ubusisiwe ozayo ebizweni leNkosi, iNkosi kaIsrayeli." 
John12:14 UJesu wasefica ithole likababhemi, wahlala phezu kwalo, njengokulotshiweyo ukuthi:" 
John12:15 Ungesabi, ndodakazi yeSiyoni; khangela, inkosi yakho iyeza, ihlezi phezu kwethole likababhemi." 
John12:16 Kodwa abafundi bakhe kabaqedisisanga lezizinto ekuqaleni. 
John12:17 Ngakho ixuku elalilaye lapho ebiza uLazaro ukuthi aphume engcwabeni, emvusa kwabafileyo, lafakaza." 
John12:18 Ngenxa yalokhu ixuku laphuma futhi uku ya mhlangabeza, ngoba lezwa ukuthi wenze lesisibonakaliso." 
John12:19 Ngakho abaFarisi bakhulumisana besithi: Liyabona ukuthi kalisizi lutho; khangelani umhlaba uyamlandela. 
John12:20 Kwakukhona amaGriki phakathi kwalabo; 
John12:21 wona-ke eza kuFiliphu, basebemcela besithi: Nkosi, sithanda ukubona uJesu." 
John12:22 UFiliphu weza watshela uAndreya; uAndreya loFiliphu basebetshela uJesu futhi. 
John12:23 UJesu wasebaphendula esithi: Ihola selifikile. 
John12:24 Ngiqinisile, ngiqinisile, ngithi kini: Ngaphandle kokuthi uhlamvu lwebele luwele emhlabathini lufe, lona luhlala lulodwa; kodwa aluba lusifa, luthela isithelo sande." 
John12:25 Yena othanda impilo yakhe uyalahlekelwa yiyo.
