John12:26 Uba umuntu engisebenzela, kangilandele; lalapho engikhona mina." 
John12:27 Khathesi umphefumulo wami ukhathazekile. 
John12:28 Baba, dumisa ibizo lakho." 
John12:29 Ngakho ixuku elalimi khonalisizwa lathi kube lomdumo. Abanye bathi: Ingilosi ikhulume laye. 
John12:30 UJesu waphendula wathi: Lelilizwi kalizanga ngenxa yami, kodwa ngenxa yenu." 
John12:31 Khathesi yisigwebo salumhlaba. 
John12:32 Mina-ke nxa ngiphakanyiswa emhlabeni. 
John12:33 Watsho-ke lokhu. 
John12:34 Ixuku lamphendula lathi: Thina sezwa emlayweni? Ingubani le iNdodana yomuntu? 
John12:35 UJesu wasesithi kubo: Kuseyisikhatshana. 
John12:36 Liselokukhanya, kholwani kukho ukukhanya, ukuze libe ngabantwana bokukhanya." 
John12:37 Lanxa wayenze izibonakaliso ezinengi kangaka phambi kwabo, kabakholwanga kuye;" 
John12:38 ukuze ligcwaliseke ilizwi likaIsaya umprofethi, alikhulumayo elokuthi: Nkosi, ngubani okholwe ukutshumayela kwethu? Lengalo yeNkosi yembulelwa bani?" 
John12:39 Ngakho babengelakho ukukholwa, ngoba uIsaya wabuya wathi:" 
John12:40 Uphumputhekisile amehlo abo. 
John12:41 UIsaya wakhuluma lezizinto. 
John12:42 Loba kunjalo-ke labanengi bababusi; 
John12:43 ngoba bathanda udumo lwabantu kulodumo lukaNkulunkulu. 
John12:44 UJesu wasememeza esithi; 
John12:45 njalo obona mina, ubona ongithumileyo." 
John12:46 Mina ngizile ngiyikukhanya emhlabeni, ukuze wonke okholwa kimi, angahlali emnyameni." 
John12:47 Njalo uba ekhona owezwayo amazwi ami angakholwa, mina kangimgwebi." 
John12:48 Yena. 
John12:49 Ngoba mina kangizikhulumelanga ngokwami. 
John12:50 Njalo ngiyazi ukuthi umlayo wakhe uyimpilo elaphakade; ngakho izinto mina engizikhulumayo, njengokutsho kukaBaba kimi, ngokunjalo ngiyazikhuluma." 
John13:1 Kwathi ungakafiki umkhosi wephasika. 
John13:2 Ukudla kwantambama sekwenziwe, udiyabhola esekufakile enhliziyweni kaJudasi Iskariyothi," 
John13:3 uJesu ekwazi ukuthi uYise unikele izinto zonke ezandleni zakhe," 
John13:4 wasukuma ekudleni kwantambama. 
John13:5 Emva kwalokhu wathela amanzi emganwini, waqala ukugezisa inyawo zabafundi, loku ze sula ngelembu ayezithandele ngalo." 
John13:6 Wasefika kuSimoni Petro; yena wasesithi kuye: Nkosi, wena ugezisa inyawo zami yini?" 
John13:7 UJesu waphendula wathi kuye: Engikwenzayo mina, kawukwazi khathesi, kodwa uzakwazi emva kwalezizinto." 
John13:8 UPetro wathi kuye: Kawusoze ugezise inyawo zami kuze kube laphakade. UJesu wamphendula wathi: Uba ngingakugezisi, kawulasabelo lami." 
John13:9 USimoni Petro wathi kuye: Nkosi, kakungabi zinyawo zami zodwa, kodwa lezandla lekhanda." 
John13:10 UJesu wathi kuye: Ogezileyo kasweli luthongaphandle kokugeziswa inyawo, kodwa uhlambulukile." 
John13:11 Ngoba wayemazi lowo owayezamnikela; ngenxa yalokhu wathi: Kalihlambulukanga lonke. 
John13:12 Esegezisile inyawo zabo, wathatha izembatho zakhe, wabuya wahlala phansi?" 
John13:13 Lina lingibiza lithi: Mfundisi. 
John13:14 Ngakho uba mina, iNkosi loMfundisi, ngigezise inyawo zenu." 
John13:15 Ngoba ngilinikile isibonelo, ukuze lenze lani njengoba mina ngenzile kini." 
John13:16 Ngiqinisile, ngiqinisile, ngithi kini: Inceku kayinkulu kulenkosi yayo." 
John13:17 Uba lisazi lezizinto, libusisiwe uba lizenza." 
John13:18 Kangikhulumi ngani lonke. 
John13:19 Sengilitshela kusukela khathesi kungakenzeki. 
John13:20 Ngiqinisile, ngiqinisile, ngithi kini: Owemukela loba ngubani engimthumileyo, wemukela mina; lowemukela mina, wemukela ongithumileyo." 
John13:21 UJesu esetshilo. 
John13:22 Ngakho abafundi bakhangelana, bengaqondi ukuthi ukhuluma ngobani." 
John13:23 Kwakweyeme esifubeni sikaJesu omunye wabafundi bakhe; 
John13:24 ngakho uSimoni Petro wamqhweba ukubuza ukuthi ngubani akhuluma ngaye. 
John13:25 Yena-ke eqamela esifubeni sikaJesu, wathi kuye: Nkosi, ngubani?" 
John13:26 UJesu waphendula wathi: Ngulowo mina engizamnika ucezu sengilutshebile. 
John13:27 Futhi emva kocezu, uSathane wasengena kuye." 
John13:28 Kodwa kakho kwababehlezi ekudleni owayekwazi ukuthi ukutsholoni kuye. 
John13:29 Ngoba abanye bacabanga ukuthi, njengoba uJudasi wayelesikhwama; loba ukuthi kanike abayanga okunye." 
John13:30 Lowo wathi eselwemukele ucezu, wahle waphuma; kwakusebusuku." 
John13:31 Ngakho kwathi esephumile, uJesu wathi: Khathesi iNdodana yomuntu idunyisiwe." 
John13:32 Uba uNkulunkulu edunyiswe kuyo. 
John13:33 Bantwanyana, ngiselani isikhatshana. Lizangidinga: Lapho mina engiya khona, lingeze leza lina; ngitsho lakini khathesi." 
John13:34 Ngilinika. 
John13:35 Ngalokhu bonke bazakwazi ukuthi lingabafundi bami, uba lilothando omunye komunye." 
John13:36 USimoni Petro wathi kuye: Nkosi, uya ngaphi." 
John13:37 UPetro wathi kuye: Nkosi, ngingekulandele khathesi ngani? Impilo yami ngizayibekela wena phansi." 
John13:38 UJesu wamphendula wathi: Impilo yakho uzayibekela mina phansi yini. 
John14:1 Inhliziyo yenu kayingakhathazeki; liyakholwa kuNkulunkulu, kholwani lakimi." 
John14:2 Ekhaya likaBaba kukhona izindlu ezinengi; kodwa uba kwaku ngenjalo, ngabe ngalitshela." 
John14:3 Njalo nxa ngihamba ngisiyalilungisela indawo, ngizabuya futhi ngilemukele kimi." 
John14:4 Lalapho mina engiya khona liyakwazi, lendlela liyayazi." 
John14:5 UTomasi wathi kuye? 
John14:6 UJesu wathi kuye: Mina ngiyindlela. 
John14:7 Uba belingazile, belizamazi loBaba." 
John14:8 UFiliphu wathi kuye: Nkosi, sitshengise uYihlo, njalo kusanele." 
John14:9 UJesu wathi kuye: Sengilani isikhathi eside kangaka, kawukangazi, Filiphu? Yena obone mina, ubone uBaba; njalo utsho njani ukuthi: Sitshengise uYihlo?" 
John14:10 Kawukholwa yini ukuthi mina ngikuBaba, loBaba ukimi." 
John14:11 Ngikholwani ukuthi mina ngikuBaba, loBaba ukimi." 
John14:12 Ngiqinisile, ngiqinisile, ngithi kini: Okholwa kimi, imisebenzi engiyenzayo uzayenza laye." 
John14:13 Njalo loba yini eliyicelayo, ukuze uYise adunyiswe eNdodaneni." 
John14:14 Uba licela loba yini ebizweni lami, mina ngiza y enza." 
John14:15 Uba lingithanda, londolozani imilayo yami." 
John14:16 Lami ngizacela kuBaba, laye uzalinika omunye uMduduzi, ukuze ahlale lani laphakade," 
John14:17 uMoya weqiniso. 
John14:18 Kangiyikulitshiya lizintandane; ngizakuza kini. 
John14:19 Kube kanti okwesikhatshana. 
John14:20 Ngalolosuku lina lizakwazi. 
John14:21 Olemilayo yami ayilondoloze, nguye ongithandayo." 
John14:22 UJudasi, ongesuye uIskariyothi, wathi kuye: Nkosi, kungani uzazibonakalisa kithi, kodwa kungeyisikho kumhlaba?" 
John14:23 UJesu waphendula wathi kuye: Uba umuntu engithanda. 
John14:24 Yena ongangithandiyo, kawalondolozi amazwi ami; lelizwi elilizwayo kayisilo elami, kodwa ngelikaBaba ongithumileyo." 
John14:25 Lezizinto ngizikhulumile kini ngihlezi lani. 
John14:26 Kodwa uMduduzi, uMoya oyiNgcwele." 
John14:27 Ukuthula ngikutshiya kini. 
John14:28 Lizwile ukuthi mina ngithe kini. 
John14:29 Njalo khathesi ngilitshelile kungakenzeki; ukuze, lapho sekusenzeka, likholwe." 
John14:30 Kangisayikukhuluma okunengi lani; 
John14:31 kodwa ukuze umhlaba wazi. 
John15:1 Mina ngilivini eliqotho, njalo uBaba ungumlimi." 
John15:2 Lonke ugatsha olukimi olungatheliyo isithelo, uyalususa; lalo lonke oluthela isithelo, uyaluthena, ukuze lwengeze ukuthela." 
John15:3 Selihlambululekile. 
John15:4 Hlalani kimi, lami kini. Njengalokhu ugatsha lungethele isithelo ngokwalo, uba lungahlali evinini, ngokunjalo lani lingeke, uba lingahlali kimi." 
John15:5 Mina ngilivini, lina lizingatsha; ngoba ngaphandle kwami lingenze lutho." 
John15:6 Uba umuntu engahlali kimi, ulahlelwa phandle njengogatsha, abe esebuna." 
John15:7 Uba lihlala kimi. 
John15:8 UBaba uyadunyiswa ngalokhu, ukuthi lithele isithelo sande." 
John15:9 Njengalokhu uBaba engithandile, lami ngilithandile; hlalani ethandweni lwami." 
John15:10 Uba lilondoloza imilayo yami, lizahlala ethandweni lwami." 
John15:11 Lezizinto ngizikhulume kini, ukuze intokozo yami ihlale kini." 
John15:12 Lo ngumlayo wami, ukuthi lithandane, njengalokhu ngilithandile." 
John15:13 Kakho olothando olukhulu kulalolu. 
John15:14 Lina lingabangane bami. 
John15:15 Kangisalibizi ngokuthi lizinceku, ngoba inceku kayikwazi ukuthi inkosi yayo yenzani; kodwa sengilibize ngokuthi lingabangane, ngoba konke engikuzwileyo kuBaba." 
John15:16 Kalingikhethanga lina, kodwa mina ngilikhethile." 
John15:17 Ngililaya lezizinto, ukuze lithandane." 
John15:18 Uba umhlaba ulizonda. 
John15:19 Uba belingabomhlaba, umhlaba ubuzathanda abawo." 
John15:20 Khumbulani ilizwi mina engalitsho kini: Inceku kayinkulu kulenkosi yayo. 
John15:21 Kodwa bazakwenza konke lokhu. 
John15:22 Uba bengingafikanga ngakhuluma labo, ngabe kabalasono." 
John15:23 Ongizondayo, uzonda loBaba." 
John15:24 Uba bengingenzanga phakathi kwabo imisebenzi kungekho omunye owayenzayo. 
John15:25 Kodwa ukuze ligcwaliseke ilizwi elilotshiweyo emlayweni wabo elokuthi. 
John15:26 Kodwa nxa esefikile uMduduzi; 
John15:27 lani futhi lizafakaza. 
John16:1 Lezizinto ngizikhulume kini. 
John16:2 Bazalimisa emasinagogeni. 
John16:3 Lalezizinto bazazenza kini, ngoba bengamazanga uBaba loba mina." 
John16:4 Kodwa ngikhulume lezizinto kini. 
John16:5 Kodwa khathesi ngiyahamba ngiya kongithumileyo? 
John16:6 Kodwa ngoba ngikhulume lezizinto kini, usizi lugcwalise inhliziyo yenu." 
John16:7 Kodwa mina ngilitshela iqiniso: Kulilungele ukuthi mina ngihambe; ngoba nxa ngingahambi, uMduduzi." 
John16:8 Nxa esefikile yena uzaqinisekisa umhlaba ngesono langokulunga langesigwebo; 
John16:9 ngesono; 
John16:10 langokulunga; 
John16:11 langesigwebo. 
John16:12 Ngiseselezinto ezinengi engingalitshela zona; 
John16:13 kodwa nxa yena esefikile, uMoya weqiniso." 
John16:14 Yena uzangidumisa. 
John16:15 Konke uBaba alakho, kungokwami." 
John16:16 Okwesikhatshana futhi kaliyikungibona. 
John16:17 Ngakho abanyekubafundi bakhe bakhulumisana besithi: Kuyini lokho akutsho kithi: Okwesikhatshana, futhi kaliyikungibona, kubuye kube yisikhatshana libe selingibona; lokuthi: Ngoba mina ngiya kuBaba?" 
John16:18 Basebesithi: Kuyini lokhu akutshoyo ukuthi: Okwesikhatshana? Kasazi ukuthi utshoni. 
John16:19 UJesu wayesesazi ukuthi babethanda ukumbuza? 
John16:20 Ngiqinisile, ngiqinisile, ngithi kini: Lina lizakhala lilile." 
John16:21 Owesifazana nxa ebeletha ulobuhlungu, ngoba ihola lakhe selifikile; kodwa nxa esebelethe usane, kasakhumbuli ubuhlungu, ngenxa yentokozo yokuthi kuzelwe umuntu emhlabeni." 
John16:22 Ngakho lani-ke lilosizi khathesi. 
John16:23 Langalolosuku kaliyikungibuza lutho. 
John16:24 Kuze kube khathesi kalicelanga lutho ebizweni lami; celani, lizakwemukeliswa, ukuze intokozo yenu igcwale." 
John16:25 Ngikhulume izinto lezi kini ngemifanekiso; kodwa isikhathi siyeza lapho ngingasayikukhuluma kini ngemifanekiso, kodwa ngizalitshela ngoBaba ngokucacileyo." 
John16:26 Ngalolosuku lizacela ebizweni lami; njalo kangitsho kini ukuthi ngizalicelela mina kuBaba; 
John16:27 ngoba uBaba uqobo uyalithanda, ngoba lina lingithandile." 
John16:28 Ngiphume kuBaba, njalo ngeza emhlabeni." 
John16:29 Abafundi bakhe bathi kuye: Khangela khathesi ukhuluma ngokucacileyo, njalo kawukhulumi lamfanekiso." 
John16:30 Khathesi siyazi ukuthi uyazi izinto zonke, njalo kawudingi ukuthi umuntu akubuze." 
John16:31 UJesu wabaphendula wathi: Selikholwa yini? 
John16:32 Khangelani, ihola liyeza, yebo selifikile." 
John16:33 Ngikhulume lezizinto kini, ukuze libe lokuthula kimi."

John17:2 njengoba uyinikile amandla phezu kwayo yonke inyama. 
John17:3 Lalokhu yimpilo elaphakade, ukuthi bazi wena." 
John17:4 Mina ngikudumisile emhlabeni; 
John17:5 khathesi-ke ngidumise wena, Baba." 
John17:6 Ngilibonakalisile ibizo lakho ebantwini. 
John17:7 Khathesi sebesazi ukuthi konke, loba yikuphi onginike khona, kuvela kuwe;" 
John17:8 ngoba amazwi onginike wona, ngibanikile wona; ba we mukela." 
John17:9 Mina ngiyabakhulekela bona; 
John17:10 njalo konke okwami kungokwakho, lokwakho kungokwami." 
John17:11 Njalo kangisekho emhlabeni. 
John17:12 Lapho ngiselabo emhlabeni, mina ngabalondoloza." 
John17:13 Kodwa khathesi ngiza kuwe. 
John17:14 Mina ngibanikile ilizwi lakho. 
John17:15 Kangiceli ukuthi ubasuse emhlabeni, kodwa ukuze ubalondoloze." 
John17:16 Kabasibo abomhlaba, njengalokhu mina ngingesuye owomhlaba." 
John17:17 Bangcwelise. 
John17:18 Njengalokhu wangithuma emhlabeni, lami ngibathumile emhlabeni." 
John17:19 Njalo mina ngizehlukanisela bona. 
John17:20 Njalo kangiceleli laba bodwa, kodwa lalabo abazakholwa kimi ngelizwi labo;" 
John17:21 ukuze bonke babe munye. 
John17:22 Lenkazimulo mina onginike yona. 
John17:23 Mina ngikubo, lawe ukimi." 
John17:24 Baba, labo onginike bona." 
John17:25 Baba olungileyo; 
John17:26 njalo ngibazisile ibizo lakho, njalo ngizabazisa lona." 
John18:1 UJesu esekhulumile lezizinto waphuma kanye labafundi bakhe. 
John18:2 Njalo uJudasi laye, owamnikelayo, wayeyazi lindawo." 
John18:3 Ngakho uJudasi, esethethe." 
John18:4 Kwathi uJesu, ekwazi konke okwakuzamehlela, waphuma wathi kubo: Lidinga bani?" 
John18:5 Bamphendula bathi: UJesu weNazaretha. UJesu wathi kubo: Mina ngingu ye. LoJudasi owamnikelayo laye wayemi labo. 
John18:6 Ngakho kuthe esithi kubo: Mina ngingu ye; bahlehla nyovane, bawela phansi." 
John18:7 Wasephinda wababuza wathi: Lidinga bani? Basebesithi: UJesu weNazaretha. 
John18:8 UJesu waphendula wathi: Ngilitshelile ukuthi mina ngingu ye; ngakho uba lidinga mina, yekelani laba bahambe;" 
John18:9 ukuze ligcwaliseke ilizwi ayelikhulumile elokuthi: Kulabo owanginika bona, angilahlekelwanga lamunye wabo." 
John18:10 Kwathi uSimoni Petro elenkemba wayihwatsha, wagadla inceku yompristi omkhulu, waquma indlebe yayo yokunene. Lebizo lenceku lalinguMalikusi." 
John18:11 UJesu wasesithi kuPetro: Faka inkemba yakho esikhwameni; inkezo uBaba anginike yona, kangiyikuyinatha yini?" 
John18:12 Ngakho isigaba, bambopha," 
John18:13 basebemusa. 
John18:14 Kwakunguye uKayafasi owayecebise amaJuda, ukuthi kwakulungile ukuthi umuntu oyedwa afele isizwe." 
John18:15 USimoni Petro wasemlandela uJesu; 
John18:16 kodwa uPetro wayemi ngaphandle emnyango. 
John18:17 Incekukazi encane engumlindisango yasisithi kuPetro: Kawusuye lawe omunye wabafundi balumuntu yini? Yena wathi: Kangisu ye. 
John18:18 Njalo izinceku labancedisi, njalo besotha; uPetro laye wayemi labo esotha." 
John18:19 Umpristi omkhulu wasembuza uJesu ngabafundi bakhe, langemfundiso yakhe." 
John18:20 UJesu wamphendula wathi: Mina ngikhulume obala emhlabeni. 
John18:21 Ubuzelani kimi? Buza labo abakuzwayo lokho engakukhuluma labo. 
John18:22 Kwathi esetshilo lezizinto, omunye wabancedisi?" 
John18:23 UJesu wamphendula wathi: Uba ngikhulume kubi, fakaza ngobubi; kodwa uba kuhle, ungitshayelani?" 
John18:24 UAnasi wasemthuma ebotshiwe kuKayafasi umpristi omkhulu. 
John18:25 Kodwa uSimoni Petro wayemi esotha. 
John18:26 Omunye wezinceku zompristi omkhulu, oyisinini somuntu uPetro aquma indlebe yakhe, wathi: Mina kangikubonanga yini esivandeni ulaye?" 
John18:27 UPetro wasebuya ephika; njalo lahle lakhala iqhude. 
John18:28 Basebemkhupha uJesu. 
John18:29 Ngakho uPilatu waphumela kubo, wathi: Limbeka cala bani lumuntu?" 
John18:30 Basebephendula bathi kuye: Uba lo ubengesuye owenza okubi, ngabe kasimnikelanga kuwe." 
John18:31 UPilatu wasesithi kubo: Mthatheni lina, limahlulele njengomlayo wakini. Ngakho amaJuda athi kuye: Kakuvunyelwa kithi ukubulala umuntu;" 
John18:32 ukuze kugcwaliseke ilizwi uJesu alikhulumayo, ukutshengisa uhlobo lokufa ayezakufa ngalo." 
John18:33 Ngakho uPilatu wabuye wangena endlini yombusi, wambiza uJesu, wathi kuye: Wena uyiNkosi yamaJuda yini?" 
John18:34 UJesu wamphendula wathi: Uyazitsholo lokhu wena yini, kumbe abanye bakutshelile ngami?" 
John18:35 UPilatu waphendula wathi: Kanti ngingumJuda mina? Isizwe sakini labapristi abakhulu bakunikele kimi; wenzeni? 
John18:36 UJesu waphendula wathi: Umbuso wami; kodwa khathesi umbuso wami kawusiwo owalapha. 
John18:37 UPilatu wasesithi kuye: Ngakho uyinkosi yini? UJesu waphendula wathi: Uyatsho wena, ukuthi mina ngiyinkosi." 
John18:38 UPilatu wathi kuye: Liyini iqiniso? Kwathi esetshilo lokhu, wabuya waphumela kumaJuda." 
John18:39 Kodwa lilomkhuba, wokuthi ngilikhululele omunye ngephasika; ngakho liyathanda ukuthi ngilikhululele iNkosi yamaJuda yini?" 
John18:40 Wonke asememeza futhi. 
John19:1 Ngakho uPilatu wamthatha uJesu, wa m tshaya ngesiswepu." 
John19:2 Labebutho beluka umqhele wameva ba wu beka ekhanda lakhe," 
John19:3 basebesithi: Bayethe, Nkosi yamaJuda! Basebemtshaya ngempama." 
John19:4 UPilatu wasebuya waphumela phandle, wathi kubo: Khangelani, ngiyamkhuphela phandle kini." 
John19:5 UJesu wasephumela phandle, ethwele umqhele wameva embethe isembatho esiyibubende. UPilatuwasesithi kubo: Khangelani lumuntu!" 
John19:6 Kwathi abapristi abakhulu labancedisi. 
John19:7 AmaJuda amphendula athi: Silomlayo thina, langokomlayo wethu ufanele ukufa." 
John19:8 Kwathi uPilatu esizwa lelolizwi, wesaba kakhulu," 
John19:9 wangena futhi endlini yombusi. 
John19:10 Khona uPilatu wathi kuye: Kawukhulumi lami yini? Kawazi yini ukuthi ngilamandla okukubethela, njalo ngilamandla okukukhulula?" 
John19:11 UJesu wamphendula wathi: Ungeke ube lamandla phezu kwami. 
John19:12 Kusukela lapho uPilatu wadinga ukumkhulula. Kodwa amaJuda amemeza athi: Uba ukhulula lo, kawusuye umngane kaKesari; wonke ozenza inkosi, uphikisana loKesari." 
John19:13 Kwathi uPilatu esizwa lelilizwi wamkhuphela phandle uJesu; 
John19:14 njalo kwakungamalungiselelo ephasika! 
John19:15 Kodwa amemeza athi: Susa, susa, mbethele." 
John19:16 Ngakho wasemnikela kubo, ukuze abethelwe." 
John19:17 Kwathi ethwele isiphambano, ethiwa ngesiHebheru yiGolgotha;" 
John19:18 lapho abambethela khona, labanye ababili kanye laye, ngapha langapha, loJesu ephakathi." 
John19:19 UPilatu wasebhala lesaziso, wa si phanyeka esiphambanweni; njalo kwakubhalwe ukuthi: UJESU UMNAZARETHA INKOSI YAMAJUDA." 
John19:20 Lalesisaziso abanengi bamaJuda basifunda, ngoba indawo lapho uJesu ayebethelwe khona yayiseduze lomuzi." 
John19:21 Abapristi abakhulu bamaJuda basebesithi kuPilatu: Ungabhali ukuthi: INkosi yamaJuda; kodwa ukuthi lo wathi: NgiyiNkosi yamaJuda. 
John19:22 UPilatu waphendula wathi: Engikubhalileyo, ngikubhalile." 
John19:23 Kwathi abebutho, sebembethele uJesu, selukiwe sonke kusukela phezulu." 
John19:24 Ngakho bakhulumisana besithi: Kasingasidabuli, kodwa asisenzele inkatho, ukuthi sizakuba ngesikabani; ukuze kugcwaliseke umbhalo othi: Babelana izembatho zami, benza inkatho yokuphosa ngesigqoko sami. Azenza-ke lezizinto amabutho." 
John19:25 Kwakumi esiphambanweni sikaJesu unina, lodadewabo kanina." 
John19:26 Ngakho uJesu ebona unina, lomfundi amthandayo bemi khona." 
John19:27 Emva kwalokho wathi kumfundi: Khangela unyoko. Kusukela ngalelohola lowomfundi wamthatha wamusa kwakhe. 
John19:28 Emva kwalokhu uJesu ekwazi ukuthi konke kwasekuphelile, ukuze kugcwaliseke umbhalo, wathi: Ngomile." 
John19:29 Kwakubekwe isitsha sigcwele iviniga. 
John19:30 Kwathi-ke uJesu elemukele iviniga, wathi: Kuphelile." 
John19:31 Ngakho amaJuda, ngoba kwakungamalungiselelo), acela uPilatu ukuthi yephulwe imilenze yabo, njalo basuswe." 
John19:32 Ngakho abebutho beza, bephula imilenze yowokuqala leyomunye ababebethelwe laye;" 
John19:33 kodwa sebefika kuJesu, kwathi bebona ukuthi wayesefile, kabayephulanga imilenze yakhe;" 
John19:34 kodwa omunye webutho wamgwaza ngomkhonto ehlangothini, njalo kwahle kwaphuma igazi lamanzi." 
John19:35 Yena owabonayo ufakazile, njalo ubufakazi bakhe buqinisile, yena-ke uyazi ukuthi ukhuluma okuliqiniso, ukuze lina likholwe." 
John19:36 Ngoba lezizinto zenzeka ukuze kugcwaliseke umbhalo othi: Kakuyikwephulwa thambo lakhe. 
John19:37 Njalo lomunye umbhalo uthi: Bazamkhangela abamgwazileyo. 
John19:38 Kwathi emva kwalezizinto uJosefa weArimathiya, wacela kuPilatu ukuthi asuse isidumbu sikaJesu; futhi uPilatu wavuma. Ngakho weza wasisusa isidumbu sikaJesu." 
John19:39 Kwasekusiza loNikodima. 
John19:40 Basebesithatha isidumbu sikaJesu, basibopha ngamalembu acolekileyo kanye lamakha." 
John19:41 Njalo kwakukhona kuleyondawo ayebethelwe khona isivande, lesivandeni kwakulengcwaba elitsha, okwakungazange kubekwe muntu kulo." 
John19:42 Basebembeka lapho uJesu ngenxa yamalungiselelo amaJuda, ngoba ingcwaba laliseduze." 
John20:1 Kwathi ngolokuqala lweviki uMariya Magadalena wafika engcwabeni ekuseni kakhulu, kusesemnyama." 
John20:2 Ngakho wagijima weza kuSimoni Petro lakomunye umfundi uJesu ayemthanda, wathi kubo: Bayisusile iNkosi engcwabeni, njalo kasazi lapho abayibeke khona." 
John20:3 Ngakho uPetro waphuma lomunye umfundi, bafika engcwabeni." 
John20:4 Basebegijima bobabili kanyekanye; omunye umfundi wasegijima phambili ngesiqubu kuloPetro, wafika kuqala engcwabeni." 
John20:5 Kwathi ekhothama elunguza. 
John20:6 USimoni Petro wasefika emlandela, wangena engcwabeni, wabona amalembu acolekileyo endlelwe," 
John20:7 lelembu lobuso elalisekhanda lakhe, lingabekwanga lamalembu acolekileyo, kodwa lendluliwe lisendaweni yalolodwa." 
John20:8 Ngakho wasengena laye omunye umfundi owayefike kuqala engcwabeni, wabona, wakholwa;" 
John20:9 ngoba babengakaqedisisi. 
John20:10 Basebesuka futhi abafundi baya kibo. 
John20:11 Kodwa uMariya wema engcwabeni phandle ekhala," 
John20:12 wasebona ingilosi ezimbili zembetheezimhlophe zihlezi, enye isemakhanda, lenye ingasenyaweni, lapho isidumbu sikaJesu ebesilele khona." 
John20:13 Zona zasezisithi kuye: Mama, ukhalelani? Wathi kuzo: Ngoba bayithethe iNkosi yami, njalo kangazi lapho abayibeke khona." 
John20:14 Kwathi esetshilo lezizinto watshibilika, wabona uJesu emi." 
John20:15 UJesu wathi kuye: Mama, ukhalelani? Udinga bani." 
John20:16 UJesu wathi kuye: Mariya! Yena watshibilika wathi kuye: Raboni! okuyikuthi: Mfundisi. 
John20:17 UJesu wathi kuye: Ungangibambi, ngoba kangikenyukeli kuBaba." 
John20:18 UMariya Magadalena weza wababikela abafundi ukuthi uyibonile iNkosi, njalo imtshele lezizinto." 
John20:19 Kwathi kusihlwa ngalolosuku, olokuqala lweviki." 
John20:20 Njalo esetshilo lokhu wabatshengisa izandla zakhelohlangothi lwakhe. 
John20:21 UJesu wasebuya esithi kubo: Ukuthula kakubekini. 
John20:22 Kwathi esetshilo lokhu waphephetha phezu kwabowathi kubo: Yemukelani uMoya oNgcwele. 
John20:23 Loba ngobani elithethelela izono zabo, bathethelelwe; loba ngobani elibamba ezabo, zibanjiwe." 
John20:24 Kodwa uTomasi, omunye wabalitshumi lambili, othiwa nguDidimusi, wayengekho labo mhla uJesu efika." 
John20:25 Ngakho abanye abafundi bathi kuye: Siyibonile iNkosi. Kodwa yena wathi kubo: Uba ngingaboni ezandleni zayo amanxeba ezipikili, njalo ngifake umunwe wami enxebeni lezipikili, njalo ngibeke izandla zami ehlangothini lwayo, kangisoze ngikholwe." 
John20:26 Njalo emva kwensuku eziyisificaminwembili abafundi bakhe babephakathi futhi, loTomasi elabo. UJesu wafika." 
John20:27 Wasesithi kuTomasi: Letha umunwe wakho lapha, ubone izandla zami; njalo letha isandla sakho, u si fake ehlangothini lwami; njalo ungabi ngongakholwayo, kodwa okholwayo." 
John20:28 UTomasi wasephendula, wathi kuye: Nkosi yami loNkulunkulu wami!" 
John20:29 UJesu wathi kuye: Ngoba usungibonile, Tomasi, ukholiwe; babusisiwe abangabonanga." 
John20:30 Njalo, ezingalotshwanga kulolugwalo." 
John20:31 Kodwa lezi zilotshiwe, ukuze likholwe ukuthi uJesu unguKristu." 
John21:1 Emva kwalezizinto uJesu wabuya wazibonakalisa; njalo wazibonakalisa ngalindlela. 
John21:2 Babendawonye oSimoni Petro, loTomasi othiwa nguDidimusi." 
John21:3 USimoni Petro wathi kubo: Ngiyagola inhlanzi. Bathi kuye: Lathi sizahamba lawe. Basebephuma bahle bangena emkhunjini. 
John21:4 Kwathi sekusemadabukakusa uJesu wema ekhunjini. 
John21:5 Ngakho uJesu wathi kubo: Bantwana, lilokudla yini." 
John21:6 Wasesithi kubo: Phosani imbule ehlangothini lokunene lomkhumbi, njalo lizathola. Basebephosa, njalo babengaselakho ukulidonsa ngenxa yobunengi benhlanzi." 
John21:7 Ngakho lowomfundi uJesu ayemthanda wathi kuPetro), waseziphosela olwandle." 
John21:8 Kodwa abanye abafundi beza ngomkolo, bedonsa imbule lenhlanzi, ngoba babengekhatshana lomhlabathi, kodwa kungaba zingalo ezingamakhulu amabili." 
John21:9 Kwathi sebekhuphukele emhlabathini, babona umlilo wamalahle." 
John21:10 UJesu wathi kubo: Lethani ezi nyezezinhlanzi elisanda kuzibamba. 
John21:11 USimoni Petro wasekhwela, wahudulela imbule emhlabathini, ligcwele inhlanzi ezinkulu, ikhulu lamatshumi amahlanu lantathu; njalo lanxa zazinengi kangaka, imbule kalidabukanga." 
John21:12 UJesu wathi kubo: Wozani. Kodwa kakho kubafundi owaba lesibindi sokumbuza ukuthi: Ungubani wena? besazi ukuthi yiNkosi. 
John21:13 UJesu wasesiza. 
John21:14 Lokhu sekungokwesithathu uJesu ebonakaliswa. 
John21:15 Sebedlile? Wathi kuye: Yebo Nkosi; wena uyazi ukuthi ngiyakuthanda. Wathi kuye: Phana amawundlu ami ukudla. 
John21:16 Wabuya wathi kuye ngokwesibili: Simoni kaJona, uyangithanda yini." 
John21:17 Wathi kuye ngokwesithathu: Simoni kaJona, uyangithanda yini. UJesu wathi kuye: Phana izimvu zami ukudla." 
John21:18 Ngiqinisile, ngiqinisile, ngithi kuwe." 
John21:19 Lalokhu wakutsho, etshengisa indlela yokufa." 
John21:20 UPetro etshibilika wabona umfundi uJesu amthandayo elandela? 
John21:21 Kwathi uPetro embona wathi kuJesu: Nkosi, lo-ke?" 
John21:22 UJesu wathi kuye: Uba ngithanda ukuthi ahlale. 
John21:23 Ngakho lelilizwi laphumela kubazalwane, ukuthi lowomfundi kayikufa; kanti uJesu katshongo kuye ukuthi kayikufa; kodwa wathi: Uba ngithanda ukuthi ahlale ngize ngifike, ulani lakho?" 
John21:24 Nguye lowomfundi ofakaza ngalezizinto, lozibhalileyo; njalo siyazi." 
John21:25 Njalo zikhona lezinye izinto ezinengi uJesu azenzayo, uba bezilotshiwe zonke ngazinye." 
Acts1:1 Umbiko wokuqala ngawenza, Teyofilu, ngakho konke uJesu aqala kokubili ukukwenza lokukufundisa," 
Acts1:2 kwaze kwaba lusuku enyuswa ngalo; 
Acts1:3 wazibonakalisa futhi kubo. 
Acts1:4 Kwathi ehlangene labo, wabalaya ukuthi bangasuki eJerusalema;" 
Acts1:5 ngoba ngeqiniso uJohane wabhabhathiza ngamanzi. 
Acts1:6 Kwathi sebebuthene bambuza bathi: Nkosi, uzabuyisela umbuso kuIsrayeli kulesisikhathi yini?" 
Acts1:7 Wasesithi kubo: Kakusikho okwenu; 
Acts1:8 kodwa lizakwemukela amandla. 
Acts1:9 Kwathi esetshilo lezizinto, wenyuswa bekhangele, leyezi lamsusa emehlweni abo." 
Acts1:10 Bathi besajolozele ezulwini, esenyuka," 
Acts1:11 njalo athi: Madoda maGalili, limeleni lijolozele ezulwini." 
Acts1:12 Basebebuyela eJerusalema. 
Acts1:13 Kwathi sebengenile, benyukela endlini ephezulu." 
Acts1:14 Bonke laba baphikelela. 
Acts1:15 Kwathi ngalezonsuku uPetro wasukuma phakathi kwabafundi, kwakulexuku labantu ndawonye elalingaba likhulu lamatshumi amabili, wathi:" 
Acts1:16 Madoda bazalwane, kwakumele ukuthi lumbhalo ugcwaliswe, uMoya oyiNgcwele awukhuluma ngaphambili ngomlomo kaDavida ngoJudasi," 
Acts1:17 ngoba wayebalwe kanye lathi. 
Acts1:18 Lo-ke wathenga isiqinti. 
Acts1:19 Njalo kwaziwa yibo bonke abakhileyo eJerusalema, saze sabizwa lesosiqinti ngolimi lwakibo ngokuthiiAkeldama." 
Acts1:20 Ngoba kulotshiwe egwalweni lweziHlabelelo ukuthi: Umuzi wakhe kawube lunxiwa, njalo kungabi khona ohlala kuwo." 
Acts1:21 Ngakho kumele ukuthi kulawomadoda ayehamba lathi kuso sonke isikhathi lapho iNkosi uJesu yayingena njalo iphuma phakathi kwethu," 
Acts1:22 kusukela ebhabhathizweni lukaJohane. 
Acts1:23 Basebemisa ababili, uJosefa othiwa nguBarsaba, othiwa futhi nguJustusi." 
Acts1:24 Basebekhuleka, omkhethileyo" 
Acts1:25 ukwemukela isabelo kulinkonzo. 
Acts1:26 Basebebapha inkatho yabo; lenkatho yadla uMathiyasi, wasebalwa kanye labaphostoli abalitshumi lanye." 
Acts2:1 Kwathi selugcwalisekile. 
Acts2:2 Kwahle kwezwakala-ke umdumo ovela ezulwini," 
Acts2:3 kwasekubonakala kubo inlimi ezehlukanisiweyo kungathi ngezomlilo, zasezihlala phezu kwalowo lalowo wabo." 
Acts2:4 Basebegcwaliswa bonke ngoMoya oNgcwele. 
Acts2:5 Kwakuhlala-ke eJerusalema amaJuda, amadoda aqotho, avela kuso sonke isizwe salezo ezingaphansi kwezulu." 
Acts2:6 Kwathi sekulalo umdumo, ixuku labuthana ndawonye lasanganiseka, ngoba ngulowo lalowo wabezwa bekhuluma ngolimi lwakibo." 
Acts2:7 Basebemangala kakhulu bonke bababaza? 
Acts2:8 Kungani, pho, thina sibezwa ngamunye wabo ngolimi lwakithi esazalwa lalo?" 
Acts2:9 AmaPathiya lamaMede," 
Acts2:10 abeFrigiya," 
Acts2:11 amaKrete. 
Acts2:12 Bonke basebemangala kakhulu? 
Acts2:13 Kodwa abanye bahleka usulu bathi: Basuthi iwayini elitsha. 
Acts2:14 Kodwa uPetro emi labalitshumi lanye. 
Acts2:15 Ngoba laba kabadakwanga, njengoba lina licabanga;" 
Acts2:16 kodwa lokhu yikho okwakhulunywa ngumprofethi uJoweli: 
Acts2:17 Njalo kuzakuthi ensukwini zokucina, utsho uNkulunkulu;" 
Acts2:18 njalo laphezu kwenceku zami laphezu kwencekukazi zami ngalezonsuku ngizathulula okoMoya wami, njalo zizaprofetha." 
Acts2:19 Njalo ngizaveza izimangaliso ezulwini phezulu; 
Acts2:20 ilanga lizaphendulwa umnyama, lenyanga igazi, lungakafiki usuku lweNkosi olukhulu loludumisekayo;" 
Acts2:21 kuzakuthi, wonke obiza ibizo leNkosi uzasindiswa." 
Acts2:22 Madoda maIsrayeli, zwanini la amazwi: UJesu weNazaretha," 
Acts2:23 yena lo esenikelwe; 
Acts2:24 yena uNkulunkulu wamvusa. 
Acts2:25 Ngoba uDavida uthi ngaye: Ngangibona iNkosi phambi kwami njalonjalo; ngoba ingakwesokunene sami, ukuze nginganyikinyeki;" 
Acts2:26 ngakho inhliziyo yami yajabula, lolimi lwami lwathokoza; ngitsho lenyama yami izahlala ethembeni;" 
Acts2:27 ngoba kawuyikutshiya umphefumulo wami esihogweni, kawuyikunikela oNgcwele wakho ukuthi abone ukubola." 
Acts2:28 Wangazisa indlela zempilo; uzangigcwalisa ngenjabulo ebusweni bakho. 
Acts2:29 Madoda bazalwane, ake ngikhulume kini ngokusobala ngokhokho uDavida." 
Acts2:30 Yena-ke engumprofethi, ekwazi ukuthi uNkulunkulu wafunga ngesifungo kuye," 
Acts2:31 ebonile ngaphambili wakhuluma ngokuvuka kukaKristu, ukuthi umphefumulo wakhe kawutshiywanga, lenyama yakhe kayikubonanga ukubola." 
Acts2:32 UJesu lo uNkulunkulu wamvusa. 
Acts2:33 Ngakho ephakanyiswe ngakwesokunene sikaNkulunkulu khathesi. 
Acts2:34 Ngoba uDavida kenyukelanga, kodwa yena uqobo lwakhe uthi: INkosi yathi eNkosini yami: Hlala ngakwesokunene sami," 
Acts2:35 ngize ngenze izitha zakho zibe yisenabelo senyawo zakho. 
Acts2:36 Ngakho indlu kaIsrayeli yonke kayazi isibili, ukuthi uNkulunkulu umenzile kokubili." 
Acts2:37 Sebekuzwa lokhubahlabeka enhliziyweni? 
Acts2:38 UPetro wasesithi kubo: Phendukani. 
Acts2:39 Ngoba isithembiso ngesenu, lesabantwana benu." 
Acts2:40 Langamanye amazwi amanengi wafakaza wakhuthaza wathi. 
Acts2:41 Ngakho abalemukelayo ilizwi lakhe ngokuthokoza babhabhathizwa. 
Acts2:42 Basebephikelela ekufundiseni kwabaphostoli lebudlelwaneni, lekuhlephuleni isinkwa lemikhulekweni." 
Acts2:43 Lokwesaba kwehlela phezu kwayo yonke imiphefumulo. 
Acts2:44 Njalo bonke abakholwayo babendawonye," 
Acts2:45 basebethengisa izinto lempahla zabo. 
Acts2:46 Insuku ngensuku basebephikelela," 
Acts2:47 bedumisa uNkulunkulu. 
Acts3:1 UPetro loJohane. 
Acts3:2 Kwasekuthwalwa indoda ethile eyayiyisiqhuli kusukela esizalweni sikanina. 
Acts3:3 Eyathi ibona uPetro loJohane sebezangena ethempelini, yacela isipho." 
Acts3:4 UPetro waseyijolozela eloJohane, wathi: Sikhangele!" 
Acts3:5 Yasibananzelela, ilindele ukuthi izakwemukela ulutho kubo." 
Acts3:6 UPetro wasesithi: Isiliva legolide kangilakho; kodwa lokho engilakho, ngikunika khona; ebizweni likaJesu Kristu umNazaretha, sukuma uhambe." 
Acts3:7 Waseyibamba ngesandla sokunene wa yi sukumisa; njalo kwahle kwaqiniswa inyawo lenqagala zayo. 
Acts3:8 Yasisithi lothu yema yasihamba. 
Acts3:9 Njalo bonke abantu bayibona ihamba, idumisa uNkulunkulu;" 
Acts3:10 basebeyazi ukuthi yiyo. 
Acts3:11 Kwathi isiqhuli esasisilisiwe sibambelele kuPetro loJohane, bemangala kakhulu." 
Acts3:12 Kwathi uPetro e ku bona lokhowaphendula ebantwini wathi: Madoda maIsrayeli? 
Acts3:13 UNkulunkulu kaAbrahama lokaIsaka lokaJakobe, uNkulunkulu wabobaba bethu." 
Acts3:14 Kodwa lina lamphika oNgcwele," 
Acts3:15 labulala uMqali. 
Acts3:16 Njalo ngokholo ebizweni lakhe. 
Acts3:17 Njalo khathesi, bazalwane, ngiyazi ukuthi la k wenza ngokungazi." 
Acts3:18 Kodwa uNkulunkulu wagcwalisa ngalindlela ngomlomo wabaprofethi bakhe bonke, ukuthi uKristu uzahlupheka." 
Acts3:19 Ngakho phendukani, ukuze kufike izikhathi zokukhudumala ezivela ebusweni beNkosi," 
Acts3:20 njalo ithume lo owamenyezelwa kini phambili, uJesu Kristu;" 
Acts3:21 okumele ukuthi izulu limemukele. 
Acts3:22 Ngoba uMozisi wathi kubobaba: INkosi uNkulunkulu wenu izalivusela umprofethi kubazalwane benu onjengami. 
Acts3:23 Njalo kuzakuthi, wonke umphefumulo, loba ngubani ongayikumlalela lowomprofethi, uzachithwa ebantwini." 
Acts3:24 Njalo labaprofethi bonke. 
Acts3:25 Lina lingabantwana babaprofethi. 
Acts3:26 UNkulunkulu. 
Acts4:1 Kwathi besakhuluma ebantwini, abapristi lenduna yethempeli labaSadusi babafikela," 
Acts4:2 benengekile ngoba babefundisa abantu. 
Acts4:3 Babadumela ngezandla. 
Acts4:4 Kodwa abanengi abalizwayo ilizwi bakholwa; lenani lamadoda lalingaba zinkulungwane ezinhlanu. 
Acts4:5 Kwasekusithi kusisa kwabuthana ababusi labadala lababhali babo eJerusalema," 
Acts4:6 loAnasi umpristi omkhulu. 
Acts4:7 Sebebamise phakathi, babuza: Lokhu lina likwenze ngawaphi amandla kumbe ngaliphi ibizo?" 
Acts4:8 Khona uPetro egcwaliswe nguMoya oNgcwele wathi kubo," 
Acts4:9 nxa thina sibuzwa lamuhla ngomsebenzi omuhle emuntwini obuthakathaka emzimbeni; 
Acts4:10 kakwaziwe yini lonke laso sonke isizwe sakoIsrayeli, ukuthi ngebizo likaJesu Kristu umNazaretha, ngaye lo umi lapha phambi kwenu esesilile." 
Acts4:11 Yena lo uyilitshe. 
Acts4:12 Njalo kalukho usindiso komunye; ngoba kalikho lelinye ibizo ngaphansi kwezulu elinikiweyo phakathi kwabantu, esimele sisindiswe ngalo." 
Acts4:13 Kwathi bebona isibindi sikaPetro loJohane," 
Acts4:14 kodwa bebona umuntu osilisiweyo emi labo, babengelakuphika lutho." 
Acts4:15 Kodwa sebebalayile ukuthi baphume phandle emphakathini, bacebisana bodwa," 
Acts4:16 besithi: Sizabenzani lababantu; 
Acts4:17 kodwa ukuze kungabe kusanda phakathi kwabantu, asibaqonqosele ukuthi bangabe besakhuluma lamuntu ngalelibizo." 
Acts4:18 Basebebabiza, babalaya ukuthi bangakhulumi lakanye njalo bangafundisi ngebizo likaJesu." 
Acts4:19 Kodwa uPetro loJohane babaphendula bathi: Yehlukanisani ukuthi kulungile phambi kukaNkulunkulu ukulalela lina kuloNkulunkulu. 
Acts4:20 Ngoba thina izinto esizibonileyo lesizizwileyo. 
Acts4:21 Kwathi sebe ba qonqosele futhi, babayekela bahamba; bengatholi lutho lokuthi bangabajezisa njani, ngenxa yabantu." 
Acts4:22 Ngoba umuntu wayeleminyaka edlula amatshumi amane esenziwa kuye lesisibonakaliso seselapho. 
Acts4:23 Kwathi sebeyekelwe basuka baya kwabakibo, bababikela konke abapristi abakhulu labadala abakutshiloyo kubo." 
Acts4:24 Kwathi bona sebezwile baphakamisela ilizwi nganhliziyonye kuNkulunkulu; 
Acts4:25 owathi ngomlomo wenceku yakho uDavida: Kungani abezizwe bexokozela, labantu banakane okuyize?" 
Acts4:26 Amakhosi omhlaba ema, lababusi bahlangana ndawonye ukumelana leNkosi;" 
Acts4:27 ngoba isibili bahlangana ndawonye bemelane," 
Acts4:28 ukwenza konke isandla sakho lecebo lakho elakumisa phambili ukuthi kwenzeke. 
Acts4:29 Njalo ngalesisikhathi, Nkosi, khangela ukusonga kwabo," 
Acts4:30 ngokuthi welule isandla sakho ukusilisa, lokuthi kwenziwe izibonakaliso lezimangaliso." 
Acts4:31 Kwathi sebekhulekile kwazanyazanyiswa indawo ababebuthene kuyo. 
Acts4:32 Lexuku labakholwayo lalinhliziyo nye. 
Acts4:33 Langamandla amakhulu. 
Acts4:34 Ngoba kwakungekho futhi oswelayo phakathi kwabo; ngoba bonke ababelemihlaba kumbe izindlu, bathengisa baletha intengo zalokho okuthengisiweyo," 
Acts4:35 ba yi beka enyaweni zabaphostoli. 
Acts4:36 Kwathi uJose owabizwa ngabaphostoli ngokuthi nguBarnabasi," 
Acts4:37 elesiqinti, wa si thengisa." 
Acts5:1 Kodwa indoda ethile uAnaniya ngebizo, loSafira umkakhe, bathengisa impahla," 
Acts5:2 yagodla entengweni, lomkakhe ekwazi." 
Acts5:3 Kodwa uPetro wathi: Ananiya, kungani uSathane?" 
Acts5:4 Sisekhona besingesiso esakho, sesithengisiwe besingekho emandleni akho yini? Kungani ukuthi ubeke lesisenzo enhliziyweni yakho." 
Acts5:5 Kwathi uAnaniya esizwa lamazwi, wawela phansi waphela." 
Acts5:6 Lamajaha asuka. 
Acts5:7 Kwasekusithi sekungaba ngamahola amathathu kwedlule, lomkakhe wangena engakwazi okwenzakeleyo." 
Acts5:8 UPetro wasemphendula wathi: Ngitshele ukuthi isiqinti lisithengise ngokungaka. Wasesithi: Yebo, ngokungaka." 
Acts5:9 UPetro wasesithi kuye: Kungani ukuthi livumelane ukulinga. 
Acts5:10 Njalo wahle wawela phansi enyaweni zakhe. 
Acts5:11 Lokwesaba okukhulu kwehlela phezu kwebandla lonke, lakubo bonke abazizwayo lezizinto." 
Acts5:12 Njalo ngezandla zabaphostoli. 
Acts5:13 Kodwa kwabanye kwakungekho olesibindi sokuzihlanganisa labo; 
Acts5:14 njalo abakholwayo bengezelelwa banda eNkosini, amaxuku womabili amadoda labesifazana;" 
Acts5:15 baze bathwalela phandle emigwaqweni abagulayo, basebe ba beka ezinhlakeni lemacansini, ukuze kuthi lapho uPetro esiza ngitsho isithunzi sibasibekele abanye babo." 
Acts5:16 Njalo lamaxuku avela emizini ezingelezeleyo babuthana ndawonye eJerusalema, beletha abagulayo." 
Acts5:17 Kwasekusukuma umpristi omkhulu labo bonke ababelaye, bagcwala umona," 
Acts5:18 babadumela abaphostoli ngezandla zabo. 
Acts5:19 Kodwa ebusuku ingilosi yeNkosi: 
Acts5:20 Hambani, njalo lime likhulume ethempelini ebantwini." 
Acts5:21 Kwathi sebezwile, bangena ethempelini labo bonke abadala babantwana bakoIsrayeli, bathumela entolongweni ukubaletha." 
Acts5:22 Kodwa kwathi abancedisi befika kababaficanga entolongweni; babuyela emuva babika," 
Acts5:23 besithi: Intolongo siyifice ivaliwe konke kuqinile, labalindi bemi phandle phambi kweminyango; kodwa sesivulile, phakathi kasificanga muntu." 
Acts5:24 Njalo kwathi umpristi lenduna yethempeli labapristi abakhulu bezwe lamazwi. 
Acts5:25 Kwasekufika omunye wabatshela wathi: Khangelani, amadoda ebeliwafake entolongweni ami ethempelini afundisa abantu." 
Acts5:26 Yasihamba induna. 
Acts5:27 Sebebalethile ba ba misa phambi komphakathi. Umpristi omkhulu wasebabuza," 
Acts5:28 esithi: Kasililayisisanga. 
Acts5:29 Kodwa uPetro labaphostoli baphendula bathi: Kumele ukulalela uNkulunkulu kulabantu. 
Acts5:30 UNkulunkulu wabobaba. 
Acts5:31 Yena lo, uNkulunkulu wamphakamisa ngesandla sakhe sokunene." 
Acts5:32 Njalo thina singabafakazi bakhe balezizinto, njalo loMoya oyiNgcwele." 
Acts5:33 Kwathi sebezwile lokhubathukuthela kakhulu. 
Acts5:34 Kwasekusukuma umFarisi othile emphakathini. 
Acts5:35 Wasesithi kubo: Madoda maIsrayeli, ziqapheleni mayelana lalababantu, elizakwenza." 
Acts5:36 Ngoba ngaphambi kwalezinsuku kwasuka uTewuda, esithi yena ngokwakhe ungumuntu, lahlanganyela laye inani lamadoda angaba ngamakhulu amane; wabulawa, labo bonke ababemlalela bachitheka baphela." 
Acts5:37 Emva kwakhe kwasuka uJudasi umGalili ensukwini zokubalwa, wadonsela abantu abanengi ngemva kwakhe; laye wabhubha, lalabo bonke ababemlalela bachitheka." 
Acts5:38 Njalo khathesi ngithi kini: Dedani kulababantu, libayekele; ngoba uba lelicebo kumbe lumsebenzi ungowabantu, uzachitheka;" 
Acts5:39 kodwa uba ungokaNkulunkulu, lingeke lawuchitha, hlezi lificwe ngitsho lingabalwayo loNkulunkulu." 
Acts5:40 Basebemlalela; sebebabizele kubo abaphostoli. 
Acts5:41 Ngakho basuka ebusweni bomphakathi. 
Acts5:42 Njalo insuku zonke, ethempelini." 
Acts6:1 Kwathi ngalezonsuku, abafundi sebandile." 
Acts6:2 Abalitshumi lambili basebebizela kubo ixuku labafundi, bathi: Kakulunganga ukuthi thina sitshiye ilizwi likaNkulunkulu." 
Acts6:3 Ngakho, bazalwane, khangelani phakathi kwenu amadoda ayisikhombisa, esingawamisa phezu kwale inswelo." 
Acts6:4 Kodwa thina sizaphikelela emkhulekweni. 
Acts6:5 Lalelilizwi lalithokozisa lonke ixuku; basebekhetha uStefane, indoda egcwele ukholo loMoya oNgcwele," 
Acts6:6 ababamisa phambi kwabaphostoli; sebekhulekile. 
Acts6:7 Lelizwi likaNkulunkulu landa, lenani labafundi lakhula kakhulu sibili eJerusalema." 
Acts6:8 Kwathi uStefane egcwele ukholo lamandla wenza izimangaliso lezibonakaliso ezinkulu phakathi kwabantu. 
Acts6:9 Kwasekusukuma abanye abesinagoge elithiwa ngelabaKhululwa, labeKurene, baphikisana loStefane." 
Acts6:10 Kodwa babengelamandla okumelana lenhlakanipho loMoya ayekhuluma ngawo. 
Acts6:11 Basebefumbathisa amadoda athi: Simzwile ekhuluma amazwi ayinhlamba amelana loMozisi loNkulunkulu. 
Acts6:12 Basebevusa abantu labadala lababhali, basebe m fikela," 
Acts6:13 basebemisa abafakazi bamanga; 
Acts6:14 ngoba simzwile esithi, uJesu lo weNazaretha uzadiliza lindawo." 
Acts6:15 Bonke ababehlezi emphakathini. 
Acts7:1 Umpristi omkhulu wasesithi: Kambe lezizinto zinjalo? 
Acts7:2 Wasesithi: Madoda, bazalwane labobaba, lalelani," 
Acts7:3 wasesithi kuye: Phuma elizweni lakini lezihlotsheni zakho, uze elizweni engizakutshengisa lona." 
Acts7:4 Wasesuka elizweni lamaKhaladiya wahlala eHarani; 
Acts7:5 kodwa kamnikanga ilifa kilo, hatshi lanyathela." 
Acts7:6 UNkulunkulu wasekhuluma kanje esithi inzalo yakhe izakuba yisihambi elizweni lemzini, bazayenza isigqili baza yi phatha kubi;" 
Acts7:7 kodwa lesosizwe, abazakuba yizigqili kuso, ngizasigweba mina, kutsho uNkulunkulu; njalo emva kwalezizinto bazaphuma, bangikhonze kulindawo." 
Acts7:8 Wasemnika isivumelwano sokusoka. 
Acts7:9 Okhokho," 
Acts7:10 wasemkhulula kuzo zonke inhlupheko zakhe, wamnika umusa lenhlakanipho phambi kukaFaro inkosi yeGibhithe; wasembeka ukuba ngumbusi phezu kweGibhithe lowendlu yakhe yonke." 
Acts7:11 Kwasekufika indlala elizweni lonke leGibhithe leleKhanani, lokuhlupheka okukhulu; labobaba bethu kabatholanga ukudla." 
Acts7:12 Kodwa uJakobe esezwile ukuthi kukhona amabele eGibhithe, wathuma obaba bethu okokuqala." 
Acts7:13 Kwathi ngokwesibili. 
Acts7:14 UJosefa wasethumela wabizela kuye uyise uJakobe. 
Acts7:15 UJakobe wasesehlela eGibhithe; 
Acts7:16 basebethwalelwa. 
Acts7:17 Kwathi sesisondele isikhathi sesithembiso uNkulunkulu ayesifunge kuAbrahama," 
Acts7:18 kwaze kwavela enye inkosi, eyayingamazi uJosefa." 
Acts7:19 Yona yasiphatha ngobuqili isizukulu sakithi, yabahlupha obaba bethu." 
Acts7:20 Ngalesosikhathi kwazalwa uMozisi. 
Acts7:21 Eselahliwe, indodakazi kaFaro yamdobha, yazondlela yena ukuthi abe yindodana." 
Acts7:22 Njalo uMozisi wafundiswa kuyo yonke inhlakanipho yamaGibhithe. 
Acts7:23 Kwathi eselesikhathi seminyaka engamatshumi amane agcweleyo, kwafika enhliziyweni yakhe." 
Acts7:24 Kwathi ebona omunye ephathwa kubi, wa m vikela wamlamulela ohlutshwayo, watshaya umGibhithe;" 
Acts7:25 njalo wayethemba ukuthi abafowabo bazaqedisisa ukuthi uNkulunkulu ubanika inkululeko ngesandla sakhe; kodwa kabaqedisisanga. 
Acts7:26 Njalo ngosuku olulandelayo wazibonakalisa kibo ababesilwa, wabalamula ngamandla, esithi: Madoda, lingabazalwane; liphathanelani kubi?" 
Acts7:27 Kodwa lowo owayemona umakhelwane wamsunduza, esithi: Ubekwe ngubani ukuba ngumbusi lomahluleli phezu kwethu?" 
Acts7:28 Usufuna ukungibulala yini, njengoba ubulele umGibhithe izolo?" 
Acts7:29 Ngalelilizwi uMozisi wasebaleka, waba ngowemzini elizweni leMadiyani." 
Acts7:30 Kwathi sekugcwaliseke iminyaka engamatshumi amane, kwabonakala kuye enkangala." 
Acts7:31 Kwathi uMozisi esebonile wamangala ngalowombono; esasondela ukuthi akhangelisise, ilizwi leNkosi lafika kuye lisithi:" 
Acts7:32 Mina nginguNkulunkulu waboyihlo, uNkulunkulu kaAbrahama loNkulunkulu kaIsaka loNkulunkulu kaJakobe." 
Acts7:33 INkosi yasisithi kuye: Khulula amanyathela enyaweni zakho; ngoba indawo omi kiyo ingumhlabathi ongcwele. 
Acts7:34 Ngikubonile lokukubona ukuhlutshwa kwabantu bami abaseGibhithe, njalo ngizwile ukububula kwabo; sengehlile ukuthi ngibakhulule; khathesi-ke woza, ngizakuthuma eGibhithe." 
Acts7:35 UMozisi lo abamalayo besithi: Ubekwe ngubani ukuba ngumbusi lomahluleli? nguye uNkulunkulu amthumayo ukuba ngumbusi lomkhululi ngesandla sengilosi eyabonakala kuye esihlahleni. 
Acts7:36 Yena wabakhupha. 
Acts7:37 Nguye lowo uMozisi owathi kubantwana bakoIsrayeli: INkosi uNkulunkulu wenu uzalivusela umprofethi kubazalwane benu onjengami; lizamuzwa yena. 
Acts7:38 Nguye lowo, ukuze asinike;" 
Acts7:39 yena obaba bethu abangavumanga ukumlalela, kodwa ba m sunduzela eceleni, basebebuyela eGibhithe ngenhliziyo zabo," 
Acts7:40 besithi kuAroni: Senzele onkulunkulu abazahamba phambi kwethu; ngoba uMozisi lo, owasikhupha elizweni iGibhithe, kasazi ukuthi wehlelwe yini." 
Acts7:41 Basebesenza ithole ngalezonsuku. 
Acts7:42 Kodwa uNkulunkulu wafulathela? 
Acts7:43 Njalo lathatha ithabhanekele likaMoloki lenkanyezi kankulunkulu wenu uRefani, imifanekiso elayenza ukuthi liyikhonze." 
Acts7:44 Obaba bethu babelalo ithabhanekele lobufakazi enkangala; 
Acts7:45 okwathi futhi obaba bethu sebelemukele balingenisa kanye; 
Acts7:46 owathola umusa phambi kukaNkulunkulu. 
Acts7:47 Kodwa uSolomoni wamakhela indlu. 
Acts7:48 Kodwa, njengokutsho komprofethi ukuthi:" 
Acts7:49 Izulu kimi liyisihlalo sobukhosi, lomhlaba uyisenabelo senyawo zami; lizangakhela indlu enjani, kutsho iNkosi; kumbe yiyiphi indawo yami yokuphumula?" 
Acts7:50 Isandla sami kasizenzanga yini zonke lezizinto? 
Acts7:51 Lina ntamo zilukhuni. 
Acts7:52 Nguwuphi owabaprofethi oyihlo abangamzingelanga; 
Acts7:53 elemukela umlayo ngokuqoqa kwezingilosi. 
Acts7:54 Bathi sebezwile lezizinto, bahlabeka enhliziyweni zabo." 
Acts7:55 Kodwa yena egcwele uMoya oNgcwele," 
Acts7:56 wasesithi: Khangelani, ngibona amazulu evulekile." 
Acts7:57 Kodwa bamemeza ngelizwi elikhulu, bavala indlebe zabo, batheleka phezu kwakhe bengqondonye;" 
Acts7:58 basebemkhuphela ngaphandle komuzi. 
Acts7:59 Bamkhanda ngamatshe uStefane. 
Acts7:60 Waseguqa ngamadolo, wamemeza ngelizwi elikhulu." 
Acts8:1 Njalo uSawuli, ngaphandle kwabaphostoli." 
Acts8:2 Amadoda akholwayo. 
Acts8:3 Kodwa uSawuli walichitha ibandla, engena izindlu ngezindlu." 
Acts8:4 Ngakho abahlakazekileyo badabula ilizwe, betshumayela ilizwi." 
Acts8:5 UFiliphu wasesehlela emzini weSamariya, watshumayela kubo uKristu." 
Acts8:6 Amaxuku aselalela nganhliziyonye okwakhulunywa nguFiliphu, esizwa njalo ebona izibonakaliso azenzayo." 
Acts8:7 Ngoba kwabanengi ababelabomoya abangcolileyo. 
Acts8:8 Kwaba khona intokozo enkulu kulowomuzi. 
Acts8:9 Njalo indoda ethile, uSimoni ngebizo, e yayikade isenza imilingo;" 
Acts8:10 abayilalelayo bonke kusukela kwabancinyane kuze kube kwabakhulu. 
Acts8:11 Basebemlalela. 
Acts8:12 Kodwa kwathi sebekholwe uFiliphu etshumayela indaba ezinhle zezinto ngombuso kaNkulunkulu langebizo likaJesu Kristu, babhabhathizwa bonke amadoda labafazi." 
Acts8:13 LoSimoni laye wakholwa, njalo esebhabhathiziwe wanamathela kuFiliphu." 
Acts8:14 Kwathi abaphostoli abaseJerusalema bezwe ukuthi iSamariya ilemukele ilizwi likaNkulunkulu; 
Acts8:15 abathi sebehlile babakhulekela, ukuze bamemukele uMoya oNgcwele;" 
Acts8:16 ngoba wayengakehleli lakoyedwa wabo. 
Acts8:17 Basebebeka izandla phezu kwabo 
Acts8:18 Njalo uSimoni esebonile ukuthi ngokubekwa kwezandla zabaphostoli uyaphiwa uMoya oyiNgcwele, waletha imali kubo," 
Acts8:19 esithi: Ngiphani lami lawomandla, ukuze kuthi loba ngubani engibeka izandla zami phezu kwakhe, emukele uMoya oNgcwele." 
Acts8:20 Kodwa uPetro wathi kuye: Isiliva sakho kanye lawe kakube sekubhubheni. 
Acts8:21 Ngoba kawulasabelo lelifa. 
Acts8:22 Ngakho phenduka kulobububi bakho, njalo ucele iNkosi, ukuthi uba kungenzeka uthethelelwe umnakano wenhliziyo yakho." 
Acts8:23 Ngoba ngibona ukuthi usenyongweni ebabayo. 
Acts8:24 USimoni wasephendula esithi: Ngikhulekelani lina eNkosini, ukuze ngingehlelwa ngolunye lwalezizinto elizikhulumileyo." 
Acts8:25 Ngakho kuthe sebefakazile bekhulumile ilizwi leNkosi, babuyela eJerusalema." 
Acts8:26 Ingilosi yeNkosi yasikhuluma; yona iyinkangala. 
Acts8:27 Wasesukuma ehamba; njalo khangela umuntu weEthiyophiya, eyayifikile eJerusalema ukukhonza," 
Acts8:28 yayisibuyela ihlezi enqoleni yayo, ibala kumprofethi uIsaya." 
Acts8:29 UMoya wasesithi kuFiliphu: Sondela uhambe lalinqola. 
Acts8:30 UFiliphu wasegijimela ku yowayizwa ibala umprofethi uIsaya, wathi: Kambe uyaqedisisa yini lezizinto ozifundayo?" 
Acts8:31 Yasisithi: Kambe ngingakwenelisa njani, ngaphandle kokuthiomunye angiqondise." 
Acts8:32 Lesehlukwana sombhalo eyayisifunda yilesi: Walethwa ekuhlatshweni njengemvu; lanjengewundlu lithule phambi komgundi walo, ngokunjalo kawuvuli umlomo wakhe." 
Acts8:33 Ekuthotshisweni kwakhe ukwahlulelwa kwakhe kwasuswa, njalo ngubani ongalandisa nge sizukulwana sakhe? Ngoba impilo yakhe iyasuswa emhlabeni." 
Acts8:34 Umthenwa wasephendula uFiliphu wathi: Ngiyakubuza, umprofethi ukhuluma lokhu ngobani? Ngaye ngokwakhe, kumbe ngomunye yini?" 
Acts8:35 UFiliphu wasevula umlomo wakhe. 
Acts8:36 Kwathi besahamba endleleni, bafika emanzini athile; lomthenwa wathi: Khangela, nankaamanzi; kuyini okungivimbela ukuthi ngibhabhathizwe?" 
Acts8:37 UFiliphu wasesithi: Uba ukholwa ngenhliziyo yonke. 
Acts8:38 Waselaya ukuthi inqola ime; basebesehlela emanzini bobabili, uFiliphu lomthenwa; wasembhabhathiza." 
Acts8:39 Kwathi sebekhuphukile emanzini, uMoya weNkosi wamhluthuna uFiliphu; njalo umthenwa kazabe esambona." 
Acts8:40 Kodwa uFiliphu waficwa eAzotu. 
Acts9:1 Kwathi uSawuli," 
Acts9:2 wacela kuye incwadi zokuya eDamaseko kumasinagoge, ukuze kuthi uba ethola abanye baleyondlela, amadoda kanye labafazi, a ba lethe eJerusalema bebotshiwe." 
Acts9:3 Kwathi ekuhambeni; njalo kwahle kwamphazimela inhlangothi zonke ukukhanya okuvela ezulwini; 
Acts9:4 njalo ewela emhlabathini, wezwa ilizwi lisithi kuye?" 
Acts9:5 Wasesithi: Ungubani, Nkosi? INkosi yasisithi: Mina nginguJesu omzingelayo; kulukhuni kuwe ukukhahlelana lezincijo." 
Acts9:6 Ethuthumela njalo emangala wathi: Nkosi, uthanda ukuthi ngenzeni." 
Acts9:7 Lamadoda ayehamba laye ayemi engelakukhuluma. 
Acts9:8 USawuli wasevuka emhlabathini; kwathi esevule amehlo akhe, kabonanga muntu. Basebe m bamba ngesandla, bamusa eDamaseko." 
Acts9:9 Wasesiba lensuku ezintathu engaboni, njalo engadli futhi enganathi." 
Acts9:10 Kwakukhona eDamaseko: Ananiya! Wasesithi: Khangela ngi lapha, Nkosi." 
Acts9:11 INkosi yasisi thikuye: Sukuma uye endleleni ethiwa iQondile, udinge endlini kaJudasi umuntu, uSawuli ngebizo, weTarsu; ngoba khangela uyakhuleka," 
Acts9:12 njalo ubonile ngombono umuntu, uAnaniya ngebizo, engena." 
Acts9:13 Kodwa uAnaniya waphendula wathi: Nkosi, ngizwile ngabanengi ngalindoda, kungakanani okubi akwenzileyo;" 
Acts9:14 lalapha ulamandla avela kubapristi abakhulu, okubopha bonke labo ababiza ibizo lakho." 
Acts9:15 Kodwa iNkosi yathi kuye: Hamba, ngoba lowo uyisitsha sami esikhethiweyo, labantwana bakoIsrayeli;" 
Acts9:16 ngoba mina ngizamtshengisa ukuthi umele ukuhlupheka kangakanani ngenxa yebizo lami. 
Acts9:17 UAnaniya wasesuka. 
Acts9:18 Kwahle kwawa emehlweni akhe kwangathi zinkwethu, wahle wabuye wabona, njalo esukuma wabhabhathizwa," 
Acts9:19 njalo esedlile wathola amandla. USawuli wasehlala labafundi ababeseDamaseko insuku ezithile. 
Acts9:20 Wahle-ke watshumayela uKristu emasinagogeni, ukuthi yena uyiNdodana kaNkulunkulu." 
Acts9:21 Njalo bonke abezwayo basanganiseka bathi: Lo kayisuye yini owachitha? 
Acts9:22 Kodwa uSawuli waqiniswa kakhulu, waphithizelisa amaJuda akhileyo eDamaseko, eqinisa ukuthi lo unguye uKristu." 
Acts9:23 Kwathi sezigcwalisiwe insuku ezinengi, amaJuda enza icebo ndawonye ukuthi ambulale;" 
Acts9:24 kodwa iqhinga lawo laziwa nguSawuli; 
Acts9:25 kodwa abafundi bamthatha ebusuku, ba m ehlisela emthangaleni." 
Acts9:26 Kwathi uSawuli esefikile eJerusalema, wazama ukuzihlanganisa labafundi; kodwa bonke bamesaba, bengakholwa ukuthi ungumfundi." 
Acts9:27 Kodwa uBarnabasi wamthatha 
Acts9:28 Wasehlala labo," 
Acts9:29 wasekhuluma ngesibindi ngebizo leNkosi uJesu. 
Acts9:30 Kodwa abazalwane sebekwazi. 
Acts9:31 Ngakho amabandla kuyo yonke iJudiya leGalili. 
Acts9:32 Kwasekusithi uPetro edabula indawo zonke. 
Acts9:33 Wasefica khona umuntu othile uEneya ngebizo, owayeselele ecansini iminyaka eyisificaminwembili, eyisigoga." 
Acts9:34 UPetro wasesithi kuye: Eneya, uJesu Kristu uyakusilisa; sukuma uzendlalele icansi. Njalo wahle wasukuma." 
Acts9:35 Basebembona bonke abakhileyo eLida. 
Acts9:36 Kwakukhona eJopha umfundikazi othile, uTabitha ngebizo." 
Acts9:37 Kwasekusithi kulezonsuku wagula wafa; sebemgezisile ba m lalisa endlini ephezulu. 
Acts9:38 Njalo njengoba iLida yayiseduze leJopha. 
Acts9:39 UPetro wasesukuma wahamba labo; okwathi esefikile ba m thatha ba m usa endlini ephezulu, labafelokazi bonke bema laye bekhala bemtshengisa izembatho lezigqoko uDorkasi ayezenzile eselabo." 
Acts9:40 Kodwa uPetro esebakhuphele phandle bonke! Wasevula amehlo akhe; wabona uPetro, walulama." 
Acts9:41 Wamelulela isandla, wamsukumisa; esebize abangcwele labafelokazi, wa ba nika ephila." 
Acts9:42 Kwasekusaziwa kuyo yonke iJopha. 
Acts9:43 Kwenzeka ukuthi ahlale eJopha insuku ezinengi loSimoni othile umtshuki wezikhumba. 
Acts10:1 Kwakukhona eKesariya indoda ethile ngebizo nguKorneliyu," 
Acts10:2 eqotho; 
Acts10:3 yabona, yasisithi kuyo: Korneliyu!" 
Acts10:4 Waseyijolozela. 
Acts10:5 Khathesi-ke thuma amadoda eJopha, ubize uSimoni othiwa futhi nguPetro;" 
Acts10:6 yena ungenisile kuSimoni othile umtshuki wezikhumba, ondlu yakhe iselwandle." 
Acts10:7 Kwathi ingilosi ebikhuluma loKorneliyu isihambile, wabiza ababili kwabendlu yakhe," 
Acts10:8 njalo eselandisile konke kubo, wabathuma eJopha." 
Acts10:9 Njalo kusisa bona besahamba sebesondela emzini, uPetro wenyukela;" 
Acts10:10 waselamba kakhulu, wafuna ukudla; kwathi bona besamlungisela, ukuhlehliswa kwengqondo kwamehlela," 
Acts10:11 wasebona izulu livulekile, lesitsha esithile sehlela kuye, njengelembu elikhulu, libotshwe ngamasondo amane, lisehliselwa emhlabeni;" 
Acts10:12 okwakukhona kulo izidalwazonke ezilenyawo ezine zomhlaba lezeganga lezihuquzelayo lenyoni zezulu. 
Acts10:13 Kwasekufika ilizwi kuye lathi: Sukuma, Petro, hlaba udle." 
Acts10:14 Kodwa uPetro wathi: Hatshi bo, Nkosi; ngoba kangizake ngidle loba yini." 
Acts10:15 Ilizwi laphinda ngokwesibili kuye: Izinto uNkulunkulu azihlambululileyo, wena ungatsho ukuthi zingcolile." 
Acts10:16 Njalo lokhu kwenzeka kwaze kwaba kathathu; lesitsha sabuya saphakanyiselwa ezulwini. 
Acts10:17 Kwathi uPetro esadidekile ngaphakathi kwakhe," 
Acts10:18 esememezile abuza ukuthi uSimoni, othiwa futhi nguPetro, ungenisile lapha yini." 
Acts10:19 Kwathi uPetro esanakana ngombono, uMoya wathi kuye: Khangela, amadoda amathathu ayakudinga." 
Acts10:20 Ngakho sukuma wehle, uhambe lawo; ngoba yimi engiwathumileyo." 
Acts10:21 UPetro wasesehlela emadodeni avela kuKorneliyu ayethunywe kuye, wathi: Khangelani, yimi elimdingayo; yisizatho bani elize ngaso?" 
Acts10:22 Basebesithi: UKorneliyu induna yekhulu, indoda elungileyo lemesabayo uNkulunkulu." 
Acts10:23 Ngakho esebabizele phakathi wa ba ngenisa. Njalo kusisa uPetro waphuma wahamba labo, labanye." 
Acts10:24 Ngosuku olulandelayo basebengena eKesariya. LoKorneliyu wayebalindele, esebizele ndawonye izihlobo zakhe labangane abazwana laye." 
Acts10:25 Kwathi sekwenzakele ukuthi uPetro angene, uKorneliyu wamhlangabeza, ewela enyaweni zakhe." 
Acts10:26 Kodwa uPetro emphakamisa, wathi: Sukuma; lami ngokwami ngingumuntu." 
Acts10:27 Njalo esakhuluma layo wangena, wafica abanengi bebuthene," 
Acts10:28 wasesithi kubo: Lina liyazi ukuthi kakuvunyelwa emuntwini ongumJuda; 
Acts10:29 ngakho-ke ngizile ngingaphikisanga nxa ngibizwa. Ngakho ngiyabuza, ukuthi ungibizele sizatho bani?" 
Acts10:30 UKorneliyu wasesithi: Ngensuku ezine ezidlulileyo," 
Acts10:31 yasisithi: Korneliyu, umkhuleko wakho uzwakele, lemisebenzi yakho yomusa ikhunjulwe phambi kukaNkulunkulu." 
Acts10:32 Ngakho thumela eJopha, ubusubiza uSimoni othiwa futhi nguPetro; yena ungenisile endlini kaSimoni umtshuki wezikhumba ngaselwandle; ozakuthi angabuya akutshele." 
Acts10:33 Ngakho ngahle ngathumela kuwe; njalo wena wenze kuhle ukuthi ufike. Ngakho khathesi sesikhona sonke phambi kukaNkulunkulu ukuze sizwe konke okulayelwe nguNkulunkulu. 
Acts10:34 Kwathi uPetro evula umlomo, wathi;" 
Acts10:35 kodwa kuso sonke isizwe. 
Acts10:36 Ilizwi alithumela kubantwana bakoIsrayeli, ngevangeli etshumayela ukuthula ngoJesu Kristu)." 
Acts10:37 Lina liyalazi ilizwi elamenyezelwa eJudiya yonke, kusukela eGalili, emva kobhabhathizo uJohane alutshumayelayo;" 
Acts10:38 uJesu weNazaretha, ukuthi uNkulunkulu wamgcoba njani ngoMoya oNgcwele langamandla." 
Acts10:39 Lathi singabafakazi bezinto zonke azenzayo elizweni lamaJuda leJerusalema. 
Acts10:40 Yena uNkulunkulu wamvusa ngosuku lwesithathu, wasemnika ukuze abonakale," 
Acts10:41 kungeyisikho kubo bonke abantu. 
Acts10:42 Wasesilaya ukuthi sitshumayele ebantwini. 
Acts10:43 Ngaye bonke abaprofethi bafakaza. 
Acts10:44 Kwathi uPetro esakhuluma lawomazwi, uMoya oyiNgcwele wehlela phezu kwabo bonke abalizwayo ilizwi." 
Acts10:45 Labokusoka abakholwayo basanganiseka; 
Acts10:46 ngoba babezwa bekhuluma ngendimi, bekhulisa uNkulunkulu:" 
Acts10:47 Ukhona yini ongala lamanzi, ukuthi laba bangabhabhathizwa?" 
Acts10:48 Waselaya ukuthi babhabhathizwe. Basebemcela ukuthi ahlale insuku ezithile. 
Acts11:1 Abaphostoli labazalwane ababeseJudiya basebesizwa ukuthi abezizwe labo balemukele ilizwi likaNkulunkulu. 
Acts11:2 Kwathi uPetro esenyukele eJerusalema," 
Acts11:3 besithi: Ungene emadodeni angasokanga, wadla lawo." 
Acts11:4 Kodwa uPetro eqala wabalandisela: 
Acts11:5 Mina ngangisemzini weJopha ngikhuleka, kwehla isitsha esithile, sinjengelembu elikhulu sisehliswa ngamasondo amane sivela ezulwini, sasesifika kimi;" 
Acts11:6 okwathi sengilikhangelisisile ngaqaphelisa, ngasengibona inyamazana ezilenyawo ezine zomhlaba lezeganga lezihuquzelayo lenyoni zezulu." 
Acts11:7 Ngasengisizwa ilizwi lisithi kimi: Sukuma, Petro, hlaba udle." 
Acts11:8 Kodwa ngathi: Hatshi bo Nkosi; ngoba loba yini engahlambulukanga kumbe engcolileyo kayizake ingene emlonyeni wami. 
Acts11:9 Kodwa ilizwi langiphendula ngokwesibili livela ezulwini lathi: Izinto uNkulunkulu azihlambululileyo, wena ungatsho ukuthi zingcolile." 
Acts11:10 Lokhu-ke kwenzeka kathathu, njalo konke kwabuye kwadonselwa phezulu ezulwini." 
Acts11:11 Njalo khangela, ngasona lesosikhathi amadoda amathathu ema phambi kwendlu engangikuyo, ethunyiwe kimi evela eKesariya." 
Acts11:12 UMoya wasesithi kimi ngihambe lawo, ngingathandabuzi; lalababazalwane abayisithupha labo bahamba lami, sasesingena endlini yendoda;" 
Acts11:13 yasisibikela ukuthi yayibone njani ingilosi imi endlini yayo, isithi kuyo: Thumela amadoda eJopha, ubize uSimoni, othiwa nguPetro," 
Acts11:14 ozakutshela amazwi. 
Acts11:15 Kwathi ngisaqala ukukhuluma, uMoya oyiNgcwele wehlela phezu kwabo." 
Acts11:16 Ngakhumbula ilizwi leNkosi. 
Acts11:17 Ngakho nxa uNkulunkulu? 
Acts11:18 Njalo bathi sebezizwile lezizinto bathula, bamdumisa uNkulunkulu." 
Acts11:19 Labo-ke abahlakazeka ngokuhlupheka, bengalikhulumi ilizwi lakoyedwa ngaphandle kumaJuda kuphela." 
Acts11:20 Kodwa kwakukhona abanye kubo, amadoda amaKuprosi." 
Acts11:21 Lesandla seNkosi sasilabo. 
Acts11:22 Zasezizwakala indaba ngabo endlebeni zebandla elaliseJerusalema; 
Acts11:23 kwathi esefikile esebona umusa kaNkulunkulu wathokoza; 
Acts11:24 ngoba wayeyindoda elungileyo. 
Acts11:25 UBarnabasi wasesiya eTarsu ukuze adinge uSawuli," 
Acts11:26 kwathi esemtholile wamletha eAntiyoki. 
Acts11:27 Kwathi ngalezonsuku kwafika eAntiyoki bevela eJerusalema. 
Acts11:28 Kwasekusukuma omunye wabo othiwa nguAgabusi. 
Acts11:29 Labafundi bazimisela ukuthi ngulowo lalowo wabo athumele njengamandla alowo lalowo; 
Acts11:30 abakwenzayo-ke. 
Acts12:1 Ngalesosikhathi uHerodi inkosi. 
Acts12:2 Wasebulala uJakobe. 
Acts12:3 Esebonile ukuthi lokhu kuyawathokozisa amaJuda; 
Acts12:4 esembambile laye wa m faka entolongweni. 
Acts12:5 Ngakho uPetro wagcinwa entolongweni; kodwa umkhuleko oqhubekayo wenziwa libandla ngaye kuNkulunkulu. 
Acts12:6 Kwathi uHerodi esezamkhupha, ngalobobusuku uPetro wayelele phakathi kwabebutho ababili; labalindi phambi komnyango babegcine intolongo." 
Acts12:7 Njalo khangela, ingilosi yeNkosi yema. Asesiwa amaketane akhe ezandleni zakhe." 
Acts12:8 Ingilosi yasisithi kuye: Bhinca, ubophe amanyathela akho. Wasesenza njalo. Yasisithi kuye: Yembatha isembatho sakho, ungilandele." 
Acts12:9 Wasephuma wayilandela; njalo wayengazi ukuthi kuliqiniso okwenziwa yingilosi, kodwa wayecabanga ukuthi." 
Acts12:10 Njalo sebedlulile abalindi bokuqala labesibili, bafika esangweni lensimbi, elokuya emzini, elabavulekela ngokwalo; basebephuma bahamba umgwaqo waba munye; njalo ingilosi yahle yamtshiya." 
Acts12:11 Kwathi uPetro, eseqaqabukile." 
Acts12:12 Kwathi esenanzelele. 
Acts12:13 Kwathi uPetro eseqoqodile esivalweni sesango, uRoda ngebizo," 
Acts12:14 kwathi isilazi ilizwi likaPetro, kayivulanga isango." 
Acts12:15 Kodwa bathi kuyo: Uyahlanya. Kodwa yaqinisisa ukuthi kunjalo. 
Acts12:16 Kodwa uPetro waqhubeka eqoqoda; sebevulile bambona, basanganiseka." 
Acts12:17 Wasebaqhweba ngesandla ukuze bathule, wabalandisela ukuthi iNkosi imkhuphe njani entolongweni. Wasephuma waya kwenye indawo." 
Acts12:18 Sekusile, kwaba khona isiphithiphithi esingesincinyane phakathi kwebutho, ukuthi wayesehlelwe yini uPetro." 
Acts12:19 Kwathi uHerodi esemdingile enga m tholi. 
Acts12:20 Njalo uHerodi. 
Acts12:21 Njalo ngosuku olumisiweyo uHerodi wembatha isembatho sobukhosi, wenza inkulumo kubo." 
Acts12:22 Abantu basebememeza besithi: Y ilizwi likaNkulunkulu njalo kayisilo elomuntu. 
Acts12:23 Njalo yahle yamtshaya ingilosi yeNkosi; wasedliwa zimpethu, waphela." 
Acts12:24 Kodwa ilizwi likaNkulunkulu lakhula landa. 
Acts12:25 UBarnabasi. 
Acts13:1 Kwakukhona eAntiyoki. 
Acts13:2 Kwathi bekhonza iNkosi. 
Acts13:3 Sebezile ukudla. 
Acts13:4 Bona-ke sebethunyiwe nguMoya oyiNgcwele. 
Acts13:5 Kwathi sebefikile eSalamisi, batshumayela ilizwi likaNkulunkulu emasinagogeni amaJuda." 
Acts13:6 Kwathi sebedabule isihlenge bafika ePhafosi," 
Acts13:7 owayelombusi uSergiyu Pawuli, indoda ehlakaniphileyo. Lo wabizela kuye uBarnabasi loSawuli edinga ukuzwa ilizwi likaNkulunkulu." 
Acts13:8 Kodwa isanuse, uElimasi, ngoba liphendulelwa njalo ibizo lakhe, waphikisana labo." 
Acts13:9 Kodwa uSawuli, onguPawuli futhi, egcwele uMoya oNgcwele" 
Acts13:10 wathi: O wena ogcwele inkohliso yonke lobuqili bonke? 
Acts13:11 Njalo khathesi khangela, isandla seNkosi si phezu kwakho, njalo uzakuba yisiphofu." 
Acts13:12 Ngalesosikhathi umbusi wabona okwenziweyo wakholwa, edidwa yimfundiso yeNkosi." 
Acts13:13 UPawuli lababelaye. 
Acts13:14 Kodwa bona bedabula besuka ePerga, bahlala phansi." 
Acts13:15 Kwathi sekufundwe umlayo, khulumani." 
Acts13:16 Kwathi uPawuli esukuma, njalo eqhweba ngesandla." 
Acts13:17 UNkulunkulu walesisizwe sakoIsrayeli. 
Acts13:18 Wasebekezelela isimilo sabo okungaba yisikhathi seminyaka engamatshumi amane enkangala. 
Acts13:19 Njalo esechithile izizwe eziyisikhombisa elizweni leKhanani. 
Acts13:20 Lemva kwalezizinto, okungaba ngokweminyaka engamakhulu amane lamatshumi amahlanu." 
Acts13:21 Njalo kusukela lapho bacela inkosi, okweminyaka engamatshumi amane." 
Acts13:22 Njalo esemkhuphile. 
Acts13:23 Enzalweni yalu muntu; 
Acts13:24 engakafiki yena uJohane wayesetshumayele kuqala. 
Acts13:25 UJohane esegcwalise uhambo lwakhe. 
Acts13:26 Madoda bazalwane, bantwana bohlanga lukaAbrahama, lalabo phakathi kwenu abesaba uNkulunkulu." 
Acts13:27 Ngoba labo abahlala eJerusalema lababusi babo; 
Acts13:28 njalo bengatholi lacala lokufa, bacela kuPilatu ukuthi abulawe." 
Acts13:29 Kwathi sebeqedile konke okulotshiweyo ngaye, ba m lalisa engcwabeni." 
Acts13:30 Kodwa uNkulunkulu wamvusa kwabafileyo; 
Acts13:31 owabonwa insuku ezinengi yilabo. 
Acts13:32 Lathi sitshumayela indaba ezinhle kini zesithembiso esenziwa kubobaba," 
Acts13:33 ukuthi uNkulunkulu usigcwalisile sona kithi, abantwana babo, emvusile uJesu." 
Acts13:34 Njalo ngokuthi wamvusa kwabafileyo. 
Acts13:35 Ngakho njalo kwenye indawouthi: Kawuyikunikela ongcwele wakho abone ukubola; 
Acts13:36 ngoba uDavida, esekhonze esakhe isizukulwana ngecebo likaNkulunkulu walala;" 
Acts13:37 kodwa lowo uNkulunkulu amvusayo, kakubonanga ukubola." 
Acts13:38 Ngakho kakwaziwe yini, madoda bazalwane, ukuthi ngalowo kutshunyayelwa kini;" 
Acts13:39 njalo kulo wonke okholwayo. 
Acts13:40 Ngakho bonani ukuthi kalehlelwa yilokhu okwakhulunywa kubaprofethi, okokuthi:" 
Acts13:41 Khangelani, zideleli, njalo limangale, litshabalale; ngoba mina ngenza umsebenzi ensukwini zenu, umsebenzi elingayikuwukholwa, nxa umuntu elilandisela." 
Acts13:42 Kwathi ekuphumeni kwamaJuda esinagogeni. 
Acts13:43 Kwathi abe sinagoge sebephumile, abanengi kumaJuda labakhonzayo." 
Acts13:44 Kwathi ngesabatha elilandelayo babuthana kwaphose kwaba ngumuzi wonke ukuzwa ilizwi likaNkulunkulu. 
Acts13:45 Kodwa amaJuda ebona amaxuku agcwaliswa ngomona, aphikisa izinto ezakhulunywa nguPawuli." 
Acts13:46 Kodwa uPawuli loBarnabasi bekhuluma ngesibindi. 
Acts13:47 Ngoba iNkosi isilayile ngokunjalo yathi: Ngikumisile ube yikukhanya kwabezizwe, ube ngowosindiso kuze kube semkhawulweni womhlaba." 
Acts13:48 Kwathi abezizwe be ku zwa bathokoza, basebelidumisa ilizwi leNkosi, basebekholwa ngobunengi obungangobalabo ababemiselwe impilo elaphakade;" 
Acts13:49 lelizwi leNkosi lasatshalaliswa elizweni lonke. 
Acts13:50 Kodwa amaJuda avusa. 
Acts13:51 Kodwa babathintithela uthuli lwenyawo zabo. 
Acts13:52 Njalo abafundi bagcwaliswa ngentokozo. 
Acts14:1 Kwasekusithi eIkoniyuma, basebekhuluma njalo kwaze kwakholwa ixuku elikhulu lamaJuda kanye lamaGriki." 
Acts14:2 Kodwa amaJuda angakholwayo. 
Acts14:3 Ngakho bahlala isikhathi eside bekhuluma ngesibindi beseNkosini. 
Acts14:4 Kodwa ixuku lomuzi lehlukaniswa phakathi; abanye basebesiba lamaJuda. 
Acts14:5 Kwathi sekulokuhlasela kwabezizwe lamaJuda kanye lababusi babo, okoku ba phatha kubi lokubakhanda ngamatshe," 
Acts14:6 sebe kw azi, lelizweni elizingelezeleyo;" 
Acts14:7 lakhona batshumayela ivangeli. 
Acts14:8 Njalo eListra. 
Acts14:9 Yona yamuzwa uPawuli ekhuluma; yena eyijolozela," 
Acts14:10 wathi ngelizwi elikhulu: Sukuma, ume ngenyawo zakho uqonde. Yasisukuma yathi lothu yahamba." 
Acts14:11 Kwathi amaxuku, ebona uPawuli akwenzileyo, aphakamisa amazwi awo." 
Acts14:12 UBarnabasi basebembiza ngokuthinguZewusi, loPawuli ngokuthinguHermesi, ngoba yena wayengumkhokheli wokukhuluma." 
Acts14:13 Njalo umpristi kaZewusi owayephambi komuzi wabo, waletha izinkabi lemigaxo emasangweni." 
Acts14:14 Kodwa abaphostoli 
Acts14:15 besithi: Madoda, lizenzelani lezizinto;" 
Acts14:16 owathi ezizukulwaneni ezidlulileyo wayekela. 
Acts14:17 Loba kunjalo kayekelanga yena ukuthi angabi lobufakazi. 
Acts14:18 Njalo bekhuluma lezizinto, bawayekelisa kalukhuni amaxuku ukuthi angabahlabeli." 
Acts14:19 Kodwa kwafika amaJuda, a m hudulela ngaphandle komuzi, ecabanga ukuthi ufile." 
Acts14:20 Kodwa kwathi abafundi bembuthanela, wasukuma wangena emzini; kusisa wasuka loBarnabasi baya eDerbe." 
Acts14:21 Njalo sebetshumayele ivangeli kulowomuzi, sebezuzile abafundi abanengi, babuyela eListra," 
Acts14:22 beqinisa imiphefumulo yabafundi. 
Acts14:23 Kwathi sebebabekele. 
Acts14:24 Basebedabula iPisidiya baya ePamfiliya. 
Acts14:25 Sebekhulumile ilizwi ePerga, behlela eAtaliya;" 
Acts14:26 basuka lapho ngomkhumbi baya eAntiyoki. 
Acts14:27 Kwathi sebefikile bahlanganisa ibandla, balandisa konke uNkulunkulu ayekwenzile labo." 
Acts14:28 Basebehlala lapho okwesikhathi esingesifitshane labafundi. 
Acts15:1 Kwasekusehla abathile bevela eJudiya. 
Acts15:2 Ngakho kwathi sekulokuphambana lokuphikisana okungekuncinyane ngoPawuli loBarnabasi bemelane labo, ngaloludaba lwempikisano." 
Acts15:3 Ngakho, kwathi sebephelekezelwe libandla." 
Acts15:4 Kwathi sebefikile eJerusalema, bemukelwa libandla labaphostoli." 
Acts15:5 Kodwa kwasukuma abanye abakholwayo abangabehlelo labaFarisi, besithi: Kufanele uku ba soka, lokubalaya bagcine umlayo kaMozisi." 
Acts15:6 Kwasekubuthana abaphostoli labadala ndawonye ukuze baluhlole loludaba. 
Acts15:7 Kwathi sebephikisene kakhulu. 
Acts15:8 Njalo uNkulunkulu umazi wenhliziyo; 
Acts15:9 futhi kehlukanisanga phakathi kwethu labo. 
Acts15:10 Pho-ke limlingelani uNkulunkulu? 
Acts15:11 Kodwa sikholwa ukuthi sisindiswa ngomusa weNkosi uJesu Kristu, ngandlelanye labo." 
Acts15:12 Ixuku lonke laselithula; laselisizwa uBarnabasi loPawuli belandisa ukuthi. 
Acts15:13 Kwathi bona sebeqedile ukukhuluma, uJakobe waphendula wathi: Madoda bazalwane, ngilalelani:" 
Acts15:14 USimeyoni. 
Acts15:15 Njalo amazwi abaprofethi ayavumelana lalokhu, njengoba kulotshiwe ukuthi:" 
Acts15:16 Emva kwalezizinto ngizabuya, ngilakhe futhi ithabhanekele likaDavida eliwileyo; njalo ngizakwakha okudilikileyo kwalo, njalo ngilimise;" 
Acts15:17 ukuze abaseleyo babantu bayidinge iNkosi, labezizwe bonke ibizo lami elibizwa phezu kwabo, itsho iNkosi eyenza lezizinto zonke." 
Acts15:18 Kwaziwa kuNkulunkulu imisebenzi yonke yakhe kusukela ephakadeni. 
Acts15:19 Ngakho mina ngiquma ukuthi; 
Acts15:20 kodwa sibabhalele ukuthi bazile amanyala ezithombe. 
Acts15:21 Ngoba uMozisi ulabo kusukela ezizukulwaneni zendulo abamtshumayelayo umuzi ngomuzi, efundwa emasinagogeni isabatha ngesabatha." 
Acts15:22 Kwasekubonakala kukuhle kubaphostoli lakubadala," 
Acts15:23 basebebhala lokhu ngesandla sabo ukuthi: Abaphostoli labadala; 
Acts15:24 njengoba sizwile ukuthi abathile abaphume kithi balikhathazile ngamazwi, bedunga imiphefumulo yenu, besithi lisokwe lilonde umthetho, bona singabalayanga;" 
Acts15:25 kwabonakala kukuhle kithi singqondonye, ukuthi siwakhethe amadoda si wa thume kini, kanye labathandekayo bethu uBarnabasi loPawuli," 
Acts15:26 abantu abanikele impilo yabo ngenxa yebizo leNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu. 
Acts15:27 Ngakho sithumile uJudasi loSilasi, abazakuthi langomlomo balandise ngokufananayo." 
Acts15:28 Ngoba kwabonakala kukuhle kuMoya oNgcwele, lakithi, ukuthi singalethesi umthwalo omkhulu, ngaphandle kwalezizinto ezifunekayo:" 
Acts15:29 Ukuthi lizile okuhlatshelwe izithombe. 
Acts15:30 Ngakho sebebakhululile beza eAntiyoki; futhi sebelihlanganisile ixuku, ba li nika incwadi." 
Acts15:31 Kwathi sebefundile, bathokoza ngenduduzo." 
Acts15:32 UJudasi kanye loSilasi. 
Acts15:33 Sebehlale isikhathi, bayekelwa bahamba ngokuthula ngabazalwane baya kubaphostoli," 
Acts15:34 kodwa kwabonakala kukuhle kuSilasi ukuthi asale khona. 
Acts15:35 UPawuli loBarnabasi. 
Acts15:36 Emva kwensuku ezithile uPawuli wasesithi kuBarnabasi: Ake sibuye sihambele abazalwane bethu emizini yonke, lapho esatshumayela khona ilizwi leNkosi, ukuthi bahlezi njani." 
Acts15:37 UBarnabasi wasehlosa ukuthatha uJohane, othiwa nguMarko, ahambe labo." 
Acts15:37 UBarnabasi wasehlosa ukuthatha uJohane, othiwa nguMarko, ahambe labo." 
Acts15:38 Kodwa uPawuli wacabanga ukuthi kufanele ukuthi bangamthathi ahambe labo lowo owabatshiya ePamfiliya, kaze aya labo emsebenzini." 
Acts15:39 Kwasekuvela ukuphikisana okukhulu, baze behlukana phakathi; uBarnabasi." 
Acts15:40 Kodwa uPawuli wakhetha uSilasi. 
Acts15:41 Wasedabula iSiriya leKilikhiya. 
Acts16:1 Wasefika eDerbe; 
Acts16:2 owayenconywa ngabazalwane. 
Acts16:3 Lo uPawuli wathanda ukuthi aphume laye, wasemthatha wa m soka." 
Acts16:4 Njalo bedabula imizi, babanika izimiso ukuzilondoloza." 
Acts16:5 Ngakho amabandla aqiniswa ekholweni, njalo anda ngenani insuku ngensuku." 
Acts16:6 Sebedabule eFrigiya," 
Acts16:7 sebefikile maqondana leMisiya bazama ukuya eBithiniya; kodwa uMoya kabavumelanga; 
Acts16:8 basebeyiceza iMisiya behlela eTrowasi. 
Acts16:9 Kwasekubonakala umbono kuPawuli ebusuku, imncenga isithi: Chaphela eMakedoniya, usisize." 
Acts16:10 Kwathi esewubonile umbono. 
Acts16:11 Ngakho sasuka eTrowasi," 
Acts16:12 sasuka lapho saya eFiliphi. 
Acts16:13 Njalo ngosuku lwesabatha saphumela ngaphandle komuzi eceleni komfula, lapho okwakufanele kwenzelwe umkhuleko khona; sasesihlala phansi sakhuluma labesifazana ababebuthene ndawonye." 
Acts16:14 Lowesifazana othile uLidiya ngebizo, ongumthengisikazi wamalembu ayibubende owemzini weTiyathira." 
Acts16:15 Kuthe esebhabhathiziwe, lendlu yakhe." 
Acts16:16 Kwasekusithi sisiya emkhulekweni. 
Acts16:17 Lo walandela uPawuli lathi, ememeza esithi: Lababantu bazinceku." 
Acts16:18 Lalokhu yakwenza insuku ezinengi. Kwathi uPawuli. 
Acts16:19 Amakhosi akhe esebonile," 
Acts16:20 esebalethile ezinduneni athi, bengamaJuda," 
Acts16:21 batshumayela imikhuba esingavunyelwa ukuyemukela siyenze. 
Acts16:22 Lexuku labelekelela, lenduna zabadabulela izembatho zabo." 
Acts16:23 Sebebatshayile imivimvinya eminengi ba ba phosela entolongweni; 
Acts16:24 yena, emukele umlayo onjalo, wabaphosela entolongweni ephakathi." 
Acts16:25 Kwathi sekungaba phakathi kobusuku behlabela amahubo endumiso kuNkulunkulu, lezibotshwa zazibezwa;" 
Acts16:26 njalo kwahle kwaba khona ukuzamazama komhlaba okukhulu, kwaze kwanyikinyeka izisekelo zentolongo." 
Acts16:27 Kwathi umlindintolongo ephaphama, esebona iminyango yentolongo ivulekile, wakhokha inkemba, ezimisele ukuzibulala, ecabanga ukuthi izibotshwa zibalekile." 
Acts16:28 Kodwa uPawuli wamemeza ngelizwi elikhulu esithi: Ungazilimazi; ngoba silapha sonke. 
Acts16:29 Wasecela isibane waphoseka phakathi, njalo wasethuthumela," 
Acts16:30 njalo esebakhuphela phandle wathi: Makhosi, kumele ngenzeni ukuze ngisindiswe?" 
Acts16:31 Basebesithi: Kholwa eNkosini uJesu Kristu, njalo uzasindiswa wena." 
Acts16:32 Basebekhuluma kuye ilizwi leNkosi, lakulabo bonke ababesendlini yakhe." 
Acts16:33 Wasebathatha ngalelohola lobusuku wa ba gezisa amanxeba. 
Acts16:34 Wasebasa endlini yakhe wabeka itafula lokudlaphambi kwabo, wasethokoza lendlu yakhe yonke bekholwa kuNkulunkulu." 
Acts16:35 Kwathi sekusile, induna zathuma amapholisa zisithi: Khulula labobantu." 
Acts16:36 Umlindintolongo wasebikela uPawuli lamazwi. 
Acts16:37 Kodwa uPawuli wathi kuwo: Basitshayile obala singalahlwanga licala, basebe si phosela entolongweni, njalo khathesi ngensitha sebesiphosela phandle yini? Hatshi bo! Kodwa kumele beze bona basikhuphe." 
Acts16:38 Amapholisa azibikela izinduna lamazwi zisizwa ukuthi bangamaRoma," 
Acts16:39 njalo zeza zabancenga, njalo za ba khupha." 
Acts16:40 Basebephuma entolongweni bangena koLidiya. 
Acts17:1 Kwathi sebedabule iAmfipholi leApoloniya, bafika eThesalonika, lapho okwakukhona isinagoge lamaJuda;" 
Acts17:2 njalo njengomkhuba kaPawuli wangena kuwo okwamasabatha amathathu," 
Acts17:3 evula etshengisa, mina engimtshumayela kini, unguKristu." 
Acts17:4 Labanye babo bakholwa, bazihlanganisa loPawuli." 
Acts17:5 Kodwa amaJuda angakholwayo, edinga ukubakhuphela ebantwini;" 
Acts17:6 kwathi engabatholi, adonsela uJasoni labazalwane abathile kubaphathi bomuzi," 
Acts17:7 uJasoni abemukeleyo. 
Acts17:8 Asedunga ixuku labaphathi bomuzi besizwa lezizinto. 
Acts17:9 Kwathi sebethethe isibambiso kuJasoni lakwabanye, abakhulula." 
Acts17:10 Njalo abazalwane. 
Acts17:11 Lawo ayekhaliphile kulalawo aweThesalonika. 
Acts17:12 Ngakho amanengi kuwo akholwa, lakwabesifazana abahloniphekayo abangamaGriki lakwabesilisa abangabalutshwana." 
Acts17:13 Kodwa kwathi amaJuda eThesalonika esekwazi ukuthi ilizwi likaNkulunkulu liyatshunyayelwa nguPawuli leBeriya, eza lakhona enyakazelisa amaxuku." 
Acts17:14 Njalo ngalesosikhathi abazalwane bahle bamthuma uPawuli kungathi uya elwandle basala khona. 
Acts17:15 Lalabo ababephelekezela uPawuli. 
Acts17:16 Kwathi uPawuli esabalindele eAtene, umoya wakhe wakhathazeka phakathi kwakhe, ebona umuzi ugcwele izithombe." 
Acts17:17 Ngakho waphikisana, lasemdangeni insuku zonke lalabo ahlangana labo." 
Acts17:18 Labathile kuzo izazi zamaEpikuri lamaStoyiki baphikisana laye. Labanye bathi: Uwumane lolu lufuna ukuthini? Kodwa abanye bathi: Kungathi ungotshumayela onkulunkulu bezizweni; ngoba ngevangeli watshumayela kibo uJesu. 
Acts17:19 Basebemthatha, bamusa eAreyopagu besithi: Singazi yini ukuthi iyini limfundiso entsha oyifundisayo?" 
Acts17:20 Ngoba uletha indaba ezimangalisayo ezithile endlebeni zethu; ngakho sifisa ukwazi ukuthi lezizinto ziyini. 
Acts17:21 Ngoba bonke abeAtene lezethekeli ezihlala khona babechitha isikhathi kungeyisikho ngolutho olunye, ngaphandle kokutshela lokuzwa into entsha." 
Acts17:22 Kwathi uPawuli esima phakathi kweAreyopagu, wathi: Madoda maAtene, ngiyabona ukuthi ezintweni zonke kungathi lilenkolelo enkulu." 
Acts17:23 Ngoba ngithe ngidabula ngikhangela izinto zenu elizikhonzayo, ngasengifica ilathi elilotshwe ukuthi: KUNKULUNKULU ONGAZIWAYO." 
Acts17:24 UNkulunkulu owenza umhlaba lakho konke okukuwo," 
Acts17:25 futhi kakhonzwa ngezandla zabantu, njengo swela ulutho;" 
Acts17:26 njalo wazenza zonke izizwe zabantu zivela egazini linye, ukuthi zihlale ebusweni bonke bomhlaba, wazimisela izikhathi eziqunyiweyo ngaphambili;" 
Acts17:27 ukuze zidinge iNkosi, ukuthi mhlawumbe sibili zimuzwe zi m thole, njalo kanti kakhatshana kulowo lalowo wethu." 
Acts17:28 Ngoba kuye siphila njalo sihamba futhi sikhona. 
Acts17:29 Ngakho lokhu siyinzalo kaNkulunkulu, kakufanele ukuthi sinakane ukuthi ubuNkulunkulu bunjengegolide kumbe isiliva loba ilitshe, okubazwe ngeminwe langokunakana kwabantu." 
Acts17:30 Ngakho izikhathi zokungazi uNkulunkulu kazinanzanga; 
Acts17:31 ngoba umisile usuku, azakwahlulela." 
Acts17:32 Kwathi besizwa ngokuvuka okwabafileyo. 
Acts17:33 Langokunjalo uPawuli waphuma phakathi kwabo. 
Acts17:34 Kodwa amadoda athile anamathela kuye, akholwa; phakathi kwawo kwakukhona loDiyonisiyu umAreyopagu, lowesifazana obizo lakhe nguDamari, labanye kanye labo." 
Acts18:1 Emva kwalezizinto uPawuli wasuka eAtene weza eKorinte. 
Acts18:2 Wasefica umJuda othile uAkwila kokuthi wonke amaJuda kawasuke eRoma, waya kubo;" 
Acts18:3 njalo ngoba babelomsebenzi ofananayo, wahlala kibo wasebenza; ngoba babengabenzi bamathente ngomsebenzi." 
Acts18:4 Wasetshumayela, wancenga amaJuda lamaGriki." 
Acts18:5 Kwathi uSilasi loTimothi. 
Acts18:6 Kwathi emelana laye ehlambaza. 
Acts18:7 Wasesuka lapho waya endlini yomunye obizo lakhe nguJustusi, okhonza uNkulunkulu, ondlu yakhe yayiseduze lesinagoge." 
Acts18:8 Kodwa uKrispusi. 
Acts18:9 INkosi yasisithi kuPawuli ebusuku: Ungesabi, kodwa khuluma njalo ungathuli;" 
Acts18:10 ngoba mina ngilawe, njalo kakho ozakuhlasela ukukwenzela okubi; ngoba ngilabantu abanengi kulumuzi." 
Acts18:11 Njalo wahlala umnyaka lenyanga eziyisithupha, efundisa ilizwi likaNkulunkulu phakathi kwabo." 
Acts18:12 Kwathi uGaliyo engumbusi," 
Acts18:13 esithi: Lo uncenga abantu ukuthi bakhonze uNkulunkulu ngokuphambene lomlayo. 
Acts18:14 Kodwa kwathi uPawuli esezavula umlomo; 
Acts18:15 kodwa uba kuyikuphikisana ngelizwi lamabizo, ziboneleni lina; ngoba mina kangithandi ukuba ngumahluleli walezizinto." 
Acts18:16 Wasewaxotsha esihlalweni sokwahlulela. 
Acts18:17 Wonke amaGriki asebamba uSostenesi. Njalo uGaliyo kaze azinanza lezizinto. 
Acts18:18 Kwathi uPawuli esahlezi insuku ezinengi, wavalelisa abazalwane." 
Acts18:19 Sebefikile eEfesu. 
Acts18:20 Sebemcelile ukuthi ahlale isikhathi esidanyana labo, kavumanga;" 
Acts18:21 kodwa wabavalelisa," 
Acts18:22 njalo esefikile eKesariya. 
Acts18:23 Njalo esechithe isikhathi esithile, wasuka, wadabula ngokulandelana ilizwe leGalathiya." 
Acts18:24 Kwathi umJuda othile uApolosi ngebizo, elamandla emibhalweni." 
Acts18:25 Lo wayefundisiwe indlela yeNkosi, njalo evutha emoyeni;" 
Acts18:26 lo waseqala ukukhuluma ngesibindi esinagogeni. 
Acts18:27 Kwathi esethanda ukuchaphela eAkaya; 
Acts18:28 ngoba waphikisa ngamandla. 
Acts19:1 Kwasekusithi, uApolosi esedabule indawo eziphakemeyo; wasefica abafundi abathile" 
Acts19:2 wathi kubo: Lamemukela yini uMoya oNgcwele mhla likholwayo? Basebesithi kuye: Kodwa kasizanga sizwe ngitsho ukuthi kukhona uMoya oNgcwele. 
Acts19:3 Wasesithi kubo: Pho labhabhathizelwa kukuphi? Basebesithi: Kubhabhathizo lukaJohane. 
Acts19:4 Kodwa uPawuli wathi: UJohane wabhabhathiza ubhabhathizo lokuphenduka. 
Acts19:5 Lalabo abezwayo babhabhathizwa ebizweni leNkosi uJesu. 
Acts19:6 Wathi uPawuli esebeke izandla phezu kwabo. 
Acts19:7 Njalo wonke amadoda ayengaba litshumi lambili. 
Acts19:8 Wasengena esinagogeni. 
Acts19:9 Kodwa kwathi abanye besiba lukhuni bengakholwa, bekhuluma kubi nga leyo ndlela phambi kwabantu." 
Acts19:10 Lalokhu kwenzeka okweminyaka emibili, amaJuda kanye lamaGriki." 
Acts19:11 UNkulunkulu wasesenza," 
Acts19:12 kwaze kwathi lakwabagulayo kwasiwa izifinyo kumbe amafasikoti. 
Acts19:13 Kwathi abanye kumihambuma yamaJuda, izanuse." 
Acts19:14 Njalo kwakukhona amadodana ayisikhombisa athile kaSikeva umJuda umpristi omkhulu akwenzayo lokho. 
Acts19:15 Kodwa umoya omubi waphendula wathi: UJesu ngiyamazi, loPawuli ngiyazi ngaye; kodwa lina lingobani?"
