Acts19:16 Lowomuntu okwakukuye umoya omubi waseseqela phezu kwabo, njalo wabehlula, wabanqoba, baze babaleka kuleyondlu benqunu belimele." 
Acts19:17 Lokhu kwasekusaziwa yibo bonke abakhileyo eEfesu; njalo lakhuliswa ibizo leNkosi uJesu. 
Acts19:18 Labanengi balabo abakholwayo beza, bevuma, bememezela izenzo zabo." 
Acts19:19 Labanengi balabo ababesenza amasalamusi baletha ingwalo ndawonye bazitshisa phambi kwabo bonke; basebebala intengo yazo, bathola izinkulungwane ezingamatshumi amahlanu zesiliva." 
Acts19:20 Ngokunjalo ilizwi leNkosi lakhula ngamandla lanqoba. 
Acts19:21 Kwathi lezizinto seziphelile, uPawuli wazimisela emoyeni." 
Acts19:22 Esethume eMakedoniya. 
Acts19:23 Kodwa ngalesosikhathi kwasuka isiphithiphithi esingesincinyane. 
Acts19:24 Ngoba umuntu othile onguDemetriyu ngebizo, umkhandi wesiliva, owenza amathempel anaesiliva kaDiyana, waletha kuzingcwethi inzuzo engencinyane;" 
Acts19:25 owabaqoqayo bona, lezisebenzi zezinto ezifananayo, wathi: Madoda, liyazi ukuthi inotho yethu ivela kulumsebenzi." 
Acts19:26 Njalo liyabona liyezwa ukuthi kungeyisikho eEfesu. 
Acts19:27 Njalo kayisikho lokhu kuphela ukuthi sisengozini yokuthi le ingxenye ifike ekutheni ingahlonitshwa, kodwa lethempeli likankulunkulukazi omkhulu uDiyana lizathiwa liyinto engesilutho, njalo lobukhulukazi bakhe buzakwehliswa, elimkhonzayo yonke iAsiya." 
Acts19:28 Kwathi be ku zwa bagcwala intukuthelo, bamemeza besithi: Mkhulu uDiyana wamaEfesu!" 
Acts19:29 Njalo umuzi wonke wagcwala isiphithiphithi. 
Acts19:30 Kwathi uPawuli efuna ukungena exukwini, abafundi kabamvumelanga." 
Acts19:31 Njalo labanye bababusi beAsiya, ababengabangane bakhe, bathuma kuye, be m ncenga ukuthi angazinikeli endaweni yokudlalela." 
Acts19:32 Ngakho abanye bamemeza okunye labanye okunye; ngoba umhlangano wawusanganisekile, njalo inengi labo lalingazi ukuthi libuthene lapho ngenxa yani." 
Acts19:33 Basebemusa phambili uAleksandro esuka exukwini. 
Acts19:34 Kodwa bathi sebekwazi ukuthi ungumJuda, kwaba lelizwi elilodwa livela kubo bonke okungaba ngamahola amabili limemeza lisithi: Mkhulu uDiyana wamaEfesu!" 
Acts19:35 Njalo kwathi umabhalane eselithulisile ixuku wathi: Madoda eEfesu, kanti kukhona yini umuntu ongaziyo ukuthi umuzi weEfesu ungumlondolozi wethempeli likankulunkulukazi omkhulu uDiyana lowento eyawa ivela kuZewusi?" 
Acts19:36 Ngakho njengoba lezizinto zingephikwe, kufanele lithule." 
Acts19:37 Ngoba lilethe lamadoda, angeyisibo abaphangi bamathempeli langahlambazi unkulunkulukazi wenu." 
Acts19:38 Ngakho uba uDemetriyu lezingcwethi kanye laye belodaba ngomuntu, amalanga okuthonisa amacala ayagcinwa, bakhona lababusi." 
Acts19:39 Kodwa uba lidinga ulutho ngezinye izinto, kuzalungiswa emhlanganweni osemthethweni." 
Acts19:40 Ngoba futhi sisengozini yokumangalelwa ngomvukela ngenxa yalamuhla, kungelambangela esingalandisa ngayo ngalesisiphithiphithi." 
Acts19:41 Njalo esetshilo lokho, wawuchitha umhlangano." 
Acts20:1 Kwathi sesiphelile isiyaluyalu, uPawuli wabizela kuye abafundi." 
Acts20:2 Kwathi esedabule lezongxenye, esebakhuthazile ngamazwi amanengi, wafika eGriki," 
Acts20:3 kwathi esehlale khonainyanga ezintathu, selenziwe iqhinga ngaye." 
Acts20:4 Wasemphelekezela kwaze kwaba seAsiya uSopatheri. 
Acts20:5 Laba sebehambe phambili basilindela. 
Acts20:6 Kodwa thina sasuka ngomkhumbi eFiliphi. 
Acts20:7 Kwathi ngo sukulokuqala lweviki, uPawuli watshumayela kubo, elungele ukusuka kusisa, waseselula ilizwi kwaze kwaba phakathi kobusuku." 
Acts20:8 Njalo kwakukhona izibane ezinengi. 
Acts20:9 Kwakuhlezi ewindini ijaha elithile ngebizo linguYutikusi, elajunywa yibuthongo obukhulu, laselidojwa lifile." 
Acts20:10 Kodwa uPawuli wehla waziphosela phezu kwalo. 
Acts20:11 Esenyukile njalo esehlephule isinkwa wadla, waxoxa labo isikhathi eside kwaze kwasa, ngokunjalo wahamba." 
Acts20:12 Basebemletha umfana ephila, basebeduduzwa hatshi lakancane." 
Acts20:13 Kodwa thina, sesihambe phambili ukuya emkhunjini, sasuka ngomkhumbi saya eAsosi, lapho siqonde ukumkhweza uPawuli; ngoba wayemisile ngokunjalo, yena ebezahamba ngenyawo." 
Acts20:14 Njalo esehlangene lathi eAsosi, samkhweza safika eMithilene," 
Acts20:15 sasuka lapho ngomkhumbi, kusisa safika maqondana leKiyosi; langomhlomunye sasondela eSamosi; sasesihlala eTrogiliumu, ngolulandelayo." 
Acts20:16 Ngoba uPawuli wayezimisele ukuyiceza iEfesu ngomkhumbi. 
Acts20:17 Kwathi eseMilethu wathumela eEfesu wabizela kuye abadala bebandla. 
Acts20:18 Kwathi sebefikile kuye, wathi kubo: Liyazi lina, ukuthi kusukela osukwini lokuqala lokufika kwami eAsiya, ngangihlezi njani isikhathi sonke phakathi kwenu," 
Acts20:19 ngakhonza iNkosi ngokuthobeka konke langezinyembezi ezinengi langezilingo ezangehlela ngamaqhinga amaJuda; 
Acts20:20 ukuthi angigodlanga lutho ngayo olusizayo," 
Acts20:21 ngifakaza kumaJuda kanye lakumaGriki. 
Acts20:22 Lakhathesi khangelani, mina ngiya eJerusalema ngibotshwe nguMoya, ngingakwazi okuzangehlela phakathi kwayo," 
Acts20:23 ngaphandle kokuthi uMoya oyiNgcwele uyangifakazela emizini yonke. 
Acts20:24 Kodwa angikhathaleli lutho lwalezizinto. 
Acts20:25 Njalo khathesi khangelani, mina ngiyazi ukuthi kalisayikubona ubuso bami lina lonke." 
Acts20:26 Ngakho ngiyafakaza kini ngalolusuku lwalamuhla, ukuthi mina ngimsulwa egazini labo bonke;" 
Acts20:27 ngoba kangigodlanga ukuthi ngilitshumayeze. 
Acts20:28 Ziqapheleni-ke lina. 
Acts20:29 Ngoba mina ngiyazi lokhu, ukuthi emva kokuhamba kwami kuzangena impisi eziphangayo phakathi kwenu, zingawuyekeli umhlambi;" 
Acts20:30 laphakathi kwenu kuzavela amadoda. 
Acts20:31 Ngakho lindani. 
Acts20:32 Lakhathesi, bazalwane, ngilinikela kuNkulunkulu." 
Acts20:33 Kangihawukelanga isiliva. 
Acts20:34 Lina-ke uqobo lwenu liyazi ukuthi lezizandla zasebenzela inswelo zami. 
Acts20:35 Kukho konke ngilitshengisile, ukuthi kumele ukuthi sisize ababuthakathaka, sikhumbule amazwi eNkosi uJesu, ukuthi yena wathi: Kubusisekile kakhulu ukupha kulokwemukela." 
Acts20:36 Njalo esetshilo lezizinto, waguqa ngamadolo akhe, wakhuleka labo bonke." 
Acts20:37 Kwaba khona ukukhala kakhulu kwabo bonke; basebewela entanyeni kaPawuli bamanga," 
Acts20:38 belosizi kakhulu ngelizwi alitshoyo. 
Acts21:1 Kwasekusithi sisuka ngomkhumbi sesehlukene labo, sahamba ngendlela eqondileyo safika eKosi, lango sukuolulandelayo eRodesi, sasuka lapho sayaePathara;" 
Acts21:2 sasesithola lapho umkhumbi ochaphela eFenekiya, sangena sahamba ngomkhumbi." 
Acts21:3 Kwathi sesiqhamuka eKuprosi. 
Acts21:4 Sesibatholile abafundi. 
Acts21:5 Kwathi sekwenzakele ukuthi siqede insuku, sasuka sahamba, njalo bonke basiphelekezela kanye labomkabo labantwana kwaze kwaba ngaphandle komuzi," 
Acts21:6 sesivalelisene, sangena emkhunjini." 
Acts21:7 Kodwa thina, sesiqedile uhambo ngomkhumbi sisuka eTire sahlala labo usuku lwaba lunye." 
Acts21:8 Kusisa thina esasiloPawuli sasuka, sahlala laye." 
Acts21:9 Yena-ke wayelamadodakazi amane, intombi, eziprofethayo." 
Acts21:10 Kwathi sesihlezi insuku ezinengi, kwehla umprofethi othile," 
Acts21:11 wasefika kithi, wathatha uzwezwe lukaPawuli: Indoda olungolwayo loluzwezwe, amaJuda eJerusalema azayibopha kanje, njalo a yi nikele ezandleni zabezizwe." 
Acts21:12 Sesizizwile lezizinto, samncenga thina kanye lalabo ababelapho, ukuthi angenyukeli eJerusalema." 
Acts21:13 Kodwa uPawuli waphendula esithi: Lenzani likhala lidabula inhliziyo yami? Ngoba mina sengilungele, kungeyisikho ukubotshwa kuphela, kodwa lokufa eJerusalema ngenxa yebizo leNkosi uJesu." 
Acts21:14 Kwathi engancengeki, sathula sathi: Kayenziwe intando yeNkosi." 
Acts21:15 Emva kwalezinsuku sasesilungiselela. 
Acts21:16 L abathilebabafundi, ebesizangenisa kuye." 
Acts21:17 Njalo sesifikile eJerusalema, abazalwane." 
Acts21:18 Kusisa uPawuli wangena lathi kuJakobe. 
Acts21:19 Kwathi esebabingelele, wabalandisela ngakunye ngakunye." 
Acts21:20 Kwathi sebe ku zwile, bayidumisa iNkosi;" 
Acts21:21 njalo sebetsheliwe ngawe. 
Acts21:22 Pho-ke kuyini? Isibili kufanele ukuthi ixuku libuthane; ngoba bazakuzwa ukuthi usufikile. 
Acts21:23 Ngakho yenza lokhu esikutsho kuwe; silamadoda amane abalesifungo phezu kwawo; 
Acts21:24 athathe kanye lawe, uzihlambulule kanye lawo." 
Acts21:25 Kodwa mayelana labezizwe abakholwayo thina sesibhalile, saquma sathibangagcini lutho olunjalo, ngaphandle kokuthi kabazile okuhlatshelwe izithombe, legazi, lokukhanyiweyo, lokufeba." 
Acts21:26 UPawuli wasewathatha amadoda, kusisa wahlanjululwa kanye lawo." 
Acts21:27 Kwathi sezizaphela insuku eziyisikhombisa," 
Acts21:28 amemeza athi: Madoda maIsrayeli, sizani! Nguye lumuntu ofundisa bonke endaweni zonke okuphambene lesizwe, lomlayo." 
Acts21:29 Ngoba ayebonile ngaphambili uTrofimu emzini elaye, amkhumbulela ukuthi uPawuli umngenisile ethempelini." 
Acts21:30 Lomuzi wonke wanyakazela, labantu bagijimela ndawonye, bamdumela uPawuli bamhudulela ngaphandle kwethempeli; leminyango yahle yavalwa." 
Acts21:31 Kuthe besafuna ukumbulala, ilizwi lafika enduneni enkulu;" 
Acts21:32 eyahle yathatha amabutho lezinduna zekhulu, yagijimela kubo." 
Acts21:33 Induna enkulu yasisondela, yabuza ukuthi ungubani, lokuthi wenzeni." 
Acts21:34 Abanye exukwini bememeza okunye labanye okunye; kodwa ingelakulazi iqiniso ngenxa yomsindo, yalaya ukuthi asiwe enkambeni yamabutho." 
Acts21:35 Kwathi esefikile ezikhwelweni, kwenzeka ukuthi athwalwe ngamabutho ngenxa yokufutheka kwexuku;" 
Acts21:36 ngoba ixuku labantu lalandela limemeza lisithi: Msuseni! 
Acts21:37 Kwathi uPawuli esezangeniswa enkambeni yamabutho: Kuvunyelwe yini ukuthi ngikhulume ulutho kuwe? Yona yasisithi: Uyasazi isiGriki yini? 
Acts21:38 Kanti kawusuye yini lowomGibhithe? 
Acts21:39 Kodwa uPawuli wathi: Mina ngingumuntu ongumJuda, weTarsu yeKilikhiya, isakhamuzi somuzi ongadelelekanga; ngiyakuncenga, ngivumela ngikhulume ebantwini." 
Acts21:40 Kwathi esemvumele, uPawuli wema ezikhwelweni:" 
Acts22:1 Madoda, bazalwane, labobaba, zwanini ukuziphendulela kwami khathesi kini." 
Acts22:2 Sebezwile ukuthi ukhuluma labo ngolimi lwamaHebheru, bathula kakhulu, wasesithi:" 
Acts22:3 Mina ngiyindoda engumJuda; 
Acts22:4 eyazingela leyondlela," 
Acts22:5 njengoba lompristi omkhulu engifakazela, lomphakathi wonke wabadala, ngaya eDamaseko, ukuthi lababekhona lapho ngibalethe eJerusalema bebotshiwe, ukuze bajeziswe." 
Acts22:6 Kwasekusithi ngisahamba sengisondela eDamaseko, sekungaba yimini enkulu, kwahle kwakhanya ukukhanya okukhulu okuvela ezulwini kungizingelezela." 
Acts22:7 Ngasengiwela phansi, ngasengisizwa ilizwi lisithi kimi: Sawuli, Sawuli, ungizingelelani?" 
Acts22:8 Mina ngasengiphendula ngathi: Ungubani, Nkosi? Wasesithi kimi: NginguJesu weNazaretha wena omzingelayo." 
Acts22:9 Lalabo ababelami bakubona ukukhanya, njalo basebesesaba, kodwa kabalizwanga ilizwi elakhuluma lami." 
Acts22:10 Ngasengisithi: Ngenzeni, Nkosi? INkosi yasisithi kimi: Sukuma uye eDamaseko; njalo uzatshelwa khona ngazo zonke izinto ozimiselwe ukuthi uzenze." 
Acts22:11 Njengoba ngangingaboni ngenxa yenkazimulo yalokhokukhanya, ngakhokhelwa ngesandla yilabo ababelami, ngafika eDamaseko." 
Acts22:12 Njalo uAnaniya othile," 
Acts22:13 weza kimi wasesima phansi kwami wathi kimi: Sawuli mzalwane, buya ubone. Njalo mina ngalesosikhathi ngasengimbona." 
Acts22:14 Wasesithi: UNkulunkulu wabobaba bethu," 
Acts22:15 ngoba uzakuba ngumfakazi wakhe. 
Acts22:16 Khathesi-ke, usalindeleni? Sukuma ubhabhathizwe." 
Acts22:17 Kwasekusithi kimi sengibuyele eJerusalema," 
Acts22:18 ngasengimbona wathi kimi: Phangisa uphume ngesiqubu eJerusalema. 
Acts22:19 Ngasengisithi: Nkosi, bayazi bona ukuthi mina ngangibafaka entolongweni;" 
Acts22:20 njalo mhla kuchithwa igazi likaStefane umfakazi wakho. 
Acts22:21 Wasesithi kimi: Hamba, ngoba mina ngizakuthuma." 
Acts22:22 Bamlalela kwaze kwafika kulelolizwi, baphakamisa ilizwi labo!" 
Acts22:23 Kwathi besamemeza, baphosa izembatho, baphosa uthuli emoyeni," 
Acts22:24 induna enkulu yalaya ukuthi angeniswe enkambeni yamabutho, ukuze yazi ukuthi kungasizatho bani bememeza ngokunjalo ngaye." 
Acts22:25 Kwathi sebemelulele phambili ngemichilo, uPawuli wathi enduneni yekhulu eyayimi lapho: Kuvunyelwe kini yini ukutshaya ngesiswepu umuntu ongumRoma?" 
Acts22:26 Induna yekhulu isizwile yasondela yatshela induna enkulu isithi: Nanzelela osuzakwenza; ngoba lumuntu ungumRoma. 
Acts22:27 Induna enkulu yasifika yathi kuye: Ngitshele, wena ungumRoma yini? Yena wathi: Yebo." 
Acts22:28 Induna enkulu yasiphendula yathi: Mina lelilungelo lokuba yisakhamuzi ngalizuza ngemali enkulu. UPawuli wasesithi: Kodwa lami ngazalwa lalo. 
Acts22:29 Ngakho labo abasebezamhlola bahle basuka kuye. Lenduna enkulu layo yesaba, isisazi ukuthi ungumRoma, lokuthi ibimbophile." 
Acts22:30 Kwathi kusisa ifuna ukwazi iqiniso, ukuthi kungani emangalelwa ngamaJuda, yamkhulula kuzibopho." 
Acts23:1 UPawuli wasewujolozela, kuze kube lamuhla." 
Acts23:2 Kodwa uAnaniya umpristi omkhulu. 
Acts23:3 UPawuli wasesithi kuye: UNkulunkulu uzakutshaya, mduli oconjwe waba mhlophe?" 
Acts23:4 Lababemi lapho bathi: Uyamthuka umpristi omkhulu kaNkulunkulu yini? 
Acts23:5 UPawuli wasesithi: Bengingazi, bazalwane, ukuthi ungumpristi omkhulu." 
Acts23:6 Kwathi uPawuli esekwazi ukuthi enye ingxenye yabo ingabaSadusi. 
Acts23:7 Kwathi esetshilo lokhu, kwavela ukuphikisana kwabaFarisi labaSadusi, lexuku ladabuka phakathi;" 
Acts23:8 ngoba abaSadusi. 
Acts23:9 Kwasekuvela ukumemeza okukhulu; kwathi ababhali behlelo labaFarisi basukuma baphika kakhulu besithi: Kasitholi bubi kulumuntu. 
Acts23:10 Kwathi sekuvele ukuphikisana okukhulu, induna enkulu yesaba ukuthi uPawuli uzadatshulwa yibo, yalaya amabutho." 
Acts23:11 Njalo ngobusuku obulandelayo iNkosi yema phansi kwakhe. 
Acts23:12 Kwathi sekusile, abanye bamaJuda benza iqhinga, bazibopha ngesiqalekiso, besithi kabayikudla lokunatha baze bambulale uPawuli." 
Acts23:13 Njalo babengaphezu kwamatshumi amane abenza lesisifungo ndawonye; 
Acts23:14 abaya kubapristi abakhulu labadala bathi: Sizibophe ngesiqalekiso esikhulu, sokuthi kasiyikudla lutho size simbulale uPawuli." 
Acts23:15 Ngakho khathesi lina kanye lomphakathi. 
Acts23:16 Kodwa indodana kadadewabo kaPawuli yezwa ngokumcathamela, yeza yangena enkambeni yamabutho, yamtshela uPawuli." 
Acts23:17 UPawuli wasebizela kuye enye yezinduna zekhulu wathi: Sana lelijaha enduneni enkulu; ngoba lilento elizayitshela yona. 
Acts23:18 Yasilithatha-ke yalisa enduneni enkulu, yasisithi: UPawuli isibotshwa ungibizele kuye wacela ukuthi ngilethe lelijaha kuwe, lilento elizakutshela yona." 
Acts23:19 Induna enkulu yasilithatha ngesandla, yasibuyela eceleni bebodwa, yabuza: Kuyini ozongitshela khona?" 
Acts23:20 Laselisithi: AmaJuda avumelene ukucela kuwe. 
Acts23:21 Ngakho wena ungavunyiswa yiwo; ngoba amadoda adlula amatshumi amane kuwo amcathamele ngokuthi angadli anganathi aze ambulale; lakhathesi alungile elindele isithembiso sakho. 
Acts23:22 Ngakho induna enkulu yasiliyekela ijaha lahamba, i li laya isithi: Ungatsheli muntu ukuthi ungibikele lezizinto." 
Acts23:23 Yasibizela kuyo induna zekhulu ezithile ezimbili, yathi: Lungisani abebutho abangamakhulu amabili ukuze bahambe baze bayefika eKesariya, labagadi bamabhiza abangamatshumi ayisikhombisa, labemikhonto abangamakhulu amabili, kusukela ngehola lesithathu lobusuku;" 
Acts23:24 lungisani lezinyamazana, ukuze ligadise uPawuli limfikise ephephile kumbusi uFelike;" 
Acts23:25 wabhala incwadi imumethe lokhu: 
Acts23:26 Klawudiyosi Lisiya kumhlekazi. 
Acts23:27 Lindoda ibibanjwe ngamaJuda, njalo ibisizabulawa yiwo." 
Acts23:28 Ngathi ngifuna ukuthi ngazi isizatho ayimangalela ngaso; 
Acts23:29 engathi ngithola ukuthi imangalelwe loba izibopho. 
Acts23:30 Kwathi sekuvelile kimi. 
Acts23:31 Abebutho-ke, njengokulaywa kwabo, bamthatha uPawuli, bamusa eAntipatri ngobusuku." 
Acts23:32 Njalo kusisa, batshiya abagadi bamabhiza ukuthi bahambe laye;" 
Acts23:33 okwathi sebefikile eKesariya, bammisa loPawuli phambi kwakhe." 
Acts23:34 Kwathi umbusi eseyifundile incwadi," 
Acts23:35 wathi: Ngizakuzwa, sebefikile labamangaleli bakho." 
Acts24:1 Kwathi emva kwensuku ezinhlanu. 
Acts24:2 Kwathi esebiziwe, uTertulo waqala uku m cala esithi: Ukuthula okukhulu sikuzuzile ngawe, lemisebenzi emihle yenzakele kulesisizwe ngokunakekela kwakho," 
Acts24:3 ngazo zonke indlela lakuzo zonke indawo siyakwemukela, ngakho konke ukubonga." 
Acts24:4 Kodwa ukuze ngingakubambeleli kakhulu, ngiyakuncenga ukuthi ngomusa wakho usizwe ngokufitshane." 
Acts24:5 Ngoba lindoda siyifice iyinkathazo, njalo ingeyenza umvukela phakathi kwamaJuda wonke;" 
Acts24:6 eyake yazama lokungcolisa ithempeli," 
Acts24:7 kodwa kwafika uLisiya induna enkulu wa m thatha ngodlakela olukhulu ezandleni zethu," 
Acts24:8 elaya abamangaleli bakhe ukuthi beze kuwe; ongathi, ngoku m buzisisa wena uqobo, ungaba lakho ukwazi kuye ngazo zonke izinto thina esimmangalela ngazo." 
Acts24:9 LamaJuda lawo avuma, esithi lezizinto zinjalo." 
Acts24:10 UPawuli wasephendula, umbusi esemqhwebile ukuthi akhulume," 
Acts24:11 njengoba ungakubona ukuthi kaku ka dluli insuku ezilitshumi lambili; 
Acts24:12 njalo kabangificanga ethempelini ngiphikisana lomuntu loba ngivusa isiphithiphithi exukwini, loba emasinagogeni, loba emzini." 
Acts24:13 Futhi bangeke baqinise ngezinto abangimangalela ngazo khathesi. 
Acts24:14 Kodwa ngiyavuma kuwe lokhu, ukuthi ngendlela abayibiza ngokuthi;" 
Acts24:15 ngilethemba kuNkulunkulu. 
Acts24:16 Njalo kulokho mina ngiyazama, ukuthi ngibe lesazela." 
Acts24:17 Kwathi emva; 
Acts24:18 ngikulezizinto; 
Acts24:19 afanele ukuba khona lapha phambi kwakho a ngi cale uba elolutho ngami; 
Acts24:20 kumbe bona ngokwabo kabatsho, ukuthi baficani okungalunganga kimi, mhla ngimi phambi komphakathi," 
Acts24:21 ngaphandle kwalelolizwi elilodwa, engalimemeza ngimi phakathi kwabo ngisithi: Ngokuvuka okwabafileyo mina ngiyehlulelwa yini lamuhla." 
Acts24:22 Kwathi uFelike wabadlulisela phambili, esezwile lezizinto esazi ngokupheleleyo;" 
Acts24:23 waselaya induna yekhulu ukuthi agcinwe uPawuli, lokuthi abe lenkululeko." 
Acts24:24 Kwathi emva kwensuku ezithile, uFelike weza loDrusila umkakhe engumJudakazi, wathumela ukubiza uPawuli, wamuzwa mayelana lokholo kuKristu." 
Acts24:25 Kwathi esakhuluma ngokulunga langokuzithiba; 
Acts24:26 njalo ngesikhathi esifananayo wayethemba futhi ukuthi uzanikwa imali nguPawuli, ukuze amkhulule; ngakho wayehlezi embizela kuye ekhuluma laye." 
Acts24:27 Kodwa sekugcwaliseke iminyaka emibili, uFelike wemukela omlandelayo uPorkiyu uFestusi; uFelike efisa ukuthokozisa amaJuda wamtshiya uPawuli ebotshiwe." 
Acts25:1 Ngakho kwathi uFestusi esengenile emkhonweni," 
Acts25:2 labapristi abakhulu bammangalela uPawuli kuye, bemncenga," 
Acts25:3 bacela ukwenzelwa umusa omelane laye, ukuthi amthume eJerusalema." 
Acts25:4 Kodwa uFestusi waphendula ngokuthi uPawuli ugciniwe eKesariya, lokuthi laye ngokwakhe uzakuya khonangokuphangisa." 
Acts25:5 Wathi: Ngakho labo abenelisayo phakathi kwenu kabehle kanye lami; uba kukhona ulutho olubi ngaleyondoda, bayimangalele." 
Acts25:6 Kwathi esehlale phakathi kwabo insuku ezedlula itshumi, wehlela walaya ukuthi uPawuli alethwe." 
Acts25:7 Kwathi esefikile, amaJuda ayehlile evela eJerusalema ema e m hanqile," 
Acts25:8 yena eziphendulela wathi. 
Acts25:9 Kodwa uFestusi ethanda ukuthabisa amaJuda, wahlulelwe khona ngalezizinto phambi kwami?" 
Acts25:10 Kodwa uPawuli wathi: Ngimi phambi kwesihlalo sokwahlulela sikaKesari. 
Acts25:11 Ngoba uba ngonile ngenze ulutho olufanele ukufa, kangali ukufa." 
Acts25:12 Khona uFestusi esekhulume lomphakathi waphendula wathi: Ulidlulisele kuKesari? Uzakuya kuKesari. 
Acts25:13 Kwathi sekudlule insuku ezithile, uAgripha inkosi loBernike bafika eKesariya, ukuze babingelele uFestusi." 
Acts25:14 Kwathi sebehlezi khona insuku ezinengi, uFestusi wayilandisela inkosi izindaba zikaPawuli," 
Acts25:15 kwathi ngiseJerusalema. 
Acts25:16 Engabaphendula ngathi: Kakusiwo umkhuba wamaRoma ukumnikela umuntu ekufeni. 
Acts25:17 Ngakho sebebuthene lapha, kangizange ngiphuze; ngo sukuolulandelayo, ngalaya ukuthi indoda ilethwe;" 
Acts25:18 leyo aba yi mangalelayo sebemi kabavezanga cala ngayo ngezinto mina ebengizicabangela," 
Acts25:19 kodwa babelokuphikisana okuthile laye, langothile uJesu owafayo, uPawuli othi ngaye uyaphila." 
Acts25:20 Kuthe mina ngisadidekile ngombuzo onje, ngathi, angathanda yini ukuya eJerusalema, ayekwahlulelwa khona ngalezozinto." 
Acts25:21 Kodwa kwathi uPawuli eselidlulisele phambili ukuthi agcinelwe ukuhlolwa yinkosi enkulu, ngalaya ukuthi agcinwe, ngize ngimthume kuKesari." 
Acts25:22 UAgripha wasesithi kuFestusi: Lami bengithanda ukuthi ngimuzwe lumuntu. Yena wathi: Kusasa uzamuzwa. 
Acts25:23 Ngakho kusisa, kwathi uAgripha loBernike befika ngokuzibonakalisa okukhulu lamadoda ayizikhulu zomuzi, uFestusi waselaya ukuthi uPawuli alethwe." 
Acts25:24 UFestusi wasesithi: Nkosi Agripha, lani lonke madoda elikhona lapha kanye lathi, liyambona lo elangicela ngaye." 
Acts25:25 Kodwa mina ngathola ukuthi kenzanga lutho olufanele ukufa, ngaquma ukumthuma." 
Acts25:26 Okungaye kangilalutho oluqinileyo engingalubhalela inkosi. Ngakho ngimlethile phambi kwenu, ikakhulu phambi kwakho, nkosi Agripha, ukuze kuthi esehloliwe ngibe lakho engingakubhala." 
Acts25:27 Ngoba ngibona kungaqondanga ukuthuma isibotshwa, kungatshengiswanga lamacala amelene laso." 
Acts26:1 UAgripha wasesithi kuPawuli: Uvunyelwe ukuzikhulumela. UPawuli waseselula isandla, waziphendulela wathi:" 
Acts26:2 Kukho konke engimangalelwa ngakho ngamaJuda; 
Acts26:3 ikakhulu ngoba uyawazi wonke amasiko lokuphikisana phakathi kwamaJuda; ngakho ngiyakuncenga, ukuthi ungizwe ngesineke." 
Acts26:4 Ngakho ukuhamba kwami konke kusukela ebutsheni, okwakuqala esizweni sakithi eJerusalema, wonke amaJuda ayakwazi," 
Acts26:5 ayangazi phambili kusukela ekuqaleni. 
Acts26:6 Lakhathesi ngimi ngithonisiswa ngenxa yethemba," 
Acts26:7 ezithemba ukufinyelela kuso izizwe zakithi ezilitshumi lambili. 
Acts26:8 Kungani kukhunjulwa ukuthi ku yintoengakholekiyo kini, nxa uNkulunkulu evusa abafileyo?" 
Acts26:9 Ngakho lami ngokwami ngangicabanga ukuthi ngangifanele ukwenza izinto ezinengi eziphambene lebizo likaJesu weNazaretha; 
Acts26:10 lami engakwenza eJerusalema. 
Acts26:11 Lemasinagogeni wonke ngabajezisa kanengi, nga ba bamba ngamandla ukuthi bahlambaze, nga ba zingela baze bafika emizini yabezizwe." 
Acts26:12 Okungazo lami ngisiya eDamaseko ngamandla langokuthunywa ngabapristi abakhulu," 
Acts26:13 emini enkulu, nkosi, ngabona endleleni ukukhanya kuvela ezulwini, kudlula ukukhanya kwelanga, kwakhanya kwangizingelezela lalabo ababehamba lami." 
Acts26:14 Kwathi sonke sesiwele phansi emhlabathini, ngezwa ilizwi likhuluma lami lisithi ngolimi lwesiHebheru: Sawuli, Sawuli, ungizingelelani? Kulukhuni kuwe ukukhahlelana lezincijo." 
Acts26:15 Mina ngasengisithi: Ungubani, Nkosi? Wasesithi: Mina nginguJesu omzingelayo." 
Acts26:16 Kodwa sukuma, njalo ume ngenyawo zakho; ngoba ngibonakelele lokho kuwe, ukuthi ngikumise," 
Acts26:17 ngikophula ebantwini lakwabezizwe, engikuthuma kubo khathesi," 
Acts26:18 ukuvula amehlo abo. 
Acts26:19 Ngakho, nkosi Agripha, kangalanga ukulalela umbono wezulwini;" 
Acts26:20 kodwa ngatshumayela kuqala kwabaseDamaseko. 
Acts26:21 Ngenxa yalezizinto amaJuda angibamba ethempelini, azama uku ngi bulala." 
Acts26:22 Ngakho ngizuzile usizo oluvela kuNkulunkulu, kuze kube lamuhla ngimi ngifakaza kubo bonke abancinyane labakhulu ukuthi zizakwenzeka," 
Acts26:23 ukuthi uKristu umele ukuhlupheka. 
Acts26:24 Kwathi esaziphendulela lezizinto. 
Acts26:25 Kodwa wathi: Kangihlanyi. 
Acts26:26 Ngoba inkosi iyazi ngalezizinto, engikhuluma ngesibindi lakuyo; ngoba ngileqiniso lokuthi akukho okunye kwalezizinto okufihlakeleyo kuyo; ngoba lokhu kakwenziwanga engonsini." 
Acts26:27 Nkosi Agripha, uyakholwa abaprofethi yini? Ngiyazi ukuthi uyakholwa." 
Acts26:28 UAgripha wasesithi kuPawuli: Usuphose wangiqinisekisa ukuthi ngibe ngumKristu. 
Acts26:29 UPawuli wasesithi: Bengingafisa kuNkulunkulu ukuthi, loba ngokulutshwana loba ngokunengi kungabi nguwe wedwa, kodwa labo bonke abangizwayo lamuhla, babe ngabanje njengoba nginjalo lami, ngaphandle kwalezizibopho." 
Acts26:30 Kwathi esekhulume lezizinto, yasukuma inkosi, lombusi;" 
Acts26:31 kwathi sebephumile bakhulumisana, besithi: Lumuntu kenzi lutho olufanele ukufa kumbe ukubotshwa." 
Acts26:32 UAgripha wasesithi kuFestusi: Lumuntu ubengakhululwa. 
Acts27:1 Kwathi sekuqunyiwe ukuthi siye eIthaliya ngomkhumbi. 
Acts27:2 Sasesingena emkhunjini weAdramithiyu, obusuzakuya endaweni zeAsiya." 
Acts27:3 Lakusisa safika eSidoni. 
Acts27:4 Sasesisuka lapho ngomkhumbi, ngoba imimoya yayiphambene lathi," 
Acts27:5 kwathi sesidabule ulwandle olungaseKilikhiya lePamfiliya, safika eMira yeLikhiya." 
Acts27:6 Lapho-ke induna yekhulu yathola umkhumbi weAleksandriya oya eIthaliya, yasikhweza kuwo." 
Acts27:7 Sasesihamba kancinyane okwensuku ezinengi, safika nzima maqondana leKinidu, umoya ungasivumeli maqondana leSalamone;" 
Acts27:8 sasesiyigudla kanzima safika endaweni ethile ethiwa yiMathekwamahle; okwakuseduze layo umuzi iLaseya. 
Acts27:9 Kwathi sekudlule isikhathi esikhulu, njalo sekuyingozi ukuhamba ngomkhumbi, ngoba lezilo lokudla laseledlule, uPawuli wa be luleka" 
Acts27:10 esithi kubo: Madoda, ngiyabona ukuthi uhambo luzakuba lengozi, kungeyisiwo owempahla lomkhumbi kuphela kodwa lowempilo zethu." 
Acts27:11 Kodwa induna yekhulu yakholwa induna yomkhumbi lomnikazi wawo kulezinto ezazitshiwo nguPawuli. 
Acts27:12 Kwathi njengoba itheku lalingalungelanga ukuhlalwa ebusika, inengi labo lacebisa ukuthi kusukwe lalapho, mhlawumbe kwenzeke ukuthi bafike eFenikisi bahlale khonaebusika, itheku leKrete elikhangele eningizimuntshonalanga lenyakathontshonalanga." 
Acts27:13 Njalo kuthe umoya weningizimu usuphephetha buthakathaka, banakana ukuthi sebekuzuzile lokho ababekuqondile, sebephakamise ingwegwesagudla eKrete." 
Acts27:14 Kodwa kungabanga yisikhathi eside umoya oyisivunguzane, othiwa iYurakilidoni, wawutshaya;" 
Acts27:15 umkhumbi wasubanjwa, wehluleka ukukhangelana lomoya, sasesiwuyekela undenda." 
Acts27:16 Sathi sesigudla phansi kwesihlengana esithile esithiwa yiKlawuda, senelisa kalukhuni ukuwubamba umkolo;" 
Acts27:17 abasebewuphanyekile, basebenzisa izincediso, sabopha ngamagoda sizingelezela umkhumbi; basebesesaba ukuthi bazaphoseka emhlabathiniweSirti, behlisa iseyili, ngokunjalo basebendenda." 
Acts27:18 Kuthe ukuthi siphoswe kakhulu yisiphepho, ngo lu landelayo baphosa impahla;" 
Acts27:19 kwathi ngolwesithathu salahla izikhali zomkhumbi ngezandla zethu uqobo. 
Acts27:20 Kwathi kungelalanga njalo kungelankanyezi ezibonakalayo insuku ezinengi, lesiphepho esingesincinyane si qinisa, kusukela lapho laseliphela ithemba lonke lokuthi sizasinda." 
Acts27:21 Kwathi sekuyisikhathi eside bengasadli, uPawuli wasesukuma phakathi kwabo, wathi: Madoda, ngabe la lalela mina." 
Acts27:22 Khathesi-ke sengileluleka ukuthi lime isibindi; ngoba kakusoze kulahleke impilo leyodwa kini, ngaphandle komkhumbi." 
Acts27:23 Ngoba," 
Acts27:24 yathi: Ungesabi Pawuli; ngoba umele ukuma phambi kukaKesari; njalo khangela, uNkulunkulu ukuphile bonke labo abahamba ngomkhumbi lawe." 
Acts27:25 Ngakho manini isibindi madoda. 
Acts27:26 Kodwa kumele. 
Acts27:27 Kwathi sekufike ubusuku betshumi lane, sasindenda sizula olwandle lweAdriya, phakathi kobusuku, abomkhumbi bakhumbula ukuthi umhlabathi othile ususondela kibo;" 
Acts27:28 basebephosa intambo yokulinganisa bathola amafathome angamatshumi amabili; sebeqhubekile kancinyane baphosa intambo yokulinganisa futhi, bathola amafathome alitshumi lanhlanu;" 
Acts27:29 njalo sesaba ukuthi mhlawumbe singatshayeka emadwaleni, basebephosela ingwegwe ezine ngemva komkhumbi, bafisa ukuthi kuse." 
Acts27:30 Abomkhumbi sebezama ukubaleka emkhunjini, basebesehlisela olwandle umkolo," 
Acts27:31 uPawuli wathi enduneni yekhulu lakwabebutho: Uba laba bengahlali emkhunjini, lingesindiswe lina." 
Acts27:32 Abebutho basebequma amagoda omkolo. 
Acts27:33 Kwasekusithi sekuzakusa, uPawuli wa ba ncenga bonke ukuthi bathathe ukudla, esithi: Lamuhla kulusuku lwetshumi lane lilindile lihlezi lingadli, lingathathi lutho." 
Acts27:34 Ngakho ngiyalincenga ukuthi lithathe ukudla; ngoba lokhu ngokosindiso lwenu; ngoba kakuyikuwa komunye unwele lwekhanda lenu. 
Acts27:35 Kwathi esetshilo lezizinto, esethethe isinkwa, wabonga uNkulunkulu phambi kwabo bonke; wa si hlephula waqala ukudla." 
Acts27:36 Basebesima isibindi bonke njalo bona bathatha ukudla. 
Acts27:37 Njalo thina sonke esasisemkhunjini sasiyimiphefumulo engamakhulu amabili lamatshumi ayisikhombisa lesithupha. 
Acts27:38 Njalo sebesuthi ukudla baphungula umkhumbi, baphosela amabele olwandle." 
Acts27:39 Kwathi sekusile, kabalazanga ilizwe; kodwa babona itheku elithile lilokhumbi, abamisa ukuthi baqhubele umkhumbi kulo, uba kungenzeka." 
Acts27:40 Basebequma ingwegwe ba zi yekela olwandle. 
Acts27:41 Basebefika bengananzelele endaweni lapho ulwandle olwaluhlangana khona bawuqhubela umkhumbi esihlabathini; njalo isihloko somkhumbi sagxumekeka sahlala singanyikinyeki, kodwa ingemuva yomkhumbi yephulwa ngamandla amagagasi." 
Acts27:42 Labebutho babeqonde ukubulala izibotshwa, hlezi ezinye zibaleke ngokuntshezela khatshana." 
Acts27:43 Kodwa induna yekhulu, ifisa ukusindisa uPawuli, yabavimbela kunjongo yabo, yasilaya ukuthi labo abakwaziyo ukuntsheza baziphosele olwandle kuqala, baye emhlabathini;" 
Acts27:44 labaseleyo, abanye ngamapulanka, labanye ngezinye zezinto zomkhumbi. Ngokunjalo-ke kwenzeka ukuthi bonke bafike emhlabathini besindile." 
Acts28:1 Kwathi sebesindile, basebesizwa ukuthi." 
Acts28:2 Labalelolizwe; ngoba babasa umlilo, basemukela sonke, ngenxa yezulu elaseliqalisile, langenxa yomqando." 
Acts28:3 UPawuli wasetheza umnyaba wenkuni, wa zi beka emlilweni, kwaphuma inyoka ngenxa yokutshisa, yanamathela esandleni sakhe." 
Acts28:4 Kwathi abalelolizwe bebona isilo silenga esandleni sakhe. 
Acts28:5 Yena-ke wasithintithela emlilweni isilo, akaze aba lengozi." 
Acts28:6 Basebelindela ukuthi uzavuvuka lokuthi awele phansi ahle afe; kwathi sebelinde isikhathieside, basebebona ukuthi kakulalutho olubi olwenzakala kuye." 
Acts28:7 Kubomakhelwane baleyondawo kwakulamasimu esikhulu sesihlenge, uPubliyo ngebizo; owasemukela wasingenisa kuhle insuku ezintathu." 
Acts28:8 Kwasekusithi uyise kaPubliyo wayelele ebanjwe luqhuqho lesisu segazi; angena kuye uPawuli, wakhuleka." 
Acts28:9 Ngakho lokho sekwenzakele, beza labanye ababesesihlengeni ababelezifo basebesiliswa;" 
Acts28:10 abasidumisa langodumo olukhulu, njalo mhla sisukayo ngomkhumbi, ba s ethesa izinto ezidingekayo." 
Acts28:11 Kwathi emva kwenyanga ezintathu sasuka ngomkhumbi weAleksandriya, owawuhlezi ebusika esihlengeni, ulophawu oluthiwangoDiyosikuroyi." 
Acts28:12 Sasesifika eSirakhuse sahlala insuku ezintathu; 
Acts28:13 sasuka lapho sahamba ngokubhoda sayafika eRegiyuma, sekudlule usuku olulodwa kwafika umoya weningizimu, safika ePuthiyoli ngosuku lwesibili;" 
Acts28:14 lapho esafica khona abazalwane, sacelwa ukuhlala labo insuku eziyisikhombisa; ngokunjalo saya-ke eRoma." 
Acts28:15 Njalo besuka lapho abazalwane sebezwile izinto ngathi, beza ukusihlangabeza baze bafika eApiyi Foruma leNdlini zeZihambi eziNtathu; okwathi uPawuli ebabona, wabonga uNkulunkulu, wema isibindi." 
Acts28:16 Sathi sesifike eRoma, induna yekhulu yanikela izibotshwa enduneni yabalindi; kodwa uPawuli wavunyelwa ukuhlala yedwa, lowebutho omlindayo." 
Acts28:17 Kwasekusithi emva kwensuku ezintathu; 
Acts28:18 wona esengihlolile. 
Acts28:19 Kodwa amaJuda ala, ngacindezeleka ukulidlulisela kuKesari, kungeyisikho ukuthi ngilolutho olokumangalela isizwe sakithi." 
Acts28:20 Ngakho ngenxa yalesisizatho ngilibizele lapha ukuthi ngi li bone ngikhulume lani; ngoba ngenxa yethemba. 
Acts28:21 Basebesithi kuye: Thina kasemukelanga izincwadi ngawe ezivela eJudiya, futhi loba ngubani wabazalwane, esefikile, kabikanga kumbe akhulume lutho olubi ngawe." 
Acts28:22 Kodwa sifisa ukuzwa izinto ozinakanayo wena; ngoba mayelana lalobububhazuka. 
Acts28:23 Njalo kwathi sebemmisele usuku, abanengi beza kuye endlini yezihambi; owabachasisela." 
Acts28:24 Abanye basebekholwa izinto azitshoyo, kodwa abanye kabakholwanga." 
Acts28:25 Kwasekusithi bengezwanani bodwa basuka bahamba, uPawuli esekhulume ilizwi laba linye lokuthi: Wayekhulume kuhle uMoya oyiNgcwele ngoIsaya umprofethi kubobaba bethu," 
Acts28:26 esithi: Hamba uye kulesisizwe ubususithi: Ngokuzwa lizakuzwa, njalo kalisoze liqedisise; lokubona lizabona, njalo kalisoze libonisise;" 
Acts28:27 ngoba inhliziyo yalesisizwe seyaba buthundu, njalo bezwa kanzima ngendlebe, lamehlo abo bawacimezile; hlezi babone ngamehlo, njalo bezwe ngendlebe, futhi baqedisise ngenhliziyo, njalo baphenduke, besengibasilisa." 
Acts28:28 Ngakho kakwaziwe kini, ukuthi usindiso lukaNkulunkulu." 
Acts28:29 Njalo kwathi esetshilo lezizinto, amaJuda asuka, elokuphikisana okukhulu phakathi kwawo." 
Acts28:30 UPawuli wasehlala iminyaka emibili egcweleyo endlini yakhe uqobo ayeyiqatshile, wemukela bonke abangena kuye," 
Acts28:31 watshumayela umbuso kaNkulunkulu, njalo wafundisa ngeNkosi uJesu Kristu." 
Romans1:1 UPawuli, inceku kaJesu Kristu, ebizelwe ukubangumphostoli" 
Romans1:2 (alithembisa ngaphambili)," 
Romans1:3 mayelana leNdodana yakhe, eyavela," 
Romans1:4 eyabonakaliswa ukuba yiNdodana kaNkulunkulu ngamandla, ngokuvuka okwabafileyo, uJesu Kristu iNkosi yethu;" 
Romans1:5 esemukela ngaye umusa," 
Romans1:6 elikuzo lani, babiziweyo bakaJesu Kristu:" 
Romans1:7 Kibo bonke abaseRoma, abathandiweyo bakaNkulunkulu, ababizelwe ukubangabangcwele." 
Romans1:8 Kuqala-ke ngibonga uNkulunkulu wami ngoJesu Kristu ngani lonke. 
Romans1:9 Ngoba uNkulunkulu ungumfakazi wami, ukuthi kangiyekeli ukulikhumbula," 
Romans1:10 ngesikhathi sonke emikhulekweni yami ekucineni. 
Romans1:11 Ngoba ngilangatha ukulibona, ukuze ngiliphe," 
Romans1:12 okuyikuthi, siduduzeke ndawonye phakathi kwenu ngokholo olukomunye lomunye, olwenu kanye lolwami." 
Romans1:13 Kanti angithandi ukuthi kungaziwa kini, bazalwane, ukuthi ngazimisela kanengi ukuza kini laphakathi kwenu, lanjengaphakathi kwezinye izizwe." 
Romans1:14 Ngilomlandu kumaGriki, kwabahlakaniphileyo kanye lakwabangahlakaniphanga;" 
Romans1:15 ngokunjalo njengokukimi ngilungele ukutshumayela ivangeli lakini abaseRoma. 
Romans1:16 Ngoba kangilanhloni ngevangeli likaKristu. 
Romans1:17 Ngoba ukulunga kukaNkulunkulu. 
Romans1:18 Ngoba ulaka lukaNkulunkulu luyabonakaliswa luvela ezulwini phezu kwakho konke ukungakhonzi uNkulunkulu lokungalungi kwabantu abavimbela iqiniso ngokungalungi; 
Romans1:19 ngoba. 
Romans1:20 Ngoba okungabonwayo kwakhe, selokhu kwadatshulwa umhlaba;" 
Romans1:21 ngoba kuthe bemazi uNkulunkulu, kaba m dumisanga njengoNkulunkulu kaba m bonga, kodwa baba." 
Romans1:22 Bezitshaya abahlakaniphileyo baba yizithutha," 
Romans1:23 lenkazimulo kaNkulunkulu ongabhubhiyo bayiphendulela. 
Romans1:24 Ngalokho-ke uNkulunkulu wabanikela emanyaleni, enkanukweni zenhliziyo zabo;" 
Romans1:25 abaphendulela iqiniso likaNkulunkulu. 
Romans1:26 Ngenxa yalokho uNkulunkulu wabanikela; 
Romans1:27 langokunjalo labesilisa bayekela ukwenza kwemvelo kowesifazana, batsha ngokukhanukana kwabo, abesilisa labesilisa benza okulihlazo, bemukeliswa phakathi kwabo umvuzo ofanele ukuduha kwabo." 
Romans1:28 Njalo njengalokhu bengavumanga ukuba lolwazi ngoNkulunkulu; 
Romans1:29 begcwaliswe konke ukungalungi, ukuphinga, ububi," 
Romans1:30 abanyeyayo," 
Romans1:31 abangelangqondo, abephula izithembiso;" 
Romans1:32 abathi besazi umlayo wokulunga kaNkulunkulu. 
Romans2:1 Ngakho kawulakuzilandulela. 
Romans2:2 Njalo siyazi ukuthi ukwahlulela kukaNkulunkulu kungokweqiniso phezu kwalabo abenza izinto ezinjalo. 
Romans2:3 Njalo ucabanga lokho yini, O muntu owahlulela abenza izinto ezinjalo, lawe uzenza lezozinto, ukuthi wena uzaphepha ukwahlulela kukaNkulunkulu?" 
Romans2:4 Kumbe uyayeyisa yini inotho yomusa wakhe? 
Romans2:5 Kodwa ngobulukhuni bakho lenhliziyo yakho engaphendukiyo uzibekela ulaka," 
Romans2:6 ozavuza lowo lalowo ngokwemisebenzi yakhe; 
Romans2:7 impilo elaphakade lokungabhubhi; 
Romans2:8 kodwa intukuthelo lolaka," 
Romans2:9 usizi; 
Romans2:10 kodwa inkazimulo lokuthula kuye wonke owenza okuhle, kumJuda kuqala lakumGriki;" 
Romans2:11 ngoba kakukho ukubandlulula umuntu kuNkulunkulu. 
Romans2:12 Ngoba bonke abonileyo bengelamlayo, bazabhubha labo bengelamlayo;" 
Romans2:13 ngoba kakusibo abezwayo umlayo abalungileyo phambi kukaNkulunkulu. 
Romans2:14 Ngoba nxa abezizwe abangelawo umlayo besenza ngokwemvelo okungokomlayo, bona, bengelawo umlayo, bangumlayo wabo ngokwabo;" 
Romans2:15 ababonakalisa ukuthi umsebenzi womlayo ulotshiwe enhliziyweni zabo; isazela sabo siyafakaza laso, lemicabango yaboi ba sole omunye komunye kumbe njalo i ba vikele omunye komunye," 
Romans2:16 ngosuku uNkulunkulu azakwahlulela ngalo imfihlo zabantu. 
Romans2:17 Khangela wena ubizwa ngokuthiungumJuda," 
Romans2:18 usazi intando yakhe," 
Romans2:19 njalo uzithembile wena ukuthi ungumholi weziphofu, ukukhanya kwabasemnyameni," 
Romans2:20 umeluleki wezithutha, umfundisi wensane, ulesimo." 
Romans2:21 Ngakho wena ofundisa omunye, kawuzifundisi yini? Wena otshumayela ukuthi ungebi, uyeba yini?" 
Romans2:22 Wena othi ungafebi, uyafeba yini?" 
Romans2:23 Wena ozincoma ngomlayo, udumaza uNkulunkulu ngokweqa umlayo yini?" 
Romans2:24 Ngoba ibizo likaNkulunkulu liyahlanjazwa, njengoba kulotshiwe." 
Romans2:25 Ngoba isibili ukusoka kuyasiza, uba usenza umlayo; kodwa uba ungumeqi womlayo, ukusoka kwakho sekuyikungasoki." 
Romans2:26 Ngakho uba ukungasoki? 
Romans2:27 Lokungasoki ngemvelo, egcwalisa umlayo, kunge kugwebe yini?" 
Romans2:28 Ngoba kayisuye umJuda o nguyengokusobala, njalo kakusikho ukusoka okusobala enyameni;" 
Romans2:29 kodwa yena ungumJuda o nguyengasese. 
Romans3:1 Pho-ke yibuphi ubungcono bomJuda, kumbe luyini usizo lokusoka?" 
Romans3:2 Kukhulu ngendlela yonke; ngoba kuqala-ke ukuthi. 
Romans3:3 Ngoba kuyini uba abanye bengakholwanga? 
Romans3:4 Phinde. 
Romans3:5 Kodwa uba ukungalungi kwethu kubonakalisa ukulunga kukaNkulunkulu, sizakuthini? Kambe uNkulunkulu kalunganga yini owehlisela ulaka.)" 
Romans3:6 Phinde? 
Romans3:7 Ngoba uba iqiniso likaNkulunkulu landisile kakhulu? 
Romans3:8 Njalo kungenjengalokhu sigconwa, lanjengoba abanye bathi thina sithi: Kasenze izinto ezimbi ukuze kuvele okuhle? Abakulahlwa kwabo kuba ngokokulunga." 
Romans3:9 Pho-ke? Singcono yini," 
Romans3:10 njengokulotshiweyo ukuthi: Kakho olungileyo, kakho loyedwa;" 
Romans3:11 kakho oqedisisayo, kakho odinga uNkulunkulu;" 
Romans3:12 bonke baphambukile, kabasizi lutho bonkana; kakho owenza okuhle, kakho ngitsho loyedwa;" 
Romans3:13 umphimbo wabo ulingcwaba elivulekileyo; bakhohlisa ngenlimi zabo; 
Romans3:14 omlomo wabo ugcwele ukuqalekisa lokubaba; 
Romans3:15 inyawo zabo ziphangisela ukuchitha igazi; 
Romans3:16 incithakalo losizi kusendleleni zabo," 
Romans3:17 njalo indlela yokuthula kabayazanga; 
Romans3:18 ukwesaba uNkulunkulu kakukho phambi kwamehlo abo. 
Romans3:19 Njalo siyazi ukuthi konke okutshoyo umlayo, ukukhuluma kibo abangaphansi komlayo;" 
Romans3:20 ngoba. 
Romans3:21 Kodwa khathesi-ke sekubonakalisiwe ukulunga kukaNkulunkulu; 
Romans3:22 ngitsho ukulunga kukaNkulunkulu ngokholo lukaJesu Kristu kibo bonke laphezu kwabo bonke abakholwayo; 
Romans3:23 ngoba bonke bonile basilele enkazimulweni kaNkulunkulu," 
Romans3:24 balungisiswa ngesihle; 
Romans3:25 uNkulunkulu; 
Romans3:26 ukuze kube yisibonakaliso sokulunga kwakhe kulesisikhathi, ukuze abe ngolungileyo lokuthi uyamlungisisa ongowokholo lukaJesu." 
Romans3:27 Ngakho kungaphi ukuzincoma? Kuvalelwe phandle. Ngomthetho bani? Hatshi bo, kodwa ngomthetho wokholo." 
Romans3:28 Ngakho siphetha ngokuthi. 
Romans3:29 Kambe u nguNkulunkulu wamaJuda kuphela? Njalo kayisuye lowabezizwe yini? Yebo lowabezizwe; 
Romans3:30 lokhu uNkulunkulu emunye. 
Romans3:31 Ngakho siyawenza umlayo ube yize ngokholo yini? Phinde. 
Romans4:1 Pho-ke sizakuthi uAbrahama ubaba wethu wazuzani ngokwenyama? 
Romans4:2 Ngoba uba uAbrahama walungisiswa ngemisebenzi. 
Romans4:3 Ngoba umbhalo uthini? Uthi: Kodwa uAbrahama wakholwa kuNkulunkulu, kwasekubalelwa kuye ukuthi yikulunga." 
Romans4:4 Kodwa kulowo osebenzayo kabalelwa iholo. 
Romans4:5 Kodwa kulowo ongasebenziyo, kodwa ekholwa kuye olungisisa oweyisa uNkulunkulu, ukholo lwakhe." 
Romans4:6 Njengoba laye uDavida ekhuluma ngokubusiswa komuntu, uNkulunkulu ambalela ukulunga esithi:" 
Romans4:7 Babusisiwe abaziphambeko zabo zithethelelwe labazono zabo zisitshekelwe. 
Romans4:8 Ubusisiwe umuntu iNkosi engasoze yambalela isono. 
Romans4:9 Ngakho lokhukubusiswa kuphezu kokusoka? Ngoba sithi: Ukholo lwabalelwa kuAbrahama ukuthi luyikulunga. 
Romans4:10 Pho lwabalelwa njani? Lapho esekusokeni yini, kumbe ekungasokini? Kungekho ekusokeni, kodwa ekungasokini." 
Romans4:11 Wasesemukela isibonakaliso sokusoka; ukuze abe nguyise wabo bonke abakholwayo lanxa b engasokanga, ukuze ukulunga kubalelwe lakibo;" 
Romans4:12 loyise wokusoka kulabo abangeyisibo bokusoka kuphela, kodwa futhi abahamba ezinyathelweni zokholo lukababa wethu uAbrahama aye lalo engakasokwa." 
Romans4:13 Ngoba kasingomlayo isithembiso kuAbrahama kumbe kunzalo yakhe, ukuthi uzakuba yindlalifa yomhlaba, kodwa ngokulunga kokholo." 
Romans4:14 Ngoba uba labo abomlayo beyizindlalifa; 
Romans4:15 ngoba umlayo ubanga ulaka. 
Romans4:16 Ngakho ku ngokholo, ukuze kube ngokomusa," 
Romans4:17 (njengokulotshiweyo ukuthi: Ngikumisile ukuthi ube nguyise wezizwe ezinengi. 
Romans4:18 Owathi emelane lethemba wakholwa ngethemba, ukuze abe nguyise wezizwe ezinengi, njengalokho okwatshiwoyo ukuthi: Izakuba njalo inzalo yakho."

Romans4:22 Ngalokho-ke kwabalelwa kuye ukuthi yikulunga. 
Romans4:23 Kakubhalwanga-ke ngenxa yakhe yedwa, ukuthi kwabalelwa kuye;" 
Romans4:24 kodwa langenxa yethu, esizabalelwa khona," 
Romans4:25 owanikelwa ngenxa yeziphambeko zethu.

Romans5:15 Kodwa kungenjengesiphambeko, sinjalo lesipho somusa. Ngoba uba ngesiphambeko soyedwa abanengi bafa." 
Romans5:16 Futhi isipho kasinjengoyedwa owonayo; ngoba isigwebo sa singesisodwa ngasekulahlweni, kodwa isipho somusa ngeseziphambeko ezinengi ngasekulungisisweni." 
Romans5:17 Ngoba uba ngesiphambeko so muntuoyedwa ukufa kwabusa ngalowo oyedwa, ikakhulu bona abemukela ubunengi bomusa lobesipho sokulunga bazabusa empilweni ngalowo oyedwa, uJesu Kristu."

Romans6:2 Phinde?

Romans7:1 Kalazi yini, bazalwane (ngoba ngikhuluma lalabo abawaziyo umlayo), ukuthi umlayo ubusa umuntu selokhu esaphila?" 
Romans7:2 Ngoba umfazi owendileyo ubotshelwe ngomlayo endodeni ephilayo; kodwa uba indoda isifile, ukhululiwe emlayweni wendoda." 
Romans7:3 Ngakho uba indoda isaphila, uzathiwa yisifebe uba esiba ngowenye indoda; kodwa uba indoda isifile, ukhululekile emlayweni, ukuze angabi yisifebe uba esiba ngowenye indoda." 
Romans7:4 Ngakho, bazalwane bami, selenziwe lafa lani emlayweni." 
Romans7:5 Ngoba sathi sisenyameni, inkanuko zesono ezingomlayo zasebenza ezithweni zethu." 
Romans7:6 Kodwa khathesi-ke sesikhululiwe emthethweni, sifile mayelana lalokho esasibanjwe yikho, ukuze sikhonze ngobutsha bomoya, njalo kungeyisikho ngobudala bokulotshiweyo." 
Romans7:7 Pho-ke sizakuthini? Umthetho uyisono yini? Phinde. 
Romans7:8 Kodwa isono, sizuze." 
Romans7:9 Mina-ke ngake ngaphila ngaphandle komlayo, njalo ngafa mina;" 
Romans7:10 njalo umthetho ongowempilo, wona waficwa yimi ungowokufa;" 
Romans7:11 ngoba isono, sizuze ithuba ngomthetho." 
Romans7:12 Ngakho umthetho ungcwele, lomlayo ungcwele." 
Romans7:13 Ngakho okulungileyo kwaba yikufa kimi yini? Phinde! Kodwa isono, ukuze sibonakaliswe ukuthi siyisono, sisebenza ukufa kimi ngokulungileyo; ukuze isono ngomthetho sibe yikonakala okukhulu kakhulu." 
Romans7:14 Ngoba siyazi ukuthi umthetho ungowomoya. 
Romans7:15 Ngoba lokhu engikwenzayo, angivumelani lakho; ngoba kakusikho engikuthandayo, lokho engikwenzayo; kodwa lokho engikuzondayo, yikho engikwenzayo." 
Romans7:16 Uba ngisenza lokho engingakuthandiyo, ngiyawuvumela umthetho ukuthi ulungile." 
Romans7:17 Kodwa khathesi-ke kakuseyimi engikwenzayo, kodwa yisono esihlala kimi." 
Romans7:18 Ngoba ngiyazi ukuthi kimi, lokhu kuyikuthi enyameni yami, kakuhlali okuhle." 
Romans7:19 Ngoba okuhle engikuthandayo, kangikwenzi; kodwa okubi engingakuthandiyo, yikho engikwenzayo." 
Romans7:20 Kodwa uba ngisenza lokho mina engingakuthandiyo, kakuseyimi engikwenzayo, kodwa yisono esihlala kimi." 
Romans7:21 Ngakho ngithola umthetho wokuthi lapho ngithanda ukwenza okuhle, okubi kukhona kimi." 
Romans7:22 Ngoba ngiyathokoza emthethweni kaNkulunkulu; 
Romans7:23 kodwa ngibona ezithweni zami. 
Romans7:24 Mina muntu olusizi! Ngubani ozangikhulula kulumzimba walokhukufa?

Romans10:3 ngoba bengakwazi ukulunga kukaNkulunkulu.

Romans10:5 Ngoba uMozisi ubhala ngo kulunga okungokomlayo, ukuthi umuntu owenza lezizinto uzaphila ngazo." 
Romans10:6 Kodwa ukulunga okungokholo kukhuluma kanje? Lokhu kuyikuthi ukumehlisa uKristu; 
Romans10:7 kumbe ukuthi: Ngubani ozakwehlela ekujuleni? Lokhu kuyikuthi ukumkhuphula uKristu kwabafileyo. 
Romans10:8 Kodwa kuthini? Ilizwi liseduze lawe, emlonyeni wakho lenhliziyweni yakho; leli yilizwi lokholo esilitshumayelayo;" 
Romans10:9 ukuthi uba uvuma ngomlomo wakho iNkosi uJesu; 
Romans10:10 ngoba ngenhliziyo omunyeuyakholwa kube yikulunga, langomlomo uyavuma kube lusindiso."

Romans10:12 Ngoba kakukho umehluko phakathi komJuda lomGriki. 
Romans10:13 Ngoba wonke loba ngubani. 
Romans10:14 Ngakho bazayibiza njani abangakholwanga kuyo? Futhi bazakholwa njani kuyo abangezwanga ngayo? Futhi bazakuzwa njani bengelamtshumayeli? 
Romans10:15 Njalo bazatshumayela njani uba bengathunywanga! 
Romans10:16 Kodwa kabalilalelanga bonke ivangeli? 
Romans10:17 Ngakho ukholo luvela ekuzweni. 
Romans10:18 Kodwa ngithi: Kabezwanga yini? Yebo sibili. 
Romans10:19 Kodwa ngithi: UIsrayeli kaqedisisanga yini? Kuqala uMozisi uthi: Mina ngizalivusela umona nga boaba ngesiso isizwe. 
Romans10:20 LoIsaya ulesibindi uthi: Ngaficwa yilabo abangangidinganga, ngabonakala kibo abangabuzanga ngami." 
Romans10:21 Kodwa kuIsrayeli uthi: Usuku lonke ngelulela izandla zami kubantu abangalaleliyo labalenkani. 
Romans11:1 Ngakho ngithi: UNkulunkulu ubalahlile yini abantu bakhe. 
Romans11:2 UNkulunkulu kabalahlanga abantu bakhe, esithi:" 
Romans11:3 Nkosi, babulele abaprofethi bakho, badilizile amalathi akho; mina-ke ngisele ngedwa, sebedinga umphefumulo wami." 
Romans11:4 Kodwa impendulo kaNkulunkulu yathini kuye? Yathi: Ngizitshiyele amadoda azinkulungwane eziyisikhombisa, angaguqanga ngedolo kuBhali." 
Romans11:5 Kunjalo-ke kukhona langalesisikhathi insali ngokukhetha komusa. 
Romans11:6 Kodwa uba kungomusa, kakusayi ngemisebenzi; uba kungenjalo umusa kawuseyiwo umusa. Kodwa aluba kusiya ngemisebenzi, akusengumusa; uba kungenjalo umsebenzi kawusengumsebenzi." 
Romans11:7 Pho-ke? Lokhu uIsrayeli ayekudinga, lokho kakutholanga, kodwa abakhethiweyo bakuthola, labanye benziwa baba lukhuni;" 
Romans11:8 njengokulotshiweyo ukuthi: UNkulunkulu wabanika umoya wobuthongo obukhulu. 
Romans11:9 LoDavida uthi: Itafula labo libe ngumjibila lesifu, lesikhubekiso, lempindiselo kibo;" 
Romans11:10 amehlo abo kafiphazwe ukuze bangaboni, njalo ugobise umhlana wabo njalonjalo." 
Romans11:11 Ngakho ngithi: Bakhubeka ukuze bawe yini? Phinde. 
Romans11:12 Kodwa uba isiphambeko sabo siyinotho yomhlaba, lokwehluleka kwabo kuyinotho yabezizwe, kakhulu kangakanani ukugcwala kwabo?" 
Romans11:13 Ngoba ngikhuluma lani bezizwe, njengalokho mina ngingumphostoli wabezizwe; ngikhulisa inkonzo yami;" 
Romans11:14 ukuthi mhlawumbe ngibavusele umona abe nyama yami. 
Romans11:15 Ngoba uba ukulahlwa kwabo kuyikubuyiswa komhlaba, ku nga ba yini ukwemukelwa, ngaphandle kokuthi kuyimpilo kwabafileyo?" 
Romans11:16 Njalo uba izithelo zokuqala zingcwele. 
Romans11:17 Kodwa uba kwephulwe ezinye ingatsha," 
Romans11:18 ungazincomi phezu kwengatsha; kodwa uba uzincoma phezu kwazo, kayisuwe othwele impande, kodwa impande wena." 
Romans11:19 Uzakuthi-ke: Ingatsha zephulwa, ukuze mina ngixhunyelwe." 
Romans11:20 Kulungile; zephulwa ngokungakholwa, wena-ke umi ngokholo;" 
Romans11:21 ngoba uba uNkulunkulu engayekelanga ingatsha zemvelo, hlezi lawe kayikukuyekela." 
Romans11:22 Khangela-ke ububele lobukhali bukaNkulunkulu; ubukhali, kulabo abawayo; kodwa kuwe, ububele, uba uhlala ebubeleni." 
Romans11:23 Lalabo futhi, uba bengahlali ekungakholweni, bazaxhunyelwa, ngoba uNkulunkulu ulamandla okubuya abaxhume." 
Romans11:24 Ngoba uba wena waqunywa emhlwathini weganga ngemvelo, wasuxhunyelelwa ngokuphambene lemvelo emhlwathini ohlanyelweyo, kakhulu kangakanani labo, aba zingatshangemvelo, bazaxhunyelelwa esihlahleni sakibo somhlwathi?" 
Romans11:25 Ngoba ngithanda ukuthi lingabi ngabangaziyo, bazalwane, ngalimfihlo;" 
Romans11:26 ngokunjalo-ke uIsrayeli wonke uzasindiswa; 
Romans11:27 njalo yilesi isivumelwano sami kibo, lapho ngizasusa izono zabo." 
Romans11:28 Ngokwevangeli bayizitha ngenxa yenu; kodwa ngokukhetha bangabathandiweyo ngenxa yabobaba; 
Romans11:29 ngoba izipho zomusa lokubiza kukaNkulunkulu. 
Romans11:30 Ngoba njengalokhu lani kade lingamlaleli uNkulunkulu, kodwa khathesi selihawukelwe ngenxa yokungalaleli kwabo;" 
Romans11:31 ngokunjalo lalabo khathesi kabalalelanga, ukuze ngesihawu senu bahawukelwe labo;" 
Romans11:32 ngoba uNkulunkulu ubavalele bonke ekungalalelini, ukuze abe lesihawu kibo bonke." 
Romans11:33 Yeka ukujula kwenotho! 
Romans11:34 Ngoba ngubani owazi ingqondo yeNkosi? Kumbe ngubani owaba ngumeluleki wayo? 
Romans11:35 Kumbe ngubani owamnika kuqala, njalo kubuyiselwe kuye?" 
Romans11:36 Ngoba konke kuvela kuye. 
Romans12:1 Ngakho, bazalwane, ngiyalincenga ukuthi, ngezihawu zikaNkulunkulu." 
Romans12:2 Njalo lingalingisi. 
Romans12:3 Ngoba ngomusa engiwuphiweyo. 
Romans12:4 Ngoba njengoba silezitho ezinengi emzimbeni munye, kodwa izitho zonke kazilamsebenzi ofananayo;" 
Romans12:5 kunjalo thina esibanengi. 
Romans12:6 Njalo silezipho ezehlukeneyo, asiprofethengokwesilinganiso sokholo;" 
Romans12:7 kumbe yikukhonza; 
Romans12:8 kumbe olayayo. 
Romans12:9 Uthando. 
Romans12:10 Thandanani kakhulu ngothando lobuzalwane; ekuhloniphaneni phathani abanye ngcono kulani; 
Romans12:11 lingabi ngamavila; 
Romans12:12 lithokoza ethembeni; libekezela ekuhluphekeni; 
Romans12:13 yabelani kunswelo zabangcwele. 
Romans12:14 Babusiseni abalizingelayo; busisani, lingaqalekisi." 
Romans12:15 Thokozani labathokozayo. 
Romans12:16 Kalibe lenhliziyonye komunye lomunye. 
Romans12:17 Lingaphindiseli muntu okubi ngokubi. 
Romans12:18 Uba kungenzeka, ng okukini."

Romans12:21 Unganqotshwa ngokubi, kodwa nqoba okubi ngokuhle." 
Romans13:1 Wonke umphefumulo. 
Romans13:2 Ngakho omelana lamandla, umelana lesimiso sikaNkulunkulu." 
Romans13:3 Ngoba ababusi kabesabeki emisebenzini emihle; 
Romans13:4 ngoba uyinceku kaNkulunkulu ukuze kube kuhle kuwe. Kodwa nxa usenza okubi, yesaba; ngoba inkemba kayiphatheli ize. Ngoba uyinceku kaNkulunkulu, ungumphindiseli wolaka kulowo owenza okubi."

Romans13:7 Ngakho phanini bonke okufaneleyo.

Romans14:2 Omunye ukholwa ukuthi angadla konke. 
Romans14:3 Lowo odlayo kangamdeleli ongadliyo. 
Romans14:4 Ungubani wena ogweba? Enkosini yayo iyema kumbe iwe. Yebo, izamiswa; ngoba uNkulunkulu ulamandla okuyimisa."

Romans14:8 Ngoba uba siphila, siphilela iNkosi; uba-ke sisifa, sifela iNkosi; ngakho loba siphila, loba sisifa, singabeNkosi."

Romans14:10 Wena-ke umgwebelani umzalwane wakho.

Romans14:13 Ngakho kasingabe sisahlulelana.

Romans14:15 Kodwa uba umzalwane wakho ekhutshwa yikudla, kawusahambi ngokothando. Ungambhubhisi ngokudla kwakho lowo, amfelayo uKristu." 
Romans14:16 Ngakho okuhle kini kakungahlanjazwa; 
Romans14:17 ngoba umbuso kaNkulunkulu kawusikho ukudla lokunatha, kodwa ukulunga lokuthula lentokozo kuMoya oNgcwele."

Romans14:21 Kuhle ukungadli inyama, lokunganathi iwayini, lokunye umzalwane wakho akhubeka ngakho kumbe acunulwe kumbe abebuthakathaka."

Romans15:4 Ngoba konke okwabhalwa ngaphambili.

Romans15:6 ukuze nganhliziyonye.

Romans15:12 Njalo futhi uIsaya uthi: Kuzakuba khona impande kaJese, lophakamela ukubusa abezizwe; abezizwe bazathembela kuye." 
Romans15:13 Kungathi-ke uNkulunkulu wethemba angaligcwalisa ngentokozo yonke langokuthula ekukholweni, ukuze lengezwe ethembeni, ngamandla kaMoya oNgcwele."

Romans15:15 Kodwa, bazalwane, ngilibhalele ngesibindi esikhulu, nganxanye," 
Romans15:16 ukuze ngibe yisikhonzi sikaJesu Kristu kwabezizwe, ngikhonze ivangeli likaNkulunkulu."

Romans15:18 ngoba kangiyikuba lesibindi sokukhuluma ulutho lwezinto uKristu angazenzanga ngami, ngelizwi langesenzo," 
Romans15:19 ngamandla ezibonakaliso lezimangaliso, ngamandla kaMoya kaNkulunkulu; ngakho kusukela eJerusalema le ndawoezizingelezeleyo kuze kufike eIliriku ngi tshumayeleivangeli likaKristu ngokupheleleyo;"

Romans15:21 kodwa, njengokulotshiweyo ukuthi: Abangatshelwanga ngaye, bazabona, labangezwanga, bazaqedisisa." 
Romans15:22 Ngenxa yalokho futhi ngavinjelwa kanengi ukuza kini; 
Romans15:23 kodwa khathesi-ke lokhu ngingaselandawo kulezizabelo," 
Romans15:24 ngokunjalo nxa ngizakuya eSpaniya, ngizakuza kini; ngoba ngithemba ukuthi ngizalibona ekudluleni, njalo ngiphelekezelwe yini khona." 
Romans15:25 Kodwa khathesi-ke ngiya eJerusalema, ngikhonze abangcwele." 
Romans15:26 Ngoba kwaba kuhle eMakedoniya. 
Romans15:27 Ngoba kwaba kuhle kibo, njalo balomlandu kibo. Ngoba uba abezizwe behlanganyela labo ezintweni zabo zomoya." 
Romans15:28 Ngakho nxa sengiqede lokhu, sengibaphawulele, ngizasuka ngiye eSpaniya ngidlule ngakini." 
Romans15:29 Ngiyazi-ke ukuthi nxa ngisiza kini. 
Romans15:30 Ngiyalincenga-ke, bazalwane, ngayo iNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu, langothando lukaMoya, ukuthi lilwise kanye lami emikhulekweni kuNkulunkulu ngami;" 
Romans15:31 ukuze ngophulwe kwabangakholwayo eJudiya; 
Romans15:32 ukuze ngentando kaNkulunkulu. 
Romans15:33 Ngakho uNkulunkulu wokuthula kabelani lonke. Ameni.

1Corinthians1:2 kubandla likaNkulunkulu eliseKorinte: 
1Corinthians1:3 Umusa kawubekini lokuthula okuvela kuNkulunkulu uBaba wethu leNkosini uJesu Kristu.

1Corinthians1:5 ukuthi kuyo yonke into linothisiwe kuye, ekukhulumeni konke," 
1Corinthians1:6 njengoba ubufakazi bukaKristu buqinisiwe kini;

1Corinthians1:8 ozaliqinisa.

1Corinthians1:10 Ngiyalincenga-ke emqondweni munye lekuboneni kunye. 
1Corinthians1:11 Ngoba ngitsheliwe ngani, bazalwane bami, ngabakoKlowe phakathi kwenu." 
1Corinthians1:12 Njalo ngitsho lokhu, kokuthi ngulowo lalowo wenu; kodwa mina okaKristu." 
1Corinthians1:13 UKristu wehlukanisiwe yini yini ebizweni likaPawuli? 
1Corinthians1:14 Ngiyambonga uNkulunkulu ukuthi kangibhabhathizanga; 
1Corinthians1:15 ukuze kungabi khona othi ngabhabhathiza ebizweni lami uqobo. 
1Corinthians1:16 Futhi ngabhabhathiza lendlu kaStefana; ngaphandle kwalokho kangazi ukuthi ngabhabhathiza omunye umuntu. 
1Corinthians1:17 Ngoba uKristu kangithumanga ukuthi ngibhabhathize, kodwa ukuthi ngitshumayele ivangeli; kungeyisikho ngenhlakanipho yelizwi."

1Corinthians1:19 Ngoba kulotshiwe ukuthi: Ngizachitha. 
1Corinthians1:20 Singaphi isihlakaniphi? Ungaphi? 
1Corinthians1:21 Ngoba kuthe bentshumayelo ukusindisa abakholwayo.

1Corinthians1:25 ngoba ubuthutha bukaNkulunkulu buhlakaniphile kulabantu, lobuthakathaka bukaNkulunkulu bulamandla kulabantu." 
1Corinthians1:26 Ngoba khangelani; 
1Corinthians1:27 kodwa uNkulunkulu ukhethile izinto zobuthutha zomhlaba, ukuze ayangise abahlakaniphileyo; njalo uNkulunkulu ukhethile okubuthakathaka komhlaba, ukuze ayangise okulamandla;" 
1Corinthians1:28 lezinto eziphansi zomhlaba lezinto ezidelelekayo uNkulunkulu uzikhethile, lezinto ezingekho;" 
1Corinthians1:29 ukuze kungabikho inyama ezincomayo phambi kwakhe.

1Corinthians7:1 Mayelana-ke lezinto elangibhalela ngazo, kuhle owesifazana." 
1Corinthians7:2 Kodwa ngenxa yokuphinga, ngulowo lalowo kumele abe lowakhe umfazi, njalo ngulowo lalowo mfaziabe leyakhe indoda." 
1Corinthians7:3 Indoda kayenanise kumfazi isifiso esihle esifaneleyo; langokunjalo lomfazi endodeni. 
1Corinthians7:4 Umfazi kalamandla phezu kowayo umzimba, kodwa umfazi." 
1Corinthians7:5 Lingagodlelani kwenu. 
1Corinthians7:6 Kodwa lokhu ngikutsho ngemvumo, kungeyisikho ngomlayo." 
1Corinthians7:7 Ngoba ngithanda. 
1Corinthians7:8 Kodwa kwabangendanga labafelokazi ngithi: Kuhle kibo uba behlala njengami. 
1Corinthians7:9 Kodwa uba bengelakuzithiba kabende; ngoba kungcono ukwenda kulokutsha. 
1Corinthians7:10 Kodwa kwabendileyo ngiyabalaya, kungeyisimi;" 
1Corinthians7:11 kodwa uba laye esehlukana, kahlale engendanga, kumbe abuyisane lendoda; lendoda kayingamlahli umfazi." 
1Corinthians7:12 Kodwa kwabanye kutsho mina. 
1Corinthians7:13 Lomfazi olendoda engakholwayo, njalo ivuma." 
1Corinthians7:14 Ngoba indoda engakholwayo yenziwa ibe ngcwele ngomfazi, lomfazi ongakholwayo wenziwa abe ngcwele ngendoda. Uba kungenjalo abantwana benu ngabangcolileyo." 
1Corinthians7:15 Uba-ke ongakholwayo ezehlukanisa, kazehlukanise; kwezinjalo umzalwane kumbe umzalwanekazi kabotshwanga; kodwa uNkulunkulu usibizele ekuthuleni." 
1Corinthians7:16 Ngoba wazi ngani umfazi? 
1Corinthians7:17 Kuphela nje njengokuthi uNkulunkulu. 
1Corinthians7:18 Ukhona yini owabizwa esokile? Kangabi ngongasokwanga. Ukhona yini owabizwa engasokanga? Kangasokwa. 
1Corinthians7:19 Ukusoka kwemilayo kaNkulunkulu. 
1Corinthians7:20 Ngulowo lalowo kahlale kubizo abizwe kulo. 
1Corinthians7:21 Wabizwa uyisigqili yini? Ungakhathazeki ngakho. Kodwa uba lawe ungakhululeka, kungcono ukusebenzise." 
1Corinthians7:22 Ngoba lo obizwa eNkosini eyisigqili ungokhululekileyo weNkosi. 
1Corinthians7:23 Lathengwa ngentengo. 
1Corinthians7:24 Ngulowo lalowo abizelwe kukho, bazalwane, kahlale kukho loNkulunkulu." 
1Corinthians7:25 Kodwa mayelana lentombi kangilawo umlayo weNkosi. 
1Corinthians7:26 Ngakho ngikhumbula ukuthi lokhu kuhle ngenxa yenkathazo ezikhona emuntwini ukubanje. 
1Corinthians7:27 Ubotshelwe emfazini yini? Ungadingi ukukhululwa. Ukhululwe emfazini yini? Ungadingi umfazi. 
1Corinthians7:28 Kodwa. 
1Corinthians7:29 Kodwa ngitsho lokhu, bazalwane, ukuthi isikhathi sifitshane; kusukela khathesi labalabafazi kababe njengabangelabo;" 
1Corinthians7:30 labakhalayo, njenga ba ngakhaliyo; labathokozayo, njenga ba ngathokoziyo; labathengayo, njenga ba ngelalutho;" 
1Corinthians7:31 labasebenzisa lumhlaba, njenga ba nga wu sebenzisisiyo." 
1Corinthians7:32 Kodwa ngithanda; 
1Corinthians7:33 kodwa othetheyo ukhathalela izinto zomhlaba, ukuthi uzamthokozisa njani umfazi." 
1Corinthians7:34 Wehlukene okweNkosi, ukuze abe ngcwele emzimbeni kanye lemoyeni; kodwa othethweyo ukhathalela okomhlaba, ukuthi uzayithokozisa njani indoda." 
1Corinthians7:35 Lalokhu ngikutsho ukuthi kube ngolwenu usizo; kungesikuthi ngiliphosele umchilo wokulikhina, kodwa ukuze lihambe ngokufaneleyo lokubambelela eNkosini kungelakuphazamiseka." 
1Corinthians7:36 Kodwa uba umuntu ebona ukuthi uziphatha ngokungafanelanga entombini yakhe, yona isikhulile, futhi kumele kwenzeke kanje, kenze akufunayo; koni; kabatshade." 
1Corinthians7:37 Kodwa omiyo enhliziyweni yakhe, engacindezelwa lutho, futhi elamandla ngesakhe isifiso, esekumisile lokhu enhliziyweni yakhe ukuthi uzagcina eyakhe intombi, wenza kuhle;" 
1Corinthians7:38 ngakho lowo owendisayo wenza kuhle; kodwa ongendisiyo wenza ngcono. 
1Corinthians7:39 Umfazi. 
1Corinthians7:40 Kodwa uyathaba kakhulu uba ehlala enjalo, ngokubona kwami." 
1Corinthians8:1 Mayelana-ke lezinto ezihlatshelwe. 
1Corinthians8:2 Uba-ke umuntu esithi uyazi ulutho, kakazi lutho njengoba kufanele ukuthi azi;" 
1Corinthians8:3 kodwa uba umuntu ethanda uNkulunkulu, yena uyaziwa nguye." 
1Corinthians8:4 Ngakho mayelana lokudla izinto omunye unkulunkulu ngaphandle koyedwa; 
1Corinthians8:5 ngoba lanxa kukhona okuthiwa ngonkulunkulu, loba kusezulwini loba kusemhlabeni (njengoba kukhona onkulunkulu abanengi, lamakhosi amanengi),"

1Corinthians8:8 Kodwa ukudla kakusisondezi kuNkulunkulu; ngoba kungesikuthi nxa sisidla, silenzuzo; njalo kungesikuthi nxa singadli, silokulahlekelwa." 
1Corinthians8:9 Qaphelani-ke.

1Corinthians9:1 Kangisuye umphostoli yini? 
1Corinthians9:2 Uba ngingesuye umphostoli kwabanye, kodwa nging uyesibili kini; ngoba lina liluphawu eNkosini."

1Corinthians9:17 Ngoba uba ngisenza lokhu ngokuzithandela, ngilomvuzo bunikelwe kimi."

1Corinthians9:25 Labo bonke abancintisanayo.

1Corinthians9:27 kodwa ngiyawudinda umzimba wami mina uqobo.

1Corinthians11:5 Kodwa wonke owesifazana okhuleka kumbe aprofethe. 
1Corinthians11:6 Ngoba uba owesifazana engagubuzeli, futhi kagele; kodwa uba kukubi kowesifazana ukugela kumbe ukuphucwa, kagutshuzelwe."

1Corinthians11:11 Kodwa indoda.

1Corinthians11:13 Ziboneleni lina; kufanele yini ukuthi owesifazana akhuleke kuNkulunkulu engambombozanga? 
1Corinthians11:14 Imvelo uqobo lwayo kayilifundisi yini, ukuthi uba indoda ilenwele ezinde, kulihlazo kuyo?" 
1Corinthians11:15 Kodwa uba owesifazana elenwele ezinde, kuludumo kuye. Ngoba inwele uziphiwe ukuthi zibe yisimbombozo." 
1Corinthians11:16 Kodwa uba umuntu. 
1Corinthians11:17 Kodwa ngokulaya lokhu kangi li babazi, ngoba libuthana ngokungekuhle kodwa ngokubi." 
1Corinthians11:18 Okokuqala ngoba nxa libuthana ebandleni, ngizwa ukuthi kukhona ukwehlukana phakathi kwenu; njalo nganxanye ngiyakukholwa." 
1Corinthians11:19 Ngoba kufanele phakathi kwenu. 
1Corinthians11:20 Ngakho nxa libuthana ndawonye, lokhukakusikho ukudla isidlo seNkosi;" 
1Corinthians11:21 ngoba ngulowo lalowo uthatha kuqala esakhe isidlo ekudleni. 
1Corinthians11:22 Kanti kalilazo izindlu zokudlela lezokunathela? Kumbe lidelela ibandla likaNkulunkulu yini abangelakho? Ngingathini kini? Ngingalibabaza kulokhu yini? Kangi li babazi.

1Corinthians11:24 isibongile ya si hlephuna.

1Corinthians11:27 Ngakho loba ngubani.

1Corinthians11:29 ngoba odlayo anathe ngokungafanelanga, uzidlela azinathele isigwebo, engawehlukanisi umzimba weNkosi." 
1Corinthians11:30 Ngenxa yalokhu banengi kini ababuthakathaka labagulayo.

1Corinthians14:4 Okhuluma ngendimi uyazakha yena, kodwa oprofethayo." 
1Corinthians14:5 Njalo ngiyathanda ukuthi lonke likhulume ngendimi, ukuze ibandla lemukele ukwakhiwa." 
1Corinthians14:6 Khathesi-ke, bazalwane, uba ngifika kini ngikhuluma ngendimi, ngizalisiza ngani, nxa ngingakhulumi kini kumbe ekwembulelweni?" 
1Corinthians14:7 Ngokunjalo izinto ezingelampilo ezikhalayo, loba umhlanga, loba ichacho, uba zinganiki umehluko ngokukhala, kuzakwaziwa njani okuvuthelwayo ngomhlanga kumbe okutshaywayo ngomqangala?" 
1Corinthians14:8 Ngoba-ke nxa uphondo? 
1Corinthians14:9 Kunjalo lani, uba linganiki inkulumo ecacileyo ngolimi, kuzakwaziwa njani okukhulunywayo? Ngoba lizakuba likhuluma emoyeni." 
1Corinthians14:10 Kukhona, nxa kungenzakala emhlabeni kodwa kawukho ongatsho lutho;" 
1Corinthians14:11 ngakho uba ngingawazi umqondo welizwi, ngizakuba ngowezizweni kulowo okhulumayo, lalowo okhulumayo uzakubangowezizweni kimi." 
1Corinthians14:12 Kunjalo lani, lokhu litshisekela iziphozomoya, dingani ukuthi livame ekwakhiweni kwebandla." 
1Corinthians14:13 Ngakho-ke okhulumayo ngendimi. 
1Corinthians14:14 Ngoba uba ngikhuleka ngendimi, umoya wami uyakhuleka, kodwa ingqondo yami kayilasithelo." 
1Corinthians14:15 Ngakho kuyini? Ngizakhuleka ngomoya, njalo ngizakhuleka langengqondo; ngizahlabelela indumiso." 
1Corinthians14:16 Uba kungenjalo, nxa ubonga ngomoya, lokhu engakwazi okutshoyo?" 
1Corinthians14:17 Ngoba isibili wena ubonga kuhle, kodwa omunye kakhiwa." 
1Corinthians14:18 Ngiyambonga uNkulunkulu wami ukuthi ngikhuluma ngendimi kakhulu kulani lonke; 
1Corinthians14:19 kodwa ebandleni ngithanda ukukhuluma amazwi amahlanu ngengqondo yami, ukuze ngifundise labanye, kulamazwi ayizinkulungwane ezilitshumi ngendimi." 
1Corinthians14:20 Bazalwane, lingabi ngabantwana engqondweni, lekunakaneni libe ngabakhulileyo." 
1Corinthians14:21 Emlayweni langezinye indebe ngizakhuluma lalesisizwe, langokunjalo labo kabayikungizwa, itsho iNkosi." 
1Corinthians14:22 Ngakho indimi zingezesibonakaliso, kungeyisikho kwabakholwayo, kodwa kwabangakholwayo; kanti isiprofetho, kungayi sisosabangakholwayo, kodwa sabakholwayo." 
1Corinthians14:23 Ngakho uba ibandla lonke libuthene ndawonye, labo bonke bakhulume ngendimi, besekungena abangafundanga?"

1Corinthians14:25 langokunjalo izinto ezifihliweyo zenhliziyo yakhe ziyadalulwa; ngokunjalo uzakuwa ngobuso. 
1Corinthians14:26 Ngakho kuyini, bazalwane? Loba nini libuthana, ngulowo lalowo wenu elesihlabelelo." 
1Corinthians14:27 Uba umuntu ekhuluma ngendimi, kakubengababili, kumbe bangadluli kwabathathu, njalo ba dedelane, lomunye kumele atolike;" 
1Corinthians14:28 kodwa uba kungekho umtoliki, kumele athule ebandleni; akhulume kuye ngokwakhe lakuNkulunkulu." 
1Corinthians14:29 Abaprofethi-ke. 
1Corinthians14:30 Kodwa uba kusembulwa komunye ohleziyo, kathule owokuqala." 
1Corinthians14:31 Ngoba lonke lingaprofetha; 
1Corinthians14:32 lemimoya yabaprofethi iyathotshiselwa abaprofethi. 
1Corinthians14:33 Ngoba uNkulunkulu kayisuye owesiphithiphithi, kodwa ngowokuthula, njengemabandleni wonke abangcwele." 
1Corinthians14:34 Abesifazana usitsho. 
1Corinthians14:35 Uba-ke bethanda ukufunda ulutho, kababuze kubomkabo ekhaya; ngoba kulihlazo kowesifazana ukukhuluma ebandleni."

1Corinthians15:1 Ngakho, bazalwane, ngilazisa ivangeli," 
1Corinthians15:2 njalo elisindiswa ngalo. 
1Corinthians15:3 Ngoba ngalinika; 
1Corinthians15:4 lokuthi wangcwatshwa; lokuthi wavuswa kwabafileyo ngosuku lwesithathu; 
1Corinthians15:5 lokuthi wabonakala; 
1Corinthians15:6 emva kwalokho wabonakala ngesikhathi sinye kubazalwane abedlula amakhulu amahlanu; 
1Corinthians15:7 emva kwalokho wabonakala kuJakobe; 
1Corinthians15:8 lekucineni njengozelwe ngesikhathi esingaqondanga. 
1Corinthians15:9 Ngoba mina ngingomncinyane ibandla likaNkulunkulu. 
1Corinthians15:10 Kodwa ngomusa, kodwa ngumusa kaNkulunkulu olami." 
1Corinthians15:11 Ngakho loba kuyi mi, loba kuyi bo, ngokunjalo siyatshumayela langokunjalo lakholwa." 
1Corinthians15:12 Kodwa uba uKristu etshunyayelwa ukuthi uvusiwe kwabafileyo, batsho njani abanye phakathi kwenu ukuthi kakukho ukuvuka okwabafileyo?" 
1Corinthians15:13 Kodwa uba kungekho ukuvuka okwabafileyo, kavuswanga laye uKristu;" 
1Corinthians15:14 uba-ke uKristu engavuswanga, ngakho ukutshumayela kwethu kuyize, lokholo lwenu lalo luyize," 
1Corinthians15:15 lathi futhi sificwa singabafakazi bamanga bakaNkulunkulu, ngoba safakaza ngoNkulunkulu ukuthi wamvusa uKristu, angamvusanga, uba-ke abafileyo bengavuswa." 
1Corinthians15:16 Ngoba uba abafileyo bengavuswa, kavuswanga laye uKristu;" 
1Corinthians15:17 njalo uba uKristu engavuswanga, ukholo lwenu luyize; lisesezonweni zenu." 
1Corinthians15:18 Ngakho lalabo abalele bekuKristu sebabhubha. 
1Corinthians15:19 Uba singabathembela kuKristu kule impilo kuphela, singabalosizi kulabo bonke abantu." 
1Corinthians15:20 Kodwa khathesi-ke uKristu uvusiwe kwabafileyo. 
1Corinthians15:21 Ngoba lokhu ngomuntu ukufa kweza. 
1Corinthians15:22 Ngoba njengalokhu kuAdamu bonke bayafa, ngokunjalo futhi kuKristu bonke bazakwenziwa baphile." 
1Corinthians15:23 Kodwa ngulowo lalowo ngesakhe isigaba; isithelo sokuqala uKristu," 
1Corinthians15:24 besekusiba yikuphela, lapho esenikela umbuso." 
1Corinthians15:25 Ngoba umele yena ukubusa, aze abeke zonke izitha zakhe ngaphansi kwenyawo zakhe." 
1Corinthians15:26 Isitha sokucina esizachithwa yikufa. 
1Corinthians15:27 Ngoba izinto zonke uzehlisele ngaphansi kwenyawo zakhe izinto zonke zehlisiwe, kusobala ukuthi ungaphandle kwazo ozehlisileyo izinto zonke ngaphansi kwakhe." 
1Corinthians15:28 Nxa izinto zonke sezehlisiwe ngaphansi kwakhe ngokwayo izazehlisa ngaphansi kwalowo owehlisela zonke izinto ngaphansi kwayo, ukuze uNkulunkulu abe yikho konke kukho konke." 
1Corinthians15:29 Pho, bazakwenzani ababhabhathizelwa abafileyo? Babhabhathizelwa labo abafileyo njani?" 
1Corinthians15:30 Kungani lathi sisengozini ihola ngehola? 
1Corinthians15:31 Ngiyafa, ngiyaqinisa ngokuzincoma ngani engilakho kuKristu Jesu iNkosi yethu." 
1Corinthians15:32 Uba ngokwabantu ngalwa, ngoba kusasa siyafa." 
1Corinthians15:33 Lingakhohliswa kuyonakalisa izimilo ezinhle. 
1Corinthians15:34 Vusani ingqondo ngokulunga. 
1Corinthians15:35 Kodwa omunye uzakuthi: Abafileyo bavuswa njani? Njalo beza lomzimba onjani? 
1Corinthians15:36 Siphukuphuku wena, kakwenziwa kuphile ngaphandle kokuthi kufe;" 
1Corinthians15:37 lalokho okuhlanyelayo, kawuhlanyeli umzimba ozakuba khona, kodwa uhlamvu oluze, mhlawumbe, olwebele kumbe olokunye nje;" 
1Corinthians15:38 kodwa uNkulunkulu uyinika umzimba njengokuthanda kwakhe, lakuleyo laleyo yenhlanyelo owayo umzimba." 
1Corinthians15:39 Inyama yonke kayisinyamanye; kodwa enye yinyama yabantu, lenye yinyama yenyamazana, lenye eyenhlanzi, lenye eyezinyoni." 
1Corinthians15:40 Ikhonalemizimba yezulwini, lemizimba yemhlabeni; kodwa inkazimulo yezulu ingenye, leyemhlabeni ingenye." 
1Corinthians15:41 Enye yinkazimulo yelanga, lenye yinkazimulo yenyanga, lenye yinkazimulo yezinkanyezi; ngoba inkanyezi yehlukile kwenye inkanyezi enkazimulweni." 
1Corinthians15:42 Kunjalo-ke ukuvuka okwabafileyo; 
1Corinthians15:43 kuhlanyelwa ekudelweni; kuhlanyelwa ebuthakathakeni, kuvuswe emandleni;" 
1Corinthians15:44 kuhlanyelwa umzimba wemvelo, kuvuswe umzimba womoya. Kukhona umzimba wemvelo, njalo kukhona umzimba womoya." 
1Corinthians15:45 Langokunjalo kulotshiwe ukuthi: Umuntu wokuqala uAdamu waba ngumphefumulo ophilayo. 
1Corinthians15:46 Kodwa okokuqala kakusikho okomoya, kodwa okwemvelo, besekusiza okomoya." 
1Corinthians15:47 Umuntu wokuqala. 
1Corinthians15:48 Njengoba enjalo owomhlabathi; lanjengoba enjalo owezulwini, banjalo labo abezulwini;" 
1Corinthians15:49 futhi njengoba silesimo sowomhlabathi, lathi sizakuba lesimo sowezulwini." 
1Corinthians15:50 Kodwa ngitsho lokhu, bazalwane, ukuthi inyama legazi." 
1Corinthians15:51 Khangelani, ngilitshela imfihlo: Kasiyikulala sonke," 
1Corinthians15:52 ngesikhatshana, ngokucwayiza kwelihlo, ekukhaleni kophondo lokucina; ngoba uphondo luzakhala, labafileyo bazavuswa bengelakubola, lathi sizaphendulwa." 
1Corinthians15:53 Ngoba lokhu okubolayo kumele ukwembatha ukungaboli kwembathe ukungafi. 
1Corinthians15:54 Nxa-ke lokho okubolayo sekwembethe ukungaboli. 
1Corinthians15:55 Lungaphi, kufa, udonsi lwakho? Kungaphi, ngcwaba, ukunqoba kwakho?" 
1Corinthians15:56 Lodonsi lokufa yisono; lamandla esono ngumlayo. 
1Corinthians15:57 Kodwa kabongwe ngeNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu.

2Corinthians1:3 Kabongwe, ngitsho uYise weNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu, uYise wobubele loNkulunkulu wenduduzo yonke,"

2Corinthians1:5 ngoba njengalokhu inhlupheko zikaKristu zengezelelekile kithi, ngokunjalo lenduduzo yethu yengezelelekile ngoKristu." 
2Corinthians1:6 Njalo loba sihlutshwa, ku ngokwenduduzo ekubekezeleni kulezizinhlupheko ezifananayo esihlupheka ngazo lathi; loba siduduzwa, ku ngokwenduduzo losindiso lwenu;" 
2Corinthians1:7 njalo ithemba lethu ngani liqinile, sisazi ukuthi njengalokhu lihlanganyela ezinhluphekweni." 
2Corinthians1:8 Ngoba kasithandi lelempilo. 
2Corinthians1:9 Kodwa thina ngokwethu sasilaso kithi isigwebo sokufa; 
2Corinthians1:10 owasophula ekufeni okungaka, losophulayo; esithemba kuye ukuthi uza s ophula futhi." 
2Corinthians1:11 Lani lisebenzela thina ndawonye ngomkhuleko. 
2Corinthians1:12 Ngoba ukuzincoma kwethu yilokhu, ubufakazi besazela sethu kodwa emuseni kaNkulunkulu, saziphatha emhlabeni, njalo ngokukhethekileyo maqondana lani." 
2Corinthians1:13 Ngoba kasilibhaleli okunye, kodwa loba izinto elizifundayo kumbe njalo lizivume; ngithemba futhi ukuthi liza zi vuma kuze kube sekupheleni;"

2Corinthians1:17 Ngakho ngiqonde lokho, besengisebenzisa yini ubulula? Kumbe izinto engizimisayo, ngimisa ngokwenyama yini, ukuze kube khona kimi uyebo, yebo; lohatshi, hatshi?"

2Corinthians7:1 Lokhu silalezizithembiso, siphelelise ubungcwele ekwesabeni uNkulunkulu." 
2Corinthians7:2 Semukeleni. 
2Corinthians7:3 Kangikhulumeli uku li sola; ngoba ngatsho phambili, ukuthi lisenhliziyweni zethu ukuthi sife ndawonye siphile ndawonye." 
2Corinthians7:4 Sikhulu isibindi kakhulu intokozo kuyo yonke inhlupheko yethu. 
2Corinthians7:5 Ngoba lekufikeni kwethu eMakedoniya, ngaphakathi ukwesaba." 
2Corinthians7:6 Kodwa uNkulunkulu, oduduza abadanileyo, wasiduduza ekufikeni;" 
2Corinthians7:7 njalo kungeyisikho ekufikeni kwakhe kuphela, kodwa langenduduzo, ngaze ngathokoza kakhulu." 
2Corinthians7:8 Ngoba lanxa ngalidabukisa. 
2Corinthians7:9 Khathesi ngiyathokoza, kungeyisikho ukuthi ladatshulwa ngenxa yethu." 
2Corinthians7:10 Ngoba ukudabuka ngokukaNkulunkulu. 
2Corinthians7:11 Ngoba khangelani, leyo into, ukuthi ladatshulwa ngokukaNkulunkulu." 
2Corinthians7:12 Uba-ke lami ngalibhalela, kungeyisikho ngenxa yalowo owonayo, njalo kungeyisikho ngenxa yalowo owoniweyo kubonakaliswe kini phambi kukaNkulunkulu." 
2Corinthians7:13 Ngalokho siduduzekile ngokuvela kini lonke; 
2Corinthians7:14 ngoba uba ngazincomela kwaba liqiniso. 
2Corinthians7:15 Isihelo sakhe sesengezelelwe kakhulu kini, lapho ekhumbula ukulalela." 
2Corinthians7:16 Ngakho ngiyathokoza ukuthi ngiyalithemba kukho konke. 
2Corinthians8:1 Sesilazisa; 
2Corinthians8:2 ukuthi ekulingweni okukhulu kwenhlupho bengezelela enothweni yokuphana kwabo. 
2Corinthians8:3 Ngoba babekhululekile njengokwamandla abo, ngiyafakaza, langaphezu kwamandla abo," 
2Corinthians8:4 ngesicelo esikhulu basincenga, ukuthi semukele isipho;" 
2Corinthians8:5 njalo kaku ba nga njengoba sathemba, kodwa bazinikela kuqala eNkosini, lakithi ngentando kaNkulunkulu." 
2Corinthians8:6 Kwaze kwathi sakhuthaza phambili, ngokunjalo awuqede futhi kini lumusa." 
2Corinthians8:7 Kodwa njengalokhu lisengezelela. 
2Corinthians8:8 Kangikhulumi njengokulawula. 
2Corinthians8:9 Ngoba liyawazi umusa weNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu, ukuthi lanxa wayenothile." 
2Corinthians8:10 Lakulokhu ngipha umbono, kungeyisikwenza kuphela, kodwa lokufisa;" 
2Corinthians8:11 kodwa khathesi-ke qedani futhi ukwenza, ukuze, njengalokhu kukhonaukukhuthalela." 
2Corinthians8:12 Ngoba uba kukhona ngalokho alakho, kungeyisikho ngalokho angelakho." 
2Corinthians8:13 Ngoba kungeyisikuthi abanye babe lenkululeko, lina-ke libe lohlupho; kodwa ngokulingana, okwalesisikhathi isengezo senu sibengesenswelo yabo," 
2Corinthians8:14 ukuze kuthi lesengezo sabo," 
2Corinthians8:15 njengokulotshiweyo ukuthi: O wabuthaokunengi, kabanga lokusalayo; lo wabuthaokuncinyane kasilelanga." 
2Corinthians8:16 Kodwa kabongwe uNkulunkulu ofaka efananayo ngani enhliziyweni kaTitosi," 
2Corinthians8:17 ukuthi isibili wemukela isikhuthazo. 
2Corinthians8:18 Njalo sithuma kanye laye umzalwane; 
2Corinthians8:19 kungeyisilokhu kuphela, kodwa ukhethiwe;" 
2Corinthians8:20 sivikela lokhu; 
2Corinthians8:21 sinakekela okuhle kungekho phambi kweNkosi kuphela kodwa laphambi kwabantu. 
2Corinthians8:22 Sasesithuma kanye labo umzalwane wethu, esimfice ezintweni ezinengi kanengi ekhuthele." 
2Corinthians8:23 Kumbe ngoTitosi, ungumhlanganyeli zamabandla, bayinkazimulo kaKristu." 
2Corinthians8:24 Ngakho bonakalisani kubo ubufakazi bothando lwenu labokuzincomela kwethu lina, laphambi kwamabandla." 
2Corinthians9:1 Ngoba mayelana lokuncedisa kakusweleki kimi ukulibhalela; 
2Corinthians9:2 ngoba ngiyazi ukukhuthala kwenu; lokutshiseka okuvela kini kubavusile abanengi. 
2Corinthians9:3 Kodwa ngithume abazalwane; 
2Corinthians9:4 hlezi mhlawumbe, nxa abeMakedoniya befika lami." 
2Corinthians9:5 Ngakho ngibona kufanele ukuthi ngikhuthaze abazalwane. 
2Corinthians9:6 Lalokhu ukuthi, ohlanyela ingcosana, laye uzavuna ingcosana; lohlanyela ngokunengi, laye uzavuna ngokunengi." 
2Corinthians9:7 Ngulowo lalowo njengalokhu azikhethela khona enhliziyweni; kungabi ngokokudonda uyamthanda onikela ngentokozo. 
2Corinthians9:8 Njalo uNkulunkulu; 
2Corinthians9:9 njengokulotshiweyo ukuthi: Uchithachithile, wanika abayanga; ukulunga kwakhe kuhlala kuze kube phakade." 
2Corinthians9:10 Njalo yena onika; 
2Corinthians9:11 linothiswe ezintweni zonke kukho konke ukuphana, okusebenza ngathi ukubongwa kuNkulunkulu;" 
2Corinthians9:12 ngoba umsebenzi; 
2Corinthians9:13 ngobufakazi kubo, lakubo bonke;" 
2Corinthians9:14 langomkhuleko wabo ngani, belilangatha ngomusa kaNkulunkulu ongelakulinganiswa phezu kwenu." 
2Corinthians9:15 Njalo kabongwe uNkulunkulu ngenxa yesipho sakhe esingakhulumekiyo. 
2Corinthians10:1 Mina-ke uPawuli ngokwami ngiyalincenga nxa ngi khona, kodwa nxa ngingekho ngilesibindi kini;" 
2Corinthians10:2 ngiya li ncenga-ke ukuthi, nxa ngikhona, ngingabi lesibindi." 
2Corinthians10:3 Ngoba lanxa sihamba enyameni kasilwi ngokwenyama; 
2Corinthians10:4 ngoba izikhali izinqaba," 
2Corinthians10:5 sehlisa iminakano lakho konke okuziphakamisela; 
2Corinthians10:6 futhi silokulungela ukuphindisela ukungalaleli konke. 
2Corinthians10:7 Likhangela. 
2Corinthians10:8 Ngoba loba ngolutho olwengezelelweyo kakhulu ngingaze ngizincome; 
2Corinthians10:9 ukuze ngingabonakali njengolethusa ngezincwadi. 
2Corinthians10:10 Ngoba kuthiwa: Incwadi zakhezinzima zilamandla. 
2Corinthians10:11 Onjalo kanakane lokhu, ukuthi njengoba sinjalo ngelizwi ngezincwadi nxa singekho, lathi sinjalo ngesenzo nxa sikhona." 
2Corinthians10:12 Ngoba kasilasibindi sokuzibalela kumbe ukuzifananisa, kabaqedisisi." 
2Corinthians10:13 Kodwa thina kasisoze sizincome sesigaba uNkulunkulu asabele sona, isilinganiso sokufika lakini." 
2Corinthians10:14 Ngoba kasizeluli ngokweqileyo ngokungathi kasifinyelelanga kini, ngoba sifikile lakini evangelini likaKristu;" 
2Corinthians10:15 kasizincomi, kodwa silethemba lokuthi, nxa lwandile ukholo lwenu, sizakhuliswa ngokwengezelelelweyo phakathi kwenu ngesigaba sethu," 
2Corinthians10:16 ukutshumayela ivangeli endaweniezingaphetsheya kwenu, singazincomi ngesigaba somunye ezintweni ezilungisiweyo." 
2Corinthians10:17 Kodwa ozincomayo, kazincome eNkosini." 
2Corinthians10:18 Ngoba kayisuye. 
2Corinthians11:1 Kungathi lingangibekezelela. 
2Corinthians11:2 Ngoba ngilobukhwele. 
2Corinthians11:3 Kodwa ngiyesaba ukuthi hlezi njengalokhu inyoka obukuKristu. 
2Corinthians11:4 Ngoba uba ofikayo. 
2Corinthians11:5 Ngoba ngithi. 
2Corinthians11:6 Njalo uba lami kini ezintweni zonke. 
2Corinthians11:7 Kumbe ngenze isono? 
2Corinthians11:8 Ngaphanga amanye amabandla, ngithatha iholo ukuze ngilisize;" 
2Corinthians11:9 lalapho ngangikhona kini ngiswele kangibanga ngumthwalo ngitsho emuntwini ukuthi ngingabi ngumthwalo kini, futhi ngizazigcina." 
2Corinthians11:10 Njengobaiqiniso likaKristu likimi. 
2Corinthians11:11 Ngenxa yani? Ngoba ngingalithandi yini. 
2Corinthians11:12 Kodwa engikwenzayo, ngizakwenza futhi, ukuze ngiqume." 
2Corinthians11:13 Ngoba abanje babe ngabaphostoli bakaKristu. 
2Corinthians11:14 Kakumangalisi-ke; ngoba uSathane. 
2Corinthians11:15 Ngakho ka ku sinto enkulu uba lazo inceku zakhe.

2Corinthians11:17 Lokho engikutshoyo, kangikutsho ngokweNkosi." 
2Corinthians11:18 Lokhu abanengi bezincoma ngokwenyama. 
2Corinthians11:19 Ngoba libekezelela abayizithutha. 
2Corinthians11:20 Ngoba liyabekezela ebusweni. 
2Corinthians11:21 Ngitsho ngenhloni) lami ngilesibindi ngakho. 
2Corinthians11:22 BangamaHebheru yini? Lami.

2Corinthians11:24 kumaJuda.

2Corinthians11:27 ekutshikatshikeni. 
2Corinthians11:28 Ngaphandle kwezinto ezingaphandle, okungicindezelayo insuku zonke yikukhathalela." 
2Corinthians11:29 Ngubani obuthakathaka, ngingabi buthakathaka lami? Ngubani okhutshekiswayo, lami ngingatshiseki?" 
2Corinthians11:30 Uba kumele ukuzincoma, ngizazincoma ngezinto zobuthakathaka bami."
