2Corinthians11:32 EDamaseko umuzi wabeDamaseko, efuna ukungibamba;" 
2Corinthians11:33 njalo ngehliswa ngewindi esilulwini ngomduli, ngasengiphepha ezandleni zayo." 
2Corinthians12:1 Qiniso ukuzincoma kakusizi lutho kimi; ngoba ngizakuya kumibono zeNkosi. 
2Corinthians12:2 Ngiyamazi umuntu ekuKristu. 
2Corinthians12:3 Ngiyamazi-ke umuntu onjalo (loba emzimbeni, loba ngaphandle komzimba, kangazi; uNkulunkulu uyazi)," 
2Corinthians12:4 ukuthi wahluthulwa muntu ukuwakhuluma. 
2Corinthians12:5 Ngizazincoma ngonjalo, kodwa ngami uqobo kangiyikuzincoma." 
2Corinthians12:6 Ngoba uba bengingathanda ukuzincoma, bengingazukuba yisithutha okungaphezu kwalokho angibona ngiyikho, kumbe akuzwa kimi," 
2Corinthians12:7 futhi ukuze ngingaphakanyiswa kakhulukazi ngobukhulukazi bezembulo, ukuze ngingaziphakamisi kakhulukazi." 
2Corinthians12:8 Ngalokho nganxusa iNkosi kathathu ukuze kusuke kimi. 
2Corinthians12:9 Yasisithi kimi: Umusa wami ukwanele; ngoba amandla ami ahlale phezu kwami. 
2Corinthians12:10 Ngakho ngiyathokoza ebuthakathakeni, khona ngilamandla." 
2Corinthians12:11 Sengize ngaba yisithutha, ngizincoma." 
2Corinthians12:12 Isibili impawu lemisebenzi yamandla. 
2Corinthians12:13 Ngoba kuyini elaba ngaphansi ngakho kwamanye amabandla. 
2Corinthians12:14 Khangelani, sengilungele ukuza kini ngokwesithathu kabafanele ukudlinzekelela abazali, kodwa abazali abantwana." 
2Corinthians12:15 Mina-ke ngizachitha ngentokozo, ngithandwa kancinyane." 
2Corinthians12:16 Kodwa ku njalo, mina kangibanga ngumthwalo kini, ngalibamba ngobuqili." 
2Corinthians12:17 Ngaliqilibezela yini engabathuma kini? 
2Corinthians12:18 Ngacela uTitosi? 
2Corinthians12:19 Licabanga futhi. 
2Corinthians12:20 Ngoba ngilovalo hlezi mhlawumbe ekufikeni kwami; 
2Corinthians12:21 hlezi ekufikeni kwami abakwenzileyo. 
2Corinthians13:1 Ngalesisikhathi sesithathu wabafakazi ababili kumbe abathathu wonke umutsho uzaqiniswa. 
2Corinthians13:2 Sengitshilo; 
2Corinthians13:3 njengoba lidinga ubufakazi; 
2Corinthians13:4 ngoba lanxa wabethelwa, kodwa sizaphila kanye laye ngamandla kaNkulunkulu kini." 
2Corinthians13:5 Zihloleni ukuthi lisekholweni; lizilinge? 
2Corinthians13:6 Ngithemba-ke ukuthi lizakwazi ukuthi thina kasisibo abalahliweyo. 
2Corinthians13:7 Njalo ngiyakhuleka kuNkulunkulu, ukuthi lingenzi lutho olubi, kungesikuthi sibonakale thina singabathembekileyo." 
2Corinthians13:8 Ngoba kasilamandla okwenza ulutho olumelana leqiniso, kodwa okweqiniso." 
2Corinthians13:9 Ngoba siyajabula nxa sibuthakathaka kwenu.

Galatians1:1 UPawuli umphostoli ongaveli ebantwini, njalo kungekho ngomuntu," 
Galatians1:2 labazalwane bonke abalami: 
Galatians1:3 Umusa kawubekini lokuthula okuvela kuNkulunkulu uBaba, leNkosini yethu uJesu Kristu," 
Galatians1:4 owazinikela ngenxa yezono zethu; 
Galatians1:5 obukuye ubukhosi kuze kube nini lanini. Ameni. 
Galatians1:6 Ngiyamangala; 
Galatians1:7 elingeyisilo elinye; kodwa bakhona abanye abalididayo bethanda ukuhlanekela ivangeli likaKristu. 
Galatians1:8 Kodwa lanxa kungaba yithi kumbe ingilosi evela ezulwini engalitshumayeza ivangeli elehlukene lalelo esalitshumayeza lona. 
Galatians1:9 Njengoba sesitshilo, lakhathesi ngiyaphinda ngithi: Uba umuntu elitshumayeza ivangeli elehlukene lalelo elalemukelayo." 
Galatians1:10 Ngoba ngincenga? Ngoba uba ngisathokozisa abantu, ngingebe yinceku kaKristu." 
Galatians1:11 Kodwa ngiyalazisa, bazalwane." 
Galatians1:12 Ngoba lami kangilemukelanga. 
Galatians1:13 Ngoba selizwile ukuhamba kwami kwakuqala; 
Galatians1:14 njalo ngangiphumelela. 
Galatians1:15 Kodwa nxa kwaba kuhle kuNkulunkulu," 
Galatians1:16 ukwembula iNdodana yakhe kimi; 
Galatians1:17 futhi kangenyukelanga eJerusalema kubo ababengabaphostoli ngaphambi kwami, kodwa ngasuka ngaya eArabhiya." 
Galatians1:18 Emva kwalokho sekwedlule iminyaka emithathu. 
Galatians1:19 Kodwa kangibonanga la munye wabaphostoli, ngaphandle kukaJakobe." 
Galatians1:20 Lezinto engilibhalela zona, khangelani, phambi kukaNkulunkulu, kangiqambi manga." 
Galatians1:21 Emva kwalokho ngaya ezabelweni. 
Galatians1:22 Njalo ngangingakaziwa ngobuso emabandleni eJudiya; 
Galatians1:23 kodwa ayesizwa nje ukuthi: Owake wasizingela, usetshumayela ukholo owake waluchitha," 
Galatians1:24 asedumisa uNkulunkulu kimi. 
Galatians2:1 Emva kwalokho sekwedlule iminyaka elitshumi lane; 
Galatians2:2 ngasengisenyuka ngesambulelo. 
Galatians2:3 Kodwa ngitsho uTitosi o waye lami; 
Galatians2:4 njalo ngenxa; 
Galatians2:5 esingabathobelanga ngokuzehlisa ngitsho okwehola. 
Galatians2:6 Kodwa kulabo okuthiwa; 
Galatians2:7 kodwa kokuphambeneyo, bebona ukuthi ngaphiwa ivangeli lokungasoki," 
Galatians2:8 ngoba owenza ngamandla kuPetro kubuphostoli bokusoka," 
Galatians2:9 bathi besazi umusa engiwuphiweyo, oJakobe;" 
Galatians2:10 kuphela ukuze sikhumbule abayanga. 
Galatians2:11 Kodwa kwathi uPetro. 
Galatians2:12 Ngoba bengakafiki abathile abavela kuJakobe. 
Galatians2:13 Lamanye futhi amaJuda azenzisa kanye laye, kwaze kwathi loBarnabasi wathatheka ngokuzenzisa kwawo." 
Galatians2:14 Kodwa kuthe sengibonile ukuthi kabahambi ngokuqonda eqinisweni levangeli? 
Galatians2:15 Thina singamaJuda," 
Galatians2:16 sisazi ukuthi umuntu kalungisiswa ngemisebenzi yomlayo kakuyikulungisiswa nyama. 
Galatians2:17 Kodwa uba thina, esidinga ukulungisiswa kuKristu, lathi uqobo sificwe siyizoni!" 
Galatians2:18 Ngoba uba ngibuye ngakhe izinto engizidilizileyo, ngitshengisa ukuthi ngingophambekayo." 
Galatians2:19 Ngoba ngomlayo. 
Galatians2:20 Ngibethelwe kanye loKristu, kodwa ngiyaphila; kakuseyimi-ke, kodwa uKristu uphila kimi." 
Galatians2:21 Kangiwutshayi ize umusa kaNkulunkulu. 
Galatians3:1 Hawu maGalathiya ayizithutha, ngubani oliloyileyo?" 
Galatians3:2 Yilokhu kuphela engithanda ukukufunda kini ukuthi: Lemukela uMoya ngemisebenzi yomlayo yini? 
Galatians3:3 Kanti liyizithutha kangaka? Liqale ngoMoya selipheleliswa ngenyama yini? 
Galatians3:4 Lahlupheka izinto ezinengi kangaka ngeze yini? Uba-ke ngitsho ngeze. 
Galatians3:5 Ngakho yena olinika uMoya losebenza imisebenzi yamandla phakathi kwenu, kungabangemisebenzi yomlayo yini, kumbe ngokuzwa kokholo?" 
Galatians3:6 NjengoAbrahama wakholwa kuNkulunkulu, kwabalelwa-ke kuye ukuthi yikulunga." 
Galatians3:7 Ngakho liyazi ukuthi labo abangabokholo. 
Galatians3:8 Lombhalo, ubona ngaphambili ukuthi uNkulunkulu." 
Galatians3:9 Ngakho abangabokholo babusiswa kanye loAbrahama okholwayo. 
Galatians3:10 Ngoba bonke abemisebenzi yomlayo bangaphansi kwesiqalekiso. 
Galatians3:11 Kodwa kusobala ukuthi ngomlayo kakulamuntu olungisiswayo phambi kukaNkulunkulu; 
Galatians3:12 kodwa umlayo kawusiwo wokholo, kodwa kuthiwa: Umuntu owenza lezizinto uzaphila kuzo." 
Galatians3:13 UKristu; 
Galatians3:14 ukuze kuthi isibusiso sikaAbrahama sifike kwabezizwe ngoKristu Jesu. 
Galatians3:15 Bazalwane, ngikhuluma njengokomuntu." 
Galatians3:16 Njalo izithembiso zakhulunywa. 
Galatians3:17 Lalokho ngiyakutsho: Umlayo oweza emva kweminyaka engamakhulu amane lamatshumi amathathu kawusesuli isivumelwano esaqiniswa nguNkulunkulu kuKristu ngaphambili. 
Galatians3:18 Ngoba uba ilifa livela emlayweni, alisaveli esithembisweni; kodwa uNkulunkulu wa li nika uAbrahama ngesithembiso." 
Galatians3:19 Pho, umlayo uyini? Wengezwa ngenxa yeziphambeko." 
Galatians3:20 Kodwa umlamuli kayisuye woyedwa. 
Galatians3:21 Pho umlayo uphambene lezithembiso zikaNkulunkulu yini? Phinde. 
Galatians3:22 Kodwa umbhalo. 
Galatians3:23 Kodwa kungakafiki ukholo. 
Galatians3:24 Ngakho umlayo; 
Galatians3:25 kodwa selufikile ukholo. 
Galatians3:26 Ngoba lonke lingabantwana bakaNkulunkulu ngokholo kuKristu Jesu. 
Galatians3:27 Ngoba lonke elabhabhathizelwa kuKristu; 
Galatians3:28 kakukho umJuda lomGriki. 
Galatians3:29 Uba-ke lingabakaKristu. 
Galatians4:1 Kodwa ngithi, ngaso sonke isikhathi indlalifa iseyingane, kayehlukananga ngalutho esigqilini lanxa ingumnikazi wakho konke;" 
Galatians4:2 kodwa ingaphansi kwabaphathi, kuze kufike isikhathi esamiswa nguyise." 
Galatians4:3 Ngokunjalo lathi, lapho si se yizingane, sasiyizigqili;" 
Galatians4:4 kodwa kwathi ukuphelela kwesikhathi sekufikile, uNkulunkulu wathuma iNdodana yakhe," 
Galatians4:5 ukuze ihlenge abangaphansi komlayo, ukuze semukele ukuma kwabantwana." 
Galatians4:6 Njengoba lingamadodana! 
Galatians4:7 Ngakho kawuseyiso isigqili, kodwa indodana; njalo uba uy indodana, futhi uy indlalifa kaNkulunkulu ngoKristu." 
Galatians4:8 Kodwa ngalesosikhathi, lingamazi uNkulunkulu;" 
Galatians4:9 kodwa khathesi lokhu selimazi uNkulunkulu, yebo kangithi lisaziwa nguNkulunkulu?" 
Galatians4:10 Ligcina izinsuku. 
Galatians4:11 Ngilovalo ngani. 
Galatians4:12 Banini njengami, ngoba lami nginjengani, bazalwane, ngiyalincenga; kalingonanga nga lutho;" 
Galatians4:13 liyazi-ke ukuthi ngobuthakathaka benyama ngatshumayela ivangeli kini," 
Galatians4:14 lokulingwa kwami okwakusenyameni yami kalikudelelanga njalo kalikwenyanyanga, kodwa langemukela njengengilosi kaNkulunkulu." 
Galatians4:15 Ngakho sasiyini isibusiso senu. 
Galatians4:16 Ngakho sengibeyisitha senu ngokulitshela iqiniso yini? 
Galatians4:17 Bayalitshisekela ngokungekuhle. 
Galatians4:18 Kodwa kuhle ukuthi litshisekelelwe kokuhle isikhathi sonke, njalo kungabi sebukhoneni bami lani kuphela." 
Galatians4:19 Bantwana bami abancane, engilomhelo futhi wokulizala," 
Galatians4:20 kodwa bengingathanda ukuba khona lani khathesi, ngiphendule ilizwi lami." 
Galatians4:21 Ngitshelani, lina elithanda ukuba ngaphansi komlayo, kaliwuzwa yini umlayo?" 
Galatians4:22 Ngoba kulotshiwe ukuthi uAbrahama wayelamadodana amabili; enye ingeyesigqilikazi. 
Galatians4:23 Kodwa eyesigqilikazi yazalwa ngokwenyama. 
Galatians4:24 Okuyizinto ezingumzekeliso; ngoba laba bayizivumelwano ezimbili; esinye esentabeni iSinayi. 
Galatians4:25 Ngoba lokhu, uAgari, kuyintaba iSinayi eseArabhiya." 
Galatians4:26 Kodwa iJerusalema ephezulu ikhululekile, engumama wethu sonke;" 
Galatians4:27 ngoba kulotshiwe ukuthi: Thokoza, wenanyumba engazaliyo; kekela umemeze, wena ongawuzwanga umhelo; ngoba abantwana botshiyiweyo banengi okwedlula kakhulu kulaye olendoda." 
Galatians4:28 Kodwa thina, bazalwane, njengoIsaka." 
Galatians4:29 Kodwa njengakulesosikhathi owazalwa ngokwenyama wamzingela yena ongowakoMoya. 
Galatians4:30 Kodwa umbhalo uthini. 
Galatians4:31 Ngakho, bazalwane, kasisibo abantwana besigqilikazi, kodwa bokhululekileyo." 
Galatians5:1 Ngakho manini liqine. 
Galatians5:2 Khangelani, mina Pawuli ngithi kini, uba lisokwa, uKristu kayikulisiza ngalutho." 
Galatians5:3 Ngiyafakaza-ke futhi kumuntu wonke osokwayo, ukuthi ulomlandu wokwenza umlayo wonke." 
Galatians5:4 Likhutshiwe. 
Galatians5:5 Ngoba thina ngoMoya silindele ngokholo ithemba lokulunga. 
Galatians5:6 Ngoba kuKristu Jesu ukusoka kumbe ukungasoki kakusizi lutho. 
Galatians5:7 Beligijima kuhle? 
Galatians5:8 Lokhukuhuga kakuveli kolibizayo. 
Galatians5:9 Imvubelo eyingcosana ibilisa inhlama yonke. 
Galatians5:10 Mina ngilethemba ngani eNkosini, loba engubani." 
Galatians5:11 Kodwa mina, bazalwane, uba ngisatshumayela ukusoka." 
Galatians5:12 Sengathi. 
Galatians5:13 Ngoba lina labizelwa enkululekweni. 
Galatians5:14 Ngoba umlayo wonke ugcwaliseka elizwini linye. 
Galatians5:15 Kodwa uba lilumana lidlana, qaphelani ukuthi lingaqedwa omunye ngomunye." 
Galatians5:16 Kodwa ngithi: Hambani ngoMoya. 
Galatians5:17 Ngoba inyama ikhanuka okuphambene loMoya, loMoya okuphambene lenyama; njalo lezizinto ziphambene." 
Galatians5:18 Kodwa uba likhokhelwa nguMoya. 
Galatians5:19 Imisebenzi yenyama-ke isobala, eyi le: Ukufeba, ukuphinga," 
Galatians5:20 ukukhonza izithombe," 
Galatians5:21 umhawu. 
Galatians5:22 Kodwa isithelo sikaMoya," 
Galatians5:23 ubumnene. 
Galatians5:24 Kodwa abakaKristu babethele inyama kanye lokuhugeka lezinkanuko. 
Galatians5:25 Uba siphila ngoMoya, njalo asihambe ngoMoya." 
Galatians5:26 Kasingazikhukhumezi, siqalane, sifelane umona." 
Galatians6:1 Bazalwane, uba-ke umuntu esehlelwa yisiphambeko esithile." 
Galatians6:2 Thwalisanani imithwalo yenu. 
Galatians6:3 Ngoba uba umuntu ezitsho ukuthi uyilutho; 
Galatians6:4 kodwa ngulowo lalowo kahlole owakhe umsebenzi, njalo kungabi ngokomunye." 
Galatians6:5 Ngoba ngulowo lalowo. 
Galatians6:6 Lofundiswa ilizwi. 
Galatians6:7 Lingakhohliswa. 
Galatians6:8 Ngoba ohlanyela kweyakhe inyama. 
Galatians6:9 Kodwa. 
Galatians6:10 Ngakho-ke njengoba silethuba. 
Galatians6:11 Bonani amabala amakhulu kangaka engilibhalela ngawo ngesami isandla. 
Galatians6:12 Bonke abafuna ukubukeka enyameni. 
Galatians6:13 Ngoba ngitsho lalabo abasokwayo kabawugcini umlayo, kodwa bafuna ukuthi lisokwe, ukuze bazincome enyameni yenu." 
Galatians6:14 Kodwa kimi kakungabi khona, lami kuwo umhlaba." 
Galatians6:15 Ngoba kuKristu Jesu ukusoka kakusizi lutho. 
Galatians6:16 Njalo bonke.

Galatians6:18 Umusa weNkosi yethu uJesu Kristu kawubelomoya wenu, bazalwane. Ameni."

Philippians1:1 UPawuli loTimothi: 
Philippians1:2 Umusa. 
Philippians1:3 Ngiyambonga," 
Philippians1:4 ngezikhathi zonke kuwo wonke umkhuleko wami ngani lonke," 
Philippians1:5 ngokuhlanganyela kwenu evangelini; 
Philippians1:6 ngilethemba lakhona lokho, ukuthi owaqalisa;" 
Philippians1:7 njengoba kulungile kimi ukuthi ngikhumbule lokhu ngani lonke, ngoba ngilani enhliziyweni." 
Philippians1:8 Ngoba uNkulunkulu ungumfakazi wami. 
Philippians1:9 Njalo ngikhuleka lokhu, ukuthi uthando lwenu," 
Philippians1:10 ukuze lizivume," 
Philippians1:11 ligcwaliswe ngezithelo zokulunga lukaNkulunkulu. 
Philippians1:12 Kodwa ngithanda ukuthi lazi, bazalwane, ukuthi izinto ezangehlelayo zenza kakhulu ukuqhutshelwa phambili kwevangeli;" 
Philippians1:13 zize izibopho esigodlweni sonke lakwabanye bonke," 
Philippians1:14 labazalwane abanengi eNkosini, beqiniswe ngezibopho zami, sebelesibindi esikhulu sokukhuluma ilizwi ngokungesabi." 
Philippians1:15 Abanye kambe batshumayela uKristu ngomona langombango, labanye kambe ngenhliziyo enhle;" 
Philippians1:16 laba batshumayela uKristu ngokuphikisana, bengelaqiniso, besithi baletha ukuhlupheka ekubotshweni kwami;" 
Philippians1:17 kodwa labo ngothando, besazi." 
Philippians1:18 Kuyini pho? Loba kunjalo kuyo yonke indlela, loba ekuzenziseni, kumbe eqinisweni, uKristu uyatshunyayelwa; kulokhu-ke ngiyathokoza, yebo ngizathokoza futhi." 
Philippians1:19 Ngoba ngiyazi ukuthi lokhu kuzaphendukela kimi esindisweni ngomkhuleko wenu," 
Philippians1:20 njengokulindela okukhulu, njengesikhathi sonke, lakhathesi uKristu uzakhuliswa emzimbeni wami, loba ngempilo, kumbe ngokufa." 
Philippians1:21 Ngoba kimi ukuphila kunguKristu, lokufa kuyinzuzo." 
Philippians1:22 Kodwa uba ukuphila enyameni kuyisithelo somsebenzi kimi, lengizakukhetha kangikwazi." 
Philippians1:23 Ngoba ngiminyezelwe ngokubili lokuba loKristu, okungcono kakhulukazi;" 
Philippians1:24 kodwa ukuhlala enyameni kuyasweleka kakhulu ngenxa yenu. 
Philippians1:25 Njalo ngilalelithemba lentokozweni yokholo," 
Philippians1:26 ukuze ukuzincoma kwenu ngami kwengezwe kuKristu Jesu kimi, ngobukhona bami kini futhi." 
Philippians1:27 Kuphela hambani," 
Philippians1:28 njalo lingethuswa ngalutho ngabaphikisayo; okuyisibonakaliso, njalo lokhu kuvela kuNkulunkulu;" 
Philippians1:29 ngoba lanikwa; 
Philippians1:30 lilokulwa.

Philippians2:2 gcwalisani intokozo yami, libe lothando olufananayo, libelenhliziyonye, ukuqonda kunye;"

Philippians2:6 owathi esesimeni," 
Philippians2:7 kodwa wazidela;

Philippians2:15 ukuze lingasoleki emhlabeni,"

Philippians2:23 Ngiyathemba-ke ukuhle ngimthume yena, nxa sengibonisisile okuqondene lami;" 
Philippians2:24 kodwa ngiyathemba eNkosini, ukuthi lami ngizakuza kini masinyane."

Philippians2:26 njengoba wayelilangatha, ngoba lezwa ukuthi wayegula;" 
Philippians2:27 ngoba njalo wagula waphosa wafa, kodwa uNkulunkulu wamhawukela, njalo kungeyisuye yena yedwa, kodwa lami, ukuze ngingabi losizi phezu kosizi." 
Philippians2:28 Ngakho ngitshisekela kakhulu ukumthuma, ukuze kuthi, nxa limbona, lithokoze futhi, losizi lwami lunciphe." 
Philippians2:29 Memukeleni-ke; 
Philippians2:30 ngoba ngenxa yomsebenzi kaKristu waphose wafa, edela impilo, ukuze aphelelise okusileleyo komsebenzi wenu kimi."

Philippians3:2 Nanzelelani izinja; 
Philippians3:3 ngoba thina siyikusoka kuKristu Jesu, njalo singathembeli enyameni;"

Philippians3:5 ngasokwa," 
Philippians3:6 ngokokukhuthala. 
Philippians3:7 Kodwa izinto ezaziyinzuzo kimi, lezo ngazibala njengencithakalo ngenxa kaKristu." 
Philippians3:8 Yebo isibili yikho konke, njalo ngakuthatha njengezibi, ukuze ngizuze uKristu," 
Philippians3:9 njalo ngificwe kuye, ngingelakho okwami ukulunga okuvela kuNkulunkulu ngokholo;" 
Philippians3:10 ukuze ngimazi yena lamandla okuvuka kwakhe ukufa kwakhe," 
Philippians3:11 uba kungenzeka ngifinyelele ekuvukeni okwabafileyo. 
Philippians3:12 Kangitsho ukuthi sengi ku bambile khona nguKristu Jesu.

1Timothy1:2 kuTimothi okuvela kuNkulunkulu uBaba wethu loJesu Kristu iNkosi yethu. 
1Timothy1:3 Njengoba ngakukhuthaza," 
1Timothy1:4 futhi bangananzeleli izinganekwane. 
1Timothy1:5 Kodwa injongo yomlayo luthando; 
1Timothy1:6 kulokhu abathile abaduhe kukho baphambukela," 
1Timothy1:7 befuna. 
1Timothy1:8 Kodwa siyazi ukuthi umlayo ulungile, uba umuntu ewusebenzisa ngokomlayo," 
1Timothy1:9 esazi lokhu, ukuthi umlayo kawubekelwa olungileyo, ababulala oyise lababulala onina, ababulala abantu," 
1Timothy1:10 izifebe," 
1Timothy1:11 njengokwevangeli lenkazimulo. 
1Timothy1:12 Ngiyambonga-ke owanginika amandla," 
1Timothy1:13 owayekade engumhlambazi; 
1Timothy1:14 kodwa umusa weNkosi. 
1Timothy1:15 Lithembekile lelilizwi; 
1Timothy1:16 kodwa ngenxa yalokhu ngahawukelwa kwabazakholwa kuye empilweni ephakade. 
1Timothy1:17 Kuyo-ke iNkosi eyisimakade. Ameni. 
1Timothy1:18 Lumlayo ngiwunika wena," 
1Timothy1:19 ubamba ukholo mayelana lokholo; 
1Timothy1:20 okukubo uHimeneyo. 
1Timothy2:1 Ngakho kuqala kukho konke ngikhuthaza kwenzelwe abantu bonke; 
1Timothy2:2 amakhosi; 
1Timothy2:3 ngoba lokhu kuhle," 
1Timothy2:4 ofuna ukuthi bonke abantu basindiswe. 
1Timothy2:5 Ngoba munye uNkulunkulu," 
1Timothy2:6 owazinikela yena ukuba lihlawulo labo bonke," 
1Timothy2:7 mina engamiselwa khona ukuba ngumtshumayeli lomphostoli. 
1Timothy2:8 Ngakho ngifisa ukuthi amadoda akhuleke kuyo yonke indawo. 
1Timothy2:9 Ngokunjalo labesifazana bazicecise ngezigqoko ezifaneleyo," 
1Timothy2:10 kodwa. 
1Timothy2:11 Owesifazana kafunde ngokuthula. 
1Timothy2:12 Kodwa kangivumeli owesifazana ukuthi afundise, kumbe abe lamandla phezu kowesilisa, kodwa abe ekuthuleni." 
1Timothy2:13 Ngoba uAdamu wabunjwa kuqala; 
1Timothy2:14 futhi uAdamu kakhohliswanga, kodwa owesifazana esekhohlisiwe waba sesiphambekweni," 
1Timothy2:15 kodwa uzasindiswa ngokuzala abantwana. 
1Timothy3:1 Lithembekile ilizwi, ufisa umsebenzi omuhle;" 
1Timothy3:2 ngakho kumele ukuthi umbonisi; 
1Timothy3:3 angabi yisidakwa; 
1Timothy3:4 ephatha kuhle owakhe umuzi," 
1Timothy3:5 ngoba uba umuntu engakwazi ukuphatha owakhe umuzi, angaligcina njani ibandla likaNkulunkulu?" 
1Timothy3:6 Kangabi ngosanda ukukholwa, hlezi ngokukhukhunyezwa." 
1Timothy3:7 Kumele futhi ukuthi abe lobufakazi obuhle. 
1Timothy3:8 Ngokunjalo abadikoni, bangafisi inzuzo embi," 
1Timothy3:9 babambe imfihlo yokholo. 
1Timothy3:10 Laba-ke kabaqale bahlolwe. 
1Timothy3:11 Ngokunjalo omka bo babe ng abahloniphekayo. 
1Timothy3:12 Abadikoni kababe ngamadoda amfazi munye. 
1Timothy3:13 Ngoba abakhonze kuhle ekholweni olukuKristu Jesu. 
1Timothy3:14 Lezizinto ngikubhalela zona, ngithemba ukuza kuwe masinyane;" 
1Timothy3:15 kodwa uba ngibambeka, ukuze wazi ukuthi kufanele uziphathe njani endlini kaNkulunkulu." 
1Timothy3:16 Kuyavunywa-ke ukuthiyinkulu imfihlo. 
1Timothy4:1 UMoya-ke lemfundiso zamadimoni," 
1Timothy4:2 ekuzenziseni kwabaqambimanga," 
1Timothy4:3 besalela ukuthathana; 
1Timothy4:4 ngoba sonke isidalwa sikaNkulunkulu sihle; 
1Timothy4:5 ngoba luyangcweliswa ngelizwi likaNkulunkulu.

1Timothy4:7 Kodwa wale inganekwane ezimbi lezezalukazi;

1Timothy4:13 Ngize ngifike, nanzelela ekubaleni, ekulayeni."

1Timothy5:1 Ungamkhalimeli; abatsha njengabafowenu;

1Timothy5:3 Hlonipha abafelokazi abangabafelokazi isibili.

1Timothy5:10 onconywa ngemisebenzi emihle.

1Timothy5:17 Abadala; 
1Timothy5:18 ngoba umbhalo uthi. 
1Timothy5:19 Ungalemukeli icala elimelana lomdala. 
1Timothy5:20 Abonayo basole. 
1Timothy5:21 Ngiya ku layisisa. 
1Timothy5:22 Ungaphangisi ukubeka izandla. 
1Timothy5:23 Ungabe usanatha amanzi wodwa, kodwa sebenzisa iwayini elilutshwana." 
1Timothy5:24 Izono; kanti ezabanye ziyalandela. 
1Timothy5:25 Ngokunjalo lemisebenzi emihle isobala.

2Timothy1:2 kuTimothi. 
2Timothy1:3 Ngiyambonga uNkulunkulu," 
2Timothy1:4 ngilangatha ukukubona, ukuze ngigcwaliswe ngentokozo," 
2Timothy1:5 nxa ngibeka emkhumbulweni ukholo olungelakuzenzisa olukuwe, njalo ngithemba ukuthi lukhona lakuwe." 
2Timothy1:6 Ngenxa yalesisizatho ngiyakukhumbuza ukuthi uvuselele isipho sikaNkulunkulu. 
2Timothy1:7 Ngoba uNkulunkulu kasinikanga umoya wobugwala. 
2Timothy1:8 Ngakho ungabi lanhloni kanye levangeli njengamandla kaNkulunkulu," 
2Timothy1:9 owasisindisayo," 
2Timothy1:10 kodwa oselubonakaliswe khathesi,"

2Timothy1:12 Ngenxa yalesisizatho lami ngiyahlupheka lezizinto. 
2Timothy1:13 Bambelela. 
2Timothy1:14 Lokhu okuhle okuphathisiweyo. 
2Timothy1:15 Uyakwazi lokhu, ukuthi bonke abaseAsiya, okukubo uFigelo loHermogene." 
2Timothy1:16 Sengathi iNkosi inganika umusa," 
2Timothy1:17 kodwa ekufikeni kwakhe eRoma, wangidingisisa;" 
2Timothy1:18 sengathi iNkosi ingamnika ukuthi athole isihawu eNkosini. 
2Timothy2:1 Ngakho wena, mntanami." 
2Timothy2:2 Lezinto owazizwa kimi. 
2Timothy2:3 Ngakho wena hlupheka ngobunzima. 
2Timothy2:4 Kakho osebenza, ukuze amkholise lowo o m buthileyo." 
2Timothy2:5 Futhi nxa umuntu laye encintisana. 
2Timothy2:6 Kufanele umlimi osebenza kakhulu emukele kuqala izithelo. 
2Timothy2:7 Nakana ngezinto engizitshoyo; njalo sengathi iNkosi ingakunika ukuqedisisa ezintweni zonke. 
2Timothy2:8 Khumbula ukuthi uJesu Kristu wavuswa kwabafileyo, owenzalo kaDavida;" 
2Timothy2:9 engihlupheka kulo okubi. 
2Timothy2:10 Ngakho ngikubekezelele konke ngenxa. 
2Timothy2:11 Lithembekile ilizwi elithi; 
2Timothy2:12 uba sibekezela; 
2Timothy2:13 uba singathembeki. 
2Timothy2:14 Ba khumbuze lezizinto. 
2Timothy2:15 Khuthalela ukuthi uziveze kuNkulunkulu uthembekile, isisebenzi esingelambangela yokuba lenhloni, esiqondisa kuhle ilizwi leqiniso." 
2Timothy2:16 Kodwa xwaya," 
2Timothy2:17 lelizwi labo lizabhibhidla okwemvukuzane; okukubo uHimeneyo loFileto; 
2Timothy2:18 abaduhileyo, begenqula ukholo lwabanye." 
2Timothy2:19 Loba kunjalo isisekelo sikaNkulunkulu. 
2Timothy2:20 Kodwa endlini enkulu. 
2Timothy2:21 Ngakho uba umuntu ezihlambulula. 
2Timothy2:22 Balekela-ke. 
2Timothy2:23 Kodwa yala ukuphikisana okobuthutha lokokungafundi, usazi ukuthi kubanga ukulwa."

2Timothy2:25 ibeluleke ngobumnene abalenkani," 
2Timothy2:26 njalo basanguluke kumjibila kadiyabhola, ababanjwe nguye entandweni yakhe."

Philemon1:2 lakuApifiya othandekayo, lakuArkipho:"

Philemon1:4 Ngiyambonga uNkulunkulu wami, ngikuphatha ngezikhathi zonke emikhulekweni yami," 
Philemon1:5 ngisizwa," 
Philemon1:6 ukuze ukuhlanganyela kokholo lwakho kube lamandla elwazini lwento yonke enhle ekini kuKristu Jesu. 
Philemon1:7 Ngoba silentokozo enkulu. 
Philemon1:8 Ngalokho, lanxa ngilesibindi esikhulu kuKristu sokuthi ngikulaye," 
Philemon1:9 kantingenxa yothando kungcono ukuthi ngincenge. 
Philemon1:10 Ngiyakuncenga," 
Philemon1:11 okade engelasizo kuwe," 
Philemon1:12 engimbuyisela kuwe; kodwa wena, memukele;" 
Philemon1:13 ebengifisa mina ukumbamba abe lami; 
Philemon1:14 kodwa kangithandanga ukwenza ulutho ngaphandle kwemvumo yakho, ukuze okuhle kwakho kungabi ngokokubanjwa ngamandla." 
Philemon1:15 Ngoba mhlawumbe wehlukaniswa lawe; 
Philemon1:16 angabe esaba njengesigqili, kodwa ngaphezu kwesigqili." 
Philemon1:17 Ngakho uba usithi ngingumhlanganyeli lawe, memukele njengami." 
Philemon1:18 Kodwa uba ekone ng olutho kumbe elomlandu, lokho kubalele kimi;" 
Philemon1:19 mina Pawuli ngibhale ngesandla sami, mina ngizahlawula ulomlandu oseleyo kimi." 
Philemon1:20 Yebo, mzalwane, sengathi ngingaba lentokozo ngawe eNkosini." 
Philemon1:21 Ngikubhalele ngithemba ukulalela kwakho, ngisazi ukuthi lawe uzakwenza okungaphezu kwalokho engikutshoyo." 
Philemon1:22 Futhi ngesikhathi esifananayo ungilungisele lami indawo. 
Philemon1:23 Uyakubingelela," 
Philemon1:24 uMarko.

Hebrews1:1 UNkulunkulu owakhuluma endulo kubobaba ngabaprofethi ngezigaba ngezigaba langendlela ezinengi," 
Hebrews1:2 kulezinsuku zokucina," 
Hebrews1:3 yona eyikubenyezela kwenkazimulo soBukhulu obuphezulu," 
Hebrews1:4 isiyenziwe yaphakama kakhulu kulezingilosi, njengalokhu izuze ilifa lebizo elikhulu kulalezo." 
Hebrews1:5 Ngoba kukuyiphi yezingilosi ake watsho kuyo ukuthi: Wena uyiNdodana yami, mina lamuhla ngikuzele?" 
Hebrews1:6 Futhi. 
Hebrews1:7 Lakuzingilosi ingilosi zakhe imimoya, lenceku zakhe ilangabi lomlilo;" 
Hebrews1:8 kodwa eNdodaneni; intonga yombuso wakho yintonga yokulunga. 
Hebrews1:9 Uthandile ukulunga, wazonda ububi; ngenxa yalokhu, uNkulunkulu, uNkulunkulu wakho ukugcobile ngamagcobo entokozo kulabanakwenu." 
Hebrews1:10 Lokuthi: Wena Nkosi, ekuqaleni wasekela umhlaba, lamazulu ayimisebenzi yezandla zakho;" 
Hebrews1:11 kuzabhubha lokho, kodwa wena umi njalonjalo; futhi kuzaguga konke njengesigqoko," 
Hebrews1:12 lanjengesembatho uzakugoqa, kuzaphendulwa-ke; kodwa wena unguwe unjalo, leminyaka yakho kayiyikuphela." 
Hebrews1:13 Kukuyiphi-ke yezingilosi ake atsho kuyo ukuthi: Hlala ngakwesokunene sami, ngize ngibeke izitha zakho zibe yisenabelo senyawo zakho?" 
Hebrews1:14 Kazisibo yini zonke omoya abasebenzayo?

Hebrews2:3 thina sizaphepha njani," 
Hebrews2:4 uNkulunkulu efakaza kanye la bongezibonakaliso. 
Hebrews2:5 Ngoba kehliselanga ngaphansi kwezingilosi, esikhuluma ngalo." 
Hebrews2:6 Kodwa omunye? kumbe indodana yomuntu, ukuthi uyinanze?" 
Hebrews2:7 Wamenza waba phansi kancinyane kulezingilosi; wamethwesa umqhele wenkazimulo lodumo; wammisa phezu kwemisebenzi yezandla zakho; 
Hebrews2:8 izinto zonke. 
Hebrews2:9 Kodwa siyambona uJesu, owenziwa waba phansi kancinyane kulezingilosi." 
Hebrews2:10 Ngoba kwakumfanele. 
Hebrews2:11 Ngoba lalowo ongcwelisayo," 
Hebrews2:12 esithi: Ngizatshumayela. 
Hebrews2:13 Futhi-ke: Mina ngizathemba kuye. 
Hebrews2:14 Ngakho njengoba abantwana behlanganyele inyama legazi," 
Hebrews2:15 abakhulule labo bonke abathi. 
Hebrews2:16 Ngoba isibili kazithatheli izingilosi, kodwa uzithathela inzalo kaAbrahama." 
Hebrews2:17 Ngenxa yalokho kwamfanela ukuthi abe njengabafo wabokuzo zonke izinto yokuthula ngezono zabantu. 
Hebrews2:18 Ngoba kulokhu, ulamandla okusiza abalingwayo." 
Hebrews3:1 Ngakho, bazalwane abangcwele," 
Hebrews3:2 othembeke kulowo owammisayo, njengoMozisi laye wayenjaloendlini yakhe yonke." 
Hebrews3:3 Ngoba kwathiwa lo ufanele udumo olukhulu kuloMozisi, njengoba ulodumo olukhulu kulendlu ayakhileyo." 
Hebrews3:4 Ngoba yonke indlu yakhiwa ngothile. 
Hebrews3:5 UMozisi; 
Hebrews3:6 kodwa uKristu njengendodana phezu kwendlu yakhe. 
Hebrews3:7 Ngakho njengoba uMoya oyiNgcwele uba lilizwa ilizwi lakhe," 
Hebrews3:8 lingazenzi zibe lukhuni inhliziyo zenu, njengekucunuleni, ngosuku lokulingwa enkangala," 
Hebrews3:9 lapho oyihlo bangilinga, bengihlola, basebebona imisebenzi yami okweminyaka engamatshumi amane;" 
Hebrews3:10 ngakho ngasithukuthelela lesosizukulwana, ngathi: Bayaduha kokuphela enhliziyweni; lalaba kabazazanga indlela zami;" 
Hebrews3:11 ngaze ngafunga ekuthukutheleni kwami ngathi: Kabayikungena ekuphumuleni kwami. 
Hebrews3:12 Nanzelelani, bazalwane, hlezi kuzakuba khona loba nini phakathi komunye wenu inhliziyo embi yokungakholwa, ekuduheni kuNkulunkulu ophilayo;" 
Hebrews3:13 kodwa khuthazanani; 
Hebrews3:14 ngoba sesibe ngabahlanganyeli bakaKristu, uba-ke sibambisisa;" 
Hebrews3:15 kusathiwa: Lamuhla uba lilizwa ilizwi lakhe, lingazenzi zibe lukhuni inhliziyo zenu, njengekucunuleni." 
Hebrews3:16 Ngoba abanye labo abaphuma eGibhithe ngoMozisi. 
Hebrews3:17 Kodwa ngobani athukutheliswa yibo okweminyaka engamatshumi amane? Kakusibo labo abonayo yini, abazidumbu zabo zawela enkangala?" 
Hebrews3:18 Ngobani-ke afunga kibo? 
Hebrews3:19 Ngakho siyabona ukuthi babengelakungena. 
Hebrews4:1 Ngakho, kasesabe, hlezi, lapho sisekhona isithembiso sokungena ekuphumuleni kwakhe, kube khona omunye wenu obonakala ukufinyelela kukho;" 
Hebrews4:2 ngoba lathi satshunyayezwa ivangeli, njengabo kulabo abalizwayo;" 
Hebrews4:3 ngoba thina esikholwayo siyangena ekuphumuleni, njengoba watsho ukuthi." 
Hebrews4:4 Ngoba utshilo; 
Hebrews4:5 lakul indawo uthifuthi: Kabayikungena ekuphumuleni kwami. 
Hebrews4:6 Ngakho lokhu kusalele ukuthi abanye bangene kukho, lalabo ngokungalaleli," 
Hebrews4:7 ubuye aqume usuku oluthile athi: Lamuhla, utsho ngoDavida uba lizalizwa ilizwi lakhe, lingazenzi zibe lukhuni inhliziyo zenu." 
Hebrews4:8 Ngoba uba uJoshuwa wayebaphumuzile, wayengayikukhuluma emva kwalokhu ngolunye usuku." 
Hebrews4:9 Ngakho kubasalele abantu bakaNkulunkulu ukuphumula kwesabatha. 
Hebrews4:10 Ngoba ongenileyo ekuphumuleni kwakhe laye usephumule emisebenzini yakhe, njengoNkulunkulu kweyakhe." 
Hebrews4:11 Ngakho asikhuthalele ukungena kulokhokuphumula, ukuze kungabi lowela kulesisibonelo." 
Hebrews4:12 Ngoba ilizwi likaNkulunkulu. 
Hebrews4:13 Futhi kakulalutho oludaliweyo olungabonakaliyo phambi kwakhe zisobala emehlweni akhe esilokuzilanda kuye. 
Hebrews4:14 Ngakho lokhu silompristi omkhulu kakhulu sethu. 
Hebrews4:15 Ngoba kasilaye. 
Hebrews4:16 Ngakho ngesikhathi esifaneleyo.

Hebrews5:2 ongababekezelela; 
Hebrews5:3 njalo ngenxa yalokhu kufanele ukuthi anikelele izono, njengokwabantu, kunjalo langokwakhe." 
Hebrews5:4 Futhi kakulamuntu. 
Hebrews5:5 Ngokunjalo loKristu kazidumisanga, lamuhla mina ngikuzele."

Hebrews5:9 esephelelisiwe;

Hebrews5:11 Esilokunengi esingakutsho.

Hebrews5:13 Ngoba wonke odla uchago kalalwazi olupheleleyo elizwini lokulunga; ngoba uyingane.

Hebrews7:1 Ngoba uMelkizedeki, owahlangabeza uAbrahama mhla ebuya ekubulaleni amakhosi, wasembusisa," 
Hebrews7:2 uAbrahama laye wamabela okwetshumi kwakho konke; 
Hebrews7:3 kalayise, kalanina, kalasendo, kalakuqala kwensuku kumbe ukuphela kwempilo, kodwa esenziwe wafanana leNdodana kaNkulunkulu." 
Hebrews7:4 Bonani-ke ukuthi mkhulu kangakanani lo, ngitsho amnika okwetshumi kwezimpango." 
Hebrews7:5 Lalabo abavela emadodaneni kaLevi; 
Hebrews7:6 kodwa yena ongabalelwa osendweni lwabo, wemukela okwetshumi." 
Hebrews7:7 Njalo kungelakuphikwa ngitsho ukuthi: Omncinyane ubusiswa ngomkhulu. 
Hebrews7:8 Lapha-ke abantu abafayo bemukela okwetshumi; kodwa lapho esemukela lowookufakazwa. 
Hebrews7:9 Kungatshiwo-ke, uLevi laye owemukela okwetshumi wanikela okwetshumi ngoAbrahama;" 
Hebrews7:10 ngoba wayesesekhalweni lukayise emhlangabeza. 
Hebrews7:11 Ngakho-ke uba kwakukhona ukuphelela, lokungatshiwo ngokwendlela kaAroni?" 
Hebrews7:12 Ngoba uba ubupristi buphendulwa, kuyadingeka ukuthi kube khona lokuphendulwa komlayo." 
Hebrews7:13 Ngoba lowo okukhulunywa ngaye lezizinto ungowesinye isizwe, okungabanga khona kuso owanakekela ilathi." 
Hebrews7:14 Ngoba kusobala ukuthi iNkosi yethu, isizwe uMozisi angakhulumanga lutho ngaso mayelana lobupristi." 
Hebrews7:15 Njalo kusesobala ngokwengezelelwe kakhulu, uba sekusima omunye umpristi njengokofuzo lukaMelkizedeki," 
Hebrews7:16 ongenziwanga ngokomthetho wesimiso senyama, kodwa ngokwamandla empilo engelakuphela;" 
Hebrews7:17 ngoba ufakaza kuze kube nininini ngokohlobo lukaMelkizedeki. 
Hebrews7:18 Ngoba ukubekwa eceleni komthetho wokuqala kwenziwa ngenxa yobuthakathaka lokungasizi lutho kwawo; 
Hebrews7:19 ngoba umlayo ngalo kuNkulunkulu. 
Hebrews7:20 Njalo okungangokuthi k enziwa nga ngaphandle kwesifungo," 
Hebrews7:21 (ngoba bona baba ngabapristi ngaphandle kwesifungo, kodwa yena ngesifungo, ngalowo owathi kuye: INkosi yafunga yathi: Wena ungumpristi kuze kube nininini ngokohlobo lukaMelkizedeki)" 
Hebrews7:22 ngalokho uJesu waba yisibambiso. 
Hebrews7:23 Lalabo babebanengi ababa ngabapristi, ngoba bavinjelwa yikufa ukuthi bahlale njalo;" 
Hebrews7:24 kodwa lo, ngenxa yokuthi uhlala kuze kube phakade, ulobupristi obungadluliyo." 
Hebrews7:25 Ngenxa yalokho laye ulamandla okusindisa ngokupheleleyo. 
Hebrews7:26 Ngoba umpristi omkhulu; 
Hebrews7:27 ongadingi insuku ngensuku mhla ezinikela yena. 
Hebrews7:28 Ngoba umlayo uyamisa abantu babe ngabapristi abakhulu, abalobuthakathaka kuze kube nininini." 
Hebrews8:1 Ngakho isiqokoqela sezinto esazikhulumayo yikuthi: Silompristi omkhulu," 
Hebrews8:2 isikhonzi, njalo kungesimuntu;" 
Hebrews8:3 ngoba wonke umpristi omkhulu umiselwe ukunikela iminikelo lemihlatshelo. 
Hebrews8:4 Ngoba uba ubesemhlabeni, ubengeyikuba ngumpristi lakanye, ngoba bakhona abapristi abanikela iminikelo ngokomlayo," 
Hebrews8:5 abakhonza isibonelo ukuthi wenze zonke izinto njengomfanekiso owaboniswa wona entabeni. 
Hebrews8:6 Kodwa khathesi-ke uzuze inkonzo. 
Hebrews8:7 Ngoba uba leso sivumelwanoesakuqala besingasoleki, bekungayikudingwa indawo yesesibili." 
Hebrews8:8 Ngoba ebasola uthi, njalo ngizakwenza isivumelwano esitsha lendlu kaIsrayeli lendlu kaJuda;" 
Hebrews8:9 esingenjengesivumelwano engasenza laboyise. 
Hebrews8:10 Ngoba yilesi engizavumelana ngaso lendlu kaIsrayeli emva kwalezonsuku, itsho iNkosi, ngizafaka zabo ngiyibhale; ngibe nguNkulunkulu kibo, bona-ke bazakuba ngabantu kimi." 
Hebrews8:11 Njalo kabayikufundisa ngulowo lalowo umakhelwane wakhe, njalo ngulowo lalowo umfowabo, esithi: Yazi iNkosi; ngoba bonke bazangazi, kusukela komncinyane wabo kuze kufike komkhulu wabo." 
Hebrews8:12 Ngoba ngizakuba lesihawu ekungalungini kwabo, lezono zabo lobubi babo kangisayikukukhumbula."

Hebrews9:28 ngokunjalo uKristu, kube lusindiso."

Hebrews12:1 Ngakho-ke lathi sigonjolozelwe liyezi elikhulu kangaka labafakazi, asilahle konke okusindayo lesono," 
Hebrews12:2 sikhangele kuJesu umqalisi lomphelelisi wokholo lwethu ngakwesokunene sesihlalo sobukhosi sikaNkulunkulu. 
Hebrews12:3 Ngakho mqapheliseni emiphefumulweni yenu. 
Hebrews12:4 Kalikamelani la khokuze kube segazini lisilwa lesono; 
Hebrews12:5 njalo selikhohliwe inkuthazo, nxa usolwa yiyo;" 
Hebrews12:6 ngoba iNkosi iyalaya emthandayo; njalo itshaye ngesiswepu yonke indodana eyemukelayo. 
Hebrews12:7 Uba likhuthazela ekulayweni, uNkulunkulu uyaliphatha njengamadodana?" 
Hebrews12:8 Kodwa uba lingelakulaywa, okuthi bonke bangabahlanganyeli bakho, ngakho lingabokufetshwa njalo kalisiwo amadodana." 
Hebrews12:9 Futhi-ke sasilabo obaba benyama yethu aba si layayo njalo sa ba hlonipha kakhulu kula lokho, siphile?" 
Hebrews12:10 Ngoba bona kambe ba si laya okwensuku ezinlutshwana, njengokubona kwabo; kodwa yena kube yikusizakala kwethu, ukuze si hlanganyele ubungcwele bakhe." 
Hebrews12:11 Lakho konke ukulaywa okukhona kakubonakali angathi ngokwentokozo, kodwa ngokosizi; emva kwalokho-ke kuyabalethela isithelo." 
Hebrews12:12 Ngakho qinisani; 
Hebrews12:13 njalo lenzele inyawo zenu. 
Hebrews12:14 Nxwanelani ukuthula; 
Hebrews12:15 liqaphelisa ukuze kungabi khona osilelayo yokubaba ikhathaze, njalo ngayo abanengi bangcoliswe;" 
Hebrews12:16 kakungabi lamuntu oyisifebe ngokudla okukodwa. 
Hebrews12:17 Ngoba liyazi ukuthi lemva kwalokho, esethanda ukudla ilifa." 
Hebrews12:18 Ngoba kalizanga entabeni engathintwa, lemlilweni ovuthayo, lekufiphaleni, lemnyameni, lesivunguvungwini," 
Hebrews12:19 lekukhaleni kophondo bancenga ukuthi kungabe kusa khulunywailizwi kibo; 
Hebrews12:20 ngoba babengelakukumela lokho okwalaywayo ukuthi: Ngitsho lenyamazana uba ithinta intaba, izakhandwa ngamatshe, kumbe itshokwe ngomtshoko;" 
Hebrews12:21 njalo, kwakusesabeka kangaka lokho okwabonwayo, uMozisi wathi: Ngilovalo, ngiyathuthumela." 
Hebrews12:22 Kodwa lize entabeni iSiyoni," 
Hebrews12:23 lemhlanganweni omkhulu lebandleni," 
Hebrews12:24 lakuJesu umlamuli. 
Hebrews12:25 Qaphelani ukuthi lingamali okhulumayo. Ngoba uba bengaphephanga, kakhulu kangakanani thina esimfulathelayo lowo okhulumaevela emazulwini;" 
Hebrews12:26 olizwi lakhe ukunyikinya kungeyisiwo umhlaba wodwa, kodwa lezulu." 
Hebrews12:27 Lalokhu ukuthi:Ngiza phinda kanye, kutshengisa ukususwa kwezinto ezinyikinywayo, kungathi ezenziweyo, ukuze kusale izinto ezinganyikinywayo." 
Hebrews12:28 Ngakho njengoba sisemukela umbuso ongelakunyikinyekiswa, asibe lomusa esingamkhonza uNkulunkulu;" 
Hebrews12:29 ngoba-ke uNkulunkulu. 
Hebrews13:1 Kalume njalo uthando lobuzalwane. 
Hebrews13:2 Lingakhohlwa ukungenisa izihambi. 
Hebrews13:3 Khumbulani, ngokungathi lani liphethwe kubiemzimbeni." 
Hebrews13:4 Umtshado. 
Hebrews13:5 Indlela yempilo kayingabi ngeyokuthanda imali. 
Hebrews13:6 Ngakho singatsho ngesibindi sithi: INkosi ingumsizi wami, njalo kangiyikwesaba umuntu azakwenza kimi." 
Hebrews13:7 Khumbulani abakhokheli benu. 
Hebrews13:8 UJesu Kristu unguye lalamuhla lephakadeni. 
Hebrews13:9 Lingaduhiswa yikhoababebambelela kukho. 
Hebrews13:10 Silalo ilathi, abangelalungelo lokudla kulo abakhonza ithabhanekele." 
Hebrews13:11 Ngoba lezozinyamazana. 
Hebrews13:12 Ngakho laye uJesu, ukuze angcwelise." 
Hebrews13:13 Ngakho-ke asiphumele kuye. 
Hebrews13:14 Ngoba kasilawo umuzi omiyo lapha. 
Hebrews13:15 Ngakho asinikele sivuma ibizo lakhe. 
Hebrews13:16 Kodwa lingakhohlwa ukwenza okuhle lokuphana. 
Hebrews13:17 Lalelani abakhokheli benu, lizehlisele ngaphansi kwabo, njalo bengabubuli; ngoba kungalisizi lokhu." 
Hebrews13:18 Sikhulekeleni, sifisa ukuhamba kuhle ezintweni zonke;" 
Hebrews13:19 njalo ngiya li ncenga ngokwengezelelwe kakhulu ukuthi li kwenze lokhu, ukuze ngibuyiselwe kini ngokuphangisa." 
Hebrews13:20 Kungathi uNkulunkulu wokuthula saphakade, iNkosi yethu uJesu," 
Hebrews13:21 angaliphelelisa kuze kube nini lanini. Ameni. 
Hebrews13:22 Kodwa ngiyalincenga, bazalwane, lemukeleni ngesineke ilizwi lenkuthazo." 
Hebrews13:23 Yazini ukuthi umzalwane ukhululwe, uba efika masinyane, ngizalibona ngilaye." 
Hebrews13:24 Bingelelani bonke abakhokheli benu bayalibingelela. 
Hebrews13:25 Umusa kawubelani lonke. Ameni. 
James1:1 UJakobe, ngiyabingelela." 
James1:2 Kubaleni njenge ntokozo yonke," 
James1:3 lisazi ukuthi ukuhlolwa kokholo; 
James1:4 kodwa ukubekezela kakube lomsebenzi opheleleyo, ukuze libe ngabapheleleyo liphelelisiwe, lingasileli ngalutho." 
James1:5 Njalo uba kukhona kini oswele inhlakanipho. 
James1:6 Kodwa kacele ekholweni eliqhutshwa ngumoya lizuliswe. 
James1:7 Ngoba lowomuntu kangacabangi ukuthi uzazuza ulutho eNkosini. 
James1:8 Indoda enhliziyombili. 
James1:9 Lomzalwane ophansi kazincome ekuphakameni kwakhe; 
James1:10 kodwa onothileyo ekuthotshisweni kwakhe. 
James1:11 Ngoba ilanga liphuma lilokutshisa, leluba labo liwohloke, lobuhle bokubonakala kwalo bunyamalale; ngokunjalo lesinothi sizanyamalala ezindleleni zaso." 
James1:12 Ubusisiwe umuntu obekezelela isilingo. 
James1:13 Kakulamuntu olingwayo omele athi: Ngilingwa nguNkulunkulu; ngoba uNkulunkulu kalasilingo sokubi, laye uqobo kalingi muntu." 
James1:14 Kodwa ngulowo lalowo uyalingwa, lapho ehudulwa ngezakhe inkanuko, ehugwa;" 
James1:15 kuthi lapho inkanuko isikhulelwe ibelethe isono. 
James1:16 Lingakhohliswa, bazalwane bami abathandekayo." 
James1:17 Sonke isipho esihle, kumbe isithunzi sokuphenduka." 
James1:18 Ngokuthanda kwakhe zezidalwa zakhe. 
James1:19 Ngakho, bazalwane bami abathandekayo, wonke umuntu umele aphangise ukuzwa, aphuze ukukhuluma;" 
James1:20 ngoba ukuthukuthela kwendoda kakwenzi ukulunga kukaNkulunkulu. 
James1:21 Ngakho selihlubule amanyala wonke. 
James1:22 Kodwa banini ngabenzi belizwi lina ngokwenu. 
James1:23 Ngoba uba umuntu; 
James1:24 ngoba iyazibuka, ibisisuka, ibisihle ikhohlwa ukuthi ibinjani." 
James1:25 Kodwa lowo okhangelisisa. 
James1:26 Uba umuntu phakathi kwenu esithi uyakholwa. 
James1:27 Ukukholwa. 
James2:1 Bazalwane bami, kungeyisikho ngokubandlulula abantu libe lokholo." 
James2:2 Ngoba uba kungena emhlanganweni wenu indoda elendandatho yegolide lesembatho esikhazimulayo, besekungena longumyanga olesembatho esingcolileyo," 
James2:3 beselinanzelela: Wena mana lapho; loba: Hlala lapha ngaphansi kwesenabelo senyawo zami; 
James2:4 pho, kalibandlululi phakathi kwenu" 
James2:5 Zwanini, bazalwane bami abathandekayo. UNkulunkulu kabakhethanga?" 
James2:6 Kodwa lina libadumazile abayanga 
James2:7 Bona kabalihlambazi? 
James2:8 Uba liphelelisa umlayo wobukhosi, lenza kuhle;" 
James2:9 kodwa uba libandlulula. 
James2:10 Ngoba loba ngubani ogcina umlayo wonke, kodwa akhubeke kokukodwa kuyo yonke." 
James2:11 Ngoba owathi: Ungafebi; uba-ke ungafebi, kodwa ubulala, usungumeqi womlayo." 
James2:12 Khulumani ngokunjalo lenze njalo, njengabazakwahlulelwa ngomlayo wenkululeko." 
James2:13 Ngoba ukwahlulelwa okungelasihawu sizincoma kukho ukwahlulela. 
James2:14 Kusizani, bazalwane bami, uba umuntu esithi ulokholo, kodwa engelamisebenzi? Lolokholo lungamsindisa yini?" 
James2:15 Uba-ke umzalwane loba umzalwanekazi njalo beswela ukudla kwensuku ngensuku," 
James2:16 omunye wenu abesesithi kibo? 
James2:17 Kunjalo lokholo, uba lungelamisebenzi, lufile ngokwalo." 
James2:18 Kodwa omunye uzakuthi: Wena ulokholo, mina-ke ngilemisebenzi: Ngitshengisa ukholo lwakho ngaphandle kwemisebenzi yakho, lami emisebenzini yami ngizakutshengisa." 
James2:19 Wena uyakholwa ukuthi uNkulunkulu munye, njalo athuthumele." 
James2:20 Kodwa uyathanda ukwazi yini, O siphukuphuku?" 
James2:21 UAbrahama ubaba wethu kalungisiswanga yini ngemisebenzi, esenikele indodana yakhe uIsaka phezu kwelathi?"

James2:23 kwasekugcwaliswa umbhalo.

James2:25 Ngokunjalo-ke loRahabi izithunywa, ese zi phumise ngenye indlela?" 
James2:26 Ngoba njengalokhu umzimba ngaphandle. 
James3:1 Lingabi abanengi, bazalwane bami, lisazi ukuthi sizakwemukela isigwebo esikhulu." 
James3:2 Ngoba sonke siyakhubeka ezintweni ezinengi. 
James3:3 Khangela, sifaka emilonyeni yamabhiza ukuze asilalele, sibe sesiqondisa umzimba wonke wawo kwenye indlela." 
James3:4 Khangela, lemikhumbi, lanxa imikhulu kangaka njalo iqhutshwa yimimoya elamandla, iyaqondiswa kwenye indlela ngephinyana nje, lapho isifiso somtshayeli esifuna khona." 
James3:5 Lunjalo lolimi luyisitho esincinyane, kanti luzincoma kakhulu. Khangela, umlilo omncinyane uyatshisa izigodo ezingakanani!" 
James3:6 Ulimi. 
James3:7 Ngoba yonke imvelo yokubili izinyamazana lezinyoni, kokubili ezihuquzelayo lezidalwa zolwandle, iyathanjiswa njalo isithanjisiwe ngemvelo yabantu;" 
James3:8 kodwa ulimi kakulamuntu ongaluthambisa; luyibubi obungelakunqotshwa, lugcwele ubuhlungu obubulalayo."

James3:11 Kambe umthombo emgodini munye ungagobhoza yini okumnandi lokubabayo? 
James3:12 Kambe, bazalwane bami, umkhiwa ungathela imihlwathi yini, loba ivini umkhiwa? Ngokunjalo kakulamthombo oveza amanzi alitshwayi lamnandi." 
James3:13 Ngubani ohlakaniphileyo loqedisisayo.

James3:16 Ngoba lapho okukhona umhawu, lapho kukhona isiphithiphithi lazo zonke izenzo ezimbi." 
James3:17 Kodwa inhlakanipho.

2Peter1:1 USimoni Petro, inceku lomphostoli kaJesu Kristu:" 
2Peter1:2 Kakwandiswe kini umusa lokuthula. 
2Peter1:3 Njengamandla akhe obuNkulunkulu asinike zonke izinto ezimayelana lempilo lokukhonza uNkulunkulu; 
2Peter1:4 okungakho siphiwe izithembiso ezinkulu kakhulu leziligugu, ukuze ngalezi libe ngabahlanganyeli bemvelo yobuNkulunkulu." 
2Peter1:5 Njalo ngenxa yalokhu-ke selenze yonke inkuthalo, yengezelelani ukulunga ekholweni lwenu," 
2Peter1:6 lelwazini ukuzithiba," 
2Peter1:7 lekwesabeni uNkulunkulu.

Revelation22:15 kodwa ngaphandle kukhona. 
Revelation22:16 Mina Jesu ngithume ingilosi yami ukufakaza. 
Revelation22:17 UMoya-ke lomakoti. 
Revelation22:18 Ngoba ngiyafakaza kuye wonke ozwa amazwi esiprofetho salolugwalo: Uba umuntu esengeza kulezizinto, uNkulunkulu uzakwengezelela kuye izinhlupheko ezilotshwe kulolugwalo;" 
Revelation22:19 njalo uba umuntu esusa okwamazwi ogwalo lwalesisiprofetho, uNkulunkulu uzasusa isabelo sakhe, l e zint weniezilotshiweyo kulolugwalo." 
Revelation22:20 Ofakaza lezizinto uthi: Yebo, ngiyeza masinyane"
